# **Legend Chapter 829**

『Heh…Flame Emperor’s Crimson Armour, huh? The fact that you could use Overlord’s Armour was surprising enough, but to think you managed to improve on it, that’s Rei for you.』

Elena spoke through the projection of the Paired Orb with an amused smile.

Set was next to Rei as he spoke with Elena and the small dragon, Yellow, was similarly next to Elena.

With all the corpses on the battlefield disposed of, Rei was spending his night talking with Elena over the Paired Orbs before his departure to the Imperial Capital the next day.

Normally, it wouldn’t have been surprising for Vihera to show up at this time, but surprisingly she didn’t make an appearance.

It seemed that she had been called to help with the preparations for tomorrow’s departure.

Although Vihera claimed that she had run away from the Bestir Empire, that didn’t mean that her popularity and ability had disappeared as well.

In fact, during the time when Mercurio’s army was still called the rebel army, many people had joined out of admiration for her..

Considering that, it wasn’t surprising for her to be entrusted with an important role during the return to the Imperial Capital.

Although Vihera was reluctant, she still accepted her role after it was requested by Mercurio, Frizione, and Shurus.

That said, it was only on the condition that she could keep her current clothing, which both Frizione and Shurus had raised concerns over.

「Noiz was very strong. Even though I won in the end, it felt like he gave the win to me, so there’s still a long way for me to go before I reach S rank.」

『…But, Rei, wouldn’t it be better to get to A rank first? You’re still only B rank right now.』

「Ah…that’s true. It wasn’t like the Adventurer’s Guild asked me to join the civil war either, I joined on my own, so it won’t count towards my guild rank.」

Rei sighed at Elena’s words.

From Theorem’s perspective, it was impossible for him to borrow Rei as a fighting force in the civil war by sending a request to the Adventurer’s Guild in the Mireana Kingdom…or even to Gilm’s guild branch. As a result the request had been directly passed to Rei by Theorem and Vihera.

They then managed to secretly ally with both the Aristocratic faction, through Elena, and the Neutral faction, through Rei, but the guild had nothing to do with it in either case.

In other words, from the guilds perspective, despite all of Rei’s contributions in the civil war, he still hadn’t completed any official requests.

『Well, in your case, your rank isn’t that important, so it’s fine, right? It’s not like you’re that desperate to reach A or S rank, are you?』

「Considering the rank restrictions on request, I would like to have as high of a rank as possible. There’s also the matter of magic stones.」

In the first place, the reason why Rei had been speeding through adventurer ranks was so that he could accept requests with rank restrictions.

Specifically, monster subjugation requests with rank restrictions.

His goal was to obtain the magic stones of stronger monsters, so while he wasn’t as concerned about his adventurer rank, now that he was B rank, he still felt that getting to a higher rank would be better.

Especially against S rank monsters like Dragons, sending a B rank adventurer…especially a solo adventurer, would normally be considered a death sentence. So, even if a request to hunt one came up, he probably wouldn’t be able to accept it.

『I see. But it’s over now, so I guess there’s nothing you can do.』

「That makes sense, now that you’ve said it.」

Rei sighed and stroked Set’s head as he watched him and Yellow chatting away with each other.

『So…when exactly do you plan on coming back? Considering we need to explain things to Daska-sama as well, I think it would be best for you to return as soon as possible.』

「Oh…about that.」

Rei seemed too embarrassed to speak after hearing Elena’s question.

Was she hoping that…he ride Set back to Gilm to see her in person?

Although he could guess what Elena was thinking, Rei could only shake his head.

「The truth is, there was a unit I led during the civil war. …Well, I never really commanded them myself, but they were considered by direct subordinates. About half the unit has said they want to go back to Gilm with me.」

It was only among those who had been affected by the tainted Wyvern leather armour at first, but as word spread through the guerrilla unit, more and more people said that they wanted to go to Gilm as well.

Some admired Rei’s strength while others were captivated by Set’s cuteness, but one of the biggest factors was that if they went with Rei to Gilm, there would be no risk of having to fight Rei even if war broke out between the Bestir Empire and Mireana Kingdom again.

Having been trained by Rei, they knew just how strong he and Set were…and they had also witnessed their power first hand, so they knew that fighting Rei and Set meant certain death.

Noiz was just as strong as Rei, but while Noiz was better at individual combat, Rei had many methods of attacking a wide area, making him more dangerous to fight compared to Noiz.

It wasn’t just the guerrilla unit who thought that, many from the punitive force felt the same.

…No, in the case of the punitive force, they had fought Rei and Set directly, so they probably never wanted to do that ever again.

Still, leaving the country they had lived in for so long was no small matter.

In that sense, the guerrilla unit, who had worked closely with Rei within Mercurio’s army, was quite unique.

『Hmm, I see. Your unit was made up of pretty elite fighters, wasn’t it?』

「Yeah. But, well, there’s a few reasons that they now feel uncomfortable staying in the Bestir Empire.」

『Uncomfortable?』

Elena seemed doubtful.

She had previously heard from Rei that the unit he led was an elite force within Mercurio’s army.

That meant those who were part of it were undoubtedly among the best in the Bestir Empire in terms of strength and discipline.

Why would such people feel uncomfortable in their own country?

But once she heard Rei’s explanation, she had to agree with the reasoning to a certain extent.

During the final battle, even if it was part of an enemy trap, they had ended up fighting against their own allies. Naturally, this made others view them quite harshly.

『…But, surely there are those who understand what happened?』

「Yeah. That’s why they’re not all coming with me. The vice-captain is Theorem’s subordinate, so he’s definitely not coming. But the ones who are coming back with me are also bringing their families and partners, so our travel speed is going to be slow. In addition, we have to transport Rhodes.」

『Rhodes? What happened to Rhodes?』

「He’s in a coma right now, with no signs of waking up. …I don’t know what to tell Elk. I just hope he regains consciousness soon.」

Elena frowned at Rei’s words.

She knew Rhodes as well.

Or rather, she knew Elk, and had been introduced to his son, Rhodes, through him.

While they weren’t particularly close, hearing that someone she knew was in a coma would naturally make her feel uncomfortable.

『Should I send word to Gilm from here? You need to let Daska-sama know you won anyway. At that time I can also…』

「Yeah, maybe.」

Rei hesitated at Elena’s suggestion.

If Elk and Min were to see Rhodes still stuck in a coma, the shock would be massive.

But if he told them now, it would still take quite a while for Rei and the others to actually get back to Gilm.

Letting them spend all that time worrying about their son seemed cruel.

Rei was undecided on what the best course of action was, but eventually shook his head.

「Let’s not tell them for now. Elk and Min might not even be in Gilm right now. I want to keep the number of people who know to minimum.」

But, even as Rei said that, he could imagine Elk and Min staying in Gilm, worrying about Rhodes.

『You think so? But…an A rank adventurer like ELk might know how to deal with whatever happened to Rhodes. Considering that, I think it would be best to let them know.』

「…I guess so. Compared to a B rank adventurer like me, it’s true that he would probably know more. Elk aside, Min is also a mage, so she should have a much better understanding of things as well.」

Elena smiled at Rei’s words.

That wasn’t how one would normally evaluate a title holding adventurer like Elk.

However, anyone who knew Elk…and more importantly, Min, would probably agree with Rei.

『So?』

「Yeah, sorry to go back and forth, but it would be a great help if you could inform Elk about the situation. In addition…once they hear about Rhodes, unless they’re on an request, they’ll definitely head this way. At the very least, Elk will and Min won’t stop him.」

『That’s true.』

Elena didn’t seem to doubt Rei’s line of thinking as she nodded.

『Alright then. I’ll let them know when I contact Daska-sama. …Still, you really do stand out, don’t you Rei? Defeating the Immovable Noiz.』

「Like I said before, I didn’t really win. It felt like he let me have the victory. Noiz saw my Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour, an improvement of the Overlord’s Armour he used, and seemed to be satisfied enough to leave. If we had kept fighting, I probably would have lost. …Actually, I can’t even say that I’ve mastered this Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour yet.」

Rei said that with a sigh. That said, despite him saying he hadn’t trained much with the skill, he could now use it much better than Overlord’s Armour.

『Hmph, I see. …Next time we meet, I’d like you to show me this Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour of yours.』

「What, you want to see it? I can show you it now. You can see it over the Paired Orb, right?」

Do you want me to show it to you now? That was what Rei thought, but Elena shot him a dissatisfied look.

『Idiot. You really don’t know how to treat a woman, do you, Rei?』

「…Eh?」

He thought about Elena’s words for a moment…before realising what she meant.

Basically, she was just using it as an excuse to tell him to come back to see her.

「Ah…right, I’m sorry. That’s what you meant.」

『Rei, you should really learn more about etiquette for these things. …Well, not that I’m one to talk about this.』

Elena’s strength wasn’t exactly in the romantic department either.

Still, as a maiden in love, she had become more attentive to the finer details.

Having a powerful rival like Vihera at Rei’s side had also sharpened her instincts for such matters as well.

Lastly, there was Ara, who was always by her side, giving her slightly incorrect knowledge on matters of love.

Of course, it wasn’t like Ara was deliberately teaching Elena the wrong things. But, like Elena, Ara was also someone who had prioritised physical training with Elena over showing up at parties with other noble ladies.

Because of that, everything that Ara knew on the matter was learned from bits and pieces of conversations she had overheard from other noble ladies discussing the topic, resulting in a rather warped understanding.

Since Ara had been born into a noble family, she would have normally been taught such things…but having admired Elena since childhood, she ended up spending her free time training as well, making her equally clueless with regards to romance.

『Anyway, putting that aside, when exactly do you think you will return?』

「Let me think. I’d like to get back to Gilm before winter properly sets in. We are leaving for the Imperial Capital tomorrow and will have a victory parade when we get there…it seems like there will be various ceremonies after that, but those are mainly for the higher ups like Mercurio and Theorem. Once I receive my reward, I can start heading back.」

Considering he had to receive his reward and the time those following him back needed to get ready, Rei estimated it would be another three to four days.

This would normally be cutting it very close for so many people…but in this case, they had Rei.

Rei could store all the luggage they had into the Misty Ring, so they only needed to carry the bare essentials on them for the journey.

This would also increase their travel speed.

A carriage filled with household items was very different to a carriage carrying only people, with regards to the speed at which horses could pull the carriages and the fatigue of the horses themselves.

As for the carriages, Theorem had already promised Rei that those in the guerrilla unit who wanted to go with Rei would receive a carriage and horses as part of their reward.

Of course, those who didn’t want either would receive more money instead.

This was the result of negotiations after so many of them expressed their desire to go with Rei to Gilm.

『…I see. So, I guess I won’t see you until spring then.』

Elena spoke with a little loneliness through the Paired Orb and Rei found himself captivated by her melancholic beauty.

+++

# **830**

『Well then, we’re heading for the Imperial Capital. …No, we’re returning home! Both armies may have their own thoughts on the subject, but I expect everyone to not cause any trouble. Remember, you are now marching under Prince Mercurio’s banner. No causing trouble, and definitely no fighting among each other. Don’t disappoint His Highness.』

Theorem’s voice echoed over the Brissa Plain.

Amplified by a mage’s wind magic, his words reached every soldier in both Mercurio’s army and the punitive force.

With that, both forces departed the Brissa Plains, the place of the largest and final battle of this civil war.

Moving ahead of both armies was Rei, the one who had made the biggest name for himself and proven his strength during the civil war.

As always, he was riding on Set’s back, advancing towards the Imperial Capital with an aura that could only be described as majestic.

The main reason Rei was at the front wasn’t just due to his high capability as a scout to detect bandits or monsters first. Rather, it was largely because he and Set had earned massive renown on the battlefield.

Rei and Set were already well known in the Bestir Empire due to the Spring War.

But after coming second in the fighting tournament and earning the most achievements in the following civil war, it was clear to everyone that he had been the most important person in the war.

With someone like that leading the march, anyone thinking of starting trouble in the back had to think twice out of respect or fear of Rei.

Ideally, for morale, Mercurio, the leader of the army, should have been at the front. But considering the potential danger, that wasn’t really an option.

It might have been different if he were in a heavily fortified carriage like Frizione, but while the First Princess could get away with riding inside one, Prince Mercurio needed to show his bravery now that the civil war was over, so he avoided riding in a carriage like that.

Of course, if there was any real danger, he would have rode inside a fortified carriage regardless, but with Theorem, Vihera, and Digma, for some reason, surrounding him, his safety was all but guaranteed.

「…Well, from what I can see, there isn’t a single enemy around.」

「But, Captain Rei, we still shouldn’t let our guard down.」

The one speaking to Rei was Pernyx, the vice captain and actual commander of the guerrilla unit.

As Rei was leading the march, the guerrilla unit was naturally behind him.

Those who had been isolated in the medical clinic due to the Wyvern leather armour incident had since returned to the unit.

Because of that, one of the reason Rei had accepted the role of leading the march to the Imperial Capital was to restore the guerrilla unit’s reputation.

As a unit under his command, he couldn’t stand them being called traitors just because they fell for Kabajid’s trap.

That said, it was well known within Mercurio’s army that the guerrilla unit was under Rei’s direct command.

Especially since their training was so intense it looked like overkill to outsiders, the sight of the guerrilla unit training had become something of a local spectacle.

Because of that, hardly anyone would call the guerrilla unit traitors to their faces. Even if they did speak of it, it was mostly whispered behind backs so it wouldn’t reach Rei’s ears.

But, the fact such words still reached Rei occasionally was proof that there were plenty of people jealous of the guerrilla unit’s existence.

To be fair, those people had a point.

They argued that despite receiving such preferential treatment, the unit hadn’t achieved results to match.

After the initial confusion settled, the guerrilla unit had managed to defeat soldiers from the punitive force, taking down commanders, knights, and even a few nobles.

Still, the initial infighting had been a huge shock to the members of Mercurio’s army.

「Besides, we’ve defeated and absorbed the punitive force into our own army. Do you really think anyone would mess with us in this situation? At the very least, I don’t think it’s something random bandits from around here would try.」

「Even so. There’s also the possibility of monsters appearing. Especially now, with winter just around the corner. Many monsters come out this time of year trying to store up food for the cold, so we need to be careful.」

「…You do know I am an adventurer, right? Though, that’s fair enough, I’m not that familiar with monsters in the Bestir Empire.」

As Rei replied to Pernyx, who was following behind him, the vice captain continued in a serious tone.

「It’s not so bad around here, but we have to pay particular attention to bear monsters.」

「…Do they hibernate in winter as well?」

「Yes. With regards to that, they aren’t too different form ordinary bears. Of course, depending on the exact species, there are some bear monsters that don’t go into hibernation.」

「Is that so, that’s interesting.」

Rei had a strong impression of bear monsters.

The first monster he had encountered in Elgin was a Water Bear after all, a bear monster that covered itself in water.

(I managed to defeat it back then, but I butchered the materials so badly that it ended up being close to worthless.)

Rei looked up at the sky with a someone distant look in his eyes.

The sky was now dotted with clouds.

It had only been a few days ago when the weather had been perfect with clear autumn skies, but it was now quite gloomy, as if reflecting the inner feelings of the nobles who had sided with the punitive force.

「Captain Rei? What’s wrong?」

A member of the guerrilla unit called out to Rei with some confusion.

Brought back to reality by that voice, Rei shook his head to say it was nothing.

「No, I just remembered when I was thrown into a forest with Set by my master. I suddenly had to fight a monster called a Water Bear.」

「Woah, really!? A Water Bear is a C rank monster, isn’t it!? Fighting something like that before even becoming an adventurer…wait, actually, with Captain Rei and Set-chan, I suddenly feel like it wouldn’t be such a big problem.」

A female former adventurer spoke with surprise before seeming to reach and understanding at her own words.

She wasn’t wrong, for an ordinary person who hadn’t even become an adventurer to fight a C rank monster was basically suicide.

But, with Rei and Set, the monster was the one more deserving of pity.

In reality, that was the case as well. As it was Rei’s first fight after coming to Elgin, he had to learn on the fly, but the fight itself ended in a flawless victory for them.

「Gurururu~!」

Set gave a cry at Rei’s words, as if saying ‘I’m amazing aren’t I!’.

Seeing Set’s reaction brought a warm feeling to the hearts of the members of the guerrilla unit.

「Yeah, the actual fight didn’t take that long. However, it was my first time stripping materials, so I struggled with that. I ended up damaging the Water Bear’s fur quite a bit, so it sold for a very low price.」

「Ah…I see. Yeah, if your first time stripping was on something big like a Water Bear, that would happen. But Captain Rei, you’d never stripped materials before that?」

「Yeah. My master who raised me since I was born did everything for me. And, even he didn’t do it directly, he would use magic to handle it somehow.」

Rei shrugged as he recited his well worn excuse.

「Thanks to that, I can strip materials decently now, but I’m still not exactly good at it. …Compared to other B rank adventurers, I’m still a lot clumsier.」

「Heh, an unexpected weakness.」

「In this case, wouldn’t you call it a flaw rather than a weakness?」

A male guerrilla unit member chimed in after hearing the female member’s words.

「Well, in my case, I used to be a mercenary, so I hardly ever stripped materials from monsters. In that sense, I’m in a similar situation to Captain Rei.」

「Hey, cut it out. Don’t go around saying that you’re the same as Captain Rei. If you’re serious, then go charge into a monster infest mountain on your own to cool your head.」

「That harsh!?」

The man seemed dumbfounded by the sudden rebuke…

「Well, you do have a point…」

Another female member in the unit spoke up, causing the man to look at her hopefully…

「If you want to be on Captain Rei’s level, you should go and ambush Immovable Noiz like Captain Rei did.」

「Hey, wait, hold on just a minute! Is there no one but enemies here!?」

The man cried out in despair, but all he got back were cold stares.

(Pathetic…saying he’s the same as Captain Rei.)

Pernyx kept a straight face while pitying the man who had made the careless remark.

The guerrilla unit led the way back towards the Imperial Capital in high spirits.

Further back behind them, there were moments when the atmosphere between the soldiers of Mercurio’s army and the punitive force felt tense, but Rei and the others didn’t have any response in particular, simply maintaining their vigilance of the surroundings.

They judged that even if things got a bit tense, it wouldn’t actually escalate into a major incident.

Also, if a real disturbance did occur, it wouldn’t be Rei and his unit suppressing it, but the soldiers stationed there.

Since two armies that were enemies just a few days ago were moving together, some friction was inevitable.

In fact, there had been some trouble even while they were disposing of the bodies.

Though, people like Gurgast had been keeping watch to suppress any such trouble.

「Ahh…I wish a monster would show up.」

Someone from the guerrilla unit muttered, as their voice echoed out.

Rather than having to deal with the tense atmosphere behind them, they hoped that a monster would show up, forcing everyone to fight together and bridging the gap between them.

It didn’t have to be a monster, bandits would do as well, but ordinary bandits wouldn’t attack an army of tens of thousands.

Even if they did, they’d probably sneak into the camp at night to steal money or supplies.

That is, if they could slip past the soldiers on night watch.

(No, they’d definitely be spotted if they went near where Set is, but maybe not in other places?)

With an army of tens of thousands, not everyone was diligent after all.

There was a good chance that there were people colluding with bandits, or that bandits had slipped someone inside. And more than anything, with the civil war over, it was a fact that many had let their guard down.

「Thinking about it, it could actually be quite dangerous.」

「Eh? What is dangerous, Captain Rei?」

Someone who overheard Rei’s murmurs asked him, but Rei shook his head to say it was nothing.

「More importantly…」

Rei looked up into the sky.

Clouds still dotted the sky, but it didn’t seem like there would be rain any time soon.

「It’s almost noon, can someone go and ask when we will stop for a break?」

Seeing that the position of the sun had risen considerably, Rei called out to someone nearby.

Checking the time on the pocket watch he took out from the Misty Ring in order to double check, he confirmed that it was just about 30 minutes to noon.

「Woah, Captain Rei. You have a watch!? It looks pretty expensive too.」

「I got it from defeating a bandit gang a while ago.」

A guerrilla unit member exclaimed in surprise after seeing Rei’s pocket watch.

However, that was to be expected.

Watches were rare magic items, not something that could be simply bought with money.

When Rei had first arrived in Gilm, he had visited various shops that sold magic items, but he had never seen one for sale.

You needed money to get a pocket watch, but above all, you needed connections.

Otherwise, you needed luck, just like how Rei had gotten his pocket watch from a mercenary group who had disguised themselves as bandits.

(Thinking about it, maybe asking for another watch as part of the reward for this request would be good. Well, just asking for a watch feels like too little, so maybe I’ll ask for other things as well.)

One of the magic items Ray had his eye on was the one Kabajid had used to kill himself.

A dagger that inflicted deadly poison and even hindered healing magic.

Regarding weapons, Rei basically only used the Death Scythe, throwing spears for ranged attacks.

But it wasn’t like he couldn’t use daggers, and if a scratch could easily become a fatal wound, it was definitely something he wanted to get his hands on.

(But that…is probably difficult. No, more likely impossible.)

It was the magic item that took the life of the First Prince. Naturally, it would be examined strictly and stored away, and the creator would be investigated in great detail.

Thinking about that, he couldn’t exactly ask for it as a reward for participating in the civil war.

(So then… what other magic items can I get? I’m feeling excited, but also kind of worried…it’s a weird feeling.)

Worried might not be the right word, but Ray was slightly concerned about how to react if he was handed something that did not fit his contributions to the war.

Though he knew Theorem and Vihera wouldn’t do something that stupid.

(Mercurio wouldn’t pull something like that because of Vihera… right?)

As he thought about that in his mind, he noticed the man who he had sent out to ask about lunch, so for now, he focused his mind on preparing for the midday meal.

+++

# **831**

A few days had passed since leaving the Brissa Plain, the combined armies traveled along the road unhindered by bandits and monsters, which Rei had initially been concerned about. Eventually, they reached a location where the Imperial Capital could be seen.

「…The Imperial Capital, huh? We were only there recently, but it feels so long ago.」

Rei muttered as he looked towards the Imperial Capital.

Indeed, it hadn’t been that long since he had gone to escort Frizione out.

But even so, it felt like an eternity had passed since he had last seen the city.

Perhaps that was proof of how intense the war had been for Mercurio’s army.

「Captain Rei, Theorem-sama is calling for you. He wants to discuss the victory parade with you.」

A voice called out from behind as Rei was admiring the Imperial Capital.

Turning around, he found Pernyx speaking to him.

His expression was stern as always, but the slight uptick at the corner of his mouth seemed to show that he was also happy to be back at the Imperial Capital.

Rei had now known Pernyx for long enough to recognise the subtle changes in his expression.

「I understand. I’ll head to the back for a bit, so I’ll leave you in command.」

「Yes sir!」

Rei nodded back at Pernyx’s earnest response before gently tapping Set on the back of his neck.

Understanding what Rei meant by that, Set gave a cry before turning around.

The horses of the guerrilla unit weren’t frightened by Set’s actions at all, probably because they had gotten somewhat used to him over the past few days.

They continued moving against the march of the army as they moved towards the center, where all the higher ups were gathered.

When soldiers from Mercurio’s army spotted Rei…or rather, Set, they waved as they took in Set’s adorable figure. However, the army wasn’t only made up of Mercurio’s army at this point, there was also the punitive force.

In fact, the punitive force still outnumbered Mercurio’s army at this point in time.

As a result, many of those soldiers still held significant fear towards Rei and Set, lowering Set’s overall popularity among the army.

「Guru~…」

Set gave a sad cry as several soldiers stiffened up at the sight of him.

Rei stroked Set’s neck.

「We were enemies just a short time ago, so it’s not too surprising for things to be like this. Here, eat this and cheer up a bit.」

Rei took some dried meat out of the Misty Ring before giving it to Set.

Set let out a slightly more energetic cry after grabbing the piece of meat with his beak and eating it.

(He’s rather easy to pacify…no, well, if Set’s happy, then I’m happy too, so it’s fine. I really don’t want to see Set in a bad mood.)

With how much Rei loved Set, he really didn’t want to see Set unhappy.

When Set was unhappy, he would look away from Rei but keep glancing back. But if their eyes met, he would look away again. He would want to talk with Rei, but also wanted to show that he was in a bad mood. While there was something cute about seeing Set sulk like that, Rei didn’t want to Set to sulk if possible.

Regaining his energy after eating the dried meat, Set continued walking against the flow of people before eventually reaching the center.

After spotting Mercurio, Theorem, and the others riding on horses, Rei was approached by one of the knights guarding them.

「Captain Rei, His Highness Mercurio is waiting for you. Please pass through.」

With those words, the knight moved his horse to the side to allow Set to pass through.

As most of the soldiers were on foot, the horses weren’t moving particularly fast.

But even so, the fact that the knight was able to control his horse to such a degree while at walking speed displayed why he had been chosen as one of the people to guard Mercurio.

In addition, although his horse hadn’t spent that much time around Set, it didn’t seem scared or restless, showing that the knight before him really was an elite…probably elite enough to rival the members of the guerrilla unit.

「Yeah, got it.」

After that brief exchange, he approached the group where Mercurio, Theorem, Vihera, and Tilleyle were.

For some reason, Digma was also with them, but no one else seemed particularly concerned about that.

It looked like it wasn’t without reason that Water Dragon Digma was as popular as he was.

Since he had already admitted defeat in battle, he wouldn’t attempt anything strange here.

While a considerable number of nobles were riding in carriages, like Frizione, many others were also on horseback.

This was probably due to the influence of people like Mercurio, Theorem, and Vihera, who were riding on horseback.

Of course, Mercurio wasn’t forcing others to ride on horseback with him.

He was riding on horseback because he needed to show others that he was in charge of the army. At the same time, he did feel more comfortable riding on horseback compared to sitting in a carriage and he also wanted to spend more time with Vihera.

「Hey, you’re here. So, I can get straight to the point?」

「I heard it was about the victory parade?」

「Yes, right. It is about the victory parade…」

Mercurio was about to continue when Theorem interrupted him.

「Your Highness, I can take it from here…」

「…Okay, I understand. I’ll leave it to you.」

「Thank you very much.」

Theorem bowed towards Mercurio before turning to Rei.

He seemed hesitant, as if reluctant to speak.

Having a bad feeling, Rei urged Theorem to go on.

「Regarding the victory parade…the original plan had been for the guerrilla unit to lead the front, but it has been changed to another unit.」

「…Why? I thought we would be leading the parade up until yesterday/」

「It was a request from the castle. Specifically from Prime Minister Pesche.」

Prime Minster Pesche. Theorem’s words reminded him of the man he had met during negotiations to participate in the fighting tournament.

He was extremely overweight, bald, and had a catfish like mustache growing from under his nose.

From the outside, he might appear like a typical useless noble, but as the Prime Minister of the Bestir Empire, he was undoubtedly a capable person.

「Why?」

「It’s a victory parade after all, it would be somewhat damaging to the Bestir Empire’s reputation to have a foreigner lead the parade. They also gave other reasons, but that seemed to be the biggest one.」

Mercurio and Theorem had been in contact with the Imperial Capital immediately after the end of the civil war.

There were tamers and summoners in Mercurio’s army who were capable of sending letters via tamed flying monsters or birds.

After a civil war of this scale, it was only natural that the Imperial Capital would want as much information as they could gather, considering the results would greatly change the balance of power within the Bestir Empire’s upper echelons.

In particular, the Imperial Army had been deeply shocked by the defeat of Shurus, who they supported.

Still, this didn’t make them let down their guard as they kept an eye on neighbouring countries, knowing that it was their job to protect the borders of the Bestir Empire.

「…I see.」

Sensing that there were likely more political reasons behind it, Rei nodded back without arguing.

He closed his eyes for 10 seconds, thinking about something, before speaking again.

「That’s right. Just to be clear, it’s not like the guerrilla unit can’t participate in the victory parade, right?」

That was the only thing Rei wouldn’t back down on.

As Rei looked at Theorem with such a look, Theorem nodded back.

「Of course. The guerrilla unit is one of the most elite units in the army. It’s impossible for them not to participate in the victory parade.」

Rei nodded at Theorem’s words.

「Then it’s fine. I do have my own thoughts, but this is ultimately a matter for the Bestir Empire. As long as you have no intention of neglecting the guerrilla unit, then it’s fine. …But…」

「I understand. Regarding the guerrilla unit, we’ll handle things appropriately. It’s true that the Wyvern incident cause a bit of a stir, but they’ve done many great things since then.」

「…That’s fine I guess. So, is that all?」

Rei’s decision was correct. While he did have his own thoughts on the matter, this was ultimately something that would affect the future of the Bestir Empire after all.

Knowing that, he didn’t try asking for anything more.

「Sorry, I would really have liked the guerrilla unit to be in a more prominent position.」

Rei shrugged his shoulders at Mercurio’s words.

Even though he had won the civil war, Mercurio was still only the next in line to the throne.

Compared to the Prime Minister…one who was trusted by the emperor, his lack of past accomplishments meant that his political position was comparatively weaker.

(Things might have been different if it had been Prince Kabajid who had won.)

Theorem thought to himself.

Unlike Mercurio, Kabajid had a proved track record as the First Prince.

It was enough that even the Prime Minister wouldn’t have been able to ignore him.

In comparison, Mercurio’s lack of achievements, regardless of his talent, placed him in a much weaker position.

(Of course…that’s only for now. I don’t know how the Prime Minster and other nobles view Prince Mercurio, but if they think of him as simply a figurehead who knows nothing, they will come to regret it eventually. I can’t wait to see what they will think at that time…)

Compared to Theorem, who was deep in thought, Rei lightly tapped Set on the neck to tell him that everything was settled and that they could head back.

However…he was stopped by someone chasing after him.

「Rei, don’t you have anything to say to me?」

As Vihera spoke somewhat sulkily, Rei spoke with a troubled expression.

「Well, it’s not that I don’t have anything to say…but you come over during our breaks, right? So I thought that there was no need to go out of my way to speak with you in front of Mercurio.」

「You know…you need to learn a little more about the hearts of women.」

Vihera sighed.

Rei looked taken aback by Vihera’s response.

Seeing that, Vihera sighed again.

「Well, that’s fine. …Anyway, are you going back to the Mireana Kingdom after the victory parade?」

「Yes, that’s the plan. However, it will probably take us some time to actually get back.」

There were members of the guerrilla unit accompanying him on the way back, so it would depend on who was going with him.

As they would likely be traveling by carriage in a group of 20-30 people, it was inevitable that the trip back would take some time.

Explaining the situation, Vihera nodded in understanding.

「I heard about it from Theorem. If possible, I would have also liked to go to Gilm with you, but…」

Her vague words seemed to indicate that she wouldn’t be able to go to Gilm with Rei.

「Are you staying in the Bestir Empire?」

Although Mercurio would be the new crown prince, there was no guarantee that there wouldn’t be some people who would underestimate him politically, if not militarily.

There would also be those who hadn’t participated in the civil war who would reject Mercurio.

Rei asked if Vihera would be staying behind to deal with those people, but she shook her head.

「No, I’ve already run away from this country. It’s one thing to come back for emergency situations like this civil war, but at any other time it would be best for me to not be here.」

「…Won’t Mercurio feel lonely?」

「That’s true. But, if he is to become the crown prince, he can’t rely on me forever. And, with Theorem here, I won’t need to worry about his safety.」

「The Demon Soldiers?」

Only Theorem was able to order the Demon Soldiers around.

The Demon Soldiers had been a major fighting force for Mercurio’s army during the civil war, although they were not with the army at this point in time.

No, that wasn’t entirely correct, there were a small number who were tasked with protecting Mercurio, but there wasn’t a group of them present in the open within the army.

Mercurio had originally wanted to include the Demon Soldiers in the victory parade, but they had expressed their desire through Theorem to remain inconspicuous.

Considering their appearances, that was understandable, but it seemed that they also didn’t want to show off their strength.

While the Demon Soldiers had used their true strength during the civil war, only those who had fought them directly new how strong they really were.

Of course, completely hiding such information about them was impossible, but as long as they remained hidden, people’s attention would eventually be drawn to other topics.

「So, with that all said…what do you plan to do?」

「I’m thinking of going to Exil. I want to see Byune again…」

Vihera replied to Rei’s question with a slightly disappointed look on her face.

+++

# **832**

『WAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAH-!』

Cheers echoed through the Imperial Capital.

They were all directed at Mercurio’s army as it marched through the city.

There was also cheering for Mercuiro and Frizione as they advanced alongside the army.

While Mercurio had been the one to request the victory parade, it was Prime Minister Pesche who had seen to the lavish preparations.

Considering it had been a civil war, a victory parade would normally have been impossible.

Mercurio had been the traitor after all and the army led by the traitor had won by defeating the Empire’s punitive force.

In fact, Pesche had originally intended the victory parade to be fore the punitive force, led by Kabajid and Shurus.

When his master, Emperor Tragist, had heard the results of the final battle, it had exceeded his expectations so much that he couldn’t help but burst into roaring laughter that echoed through the entire audience hall.

While it may have appeared to be a civil war, it was really a war to decide on the heir to the throne.

No, in fact, it could be said that it had been the whole point of the war.

That was why a victory parade had been prepared, regardless of who had won.

(Still, it is a bit strange for father to be so nonchalant about so many deaths.)

Mercurio kept his true feelings to himself has he rode down the main street on horseback while waving to people.

The people seemed excited as he waved at them.

Many cheered loudly as they hoped for the prince to wave back at them.

「Theorem, did Shurus and the rest of the punitive force make it into the Imperial Capital safely?」

Smiling as he waved, Mercurio asked Theorem, who was close by him.

「Yes. They all entered through the north gate.」

「…I see.」

With how big the Imperial Capital was, there were naturally many gates around it.

There was of course the largest one, the main gate, and the gate close to it for nobles.

However, among all the gates, there were also a few special gates.

One of those gates was the gate at the north end of the Imperial Capital.

That gate was primarily used by those with shady backgrounds that couldn’t be made public, and it was through that gate that the defeated punitive force entered the Imperial Capital.

It was at this time that the adventurers, mercenaries, and volunteer soldiers who had participated in the war paid their fines. Some were able to pay immediately while those who didn’t have the money on hand were asked where they lived and told to pay the fine at a later date.

Naturally, some people tried to avoid paying the fine entirely, but considering it was only a few silver coins and the fact that they wouldn’t be able to work in or around the Imperial Capital if they didn’t pay the fine, most paid up.

Also, depending on who the noble was that hired them, some had their fine paid on their behalf…but such nobles were extremely rare.

The whole point of the fine was formal, even if symbolic, punishment after all.

The majority of those who had been paid in advance had no issues paying the fine.

For those who had already spent the money they had been paid, it was still possible to pay up with just a few days of work.

Of course, there were still those who absolutely didn’t want to pay the fine.

Many of those people were overly confident in their own strength, insisting that they still hadn’t lost even after the end of the civil war.

Those people had two options, they could either stubbornly refuse to pay the fine, be captured by the guards, and forced to pay an even larger fine, or escape from the Imperial Capital.

But, even if they could escape, they only place they could go to was away from cities.

Soldiers wouldn’t be sent out to pursue them over a few silver coins, but if it was ever found out that they had run away without paying their fine, they could receive a much heavier fine…or worse, be arrested.

In other words, their only real option would be to hole up in the countryside, out of practical reach from the government.

If they really didn’t like the countryside, leaving the Bestir Empire was also an options.

But, how many people would go that far just to avoid paying a fine of a few silver coins? …It wasn’t that they didn’t exist, but such people were not common.

「I still need Shurus to be in service of me. I’ll leave the groundwork to you.」

「Yes. I will be sending one of my men to Prince Shurus.」

「Is that so, that’s good to hear. As for the nobles who were part of the punitive force…」

「Everything there is fine as well.」

Mercurio and Theorem continued to smile and wave at people as they exchanged words like that.

Another such person receiving cheers was Frizione, who also smiled and waved at people from her carriage window.

「Oh? What’s going on over there?」

「Y-Yes. Well…Princess Frizione is interested in these sorts of things, right?」

The maid riding in the carriage alongside her as her attendant was taken by surprise as she replied.

However, Feizione just nodded in agreement as she smiled and waved at the people they passed by.

「For a woman in the castle, the love lives of others are the ultimate entertainment. This is regardless of whether they are a maid, a noble, or royalty.」

「I certainly won’t deny that, but…」

「Then tell me. Besides, it’s related to the White Rose Knights, so it’s not unrelated to me, right?」

「That is, well…I guess you are right. No, but…」

The maid hesitated at Frizione’s reasoning.

「Come on, just tell me. You saw it, right?」

「…I understand. But, Princess, you should be more concerned about your own love affairs, not the love affairs of others. Being single at your age isn’t good for many reasons. You’ve received marriage proposals from nobles in the Bestir Empire, royalty from neighbouring countries, and even from the Mireana Kingdom.」

「What are you talking about? Love affairs are interesting because they involve other people. Come on, hurry up.」

The maid sighed in resignation before speaking, unable to believe that Frizione was saying such words as she smiled and waved at people.

「Justina was talking to the gatekeeper. They had a lot going on between them at first, especially when we were leaving the Imperial Capital. But, as they continued to talk, they became more comfortable with each other. You wouldn’t have been able to tell from just Justina’s behaviour though.」

「I see. Well then, she’ll have to try a little harder. But, since she went all the way to the noble gate, it’s impossible that she doesn’t hold any feelings, right?」

As Frizione spoke with her maid, the memory of her own escape from the Imperial Capital came to mind.

As White Rose Knight, Justina had had a rather confrontational exchange with a gatekeeper at the noble gate.

But, no matter how it had started, it seemed that the two of them were now on what could be considered friendly terms.

「But, the boy is of noble descent, right? I imagine his partner would need to be of suitable standing as well…the fact that he is a gatekeeper at the noble gate would suggest he is a noble?」

「Yes. However, as he is the third son of Baron Ashdan, there might be some issues with regards to status.」

「…I see. If anything happens, please be prepared to help.」

「Is that okay? I wouldn’t think Baron Ashden would be happy about it.」

Even as a noble of the lowest rank among nobles with land, it wasn’t strange for a baron to consider a political marriage to further the family’s development. …No, in this case, it was precisely because he was a low ranking noble that he would be greedier for higher status.

The rank of knight was a title valid for only a single generation, typically awarded to commoners who had made some level of achievement. So while Justina was a knight, she was a knight with regards to title but not in the military sense.

With further achievements, a knight could become a baron, the difficulty of that was vastly greater than that of becoming a knight in the first place.

「Justina’s father, like Baron Ashden, is extremely ambitious. Isn’t that why Justina joined the White Rose Knights?」

While Justina didn’t have the skills to become a unit captain, Frizione’s impression of her was that she had a good heart.

Of course, those with bad personalities or character were usually rejected before they could join the White Rose Knights.

「In any case, there aren’t many opportunities to meet new people within the White Rose Knights, so let’s just support Justina’s encounter…while making sure that everyone understands the situation, of course.」

「…If anything, aren’t you just looking forward to the whole thing?」

Frizione pretended not to hear the maid’s suspicious tone as she waved to the people outside.

Deciding that there was no point in saying anything more, the maid changed the topic abruptly.

「More importantly, Princess Frizione. With the end of the civil war, it has been decided that Prince Mercurio will be the next in line to the throne. Are you happy about that?」

「Well, who knows?」

「I was thinking that if Princess Frizione had been a little more determined, you could have been next in line instead of Prince Mercurio.」

「…That’s impossible. With Rei at his side, there would have been nothing we could do. That is, unless we had Noiz with us. And…while it is true that I once wanted the throne…I now believe that assisting Mercurio is enough to achieve my goals.」

「Everyone’s…happiness?」

「I wouldn’t go that far. The truth is that many people died in this civil war. It’s impossible to say that everyone will be happy. But…even so, I want to make as many people happy as possible. To achieve that, we need to build friendly relations with the Mireana Kingdom, not a hostile one.」

Of course, Frizione knew that building a friendly relationship with the Mireana Kingdom wouldn’t be easy.

As a land locked empire surrounded by mountains, gaining access to the sea was essential.

Up until now, they had hoped to gain access to the sea by occupying the Mireana Kingdom with their superior national power and military might.

Of course, it wasn’t just about the sea.

While the Mireana Kingdom wasn’t as strong as the Bestir Empire, it was still a powerful nation.

That much was evident from the fact that it still existed despite being at war with the Bestir Empire for so many years.

It wasn’t hard to imagine how much benefit the Bestir Empire would gain from annexing such a country.

Adding on to that, there had been past attempts to establish friendly relations with the Mireana Kingdom, but those efforts had all fallen through.

It was because of those failed attempts at establishing friendly relations that had led to the Bestir Empire current stance of occupation and annexation instead.

「But…if we fight to forcefully annex them, it will undoubtedly spark a fire. Especially now that Rei is with the Mireana Kingdom and it is highly likely that Vihera will side with Rei in the event of war. Rei managed to defeat the S ranked Noiz and Vihera also defeated the A ranked Digma. In addition…Digma has hinted at leaving the Bestir Empire. I don’t think we can achieve much by fighting the Mireana Kingdom.」

Though she was still smiling, Frizoine’s words carried an opposing feeling of melancholy.

「Wow…that’s impressive, Captain Rei.」

Near the rear of Mercurio’s army.

There, the guerrilla soldier spoke in surprise as the people cheered for them.

They had never been treated like this before and excitement began to form in their eyes after the initial surprise.

「That’s true. I definitely didn’t expect them to have made such extensive preparations.」

For Rei, this had been a civil war, so while they had won, he had even considered the possibility that they could be attacked as soon as they entered the Imperial Capital.

However, they hadn’t been greeted by soldiers upon entering, but by cheering crowds.

「I’m sure there are various behind the scenes arrangements, political dealings, and so on…」

「Guru~?」

Set turned around to look at Rei with head tilted.

「No, it’s nothing. Anyway, our top priority right now is to finish this victory parade.」

Rubbing the back of Set’s neck, Rei took off the hood of his Dragon Robe, at Theorem’s request, as they joined the procession in an unfamiliar manner.

Those familiar with the fighting tournament cheered loudly at Rei’s appearance, and even those with untrained eyes couldn’t help but sigh in admiration at Rei’s feminine looking face.

…Of course, the latter also included admiration for Set, who Rei was riding.

+++

# **833**

The victory parade passed through the main street of the Imperial Capital before arriving at it’s end point, the castle.

Of course, the parade didn’t immediately disband after arriving at the castle, that would only happen after the Emperor’s speech.

That said, most of Mercurio’s army wouldn’t be granted an audience with the Emperor, only members of the royal family and nobles would be present for that.

Adventurers, mercenaries, and volunteer soldiers would escorted to other parts of the castle, where a victory party that Theorem had requested Prime Minister Pesche to set up was being held.

Needless to say, this was already special treatment for them. They would normally not even be allowed into the castle, but in this case, they could eat, drink, and celebrate inside the castle.

For those who didn’t want to bother with the formalities of an audience with the Emperor, it was one of the best rewards they could receive.

Of course, an opportunity to meet the Emperor was something that would only happen once in lifetime for many…no, rather, most people would never even have the chance in their lifetime.

Because of that, there were still quite a few people who were disappointed to be guided here instead.

「Ahh, lucky for us. Listening to important people talking is just boring. Don’t you think so, Captain Rei?」

One of the guerrilla fighters, who was drinking wine like water, asked Rei, who was eating food without so much as a single glance at the drink.

「You’re right. Not to mention it seems like I’m quite disliked by people within the castle.」

As the leader of the elite guerrilla unit in Mercurio’s army, Rei had been qualified to meet the Emperor.

But, he had also skipped out on the fighting tournament’s formal award ceremony as he had no interest in it.

To Rei, he had already attended the award ceremony on the arena…but for the people who worked in the castle, that had just been a simple ceremony for show.

The real award ceremony was the one held at the castle.

However, by the time that ceremony took place, Noiz, who had won the tournament, had already left for the Demon Mountains, while Rei, the runner up, had also left the Imperial Capital.

What’s more, while it hadn’t been clear at the time, Rei had left to side with the then rebel army.

Naturally, the nobles and officials who presided over the ceremony were not happy with Rei’s actions.

No, in fact, they were rather bitter about it.

Their bitterness undoubtedly included any resentment against Noiz, who had never appeared in any such ceremonies.

For that reason, one of the officials in charge of the audience with the Emperor had asked Rei rather nastily if he would be attending.

Rei hadn’t appeared at the award ceremony after all, so surely he didn’t need to attend this audience either, right?

The official probably expected Rei to ask to attend in a panic.

However, Rei did the opposite and took the opportunity to leave for the victory party instead.

The nobles from Mercurio’s army, who were attending the audience, had watched the exchange between Rei and the official nervously.

They held their breaths as they wondered if Rei would explode at the official without realising who they were.

Naturally, the person talking to Rei was a rather high ranking official who knew that Rei had come second in the fighting tournament.

But, strictly speaking, those were the achievements of an adventurer such achievements meant nothing to civil servants like themselves…or so they thought.

They weren’t entirely wrong either. To the officials, Rei was just another adventurer after all.

Unfortunately, because they were always in the castle, they had only heard of Rei’s achievements on the battlefield…through word of mouth reports.

If they had known what Rei was really capable of, they probably wouldn’t have treated him like that. He was a god-like figure on the battlefield after all…that might be an exaggeration, but he was still more than capable of taking on an entire army by himself, as the trump card of Mercurio’s army.

Rei was quite happy to be kicked out of the audience, but to those in Mercurio’s army, it was completely unforgivable.

Even those in the White Rose Knights who didn’t like Rei that much were outraged, saying this wasn’t the way a hero should be treated.

As Rei left, the official was given harsh glares by the nobles as they slinked out the room.

Several people even asked Theorem, Mercurio, and Frizione if they should call Rei back, but knowing that Rei disliked events like audiences, the three of them refused.

「Fufu~, what fools. They don’t know what would happen if they made you their enemy. …But I’ll say this, they’re not the only ones like that.」

Vihera came over to Rei with a plateful of juicy fruits as she sat down next to him.

Rei took a slice of what looked like a white Kiwi fruit from the plate Vihera held and popped it into his mouth.

「-!?」

Rei’s expression froze in shock as soon as he tasted it.

He had expected it to taste sweet and sour like a Kiwi fruit, but instead a rich sweetness without a hint of sourness spread through his mouth.

Vihera seemed quite puzzled by Rei’s reaction.

(Vihera didn’t seem too surprised or anything, so that means that this is just the normal taste to her.)

Looking back at the fruit, Rei picked up another slice to eat.

Even though he now expected it, the sweetness still delighted Rei.

The texture and taste combined reminded Rei of mangoes.

And yet, it really did look like slices of a Kiwi fruit, so it wasn’t surprising that Rei would mistake it for one.

「What’s wrong? You seemed quite surprised?」

「No, it’s nothing. The fruit was just more delicious than I expected.」

「Yeah, that’s true. It’s something grown using special methods and is only available from stores that provide for the royal family.」

Murmurs started to be heard.

Not just from the guerrillas around Rei…but from soldiers in other units as well.

A fruit grown using special methods only available from stores that provide for the royal family.

Hearing something like that, it was only natural to want to try it at least once.

They were currently attending a party being held inside the castle, but for most, this would probably be the only time they would ever be allowed inside the castle…as a result, they were quite intrigued by food that only the Emperor and his family could eat.

Of course, while such fruit was primarily provided to the royal family, it wouldn’t be that difficult for a high ranking noble to obtain some for themselves.

「Wow, it’s sweet! …But it doesn’t linger, the taste cleans itself once I swallow it.」

「Delicious…truly delicious…」

「It’s amazing! This is definitely not the kind of food we would normally be able to eat.」

The soldiers all praised the fruit.

Seeing that all the fruit except what was on her plate was gone in an instant, Vihera turned to glance at a maid waiting in the corner of the room.

The maid seemed to understand what Vihera met from just that glance. She was happy that Vihera had asked her to help and bowed with a broad smile before leaving the hall where the party was being held.

Of course, they normally wouldn’t serve food intended for royalty that easily.

But, Vihera was present.

While Vihera claimed to have run away from the Bestir Empire, as could be seen from Gurgast and Tilleyle, her influence was still by no means small.

Naturally, as with the maids, there were many in the castle who still admired Vihera. Even putting Vihera aside, the only people present were soldiers who had served in Mercurio’s army, which had won the civil war, thus giving Mercurio the right to inherit the throne. Because of that, leaving a good impression on them wouldn’t be a bad thing either.

「So, Rei. What do you plan to do now…?」

Vihera was about to ask something when she noticed several people enter the hall.

It wasn’t just Rei and Vihera either. Many of the soldiers, who had been drinking and eating noisily, noticed them as well.

That was because they looked very out of place in this location.

The guerrilla soldiers in particular looked annoyed when they saw a familiar figure among those who had just entered the hall.

That was right, it was the official who had nastily asked Rei if he intended to attend the audience with the Emperor.

As someone who hated such troublesome events, Rei had been more than happy to not attend, but the guerrilla soldiers were not as amused, seeing their commander treated so rudely.

Because of that, they all cast unfriendly gazes at the man as he entered.

The group seemed immediately aware that they weren’t welcome.

They stopped in their tracks for a moment before one of them took a step forward and the others followed behind them.

Then, after reaching Rei, the person at the front bowed as he spoke.

「Your Highness Vihera, it has been a long time.」

「Yes, it’s been a while. I never thought you’d show up.」

「…One of us did something stupid. Nice to meet you, Crimson Rei-dono. I am Jeev Lasno, Quelda’s superior, the one who was rude to you.」

Jeev gave a deep bow towards Rei, just as deep as the one he had given Vihera.

He looked to be in his fifties and was about a head taller than Rei.

He was of average build and while his expression was gentle, his eyes held a depth that seemed to see right through to the soul of the person he was speaking to.

He grabbed Quelda’s head as he forced him to bow.

「Quelda, do you have anything to say?」

「Y-Yes! I am so, so sorry for my rudeness towards you, Rei-dono.」

Jeev’s words seemed to have made Quelda quite nervous. The way he gave his apology made it hard to believe that he was the same person who had been so arrogant towards Rei before.

「I would also like to apologise…Rei-dono, I am so sorry.」

Jeev bowed again.

Rei and the guerrilla soldiers just looked at them in surprise.

There were confused as to why they seemed to be doing this after being so hostile to Rei before.

Among the people present, only Vihera seemed to see it as only natural.

Jeev held a fairly high rank even among officials, and as such was naturally quick to pick up on things.

He predicted that opposing Rei in their current situation would likely cause the Bestir Empire to suffer significant damage.

(No, even if it wasn’t Jeev but someone else, I think anyone with a brain would think of that. To deal with Rei in any way right now would need someone like Noiz. …Oh, well, I guess Gurgast might be willing to fight. If he hadn’t returned to his territory already, he would have happily brought up the matter at this point.)

Vihera had the random thought as the figure of Gurgast, who had returned to his territory rather than participate in the victory parade, popped up in her mind.

Both Mercurio and Theorem had requested that Gurgast participate, but Gurgast refused to listen to them.

While he was one of Mercurio’s strongest fighters and undoubtedly the one who had achieved the most accolades in the war, none of it meant anything to him, so he just went back home.

「No, don’t worry about it. I’m not that good with formal events anyway. I’m more comfortable having fun with everyone else like this. …Anyway, if you’re worried about me, please take care of Set as well.」

The mention of Set reminded Jeev of Rei’s familiar, the Griffon. Jeev smiled as he nodded in response.

「He’s eating over at the stables.」

「I see. I wish he could have been here too.」

Hearing Rei’s words, not just the guerrillas but also the soldiers nodded in agreement.

Set was seen as a symbol of death among the punitive force, but to Mercurio’s army, he was closer to a guardian angel and many of them wished to witness Set’s cuteness up close.

Jeev bowed his head towards Rei as he smiled wryly.

「I’m afraid I can only decline your request.」

No matter what, allowing a Griffon into the castle was still considered to be too dangerous, so Set had to wait at the stables.

Of course, as Jeev said, Set was being fed copious amounts of food.

There were some people who had been unhappy about having to serve food to a Griffon at first.

That said, the people who had been entrusted with taking care of Set were gradually captivated by his appetite and friendly nature…although no one present knew of that.

As for Rei, he had pretty much expected that to be the case.

「More importantly…His Majesty the Emperor wishes to meet with you privately.」

Jeev said that to Rei as if it weren’t anything special.

+++

# **834**

Rei was surprised to hear from Jeev that the Emperor wanted to meet with him, but Vihera was even more surprised.

Before she had run away from the Bestir Empire, Vihera had only spoken to her father a few times a month at most.

While she held no affection towards her father, she still respected him for leading a nation as great as the Bestir Empire.

Hearing that someone like that wanted to meet with Rei, it was only natural for her to suspect political motives.

Vihera felt uneasy knowing that Rei disliked such things, but Jeev’s next words were even more surprising to her.

「Your Highness Vihera…no, Vihera-sama, if you wouldn’t mind, you are also invited to join.」

「…Me as well?」

「Yes. Vihera-sama performed admirably in battle, so I believe that is the reason why.」

「I ran away from this country though…is it still okay?」

As Vihera asked for confirmation, Jeev nodded with a smile.

「Of course. His Majest Tragist is fully aware of that. It doesn’t seem to be an issue, so I don’t believe there is anything to worry about. It has been a long tim since you last saw His Majest the Emperor, so I would like you to enjoy your time.」

「Even before I ran away, father…no, I’d only seen His Majesty a few times a month.」

「Surely you must realise that governing a country as vast as the Bestir Empire means that he simply cannot have that much free time?」

Vihera shrugged her shoulders as if saying ‘I guess so’ at Jeev’s reproachful words.

As she did that, her chest shook, drawing the attention of the officials around her…as well as the soldiers.

「Mm, ahem. Vihera-sama, I think you should dress a little more modestly when you meet with His Majesty Tragist. His Majesty would surely be dismayed to see his daughter dressed so provocatively.」

Befitting his station, Jeev spoke those words without sparing even a single glance at Vihera’s chest.

However, Vihera didn’t seem to care for Jeev’s words as she smiled and spoke again.

「Really? I don’t think father would mind my outfit. Besides, I’m an adventurer now, unfortunately. These are all the clothes I brought.」

「…Won’t you catch a cold in this cold weather?」

「Don’t worry, I’ve considered all those thing carefully. Despite how they look, these clothes are actually quite warm.」

With what you’re wearing? Jeev couldn’t help but question Vihera’s response and he wasn’t wrong to do so.

Vihera’s cloths appeared to be thin, nearly see through garments.

The only thing she wore under them to cover her attention grabbing body were her undergarments.

It was the kind of attire commonly worn by prostitutes or dancers, certainly not what Jeev would think of when the word ‘clothing’ was mentioned.

「Yes. To be exact, it is the effect of a magic item.」

「…Ah, I see. I thought your outfit was just provocative, but it is also a magic item.」

「Yes. …Considering that it is provocative though, you don’t seem particularly interested.」

Clad in such clothes, Vihera knew that her beauty and physique would draw the arousal of men around her.

And while she didn’t expect people to look at her with leering gazes, given her position as a former member of the royal family, she still expected that she would receive casual glances from people like the soldiers…repeated casual glances.

Jeev was almost distracted by her for a moment, but ultimately, that was all.

「Although I may look like this, I have a loving wife.」

「You’re still as devoted as ever. So, what do we do? I’ve only brought these clothes and I Vihera the adventurer now, so I have no intention of taking them off carelessly.」

That was, of course, a lie.

In the first place, as a magic item, such clothes were quite expensive and not something she could easily keep spares of in case of emergencies.

That was why she did actually have other clothes to change into, were something to happen.

But, it was also true that as an adventurer, her current clothes also doubled as her formal attire.

She would probably have to leave her weapons behind, like her gauntlets and greaves, before meeting with the Emperor, but she had no intention of taking off her current clothes.

「Besides…there’s only one person in this world that I’m willing to take them off for to show what’s underneath.」

Vihera cast a side glance towards Rei, who was listening in while eating the food on his plate.

Rei brushed her words aside with a troubled smile.

Seeing their interaction, Jeev seemed to understand their relationship.

He thought for a moment before nodding reluctantly.

「I understand. His Majesty Tragist isn’t one to overly care for small matters such as this. If Vihera-sama says so, there shouldn’t be any problems.」

As Jeev spoke reluctantly…very, very reluctantly, Vihera gave a beautiful smile.

The other officials with Jeev glanced at him, wondering if that was really okay. However, the fact that their eyes repeatedly drifted back to Vihera made their thoughts completely unconvincing.

As for Quelda, who knew if it was good or bad luck that Jeev was still holding his head down, causing him to be unable to see Vihera’s body.

At the very least, it did mean that Jeev’s opinion of him didn’t drop any further.

…Although his attitude towards Rei meant that his reputation had already taken a big hit.

「Well then, shall we get going? His Majesty Tragist is waiting for us.」

「Now? Is the audience already over?」

Vihera was surprised by Jeev’s casual words.

Rei felt the same as he also asked Jeev.

「Right now?」

「Yes. The audience has already ended, so this is the time for the royal family to discuss their own matters by themselves. …There is also the matter of Prince Kabajid.」

Jeev’s words convinced Rei, but raised a new question at the same time.

Based on what Jeev said, there was no problem in calling Vihera over.

She might have run away from the country, but she was still family member and would mourn Kabajid’s death.

But, why was he being called over?

(Is it because I played an active role in the civil war? No, if that were the case, there would be no need to invite me during a time for family matters…)

Rei was still skeptical, but Vihera placed a hand on his shoulder.

「There’s no point worrying about it. Father does some crazy things sometimes, so this isn’t that strange. Besides, it would be rude to keep him waiting. Let’s go.」

Vihera’s words made Rei stand to his feet.

In the end, it would be rude to keep someone like the Emperor waiting, and it was also true that he was somewhat intrigued by person that was Tragist.

While Rei had met members of the royal family, such as Vihera, Mercurio, and Frizione, and opposed others, such as Shurus and Kabajid, he had yet to meet with the Emperor in person.

He had only seen Tragist from afar in the arena, but even then, he had felt an overwhelming presence from the man.

All that considered, it wasn’t a surprise that Rei was interested with meeting in person.

「It seems you’re interested. In that case, let’s go.」

Smiling at Rei’s response, Jeev led Rei and Vihera out of the hall.

The guerrilla unit and the other soldiers watched them leave with looks of surprise on their faces.

「Vihera-sama is one thing, but even Captain Rei was summoned by His Majesty the Emperor…that’s quite impressive.」

「You’re right. But, you could have guessed, right? Everyone can see that Vihera-sama is smitten with Captain Rei. In other words…is he going to ask for her hand in marriage?」

「…Asking His Majesty the Emperor?」

「…Surely Captain Rei won’t get into a fist fight with His Majesty Emperor?」

『…』

With just those words, all conversation in the surroundings went quiet.

In this large hall, the drunken revelry of those who hadn’t even noticed Jeev and his companions’ entry into the hall seemed so much louder to the soldiers’ ears.

「Rei-dono, I’m sorry, but I would like you to hand over any weapons.」

After walking about 10 minutes from the hall, they arrived at a room closer to the outside of the castle and Jeev turned to Rei before speaking.

「Weapons? …Is this fine?」

Taking off the Mithril Knife at his waist, sheath included, he handed it over to Jeev.

Jeev took it, but still shook his head.

「We are aware that you, Rei-sama, have an item box. It contains several weapons. Furthermore, by using the item box, you can instantly take out anything you want. So…given that you are a titled adventurer, I can’t let you meet with His Majesty Tragist with such weapons…or similarly dangerous equipment.」

「…I see.」

Thinking it made sense, Rei nodded his head.

While he still wasn’t quite aware of it himself, Rei currently possessed the strength to defeat Noiz. In addition, he was technically an adventurer from the Mireana Kingdom, which had been in conflict with the Bestir Empire for many years, not to mention he had fought against the punitive force in the recent civil war.

…Taking all that into consideration, it wasn’t so surprising that he would be seen as a potential enemy.

But…that didn’t mean that Rei would just hand over the Misty Ring, his lifeline, so easily.

It would be fatal if someone were to run off with it…well, that was a bit of exaggeration, but it would still be quite devastating.

「I’m sorry, but this is my lifeline. I can’t give it to you. If I absolutely have to give it to you, then I can only decline the audience.」

All the officials except Jeev widened their eyes at Rei’s response.

From the perspective of someone in the Bestir Empire, they never imagined that someone would refuse a summons from the Emperor.

Of course, this had nothing to do with the fact that Rei was from the Mireana Kingdom.

Even among people from the Mireana Kingdom, most would unconditionally comply with the requirements if the Emperor asked to meet with them while they were in the Bestir Empire.

This was naturally due to the difference in Rei’s values.

While Jeev didn’t fully understand the reasoning behind Rei’s words, he still took out a small box from his pocket.

「You certainly have a point, Rei-dono. It’s true that many people in this country hold grudges against you, so I understand that you would rather not hand over your item box. So…how about this? You can put your item box inside this box, lock it, and then keep the box and key with you.」

「…I see.」

Jeev’s idea was certainly easier for Rei to accept.

In essence, the goal was to make it so that Rei couldn’t immediately access his item box, so there was no need to give it over to someone else to hold onto.

「Just to be clear, there’s no tricks with the lock right? For example, being unable to be unlocked after locking…」

「Yes, you can see here.」

Jeev locked and unlocked the box several times as he spoke.

Seeing that, Rei seemed to relax. He put the Misty Ring into the box and locked it before holding onto it in his hand.

「…Rei-dono, you seem to have forgotten something.」

Just as everyone gave a sigh of relief, Jeev’s voice echoed out again.

「I forgot something?」

「Yes. The magic item at your waist. That’s also a weapon, is it not?」

Nebula’s Eye, which used magic power to create arrowheads.

It was something he had acquired after coming to the Bestir Empire.

「…You’ve got quite the sharp eye.」

Rei muttered quietly as he took it off his belt and handed it to the man holding his Mithril Knife.

He always wanted to have at least one weapon on him in case of emergencies, but he had now essentially given them up.

Of course, his physical abilities were still superior to many people and with Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour, it didn’t make too much of a difference whether he was carrying a weapon on him or not.

Vihera followed suite by handing over her gauntlets and greaves.

「Then, I will return these after your audience is over.」

Jeev gave a deep bow before knocking on the door.

+++

# **835**

The room was quite spacious by Rei’s standards, about 20 tatami (33 square meters) in size.

However, considering it was a room where the Emperor of the Bestir Empire and his children were going to meet, it was actually quite small.

Present in the room were the Emperor of the Bestir Empire, Tragist, the Second Prince, Shurus, the First Princess, Frizione, and the Third Prince, Mercurio.

Along with them were their respective bodyguards or aides, Amare was by Shurus, Angela by Frizione, and Theorem by Mercurio.

Behind the Emperor were also figures clad in lavish armour.

(Come to think of it, does Vihera need bodyguards or aides as well? …She probably doesn’t need a bodyguard though.)

Vihera was already strong enough to defeat titled A rank adventurers, so ordinary guards would probably only get in the way.

A bodyguard who would only be a hindrance in the event something happened couldn’t really be called a bodyguard.

(In that case, am I supposed to play the role of her bodyguard?)

The thought crossed Rei’s mind, but even with the number of bodyguards, most people present were not carrying weapons.

The only exceptions were the ten or so knights who were standing behind Tragist.

Rei could tell that they were quite skilled and strong, so they were probably the Royal Guard, those tasked with protecting the Emperor’s safety.

And, since even Rei could tell that they were wearing high quality equipment, there was no doubt that they were probably high ranking Royal Guards.

(I suppose that is only to be expected, since they are the Emperor’s bodyguards…although I don’t seem to recall seeing them during the tournament.)

Recalling the tournament, Rei immediately realised why.

Noiz had been with the Emperor at the time.

With Noiz, his friend, at his side, there was no way anyone would try to mess with the Emperor.

(Since people assume I can defeat Noiz, it now makes sense why they are so cautious with me. …I see, that’s why their gazes are so wary of me. Even if my weapons are taken away, I can still use Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour.)

Of course, being an adventurer from the Mireana Kingdom was also a reason to be wary of Rei.

As he thought about that, Rei turned to look over at the royal family, who were seated on sofas in the middle of the room.

As he looked, a question suddenly arose in his mind.

「Vihera, what about your mother? Or Frizione’s mother?」

As Rei asked in a low voice, Vihera nodded back.

「My mother and Frizione’s mother have both passed away, but Shurus’ mother is still alive. That said, in the Bestir Empire, the Empress generally has no political power. At least publicly. This might appear to be a family meeting, but in reality, it is a political matter.」

「…Isn’t that strange? Normally, wouldn’t the family of the empress or a concubine hold a lot of power?」

「Do you think someone like my father would let that happen?」

With just those words, Rei understood everything.

Tragist was someone who carried a strong presence.

That much was clear from the speech he had heard during the fighting tournament.

If asked whether someone like that would allow his Empress to do whatever she wanted, Rei could only say that was impossible.

「What’s the matter? Come over here. I called you two over because I wanted to hear things from you directly.」

Tragist, seated on his own sofa, called out to Rei and Vihera.

The two of them couldn’t ignore the Emperor’s urging and headed to the center of the room.

As Rei did so, he felt the Royal Guard’s eyes focus on him, watching his every move intensely. Internally, Rei was quite impressed.

However, his admiration didn’t come from the fact that they were so focused on him, but that they didn’t seem to be taken aback by Vihera’s outfit. In reality though, Rei was quite off the amrk.

The two of them bowed as they reached the center of the room.

「It’s been a long time, father. I never thought you’d call for me after I ran away from the country…」

「Nice to meet you, Your Majesty Tragist. I am Rei, a B rank adventurer from the Mireana Kingdom.」

Rei had treated Mercurio, Shurus, and Kabajid, Vihera’s siblings, as he would talking with his own friends…but, he couldn’t really do that with Tragist, Emperor of the Bestir Empire.

If he really were to do that, it could quite quickly become an international incident.

「Hmm. I’m glad to see that you’re doing well, Vihera. But, isn’t that outfit too attention grabbing for me?」

Frizione’s eyes narrowed at Tragist’s words.
