She looked at Vihera reproachfully, as if saying ‘How could you wear such attire to something like this’.

「Fufufu. If I were still the Second Princess, I might have worn a dress, but…I’m no longer royalty, I’m just an adventurer. That’s why I came here dressed like this.」

Shurus opened his mouth, wanting to say something to Vihera in response…but, Tragist’s laughter echoed through the room before he could interject.

「HAHAHAHA-! I see, I see. If you consider yourself an adventurer, then that’s fine. To be honest, I had high hopes for you too. And you’ve exceeded even my expectations. No, it really is amusing.」

Tragist picked up a glass of wine from the table in front of him as he laughed.

He downed it in one gulp before pouring himself some more.

Next, he turned to Rei.

「This is the first time I’ve met you in person.」

「Yes. I’m very sorry about the award ceremony.」

「Don’t worry about it. Noiz wasn’t there anyway. In fact, because you were there either, it was an amusing award ceremony without the first or second place winners. Besides…you were busy at the time, weren’t you?」

「…I don’t know what you’re talking about.」

While Rei knew that his actions had been exposed, he couldn’t bring himself to admit it and could only pretend he didn’t understand.

Seeing Rei’s response, a ferocious smile appeared on Tragist’s face.

While that was only a change in his expression, the aura he gave off definitely changed in that moment.

The psychological pressure he gave off was so strong that Rei could almost feel it as physical pressure.

(I see. So this…is Emperor Tragist.)

He had felt the same sensation from Tragist during the tournament. …No, now that he was so close and Tragist’s focus was solely on himself, Rei could feel that his presence was even stronger than during the tournament.

Looking at the man before him, the impression of a lion that Rei had felt back then grew even more vivid, and it definitely wasn’t just his imagination.

「Father. Could you not provoke Rei so much? You know he’s strong despite how he looks, right? Knowing you, father, you were probably gathering information on us during the civil war.」

Vihera’s voice rang out, breaking the tension in the room.

Hearing Vihera’s voice, Shurus appeared shocked and incredulous, Frizione sighed with an ‘it can’t be helped’, and Mercurio smiled, as if saying ‘as expected of my sister’.

Although they all had different reactions, the atmosphere became noticeably more harmonious as a result.

「I see. It certainly does seem that he was quite important. …You’re Crimson Rei, aren’t you? What do you think? Would you like to serve the Bestir Empire? If you do, I promise you’ll be treated accordingly.」

Rei was taken aback by the sudden question.

He was quite aware of the damage he had caused to the Bestir Empire, so he never expected the Emperor himself to make such an invitation.

In fact, others who knew what Rei had done were also greatly surprised, so it was easy to see how unexpected the offer had been.

But, at the same time, it also wasn’t uncommon to try and befriend someone that they would rather not antagonise.

It was precisely because of this that such people were better off as allies rather than enemies.

In particular, rumours had already started to spread that Rei had defeated Noiz.

While Rei would never admit it himself, it was a fact that Noiz had been the first to leave in his fight against Rei.

The punitive force soldiers had seen it themselves.

It wasn’t just because of his actual strength, but also his reputation, that the Emperor of the Bestir Empire wanted to take Rei in.

However, despite knowing that…or rather, because he knew that, Rei shook his head.

「I’m sorry. I…have no intention of serving the Bestir Empire. Not just the Bestir Empire, but any other country or noble either. …At least not for now.」

「…Heh, you’re still calm after turning down my offer. You’ve got guts. And that’s why you were able to make it all the way to the finals of the fighting tournament. I’m starting to really want you. What the Bestir Empire needs is strength, in every sense of the word. Surely someone like you wouldn’t be comfortable in the Mireana Kingdom?」

「That would be true in the Royal Capital. However, I usually live in Gilm, at the frontier. No one bothers me about my status there…well, not no one, but not that many either.」

The figure of the merchant who had once tried to steal Set and his Misty Ring crossed his mind.

While the man hadn’t been a noble, he had still wielded considerable influence within Gilm.

But even he was eventually brought down by Rei.

Of course, it wasn’t entirely Rei’s doing, it could be said that the merchant had brought it on himself in many ways.

(Come to think of it, an alchemist from the Bestir Empire had been involved back then. It was also the first time I directly fought a Demon Soldier.)

Rei was suddenly filled with nostalgia as he recalled those memories.

In reality, it had only been a year ago, but recent events had been so intense that it felt like it had been so long ago.

「Hmm, why are you so reluctant to serve those in power? Many people I know would want to serve their country, attain nobility, and reach for even higher positions.」

「I know that there are many people who want to achieve higher positions, but I have no interest in power personally. Surely there are others in the Bestir Empire, like Noiz, who aren’t interested in having power either?」

「Hahaha. That’s true. But, you also have to consider that Noiz is an S ranked adventurer, one of only three in the world.」

Tragist’s laughter echoed through the room again as he exchanged words with Rei, the pressure from his aura gradually creeping out again.

「It’s because of their strength that they have power. Isn’t that right?」

「You’re not wrong. Noiz has the strength, so no one can blame him for doing whatever he wants. …As long as he doesn’t break the law, of course.」

「As expected.」

Even if you said strength was everything, if Noiz were to do something that clearly violated the laws of the Bestir Empire, the Bestir Empire wouldn’t tolerate it.

「…Well, I’ve digressed. Regardless, the Bestir Empire needs more strength. You understand that?」

After losing the Spring War, a civil war had broken out. In the midst of all that, an adventurer from the Mireana Kingdom had come second in their fighting tournament.

It was basically a coincidence that Rei was involved in all this, but it was also true as a result Rei’s involvement, the perception that the Bestir Empire was nothing to be feared of had started to spread among neighbouring countries.

Even those that didn’t quite go that far had started to consider that they could potentially challenge the Bestir Empire and win.

The Bestir Empire was starting to be looked down on by its neighbours and vassal states.

Tragist was aware of all this, but he had still not interfered with the civil war.

As a result, he had obtained a stronger heir to the throne, so he didn’t believe it to be a problem.

However, there was a separate issue that if things continued as they were, there was potential for vassal states and occupied territories to start fighting for independence.

For Tragist, it would have been best if he had been able to bring Rei into his ranks, but Rei had turned down his offer to serve.

「In that case…how about a honorary nobility? You won’t be given any territory and won’t have any responsibilities. You’d be a noble in name only…but that would let you move freely through the Bestir Empire. That’s right, let’s make you something like an Earl.」

Tragist spoke as he took a sip wine, gazing at Rei like a carnivorous beast refusing to let its prey go.

+++

# **836**

At first, Rei didn’t understand what Tragist was saying to him.

To be exact, it wasn’t that he didn’t understand what Tragist was saying.

Rather, he didn’t understand why Tragist was saying it.

Rei had already told him he planned to stay in the Mireana Kingdom.

So why?

Rei wasn’t the only one present to think that way, others shared the same thought as well.

Most shocked by the offer were the Royal Guards standing guard behind Tragist.

Unsurprisingly, the majority of the Royal Guard were made up of people of noble birth.

There were a few former adventurers, but they made up minuscule number.

Part of the reason was because nobles were given preferential treatment, but it was also because being a Royal Guard required good etiquette in addition to skill.

Naturally, those who could only boast about their family background or tried to join through connections were rejected without question.

Past that…a Royal Guard needed to reach a threshold of strength, have good etiquette, and a strong sense of loyalty towards the royal family. The Royal Guards were made up of such people.

That was why it was hard for them to believe that Tragist would make Rei and honourary noble.

「Your Majesty Tragist, that is…」

One of the Royal Guards tried to speak up, but Tragist just glanced at them silently.

After receiving that gaze, the Royal Guard was unable to continue speaking.

Normally, to attain nobility, an commoner would need to attain some level of achievement to earn the quasi-noble status of knight. After that, only by performing several more achievements would they then be given the rank of baron, the lowest rank among nobles…that was how it usually worked.

Of course, the achievements needed to become a baron from a knight were not simple.

As proof of that, it had been over a decade since the last time a knight had been promoted to baron.

The barrier to becoming a noble was so harsh, but here was Tragist, offering to grand Rei the title of Earl.

As Royal Guards who took great pride in their nobility, this was something they couldn’t accept.

But, it didn’t mean they couldn’t do anything about it either.

If it had been a powerless commoner who received such a promotion, they would probably be able to pull some string behind the scenes.

Of course, they would have to be very careful as they would be dealing with a talent that Emperor Tragist wanted, but they could still do it if they really wanted to.

However, the problem was that Rei wasn’t a powerless commoner.

Well, he wasn’t a noble right now, so calling him a commoner was technically correct in terms of status. But, he was also a high ranking adventurer in addition to holding the title of Crimson, an infamous fighter within the Bestir Empire.

It was clear from Rei’s actions up until this point that if they were to act carelessly, the backlash would be severe.

In the best case, they might be able make it seem like it was Rei who was making enemies with the Bestir Empire, but objectively, the chance of such a plan succeeding was extremely low.

After all, Rei was close to others in positions of status and power, such as Mercurio, Theorem, Frizione, and Angela.

If they made a mistake at any point, their own families could be destroyed, so none of them wanted to take the risk.

If Rei’s circle of friends were ordinary, they could probably have incited some brainless noble to do it in their place…but with these people in Rei’s circle, there was a high chance that anything they did would be traced back to them.

With all that in mind, the Royal Guards could only pray that Rei would turn down Tragist’s offer.

「Even if you say that…as I said earlier, I plan to remain with the Mireana Kingdom. I think it would be a bad idea for me to receive a title in the Bestir Empire in such a situation, even if I have no actual responsibilities.」

「I see, that is true. But, why are you siding with the Mireana Kingdom? This is a genuine question, don’t you find the Mireana Kingdom a difficult place to live in?」

Tragist’s expression didn’t suggest any scheming, but rather lack of understanding for Rei’s decision.

「You’re right. I won’t deny that. But, as I said earlier, my base of work is in Gilm, at the frontier. So nothing really bothers me there.」

「…I would really like to bestow a title on you, and you would still refuse?」

「Yes. I have no real loyalty or patriotism towards the Mireana Kingdom. But, if there’s a chance it will put me against the people of Gilm that I’ve become friendly with, even if it’s few in number, I’m afraid I can only refuse the title.」

「That’s a shame.」

Tragist muttered to himself, but with everyone else silent, listening to their exchange, his voice was heard by everyone.

That was why they could all tell his words came from his heart.

「That isn’t the case though, right? I know I shouldn’t be the one saying this, but the Bestir Empire has many talented people. Adding someone like me into the mix would only distort the way the Bestir Empire is.」

「Distort? That’s fine. Everyone wants stability, but too much stability leads to stagnation. And, stagnation breeds corruption, just like the waters of a dammed river will go rotten. It’s better for the Bestir Empire to constantly be in change. At least, that’s what I believe and how I’ve been able to develop the Bestir Empire to this point.」

Tragist’s words were spoken with absolute pride in his own belief, without any hint of doubt.

(I see. So this is the Emperor of a great nation like the Bestir Empire…no, perhaps it’s because he is like this that the Bestir Empire is able to be a great nation.)

Rei could understand why Tragist held such a powerful presence.

「I understand what you’re saying, but I still must decline the title.」

If he gave vague responses here, it could result in potential misunderstandings.

Realising that, Rei continued to state his refusal clear.

「…You’re really going to refuse after I’ve asked so many times?」

「Yes. I’m very sorry.」

Tragist’s gaze was sharp, even menacing, as he looked at Rei.

Despite knowing that his answer could potentially lead to a fight, he still spoke clearly.

If he had left his Misty Ring outside, he might have compromised.

However, the Misty Ring was still in his possession. It was in a locked box, but he also held the key.

Most importantly, if a fight really were to break out, Rei still had access to Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour.

Unlike magic, which required a casting medium, like the Death Scythe in Rei’s case, skills could be used without one.

In other words, Rei’s confidence came from his belief that he would be able to handle things if push came to shove.

If a fight really were to break out, his only opponents would probably be Theorem, Angela, and the Royal Guards.

Technically speaking, Vihera would have been his strongest opponent, but given how things had gone, Rei didn’t think she would side against him.

Tension filled the room as it began to feel like just breathing would drain your energy.

It was Tragist who had caused the tension, and it was also Tragist who broke it.

「HAHAHAHAHA-. You still refuse, even after I’ve said so much. I like it.」

His laughter was so intense that one wondered where tension had all gone.

But, no one present would say that to Tragist.

Hearing his laughter, Rei thought that Noiz was probably the only person who might have interjected at this point, but Tragist soon suppressed his laughter as he spoke again.

「That’s right. I believe Theorem and Mercurio promised to reward you with a magic item?」

It was a casual remark from Tragist, but the two names he mentioned stiffened up upon hearing his words.

It was true that Rei had been hired in exchange for a magic item.

However, that was only something that Rei, Theorem, Mercurio, Vihera, and Elena, who wasn’t present, should have known.

At the very least, such information should only have been known to the former four within the Bestir Empire.

And, none of them had ever mentioned it to Tragist.

Yet, somehow, Tragist knew about it.

This meant that Tragist’s information network stretched far deeper than any of them had expected.

Tragist noticed their reactions, but didn’t show any reaction himself as he continued to speak with Rei.

「Yes, I quite like you. You said you didn’t want a title, even if it was just in name. And, you have the power to fight against Noiz on equal terms at such a young age. I have to say, this is all quite refreshing. …Therefore, I shall give you this.」

With those words, Tragist pulled out a metal card from his pocket.

The faces of those around him twitched after seeing it.

While not to the same extent as when Tragist said he would give Rei a title, those who saw the metal card still had expressions of shock.

Tragist slid the metal card across the table towards Vihera.

Vihera picked it up before placing it in Rei’s hand.

From the reactions of the people around him, Rei realised that the metal card must be something important. He hesitated for a moment, but since the Emperor had already given it to him, he couldn’t just turn it down, so he turned to look at what it was.

「This is…」

Rei had no experience with regards to art.

But even so, he could only voice his admiration at the intricate carvings present on the metal card.

No scene in particular was depicted by the carvings. But the intricate design, consisting of overlapping curves and lines, gave the viewer a contradicting impression of both simplicity and complexity.

Most importantly were the words engraved on the card, 『This person is a friend of the Bestir Empire』.

「A friend of the Bestir Empire. This represents that position. My thoughts…will you accept them?」

Having already so much turned down, he wouldn’t accept any further refusals.

Tragist’s implicit words made Rei hesitant.

It was true that this metal card would be much more preferable to honourary nobility.

Becoming a honourary noble would necessitate a public announcement both here and abroad, which would have made it difficult for Rei to return to the Mireana Kingdom.

At the very least, the Mireana Kingdom would probably start watching him much more cautiously and he wouldn’t be able to be as carefree as he was now.

…All that said, with his title of Crimson and a Griffon as his familiar, Rei’s name was already far more widespread than he knew himself. He was already somewhat more restricted than before, he just hadn’t realised it.

(What would happen if I accept this? If I show it within the Mireana Kingdom, it will definitely result in many unfortunate events. But, unlike becoming a noble, it probably won’t be made public…right? In that case, I can just store it inside the Misty Ring, just in case…)

Thinking that far, Rei asked, just to make sure.

「If I accept this metal card, would it be made public domestically and internationally?」

Tragist shook his head at Rei’s words with an amused expression.

「This is different from a noble title, it is merely a personal matter. Therefore, I have no intention of making it public. But, if you want me to make it public, I wouldn’t hesitate to consider it. Would you like me to?」

「No, in that case, I’ll accept this gratefully.」

With those words, Rei bowed as he placed the metal card back on the table.

Having been told that much, Rei really couldn’t refuse the offer by Tragist, Emperor of the Bestir Empire.

Also, as Tragist had understood his position and given him something that didn’t need to be made public, Rei accepted it, despite still feeling a little uneasy about it.

「That’s right. If you say that then it was worth preparing it for you. Hahahaha.」

Tragist’s amused laughter echoed through the room.

At his laughter, everyone else finally breathed a sigh of relief.

What Rei didn’t realise at this time was that if thing went poorly, this metal card had the potential to be a bigger bombshell than even a noble title.

# **837**

「Hmm, I see. it’s true that Orcs will form settlements when a higher ranking species is born among them. And, once a settlement is established, there will inevitably be great damage to the surrounding towns and villages. Considering all that, it is true that it would be best to destroy them while the settlement is still in its early stages. If you hesitate, it is entirely possible that the Orcs’ power will grow to the point that the noble who governs the territory will no longer be able to control them.」

Tragist nodded in understanding after hearing Rei talk about the time he had attacked an Orc settlement.

「But, father, Orcs are still low ranking monsters. And, because they have similar physiques to humans, the military finds them useful for combat training. Of course, we should still avoid causing damage to their surroundings.」

Shurus, who had been listening in to the conversation between Tragist and Rei, spoke up.

He wasn’t wrong. Orcs possessed a certain level of intelligence and strength in addition to their good reproductive ability, making them perfect opponents for the army to gain combat experience.

「Shurus, that might be true from the perspective of the army, but for those who live and travel through the area, Orc settlements are a nightmare, especially for the women.」

Orcs were basically a male only monster species, needing females from other races to reproduce.

And, the most common victims were humans.

Of course, they also posed a danger to demi-humans…such as Elves, Dwarves, and Beastkin, but there was no denying that ordinary humans were the most common.

「I know. That’s why we immediately send in the army whenever we hear of an Orc settlement. It’s not like we’re deliberately neglecting them in order for them to expand.」

Perhaps Shurus felt that Vihera was implying the Imperial Army was deliberately letting Orc cause damage for their training, causing him to reply in an annoyed tone.

After accepting the metal card from Tragist, the atmosphere in the room had softened considerably.

At present, Rei was talking about the adventurer requests he had received in the past, causing discussion to heat up.

Most of the people present were actively serving Bestir Empire in some form, so while they had some knowledge of what adventurers did, few of them knew what the life of an adventurer was reall like.

Vihera was the exception of course, having run away from the Bestir Empire to be an adventurer in the Mireana Kingdom. But even in Vihera’s case, she had mostly sought out strong opponents as she explored the dungeon in Exil.

That said, her stories of exploring the dungeon were so realistic that everyone…even the Royal Guards, listened in with interest.

(Well, it’s only natural that they would be interested in Exil. Of course, the Bestir Empire has Labyrinth Cities as well, so anything learned there could be put to good use running them here.)

Occasionally, at Vihera’s urging, Rei would add his own explanations, and as he talked about events from when he wasn’t with Vihera, Rei began to understand why they were so interested.

The conversations continued on.

Although Shurus initially held a negative impression of Rei, which was understandable considering the reason for his defeat in the civil war, he gradually grew intrigued by Rei’s stories of fighting monsters.

Shurus had always held a keen interest in military affairs. While his talent for combat was inferior to Vihera’s, it was still fair to say he was a highly capable fighter.

That was why he had been so well received by the Imperial Army.

「If there was one monster that left a big impression on me, it would have to be the Gamelion. It’s a monster that is in season in the Bestir Empire right now, when I first heard of it, I was told it was a rabbit monster…」

「Hmm, that’s right. I remember being surprised the first time I saw a Gamelion as well.」

It was true that Gamelions were a kind of rabbit monster, but it was massively larger. They also had gigantic fangs for killing and devouring its prey and blade like ears. Anyone who saw a Gamelion would be unlikely to consider it a rabbit.

Like that, Rei talked about the monsters he had fought as an adventurer for the next 30 minutes.

By the end of it, not just Shurus but even the Royal Guards, who held their own thoughts regarding Rei, were drawn into the conversation.

Thirsty from all the talking, Rei paused to drink some cold tea.

Perhaps thinking that they had reached a break in the conversation, Theorem, who had also been listening with interest, spoke up.

「So, Rei. I’d like to talk to you about your reward for everything…」

「Here?」Rei’s eyes widened slightly, as he had never expected the topic of his reward to come up during an audience with the Emperor, let alone a private gathering of the Royal Family.

But Theorem simply nodded without any particular reaction.

「Yes. His Highness Mercurio said that your reward should be an heirloom passed down through the Royal Family.」

Perhaps he had already anticipated that something like this would happen. Tragist just watched the conversation unfold without saying anything in response to Theorem’s words.

Neither Shurus nor the Royal Guards seemed annoyed by the matter either.

It might have been different if Theorem had brought the matter up as soon as Rei entered the room, but maybe because everyone had been happily listening to Rei’s stories up until now, they didn’t seem particularly opposed to Theorem bringing the matter up.

(Perhaps that was his intention from the beginning?)

Rei seemed to understand why Shurus had brought up Gamelions earlier.

That didn’t mean he was unhappy about it though.

While Rei wouldn’t go as far as to say he was happy about it…it was certainly reassuring that Shurus wasn’t openly expressing his dislike of him.

「So, as for your reward…I’ve prepared something called the New Moon Ring.」

At Theorem’s words, it wasn’t Rei…but Shurus and Frizione who expressed surprise.

The Royal Guard didn’t seem to understand why Shurus was so surprised.

It was a family heirloom after all, so it wasn’t surprising that the Royal Guard didn’t know what kind of magic item it was, unless they were of a certain rank.

Amare and Angela were similarly unfamiliar with what the New Moon Ring was as they watched the conversation unfold.

「Theorem…are you serious?」

「Yes, Your Highness Shurus.」

「But, that magic item…oh, that’s right. Come to think of it, Rei’s magic power is…」

「Yes. That’s why it’s the New Moon Ring.」

Perhaps getting a little impatient at their cryptic conversation, Rei interjected.

「It would be helpful if you could explain everything instead of making me figure it out on my own.」

Theorem nodded at Rei’s words.

「The New Moon Ring is a magic item excavated from the ruins of an ancient magical civilisation. It has the ability to conceal the wearer’s magic power.」

「…Is that it?」

Contrary to its impressive sounding name, the New Moon Ring didn’t seem to have an as impressive effect.

However, Theorem shook his head.

「That’s all…? I wouldn’t say that these types of magic items don’t exist, but they are quite rare. They need extremely skilled artisans and rare materials to make. In addition…」

Theorem spoke up as Rei’s reaction was far from what he had expected.

Vihera continued from where Theorem left off.

「Rei, you do realise that your magic power is incomparably larger than most mages, right?」

「Of course.」

While Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour had reduced the magic power consumption to some extent compared to Overlord’s Armour, it still used enough magic power that an ordinary mage would have been unable to sustain it for more than a few seconds.

As for Overlord’s Armour, Rei had only been able to use it due to his massive magic power.

In terms of magic power alone, Rei was probably near the pinnacle of all of Elgin.

It was quite possible that there wasn’t a single other human in this world who possessed more magic power than Rei.

No one could say for sure though, because abnormal people would appear from time to time.

「Then did you know that some mages…no, not just mages, but some people have the ability to sense the magic power of others? Of course, there aren’t that many people who can do that. Maybe one every 50…no, every 100 mages.」

「I know. I’ve met several people who can see magic power. I also know of someone who had magic eyes that could see magic power directly.」

The figure of a solo adventurer, like himself, flash through his mind.

「Then you understand, right? For example, even if you tried to do something stealthy, if there is someone who can sense magic power, it would be impossible for you to hide from them.」

「…I see. So, this New Moon Ring…」

Rei nodded in response to Vihera’s explanation as he finally understood the benefits of the New Moon Ring.

「Yes. As Theorem said earlier, the New Moon Ring hides the wearer’s magic power. Of course, it doesn’t actually reduce your magic power, it only hides what others can see. It’s also very rare, it’s the only magic item of its kind that we have excavated from the ruins of the ancient magical civilisation. Within the Bestir Empire at least.」

「If that’s true, then this is quite a valuable magic item for me.」

「That does seem to be the case. It’s a type of magic item that alchemists can still create, but I think the New Moon Ring is the only one capable of fully hiding your magic power.」

No matter how stealthy Rei was, he couldn’t do much about his movements being revealed due to his magic power.

In such situations, a magic item that could prevent that from happening was extremely useful.

Rei thought about it for a few seconds before nodding back at Theorem.

「I understand. The New Moon Ring will be my reward. I’ve received this as well.」

Rei turned to look at the metal card that was still on the table.

There was no doubt that the metal card was already a very valuable item.

Tragist had already told him that possessing that card allowed him to do almost anything within the Bestir Empire, so it was definitely a good item to have in emergency cases.

「In that case, please wait a moment. Prince Mercurio, is that okay?」

「Yes, I’ll be gone for a moment. Is that okay, father?」

「Yes. This is something you decided yourself. If you’re going to give it as a reward for Rei’s strength, I have no complaints.」

With Tragist’s words, no one could present any further objections and it was decided that Rei’s reward would be the New Moon Ring.

「We will be back soon.」

With those words, Theorem left the room with Mercurio.

There was no need to say why they were leaving.

Rei saw them off as he waited for them to return with the New Moon Ring.

「Rei.」

Tragist called out to Rei again.

「What’s the matter?」

「When will you be leaving the Imperial Capital?」

「Probably within the next few days…I think. There are quite a number of people who want to leave with me after the civil war, so I will be heading back to Gilm with them.」

「…I see. Are you poaching them from me?」

Tragist’s gaze sharpened for a moment, but Rei shook his head.

「That is not my intention. It wasn’t something I asked them to do after all. I think they might have just become attached after working together for so long.」

To be exact, some admired Rei and Set’s power, some like his generosity towards his allies, and others were overwhelmed by Set’s cuteness…there were quite a range of thoughts.

But, the biggest factor was that if they ever had to fight against the Bestir Empire, that would mean fighting against Rei.

Having witnessed Rei’s strength in person, they would rather not have to do something like that.

「Many former members of the guerrilla unit were quite enamoured with Rei, so it’s understandable. In fact, if Rei had tried to poach everyone, I think the whole unit would have agreed…oh, no, Pelnyx wouldn’t have followed Rei.」

As they were conversing, Theorem and Mercurio returned to the room.

They had a small, but luxuriously decorated jewelry box with them.

「…Please accept this. This is your reward for the request.」

Theorem opened the lid of the jewelry box before handing it to Rei.

Inside was a ring that seemed to be made from some kind of magic metal.

There weren’t any gems attached to it, and depending on how you viewed it, it looked like something you could find for sale at a street stall.

However, true to it’s name, its lustrous black colour, like a condensed form of night, would catch peoples’ eyes.

That was the only thing inside the jewelry box…the New Moon Ring, nothing else.

Well, the jewelry box itself was worth a fortune on its own.

At Theorem’s prompting, Rei gently picked up the ring.

He slipped the ring onto his left index finger as everyone else watched.

As he did so, the ring, which was slightly larger than his finger, shrunk to a perfect fit.

「Rei’s magic power has dropped to just above the level of an average mage…」

Theorem, who could sense magic power, muttered out loud and his words echoed through the room.

# **838**

「Eh…ah…?」

After being woken up by the light streaming in through the window, Rei looked around, momentarily unaware of where he was.

After realising he was in a luxurious bed, the finest he had ever slept in, even including Earth, he finally remembered where he was.

「That’s right, I ended up staying the night in the castle.」

Muttering to himself, he turned to look at his left index finger, where a midnight coloured ring could be seen.

「The New Moon Ring, huh. It’s still here.」

There were ordinary magic items which were capable of hiding magic power as well.

But, when Rei wore such magic items, they would be unable to fully absorb his magic power, rendering them ineffective…or even destroying them.

As he lacked the ability to see magic power himself, Rei couldn’t quite tell the difference, but he had been given another magic item with similar effects to the New Moon Ring to test and it had crumbled to dust, unable to withstand his magic power.

「Regardless, if wearing this ring means I can hide my magic power from people who can sense it, then I’m quite lucky. Turning down the tournament reward wasn’t such a bad thing after all. And, if I had received anything more after the metal card, it would probably have caused some trouble.」

Rei muttered out loud as he savoured the feeling of the bed, which was soft, but had enough bounce to support his entire weight.

Last night, Tragist had asked Rei what he wanted to do with the runner up prize from the fighting tournament, but he had turned in down in light of the metal card.

He looked at the New Moon Ring again as he enjoyed the bed.

The last time he had stayed at the castle to guard Frizione, he had been in a detached hut of sorts which only had an ordinary bed.

…Of course, it was only ordinary by the castle’s standards.

That place was somewhere Frizione would stay at from time to time, but it was unlikely for her to ever stay the night there, so the bed hadn’t been of particularly high quality.

In comparison, the room Rei had just woken up in was a room reserved for honoured guests…highly honoured guests at that.

Naturally, the room was fitted out with the finest furniture and it was Rei’s first time sleeping in a bed like this.

「I wonder if I could ask for the bed as a reward?」

Just as he was thinking about that, he heard a knock on the door.

「Come in.」

A maid who could only be described as beautiful entered the room after Rei’s response.

She was slightly older than Rei.

The maid was someone that Tragist had assigned to Rei.

She had told Rei that she would be available to entertain him at night if he wanted, but Rei couldn’t say yes, let alone in front of Vihera, so she was just working as a regular maid.

「Pardon me, Rei-sama. Regarding breakfast, Vihera-sama asked if you would like to join her…」

Rei nodded, strangely happy to hear Vihera not being referred to as Her Highness.

「I understand. Is breakfast now?」

「No, it’s in 30 minutes from now.」

「…Knowing Vihera, I would have thought she would want to eat immediately.」

Rei scratched his head as he spoke and the maid gave a slight smile.

「Vihera-sama is dining with a man, so surely she must have to prepare some things?」

「You say she needs to prepare. Dinner might be one thing, but this is only breakfast right? I don’t think she would need to prepare that much for it.」

「That’s no good, Rei-sama. You don’t understand a woman’s heart. Women want men…especially the men they love…to see them as beautifully as possible.」

Vihera’s feelings for Rei were already well known, not to mention her attitude towards him.

Given Vihera’s popularity, it was no exaggeration to say that the matter had spread through the whole castle already.

Frizione being one of the prime people spreading the information.

「Anyway, I get what you’re saying. Then, I should get ready too. Also, have you heard anything about Set?」

Last night, when Rei decided to stay at the castle, one issue that arose was naturally Set.

Very few people in the castle had ever come in contact with a Griffon after all.

The only exception were the people who had served in Mercurio’s army that Rei had asked to take care of Set before.

However, Set was also far smarter than the people around him.

When Rei said that he would be staying at the castle for the night, Set had made his way to the stables on his own before lying down, not causing any trouble at all.

Fortunately…or unfortunately, the number of horses present in the castle stables had been reduced due to the civil war, so Set wasn’t pressed for space.

At Rei’s query about Set, the maid smiled before saying that there was no problem.

「I heard that he ate the equivalent of 20 people’s worth of food for breakfast.」

「…He really is taking advantage of this to eat as much as he wants.」

While Set did eat a lot, he would usually control himself…eating until he was 80% full.

However, perhaps realising that he didn’t need to restrain himself here, Set was currently eating as much as he wanted.

He wasn’t eating ordinary animal food either, but food prepared by the castle chefs.

The chefs seemed unhappy at first when they were told to prepare food for a tamed monster rather than people, but after seeing Set eat so happily the night before, they started to cook more willingly.

「Many people originally thought of Griffons as terrifying monsters, but seeing him be so friendly…and eating so happily.」

From the maid’s words, Rei realised that she was one of the ones taking care of Set and got ready to head out while hearing her excited chatter about Set.

「Did I keep you waiting?」

「No, I just got here.」

When Rei entered the room the maid had guided him to, Vihera was already sitting in a chair, sipping on some tea.

As a former member of royalty, her manner of drinking tea was elegant. However…

(Such an outfit inside the castle, particularly in the morning…it’s not just out of place, it’s very provocative.)

As Rei sat down at the table where breakfast was being served, he admired Vihera, who was dressed in her usual seductive outfit.

「Good morning, Rei.」

「Oh, good morning. So, why did you invite me to breakfast?」

「…Look, Rei, you’ll be leaving the Imperial Capital in a few days, right? And I’ll be heading to Exil. So, is it really strange for me to want to spend a little more time with the person I love?」

The eyes of the maids waiting in the corners of the room lit up at Vihera’s plain declaration of love.

Like Frizione, Vihera was quite popular with the people.

So it was only natural that they would be interested in Vihera’s love life.

The same was true of the maid who guided Rei here, who exchanged silent glances with her fellow maids.

「…Well, if that’s what you want, that’s fine.」

Rei spoke as he looked at the table.

Brown bread was the staple food of the Bestir Empire, but the basket on the table held freshly baked white bread.

It must have only just been baked. Rei reached for the delicious looking bread.

Seeing that, Vihera glanced over at the maids.

Seeing her glance, the maids left the room to bring in more dishes.

「So, you’re leaving the castle after this?」

Vihera seemed to wait for the moment that only she and Rei were in the room before asking.

Rei nodded back without hesitation.

「Yeah. The people who will be leaving for Gilm with me have already been packing since last night. Fortunately, they’re all from the Imperial Capital or the local area, so it shouldn’t take them that long to be ready.」

「I see. I’m planning on going with you until the border, is that okay?」

Whether they were going to Exil or Gilm, the route to the border was still the same.

Because of that, Vihera’s desire as a maiden in love was to stay with Rei until then.

Rei nodded back immediately, unaware of Vihera’s thoughts, just assuming that she would rather travel in a group than alone…and with people she knew if possible.

「Yes. That’s fine. But the question is how to keep in touch. I can’t keep staying in the castle like this…and the only inn I know in the Imperial Capital is the Eternal Sky Pavilion.」

The Eternal Sky Pavilion was the highest class inn in the Bestir Empire. Not only was it expensive, but you also couldn’t just show up without a reservation.

「Then, what are you going to do? Stay at the castle?」

「No, I’ll probably just find a random inn somewhere in the Imperial Capital. Or I might stay with one of the people who will be coming to Gilm with me in exchange for helping them move things.」

As he replied, the maids returned with more food.

Salads, soups, and various other dishes were laid out on the table.

There were some meat dishes, but they were clearly intended for breakfast. The meat was steamed to remove excess fat before being topped with some sort of fruit sauce.

There were also several fish, vegetable, and egg dishes, each of which were refreshing. …Of course, the portions were quite large as well.

This was because Vihera had told the chef to make bigger portions in advance, knowing Rei’s appetite.

「Well then, let’s eat first.」

And so breakfast began at Vihera’s words.

As expected of food cooked by the head chef at the castle, each dish went straight into Rei’s mouth.

Vihera was used to the sight of Rei eating, so she didn’t mind as she ate and conversed with Rei. The same couldn’t be said for the maids though.

Rei didn’t have a particularly large build and his face could even be called feminine.

Putting aside his personality and lack of knowledge on etiquette, he had an appearance that others would admire.

That was why it was only natural that they would be surprised seeing such a person stuff two, three, or even four servings of food into his mouth, one after the other.

Amidst all this, Vihera smiled as she watched Rei devoured the food.

「You’re eating quite well, aren’t you?」

「The food here is very delicious.」

「Fufu~, thanks. I’ll convey your thoughts to the chef later.」

The sight of food disappearing in the blink of an eye as they continued their pleasant conversation was quite strange in many ways.

「By the way, I’m going to Exil, but you’re going straight back to Gilm, right?」

「Yes, that’s the plan. …Or rather, that’s what the people from the guerrilla unit are planning to do.」

「No, I know that, but…if you’re going back to Gilm at this time, does that mean you’ll be staying there until spring?」

「I guess so. Well, it would be a different story if something unplanned were to happen.」

「Something unplanned?」

「Well, like the Bestir Empire attacking the Mireana Kingdom again.」

「That’s unlikely. …Considering my father’s personality, I can’t say for certain. But at the very least, I don’t think Mercurio will do anything.」

Vihera muttered as she stuffed some salad into her mouth. But Rei shook his head.

「You know how things are, don’t you? It’s true that Mercurio did win the civil war and has assumed the position of next in line to the throne. But, he’s still only the next in line. That means that if the current emperor tries to do something, he can only try to stop it, he can’t say for sure. …And the current emperor has quite the hardline stance against the Mireana Kingdom.」

That was an undeniable fact.

As planned, Rei had succeeded in creating a pro-Mireana Kingdom faction within the Bestir Empire.

And, that faction was centered around the next in line to the throne.

However, if Emperor Tragist were to launch another war against the Mireana Kingdom, Mercurio would only be able to express his opinion from his position, he couldn’t stop the decision.

If he did, it would only result in a repeat of the previous civil war.

…However, rather than Shurus, his opponent would be Tragist. The Emperor himself.

If you were to ask if Mercurio could beat Tragist, it was nigh impossible.

If a civil war like that did break out, the Imperial Army, which had stayed neutral for the duration of the previous civil war, would turn on him, not to mention the other nobles who had stayed out of the conflict.

In other words…unlike the civil war that has just ended, which could be considered a balanced fight, a civil war against the Emperor would just result in a massacre.

「…I hope that doesn’t happen.」

Rei’s words echoed through the room…and Vihera nodded in response.

(If that were to happen…I guess my job would be to threaten the Bestir Empire’s rear.)

Considering his strength as an one man army that specialised in annihilation magic, the thought crossed Rei’s mind.

# **839**

「Captain Rei, could you store this for me?」

At an inn in the Imperial Capital.

There, Rei was storing various items into his Misty Ring at the request of a guerrilla unit member.

「Yes, that’s fine. You’re by yourself? Is there anyone else you’re bringing with you?」

「Ah, right. I’m an orphan, so I don’t have any relatives.」

「What about your party? Or did you also work solo like myself?」

「No, of course I was in a party. But, shortly before the civil war, some issues came up regarding reward distribution.」

「I see.」

As Rei stored the man’s spare armour into the Misty Ring, he gave a nod in response to his words.

An adventurer party was able to complete quests more reliably as well as ensure their individual chances of survival would be higher.

However, as group of adventurers, as a party grew larger, so did the web of relationships between individuals.

As an adventurer himself, Rei knew that this could easily lead to parties disbanding and he had seen various parties arguing on various occasions about splitting rewards and interpersonal relationships.

「Considering that, it’s easier for solo adventurers like myself.」

「…It might be understandable for low rank adventurers, but once you reach a certain point, it’s hard to stay solo. You either have to have overwhelming strength, like Captain Rei, or a special skill that no one can copy.」

「Really? …Well, I guess that’s true. In my case I have Set, so I don’t really need a party. So, is this everything?」

Rei asked as he saw a backpack filled with camping gear, to which the man nodded.

「Yes, that’s all. Everything else are items I still need to use, so you can leave them here. I just need to put them into the carriage I was given as a reward. …Well, honestly, one of the reasons I want to go to the Mireana Kingdom with you was because I didn’t want to stay in the Imperial Capital and be reminded of the issues that happened within my old party.」

「Looking for a fresh start? …Well, if you’re coming with me, you can do what you want. You know where we’re meeting, right? Outside the main gate in two days, around 9am. Make sure you complete the necessary procedures to leave the Imperial Capital early.」

「Yes, thank you very much.」

「…I’ll say this first, but if you can’t make it for whatever reason, tell me in advance. If you disappear without telling me anything, I’ll have to dispose of your items.」

「Yes, I have been told that already.」

「That’s fine then. See you in two days.」

With that brief exchange, Rei left the room.

He had to take care of the luggage of over 10 people, so he didn’t have much time to dally around.

Rei had just gone to collect the luggage of a single adventurer who lived at an inn, so there hadn’t been too much to store.

The adventurer had even packed everything beforehand, but it had still taken Rei 30 minutes to store everything.

Of course, that was partly due to the fact that he slowed down to talk with the adventurer as he stored everything away.

After that, Rei left the inn to meet back up with Set, who was waiting outside. …However, Rei had to weave his way around the people who were keeping their distance from Set.

Set might have been treated like an adorable pet by those in Mercurio’s army, but that was only because they had gotten used to his presence.

To the people in the Imperial Captial, Griffons were something most of them had never seen in their lives, they only had a strong impression of Griffons due to the fact that they were A rank monsters.

Considering that, it wasn’t surprising that most people would find it hard to approach Set.

Among those keeping a distance were soldiers, but they didn’t make any moves themselves as they could see that Set was wearing a Necklace of Subservient Monster and, most importantly…

「Sorry, but could you step back for a moment?」

「C-Crimson Rei…」

Because they knew that the Griffon belonged to Rei.

Rei was the reason the Bestire Empire had been defeated in the Spring War and, although he had lost to Noiz in the fighting tournament, he had still come second, appearing to be evenly matched. His achievements in the recent civil war could even be considered the highest.

It was said that Rei’s name was now more well known in the Bestir Empire than the Mireana Kingdom, where he had come from.

But, there wasn’t much the soldiers could do to him.

Rei hadn’t committed any crimes after all.

「Gururu~」

Set gave a happy cry after spotting Rei.

Surprised by Set’s reaction, the ring of people around him only grew.

(If they were scared of Set, they probably wouldn’t have gathered around him…maybe they’re a little interested? That would be nice.

Looking around as he thought, Rei took out a sandwich from the Misty Ring as he gave it to Set where everyone could see.

「Guru~?」

Is it okay to eat it here? Set seemed to ask as he tilted his head. Rei nodded…and the next moment, the sandwich disappeared from his hadn.

「Gururu~, Gururururu~!」

Set gave happy cries as he ate the sandwich.

To outsiders, he looked just like an adorable pet.

Those watching from the surroundings didn’t seem to understand what was going on at first.

(Hopefully this will ease their fear of Set, even if just a little.

Stroking Set as he ate the sandwich, Rei started to think about where he needed to go next.

「Hey, what were you assuming? I have no plans to leave the Imperial Capital!」

After giving Set a sandwich, Rei had gone to his next destination and was about to to knock when he heard voices coming from inside.

「Come on, it will be fine. Besides, if I stay in the Bestir Empire, I might have to fight Captain Rei on the battlefield. That’s definitely more dangerous.」

「Then why don’t you just stop being an adventurer? You’ve always said you would look to help out at my parents’ house, right? If you can work there, why do you have to do such dangerous work as an adventurer?」

「Isn’t the pay is too different!?」

「That’s true…but even if the pay is good, it’s not worth the risk. Aren’t you just selling your life? You can’t keep doing that kind of work forever!」

「I know that. I don’t believe I can be an adventurer forever either. But I can still do it now. So, I want to make some money while I still can…」

「Don’t be ridiculous! You’ve been spending every coin you earned!」

Hearing such voices from inside, Rei didn’t knock.

He couldn’t imagine carrying out a proper conversion with them right now if he did knock.

While he wasn’t sure if it was a marital dispute or a lover’s quarrel, he would definitely be dragged into it.

「…Let’s go check out the other places first and come back here later.」

「Guru~」

Set gave a cry in agreement with Rei’s words.

Better safe than sorry, Rei thought as he left.

He had the suspicion that the male adventurer inside the house might not be able to follow him back to Gilm.

「Oh, Set-chan! …Mm, ahem. Captain Rei, you came here quite quickly.」

Seeing the woman’s wide smile as she opened the door, Rei sighed.

「Am I just an afterthought? Well, that’s fine. You seem to live in a much nicer place than I expected…why are you an adventurer again?」

「Ahaha. Well, I run quite a big shop, so there’s a lot I do.」

「…But, you’re coming with me? If you run a shop, you won’t be able to bring your family with you, right?」

「Yes. That’s why I’m going to the Mireana Kingdom by myself.」

Despite the fact it could be the last time she would see her family again, the woman smiled without a trace of sadness on her face.

「Is everything okay?」

「Yes? …Oh, it’s note like I hate my family or anything. My shop also does business in the Mireana Kingdom, so it won’t be that hard to keep in contact with them.」

「I see. If that’s okay with you, I won’t say any more. So, where’s your luggage?」

「It’s all packed already. Please come in. …Ah, sorry, Set. I can’t bring a Griffon inside…」

With those words, the woman went back inside, only to return shortly.

In her hand was a plate with large pieces of stewed meat on it.

The rich aroma it gave off and the rising steam made it clear that the food had been freshly cooked.

「It might take a while, so enjoy this Orc stew while you wait.」

「Gururururu~!」

Set gave a happy cry, his round eyes urging her to hurry up.

While Set’s eyes gave the woman the urge to stroke him, she refrained from doing so as she wanted Rei to collect her luggage first and placed the plate onto the ground.

Leaving behind Set, who was still giving happy cries as he ate the stew, and bringing Rei inside the house…she seemed to be letting go of something, like saying goodbye to a former lover she still held feelings for.

Along the way, they ran into a middle aged woman in her forties, probably a maid, who bowed towards Rei. Eventually, they arrived at the woman’s room at the back of the house.

「So, Captain Rei. Here’s all my luggage, I’m leaving it all in your care!」

「…You…where are you planning on going?」

Rei muttered in exasperation as he looked at the luggage inside the room.

The room was about 10 tatami in size, which was spacious by Rei’s standards, but not particularly big in Elgin.

Of course, this was the Imperial Capital, where the price of land was expensive, so it could still be considered quite a big room.

However…Rei’s reaction was due to the amount of luggage packed inside the room.

There was clearly too much. Way too much.

At the very least, it was too much to fit inside an adventurer’s lodging in an inn.

「Isn’t this too much? What kind of place are you planning on staying at in Gilm?」

「Ah, no. It will be fine. I’m planning on renting a house with some friends. This luggage also contains some things I will be selling.」

「…I see. Is that okay?」

Renting a house. The idea had never occurred to Rei.

Perhaps it was because his father had owned the house he lived in back in Japan.

(Renting, huh. Since I have the money, maybe I should buy a house. That way, Set wouldn’t be confined to the stables and would be able to wander about in the garden or something…but the Dusk Wheat Inn is also quite good.

The Dusk Wheat inn was outfitted with various magic items, allowing for a comfortable life on par with modern Japan.

In comparison, Rei definitely wouldn’t be able to live as comfortably if he rented or bought a house.

(Plus, I’d have to do my own cleaning. …Maybe a maid? No, that wouldn’t be a good idea considering the secrets I have.)

Rei thought about it some more before eventually decided that the Dusk Wheat Inn was still his best option for now.

…Now that he had grown accustomed to living in one of the finest inns in Gilm, it wasn’t that easy to lower his quality of life.

「Captain Rei, what’s wrong?」

「Ah? Oh, nothing. By the way, how many people are planning to live in the house you’re renting?」

Rei asked as he started to store everything into the Misty Ring. The woman thought for a moment before speaking.

「We haven’t officially agreed on everyone yet, but for now, it will include all the women. As for the men…well, I’m not sure. That’s up for discussion.」

「You don’t mind living with men?」

「Of course. As an adventurer, it’s not uncommon to have to sleep alongside men during a request. …Well, there are always those who get carried away and try to make a move, but I’ve trained myself to deal with that kind of thing.」

Coming from a woman who was part of an elite guerrilla unit, Rei could only agree.

She was more than capable of dealing with random men who tried to attack her.

That was the kind of strength she had and why she had been selected for the guerrilla unit in the first place.

She even made the gesture of crushing something in her hands as she spoke, which Rei pretended not to see.

「Just so you know, if you plan on becoming an adventurer in Gilm, it’s pretty tough, being on the frontier. It will be winter by the time we get there as well, so the guild’s requests will be a lot harder.」

「Ahh…that’s true. But, if we can sell the items that you’ve just stored for me, we should be able to get through winter somehow. Besides, the reward for this request was pretty substantial. Even with the carriage as a special reward, it’s enough to live comfortably for six months.」

As the woman spoke with a smile, Rei thought that it wasn’t that surprising for members of the guerrilla unit to be rewarded so much, considering it was an elite unit.

Even Rei himself had received an artifact from an ancient magical civilisation…the New Moon Ring, something that was probably worth several light gold Coins.

「Well, captain. That’s all my luggage, so please head over to everyone else’s place. There are still people waiting, right?」

「…Your words are a bit too suggestive out of context.」

Rei muttered, leaving the woman behind, who was laughing at Rei’s reaction, before heading to the next location.

For now, he planned on leaving the house where he had heard people arguing for last.

That was what he thought as he left.

+++

# **840**

「Ahh…what nice weather.」

Rei muttered to himself after waking up to to the sunlight pouring in through the window.

Looking out the window, he saw a clear blue sky, a stark contrast to the rain the day before.

The sun was unusually asserting it’s dominance in this season as changed from autumn to winter.

Rei gazed out the window for a moment before pulling himself together and getting ready to leave.

Two days had passed since he left the castle. He’d spent that time busily using the Misty Ring to store the luggage of the former guerrilla members who were following him back to Gilm as well as mediating arguments or discussions between the families and girlfriends of the members who had decided to head to Gilm…or more specifically, the Mireana Kingdom, on their own.

「Set must be feeling lonely as well.」

Even among inns in the Imperial Capital, there weren’t many who could take care of a Griffon like Set.

Such places usually also required reservations and had various strict rules.

Of course, Rei understood why.

No matter how docile Set was, he was still a Griffon, which meant many places couldn’t handle the responsibility if anything were to happen.

Many places thought that way.

In fact, several inns had refused to let Set stay there because of that. As a result, Rei had given up on letting Set stay at an inn.

What could he do then? Rather than staying at an inn in the Imperial Capital, Rei decided to let Set go out instead.

The guards at the main gate all frowned a little, but it was well known by this point that Set was Rei’s familiar and that he wouldn’t attack people for no reason, so they didn’t do anything to stop him.

…However, Rei was also told that if he let Set run about and something happened…they wouldn’t be held responsible if an adventurer tried to hunt Set.

「Still, I don’t think anyone is capable of doing anything to Set, who is now considered to be a rare species of Griffon. Even if they’re not a soldier who fought in the civil war, they should know what will happen if they try and mess with Set.」

To the soldiers who had fought in the civil war…especially those who had been on the side of the punitive force, it had been truly devastating to be on the receiving end of long range attacks from the sky, like fire breath, where their attacks couldn’t reach. Even when Set did land, they were then battered by his powerful attacks.

Most of the punitive force soldiers had since paid their fines and were free, so it was only natural that word about Set would have spread from them.

With such well known risks, Rei couldn’t imagine anyone going out of their way, risking their lives, to do anything to Set.

…That said, although Rei didn’t know it, there were indeed a few people who heard that Set was running about outside the Imperial Capital and tried to find him.

However, they were merchants, not adventurers.

In addition, their goal wasn’t to capture or kill Set, but to get some of his fur and feathers.

Of course, finding Set wasn’t that easy and most people never even saw him. However, there were a few that did manage to find Set, trading food for some materials. As materials from a Griffon…and a rare species at that, the fur and feathers they got brought in significant income.

The blacksmiths, weapon smiths, armour smiths, and alchemists, all of which had increased in recent years due to national policy, were all caught up in the market fluctuations as a result of the materials from Set. This even had a slight impact on the Imperial Capital’s economy…but Rei never found out any of this.

「It’s 7am now. If I have breakfast and start heading over, I should be just in time for the meeting time specified.」

Rei left the room after checking the time on the pocket watch he took out from the Misty Ring.

He then ate breakfast in the dining room on the first floor, as was standard of inns of this type, before getting ready and leaving the inn.

「Crim-! …Please submit your adventurer card.」

As Rei handed over his guild card at the main gate to complete the procedures for leaving the city, the soldier in charge twitched for a moment.

He naturally knew who Rei was, but never expected to actually meet him.

While Rei was at the main gate, there were many other merchants, adventurers, and travelers leaving the Imperial Capital, so with the hood of his Dragon Robe up, no one recognised him and caused a fuss.

Taking the opportunity, Rei completed the brief procedures and headed out of the Imperial Capital, walking a short distance away to where eight carriages were parked.

Since it was just outside the main gate, there were several other groups similar to the one Rei was headed for.

While it would have been easier to leave as a group, there were a number of people in similar situations to Rei who couldn’t do that.

Regardless, Rei headed over to the group without hesitation after seeing several familiar figures.

Most importantly, he saw Set among them, receiving sandwiches, skewers, and dried meat from some of them.

(Well, it’s not that strange to see Set here.)

While Set was merciless towards his enemies, he was usually quite friendly.

As a result, it was only natural that Set would go over to people he knew with a “pay attention to me, pay attention to me” attitude.

While the members of the guerrilla unit were preoccupied with pampering Set, the others who were going with them…the ones who hadn’t heard about Set, kept their distance apprehensively.

As Rei approached the rather strange group to outsiders, he was spotted by a member of the guerrilla unit who was standing guard.

With their large number of carriages and low number of people for that number of carriages, the group was likely to attract the attention of bandits and unscrupulous mercenaries. If they were very unlucky, they might even draw the attention of nobles.

That was why there was someone standing guard.

「Captain Rei, good morning.」

The first to respond to the guard’s words after they saw Rei wasn’t the rest of the guerrilla unit…but Set.

Set, who had been munching on the food he had been given, gave a cry as he immediately ran over to Rei.

「Gururururu~!」

Set, with his beak still covered in sauce from the food he had been eating, rubbed his head against Rei.

Rei called out to the familiar faces who came over to him as he patted Set’s head.

「There are quite a number of carriages for the people we have.」

「Yes. We thought the carriages and horses would be considered part of our reward for fighting in the civil war, but these were all given separately. This is all thanks to Captain Rei.」

A member of the guerrilla unit spoke up happily.

That was only natural.

Carriages were expensive and the horses that pulled them were equally so.

Rei could see that the horses were quite good as well…he wouldn’t call them top class, but they definitely weren’t poor quality either.

Judging from their fear of Set though, they probably hadn’t undergone any special training.

「Theorem and Mercurio really spent money on this.」

「You are right. To be honest, I wonder if we really deserve this. It does mean we’re being recognised for our efforts though.」

Just as they said, this was an exceptional reward.

Having both a horse and carriage was a great advantage for an adventurer. As for those who couldn’t afford to keep them, they could still make a decent amount of money by selling them.

(It’s really generous…maybe a little too generous.)

Since they had already received their original compensation as well, Rei felt that the rewards were a little excessive.

「What do you think?」

Rei asked the person he sensed approaching from behind him.

「Well, I guess it’s a sign that they want to stay on friendly terms with you.」

Vihera, dressed in her usual outfit, spoke with a smile.

「I would be happy for them to do that, but is it really worth all this? Horses and carriages aren’t cheap, right?」

「You know, Rei. He’s now the next in line to the throne to the Bestir Empire. If this can help maintain your friendship, I think it’s actually a rather small price to pay.」

「You think so?」

「Yes. …Good morning, Rei. You too, Set.」

「Yeah, good morning. …This is all a bit out of order, but are you ready?」

As they exchanged greetings, Rei looked at Vihera’s horse.

Her horse appeared to be of very high quality.

That much was clear from the fact that it didn’t seem intimidated by Set’s presence.

Vihera also had a pile of luggage behind her which, despite the weight, the horse didn’t seem to have any issue carrying.

Of course, that was only for now. As they kept moving, the luggage would eventually become a literal burden.

Vihera naturally understood that…

「Rei, could I ask you to help?」

Nodding at Vihera’s words, Rei lightly patted Set before going over to Vihera’s horse and storing her luggage into the Misty Ring.

As he did so, Rei suddenly realised that the horse looked familiar.

「This horse…」

「Oh, you noticed?」

「Is this the horse you rode during the civil war? The same horse you rode during the victory parade?」

「Yes. It’s a horse Mercurio prepared for me. It’s smart, fast, and strong. It’s a top class horse.」

Rei was convinced by her words.

Mercurio cared greatly for his sister. Naturally, he would only give the best horse to Vihera.

As he thought about that, a sudden memory came to his mind. During the civil war, hadn’t someone fallen in love with Vihera at first sight…or rather, first fight?

「What happened to Digma?」

「…You’re asking me that?」

Rei didn’t seem to understand why Vihera was glaring at him for a moment, but soon realised why.

(Oh right. Vihera has feelings for me. It’s not a pleasant thing to hear me ask about.)

Even so, Digma was highly skilled and his Elven water spirit magic would have been useful on this journey.

Even with the Dagger of Flowing Water, it would be difficult to provide water for nearly 30 people, not to mention those who would join them along the way.

Not in terms of magic power of course, but the amount of effort required.

That was why Rei felt it would be a little easier if Digma had come along, but…

「No, it’s nothing. You’ll be with us until we get to the Mireana Kingdom, so I’ll be in your care.」

「Yes.」

Perhaps bringing up Digma had displeased Vihera, she only nodded and gave a brief response to Rei.

But, that was only natural.

While Rei had been storing the luggage of the the various people coming with him, replenishing his food and supplies, and even buying some spears for throwing, Vihera had been approached by Digma several times.

Vihera understood that she had the looks and body that attracted men.

But, even for her, Digma’s passionate advances were becoming a bit of a hassle.

It was only natural as Digma didn’t seem to care for her rejections.

In the end, all she could really do was to ignore him.

Sensing Vihera’s mood, Rei judged that it would be dangerous to broach the subject any further and called out to the other guerrilla unit members who had used the time to shift away from them.

「So, is everyone ready to depart?」

「Ehh…we’re still missing a few people. The rest are waiting at a village on the way to the Mireana Kingdom, so we’ll meet with them there.」

At their words, Rei took out his pocket watch from the Misty Ring.

It was currently 9:13am.

It was past the agreed time, but since clocks were extremely rare in this world, he wasn’t too particular about the exact time.

They would be scolded if they were a few hours late, but he would tolerate this level of lateness.

Of course, it was always better to arrive early.

「In that case, we’ll leave as soon as those who have yet to arrive get here, so just make sure you’re ready to go at any time.」

「Yes. …Well, I’ve left most of my luggage with Captain Rei, so there’s no need to organise much. We can just hop into a carriage and get going when we are ready to leave.」

Rei agreed as he spoke again.

「Oh, that’s right. From here until we reach the Mireana Kingdom, you’ll be in charge of managing the group we’re traveling with. …Sergio, right?」

「Eh? Me?」

「Yes. This isn’t the guerrilla unit any more and Pelnyx, who was my vice captain, has gone back to Theorem. That means we need someone aside from me to help lead the group.」

「…Wouldn’t Her Highness Vihera be better?」

Sergio asked as he glanced over at Vihera, who was playing with Set. However, Rei shook his head.

「No, Vihera will be leaving us once we enter the Mireana Kingdom. So it would be better for me to ask you do to this from the beginning, right?」

At those words, Sergio reluctantly agreed to take on the role of group leader.

Just in time as well, as the few remaining people emerged from the main gate and the group set off for the Mireana Kingdom.

+++

# **841**

Their journey after leaving the Imperial Capital was very smooth.

Rei had thought that bandits might have become more rampant after the end of the civil war, but not a single bandit showed up at all and neither did any monster.

Rei himself had been hopeful that bandits would show up so that he could supplement his existing funds.

While he wasn’t in any particular need of money, he wasn’t exactly a saint either. …Well, considering everything that Rei had done up to this point, almost no one would call Rei a saint.

In any case, Rei was more than happy to take down any bandits who attacked them and loot all the treasures they had hoarded without any guilt.

At the same time, he would be restoring the security of the local area…but it appeared his thinking was a bit naive.

「I’m bored.」

「Guru~…」

Rei and Set both muttered out loud as the moved ahead on their own.

Vihera and former guerrilla unit members were already familiar with Set so that wasn’t an issue, but their family members, lovers, and even some friends who were heading to the Mireana Kingdom with them were not as used to Set.

No, if it had been just people, they might have been able to get along with Set.

But…horses were different.

If the horses weren’t used to Set, it wasn’t something that could be fixed in a day or two.

Based on Rei’s prior experience, even if the horses were stabled with Set all day, it would still take around 5 days for the horses to not be as restless.

Vihera’s horse, which had undergone rigorous training and wasn’t afraid of Set, but she had stayed behind with the carriages.

The reason for this was if both Rei and Vihera were to move ahead of the group, they might not be able to respond in time to bandit or monster attacks.

Because of that, Vihera and the guerrilla unit members stuck with the carriages to protect them.

With Vihera and the guerrilla unit members, it wouldn’t be a big deal for them to handle bandits or monsters.

「Well…at least the weather’s not bad.」

Rei spoke as he looked up at the sky.

It had been sunny when they had left the Imperial Capital and the only change after several hours was the appearance of some clouds.

They weren’t rain clouds though, so Rei wasn’t particularly concerned.

If they had been traveling normally, even the guerrilla unit members would have lost stamina in the rain.

But, with everyone riding in carriages, Rei didn’t need to worry about it at all, which made him quite pleased.

As he looked up into the sky and thought about that, he could hear the sound of horse hooves from behind.

(Oh, that’s right. It would probably be better for Vihera to be inside a carriage if it rains.)

Considering Vihera’s clothes…it wouldn’t be a happy event for anyone if she were to get drenched in the cold autumn rain.

Her clothes were already thin enough to be semi translucent, so what would happen if they were soaked with rain? Naturally, she would draw even more attention from the men, resulting in the women in the group…especially lovers, wives, and sisters of the men from the guerrilla unit to give them sharp glares.

As they didn’t want to put themselves under such unneeded stress inside the small confines of a carriage, most of the group had already considering bringing Vihera inside if it did start to rain.

…As a side note, for the members of the guerrilla unit who were single and coming along by themselves, being inside a carriage with a rain soaked Vihera was nothing but a reward to them.

Of course, they all knew Vihera’s strength, so they wouldn’t attempt anything inappropriate.

In that sense, Rei would be the one in the most awkward situation if it did start to rain.

If he got inside a carriage, Set would feel lonely, but if Set got too close the carriages, the horses would get spooked.

It wasn’t like he could be apart from Rei, but Set would rather not be so close to Rei yet unable to be by his side.

(In other words, if it does start to rain, I’ll have to consider getting wet with Set. I won’t catch a cold, but I still don’t like the feeling of getting soaked.

Rei’s Dragon Robe automatically adjusted the wearer’s temperature to a comfortable level and his body had been made by Zepairu and his fellow mages.

It was highly unlikely that Rei would catch a cold from getting wet in the rain.

「Well, I guess I’ll think about it when it happens. It doesn’t seem like I need to worry about rain for now.」

「Guru~?」

What’s wrong? Set seemed to ask as he tilted his head. Rei shook his head to tell him it was nothing as he patted Set.

Set’s eyes narrowed and he gave a cry as they continued along the road.

The temperature was only around 10C, which wasn’t too cold, but also not warm enough for many people to comfortably walk and talk.

In fact, the people driving the carriages were all wearing appropriate winter clothes.

As they walked along the road, Set turned to look at a forest growing a short distance from the road and gave a cry.

Seeing Set’s actions, Rei immediately wondered if it was an enemy. That was what Rei thought, but there weren’t any signs of anyone coming towards them.

Instead, it was a bear, not even a monster, looking food in preparation for hibernation.

The bear seemed to quickly realise the difference in strength and made a rapid retreat from where it had come from.

If it had been an ordinary traveler passing though instead, they might have been attacked…so in that sense, it was bad luck for the bear and good luck for ordinary travelers.

「Guru~…」

As for Set, he gave a regretful cry at the missed opportunity to eat bear meat.

However, he then seemed to remember that the bear he had caught while Rei was staying with Frizione in the castle was still in Rei’s Misty Ring and calmed back down as he gave another cry.

「…What is it?」

Rei was a little puzzled.

While he could generally understand what Set was thinking, he still couldn’t pick out the finer details.

So, looking at Set right now, all he could tell was that he seemed happy at finding something, then disappointed, then happy again after seeming to remember something.

The main reason for Rei’s confusion was that he couldn’t quite pinpoint what had made Set happy again at the end.

「Gurururururu~!」

Watching Set give more happy cries, Rei just looked on in confusion.

Several hours later, the sun was now directly above them and Rei and the group decided to stop for a lunch break by the side of the road.

Most groups would rely on easily eatable foods, such as toasted brown bread and dried meat.

Others would cook something up with ingredients they brought, but even they would have to start a fire before cooking…

The luckiest would have bought pre-prepared sandwiches which they could immediately eat.

But that was mostly a luxury for the first day after leaving the Imperial Capital and only when the weather wasn’t hot.

So, considering all that…Rei’s group was extremely fortunate.

Rei took out a pot from the Misty Ring filled with freshly made stew as well as freshly baked bread and a large number of grilled skewers.

While everyone shouted in joy, the only one who seemed dissatisfied was Set, who wanted to eat his bear meat.

「Heh…adventurers eat pretty well, don’t they?」

One of the women murmured as she lit a fire to warm herself up rather than to cook anything.

She was one of the people who was coming along as a family member rather than a guerrilla force member.

However, the adventurers would be in trouble if others thought that this was what they always had to eat…

「No way. We usually just eat dried meat or something similar. The only reason we can eat freshly cooked food like this is because Captain Rei has an item box.」

Rei spoke after seeing a guerrilla member hurriedly respond.

「Why do you still call me captain? The guerrilla unit has already been disbanded.」

「That’s not true! The guerrilla uni has been disbanded, but for me, Captain Rei will always be Captain Rei!」

The first person to respond after the man’s words was a middle aged woman who seemed to be from the man’s family.

「Ah, I can’t belive that Marno has come to respect someone so much… Thank you Rei-san.」

「Hey, mum! What are you saying to Captain Rei!」

The man called Marno hurriedly stopped the middle aged woman, who placed her plate of stew on the ground as she bowed her head towards Rei.

However, his mother didn’t seem to care at all…instead she just lightly patted her son on the head before making him bow to Rei as well.

「Hey, you should say thank you too! It’s true, you’re usually just all talk.」

「Mum! Please stop doing this in front of everyone!」

Seeing Marno’s reaction, everyone burst into laughter as they ate lunch around the fire.

Food was something that soothed people’s hearts after all.

Even those who had been a little timid towards Set when they first left the Imperial Capital had gradually opened up after eating together.

Of course, they were still to nervous to try petting Set, but at the very least they were no longer frightened by him.
