Part of it was also because the guerrilla squad members had desperately described Set’s cuteness to them inside the carriages and seeing Set so happy after Rei fed him.

「Gurururu~」

Set’s earlier grumpy demeanor about the lack of bear had disappeared as soon as he sank his beak into a plateful of stew.

Seeing Set like that, most of the group had somewhat relaxed expressions on their faces.

「Captain Rei…no, Rei-san. If we continue along this road, it will eventually split. One way will go straight to the Mireana Kingdom, which I think is the one you would have taken to get to the Imperial Capital. The other way will be a bit of a detour, but there is one person waiting for us at a village that way…」

After finishing lunch and resting for a bit, Sergio called out to Rei.

「If we take that detour, how far will it be to the Mireana Kingdom?」

「Well, just a bit further, not too big of a difference.」

「Then it should be fine. We’ll stay at the village for the night.」

「Hmm. Well, that’s fine. As for me, I would like to stay in the same room as Rei.」

She must have been listening in to their conversation. Vihera leaned over towards Rei as she spoke.

Many of those watching were surprised.

Everyone knew Vihera like Rei, but they didn’t think she would be so open about it in front of everyone.

「That won’t happen. Even if we stay at an inn, we will have different rooms. It might be a different matter if we booked a big room instead.」

「Hmm, but the village we’re going too isn’t that bid, so I think people will have to share some rooms, right?」

Hearing her words, Rei looked around silently.

Including himself and Vihera, there were about 20 people with them.

In places like Gilm or the Imperial Capital, where there were large inns, it might have been possible. But, securing individual rooms for so many people at a small village inn would likely be impossible for the number of people they had.

「In the worst case, I have my magic tent…」

Rei’s magic tent was extremely luxurious compared to what most inns in the area could provide.

If there really wasn’t enough room, the tent would be better than whatever the inn could offer.

Of course, there were magic tents that were even more luxurious than Rei’s. After giving Rei his magic tent as a reward, Daska had since acquired an even more advanced magic tent.

「But, how many people can fit in Rei-san’s magic tent.」

「If you don’t mind sleeping on a sofa or on the floor, about half the people here could probably get some rest.」

「In that case, I think we’ll put up as many people as we can in the inn and the rest inside the house of the person we’re meeting up with. If there’s anyone else left, they can sleep in Rei-san’s magic tent.」

At Sergio’s words, Rei nodded, indicating he was fine with that arrangement.

「While it’s fine to stay inside my magic tent, please don’t try to do anything strange. Although I don’t think anyone here would do anything like that.」

「Hahaha. With Rei-san and Set here, I don’t think anyone would be willing to try anything. However if someone did…they would probably regret it in various ways. I would also regret traveling with someone like that.」

Sergio seemed to be telling something to the people around him as he laughed.

It was true that everyone present would be traveling together until they reached the Mireana Kingdom.

However, many of them had also just met for the first time today, so it was impossible them to fully trust everyone else.

+++

# **842**

After finishing lunch, Rei’s group set off once again arriving at the village just as evening approached.

There were only a few soldiers stationed at the village, but the wall that surrounded it was enough to protect them from the various monsters that could be found near the Imperial Capital.

The village was on a side road, off the main road, so despite it’s proximity to the Imperial Capital, it had less than 200 people living there.

The soldiers that guarded the village gates had likely grown up in the village.

So, when they first saw nearly 10 carriages approaching, their first thought was if they were being attacked by bandits.

Their thinking wasn’t entirely wrong.

As the seasons moved from autumn to winter, bandits who preferred not to do their work in the cold would stockpile food, money, and women now instead.

And, although the village was close to the Imperial Capital, its distance from the main road meant that it wasn’t uncommon for bandits to show up.

That was why nearly 20 soldiers were stationed in such a small village.

The Bestir Empire wouldn’t be happy to see bandits attack a village so close to the capital and potentially turn it into their base after all.

「Halt! You guys…what are you…a Griffon?!」

One of the soldiers spotted Set leading the carriages as he shouted out.

His eyes had initially been focused on the carriages, but now that he had seen Set, the Griffon clearly stood out more.

「H-Hey. What do we do?」

「No, even if you ask me that…」

His fellow guard was at a loss on how to respond.

They were soldiers sent to guard the village, so they had to find out the intentions of the group approaching the village.

(But still, a Griffon…huh? Griffon? Oh, a Griffon!)

As the guard wondered what to do, the word ‘Griffon’ brought back memories.

There had been an adventurer from the Mireana Kingdom who had placed second in the fighting tournament and played a big part in the civil war.

The reason the guard knew about this was because someone from the village had also participated in the civil war.

They were a skilled adventurer and had said something about their boss coming soon to take them out of the village?

The guard had been surprised when he first saw the carriages and the Griffon but, after thinking about it, he was able to respond quickly.

「Hey, go get Dietz. This group is probably the people he was talking about.」

「…Oh」

The guard quickly brought his panicked partner back to his senses before sending them running back to the village.

As he saw them off, the guard gripped the shaft of his spear tightly in case anything were to happen before calling out to the approaching group.

「Welcome to Elton Village. It’s rare for such a large group of people to show up, so I’m a bit surprised, but I’ve heard from Dietz. You are Crimson Rei’s group…is that right?」

Even as he asked the question, the guard was sure that he couldn’t have mistaken such a distinctive group.

The fact that they had a Griffon with them made it nearly impossible for him to be wrong.

And, of course, the person riding on the Griffon’s back, Rei, nodded back.

「Yes. We’re meeting…or rather, we’re here to pick some people up before heading to the Mireana Kingdom. Also, we’d like to find rooms to stay in the village for the night. Are there any rooms available?」

「Wait a moment. I’ve called for Dietz.」

The guard responded to Rei.

He also caught sight of Vihera but didn’t seem to recognise who she was and looked away after a glance.

Still, the guard seemed to have a strong sense of propriety as he didn’t stare at her.

Because of that, it was only natural that both Rei and Vihera felt quite good abut this guard.

「Okay, I understand. Then, could you at least start on clearing us for entry?」

The soldier hesitated for a moment as Rei showed his guild card, but decided that checking 20 people would take a while so might as well start now.

「You’re right. It would be better than wasting time here. Then, please give me your identity documents. Also, the Griffon will need a Necklace of Subservient Monster.」

Following the guard’s request, Rei handed over his guild card.

The guard was surprised to see that Rei was a B rank adventurer and that it was also barely scratched, having mostly been stored inside the Misty Ring.

Normally, guild cards would have a wide range of scratches and damage on them, big and small.

As the guard thought about that, he went through each person’s documents before eventually hearing footsteps from behind.

He didn’t even need to think about who it was.

「Sorry, I knew Captain Rei would be coming, but I had some things I needed to deal with.」

「You’re late, Dietz. …So, is this really the Captain Rei you were talking about? Well, seeing as he’s brought a Griffon with, it couldn’t be anyone else.」

「Of course. I’ve never seen anyone else other than Captain Rei with a Griffon as a familiar. …Captain Rei, I’m sorry for bothering you.」

Rei shook his head as Dietz bowed towards him.

「It’s only a small detour, so don’t worry about it. Are you ready?」

「Yes.」

「That’s good. …Oh, and the guerrilla unit has been disbanded, so you don’t have to call me captain anymore.」

「Is that so? Then, how about Big Bro Rei?」

「…No matter how you look at it, you’re the older one here.」

Rei still looked fifteen while Dietz was in his mid twenties.

To others, there was a 10 year age gap between them, so it felt strange that the older one was calling the younger one ‘Big Bro’.

「Hmm, then let’s go with Rei-san.」

「That would be better.」

After his brief exchange with Rei, Dietz turned his attention back to the guard.

「So, can Rei and the others enter the village now?」

「Wait a bit longer. It will take some time to check 20 people.」

After replying to Dietz, the guard and his partner, who had returned with Dietz, began checking peoples’ identities again.

That said, as Dietz was an acquaintance of the villagers and considering Rei’s fame, there was little reason to suspect anyone.

In the end, they were allowed into the village after a cursory check.

「So, here is your Necklace of Subservient Monster. If any probably occur with your familiar, it will be your responsibility.」

After hearing the standard explanation on monster tamer responsibilities, they entered the village.

「Dietz, could you show us to the inn first? With so many of us, can we all stay there?」

Rei asked Dietz after getting off Set and walking into the village together.

Considering the village’s proximity to the Imperial Capital, it wasn’t that isolated.

Many people were looking at Rei with interest from various windows.

Still, they were too scared to approach with a Griffon present, so they just watched from afar.

「No, the village inn isns’t that big, so…we could probably manage about 15 people…the rest can probably fit inside my house…」

「Oh, that’s a bit much. Maybe I should sleep inside the magic tent with Rei after all?」

Vihera interjected, as if it were only natural for her to sleep in the same room as Rei.

Rei had turned her down previously, but it seems she hadn’t thought much of it.

「Vihera, I already told you earlier.」

「Oh, but that would be better, wouldn’t it? Despite my appearance, I’m quite famous in the Bestir Empire. If I were to share a room with anyone else, they’d be quite nervous about it.」

「…Ah, you’re right. Any woman sharing a room with Vihera-sama would feel nervous and awkward.」

Vihera nodded in agreement with Dietz’ words as she continued.

「But that said, there aren’t that many inn rooms, so I can’t just take one all for myself, right? So it would be best if I slept in the magic tent with Rei.」

「You’re right if you put it that way…」

Vihera was certainly right.

But, knowing how Vihera felt about him, Rei couldn’t accept it so easily.

(It would have been fine if it were anyone else…)

But, Rei’s only other option was to give Vihera her own room at the inn, making others stay at the home of the villagers for a small fee.

Eventually, Rei somehow managed to get his way, convincing Vihera to sleep inside his magic tent on her own.

「Seriously, such a beautiful woman is offering to sleep with you…who knows, maybe I’ll regret it later? Well, with Rei, I’ll make any regrets disappear in an instant.」

Vihera was disappointed but still smiled.

As for Rhodes, who was still unconscious, Rei had paid some of the people traveling with him to take care of him on the journey back.

Of course, he wasn’t paying out of his own pocket, he planned to get his money back once he met with Elk again.

In addition, taking care of Rhodes mostly consisted of making sure he didn’t roll off his specially prepared bed from the swaying of the carriages, wiping him down, and taking care of his personal needs. For those traveling to Gilm with Rei, it was a competitive opportunity to make some extra money.

(Well, if Rhodes were to find out he was being looked after like this, he’d probably be pretty shocked…but that would be his fault for not waking up.)

While it was a pretty serious issue for a man of Rhodes’ age, the fact that someone needed to take care of him like this, Rei was pretty nonchalant about it as he made his way through the village.

『Hmm, so it seems your first day of travel went smoothly.』

That night, Rei was using the Paired Orbs to talk with Elena inside his magic tent.

「Yeah, things are going according to plan for now…well, if things don’t go according to plan on the first day, who knows what will happen in future.」

『Fufu, that’s true. But you should still be careful. I probably don’t need to tell you this Rei, but sudden accidents can happen at any time. Especially when you’re traveling in a group.』

Rei nodded in response to Elena’s words.

「I guess so. Even though everything has mostly gone according to plan, they are still a bit scared of Set and all that. Well, they seemed to be okay during lunch, so they should be better by tomorrow.」

「Gururu~?」

Set popped his head through the entrance of the magic tent and gave a cry asking if someone had called for him.

『Kyukyu~?』

Perhaps in response to Set’s voice, Yellow’s voice was heard from the other side of Paired Orbs, eyes darting around as they searched for Set.

Elena reached out to stroke Yellow’s black scales as she spoke.

『So, what happened with Vihera?』

「Uhh…she’s staying at the inn in her own room tonight. I was going to let her stay here, but, well…」

Rei hesitated, finding it difficult to give the right answer, as Elena nodded in understanding.

『I see, I get it.』

Elena understood Vihera’s personality.

She was honest and passionate about her feelings.

From Elena’s perspective, it was almost a given that Vihera would have that kind of relationship with Rei.

However, the thought of Vihera getting ahead in her relationship with Rei before she did was not very appealing.

As Rei saw Elena’s complex expression, he suddenly remembered the metal card he had received from Tragist.

The card with ‘Friend of the Empire’ engraved on it.

(It’s probably quite a ridiculous item…should I tell Elena about it? Well, it’s not like I was told to hide it…)

Reaching that conclusion, Rei took out the metal card from the Misty Ring.

「Elena, I received this while I was over there.」

『Eh? …Is that some kind of card?』

Looking at the metal card in Rei’s hand, Elena tilted her head on the other side of the Paired Orb.

Rei explained how he had received the card from Tragist after being momentarily distracted by the sway of Elena’s golden hair.

『…I see. I understand that you couldn’t refuse, but it was still a bit reckless of you. Still, it’s better than becoming a noble of the Bestir Empire I guess.』

Elena frowned slightly as she muttered out loud, groaning at the thought of how troublesome this was going to be.

(If this were to become known, it wouldn’t be surprising for it to cause a commotion. We need to do as much groundwork as possible before then I guess.)

Elena spoke up again, impressed by Rei’s audacity in the series of events that had led up to this.

『When you report back to Daska-sama in Gilm, you should also mention the matter of the metal card. Make sure no one else sees it though. I’ll contact father about it tomorrow.』

Elena’s words made Rei wonder if it was going to be troublesome after all…he couldn’t help but look up at the ceiling of the magic tent.

+++

# **843**

It had been 10 days since Dietz had joined the group and they had left Elton Village.

Rei’s group was making good progress on the road.

Fortunately, Dietz was by himself, so there weren’t any particular issues after he joined.

That was to be expected, considering he and the others had served together in the guerrilla unit during the civil war.

Of course, that wasn’t to say their journey was uneventful.

Dietz grew close to the sister of a former guerrilla unit member, which led to some sparring between them and Dietz, they were attacked by some Goblins who were unaware of Set’s presence, they met with several other former guerrilla unit members at a village along the way, and they defeated some bandits who attacked them and raided their hideout instead. There were also a few other minor incidents, but nothing major had happened by the time Rei’s group made it to the Selemus Plains.

「We’re back.」

Rei muttered thoughtfully as he looked out towards the Selemus Plains.

For Rei, he hadn’t really spent that much time in the Bestir Empire.

However, it had been a rather intense time with the fighting tournament, attacks from assassins, and participating in the civil war. It felt like so much time had passed since he had first arrived.

(Fulfilling…is not quite how I’d describe it, but things still turned out well. I guess most of the problems I came here for were also resolved.)

The fighting tournament had ended safely, making it to second place himself, and Mercurio had also won the civil war.

But, what relieved Rei the most was, of course, the underground organisation that had been targeting him…Requiem’s Toll.

Requiem’s Toll had targeted Rei countless times, using both Mulla and Sistoi.

However, Rei had managed to capture the two of them eventually and handed them over to Theorem.

With the information he was able to extract from the two of them, Theorem had quickly issued orders.

Several bases belonging to Requiem’s Toll had been raided as a result, leading to the successful capture of a number of people.

However, eliminating such a well known organisation as Requiem’s Toll, which conducted many hidden tasks within the Bestir Empire, would lead to chaos not only in the Imperial Capital but throughout the empire as well…it was also in the interests of the higher ups within Requiem’s Toll to preserve their organisation. On Theorem’s side, he wanted an intelligence organisation that could serve as his hands and feet, so their goals aligned on that matter and Requiem’s Toll ultimately came under Mercurio’s command.

Vihera had received a report about that from the Imperial Capital before telling Rei. Rei’s eyes had gone wide in shock at the time, causing everyone else to wonder what had happened.

「That’s right. At our current speed, you should be able to reach Gilm before the first snow fall.」

Vihera muttered as she looked over at the people who had joined the group after they had left the Imperial Capital.

Vihera would only be able to stay with Rei until the entered the Mireana Kingdom after all. In other words, after they crossed the Selemus Plains.

To be exact, they would have to cross the Selemus Plains, enter the Mireana Kingdom, and then get to the fork in the road that led to Exil and Gilm. But, regardless, they would reach that point soon after crossing the Selemus Plains.

(And that would mean saying goodbye to Rei for now…wouldn’t it?)

Vihera felt sad as she thought about it, but she was naturally planning on heading to Gilm after finishing her business in Exil.

(Compared to Elena, who is tied down to her Duke’s family, I have an overwhelming advantage in terms of where I can go, having run away. So, I’ll have to take full advantage of that.)

Thinking positively, Vihera smiled at Rei, who looked back at her suspiciously as she spoke.

「What’s wrong?」

「No, you just seem to be thinking of something.」

「Fufu~, it’s nothing. I was just feeling a little lonely thinking about having to part with you after we enter the Mireana Kingdom.」

「That is…」

Rei wasn’t quite sure how to respond to Vihera’s seductive expression.

For the two of them, their exchange of words was very much unfamiliar territory, but to everyone else watching, they could only see it as a sweet moment between lovers.

「Rei-san, let’s head into the Selemus Plains. We’ll end up having to spend the night there, so I want to get as far in as we can before then.」

Sergio’s words made Rei realise that there was no point in continuing the conversation with Vihera as turned around.

Behind him, a group of carriages were parked together, with former guerrilla unit members, their families, lovers, and friends all gazing curiously towards the Selemus Plains.

It wasn’t just the people either, but the horses as well, who seem to have gotten used to Set’s presence.

That was right. The horses had been scared of Set when they first left the Imperial Capital, but they had settled down greatly after all this time.

Of course, a few horses were still nervous around Set, so the ones who were handling it better were switched to pulling the carriages at the front.

This buffer between the horses that were still not quite used to Set allowed Set to move together with the group.

Rei called out towards the carriages.

「We’re about to enter the Selemus Plains. As many of you probably know, we won’t need to worry about bandits there. However, there will be undead roaming around, so we’ll need to keep an eye out for them. The undead are particularly active at night, so remember to stay vigilant.」

Everyone’s expressions tightened at Rei’s words.

In fact, aside from Rei and Vihera, only a few people present had ever been to the Selemus Plains.

Most of them…including the former guerrilla unit members…hadn’t participated in the Spring War.

Some had been skilled enough to avoid participating due to their instincts while other had been unavailable due to requests they were doing.

The few who had been here before were all former soldiers.

「Also, while there shouldn’t be that many undead, they do still move around during the day, to please be very careful. Don’t do anything reckless. Also, we won’t be stopping for lunch like we’ve been doing so far. I will hand out sandwiches to each of you before we head in, so eat those instead.」

With those words, Rei handed baskets of sandwiches to each carriage.

Considering the dangers of the Selemus Plains, these sandwiches had been bought at a restaurant in the last village they stopped at.

Of course, Rei hadn’t paid for them, Sergio had collected fees from each carriage to buy the sandwiches.

「So, does anyone have any questions?」

At Rei’s words, a former guerrilla unit member raised his hand.

「What are our plans for night watch?」

「I had been planning to leave it entirely to Set, but with so many people, we can’t really do that.」

His words caused murmurs to break out among the group.

Of course, they hadn’t spent every night before reaching the Selemus Plains in a village.

They had camped out in tents for several nights, but each time the night watch had been left to Set.

The main reason was that they weren’t in a particularly remote area where they could be attacked by powerful monsters.

But Rei had just said that Set alone might not be sufficient enough. Implying that the level of danger would be much greater than before.

「What’s the plan then?」

「Yes, you all and I will be keeping watch as well.」

「…So, will you two be the only ones keeping watch? Or…」

The man hesitated as he looked over at the people that had come with him.

He was basically asking if any of them would also be keeping watch as well, but Rei shook his head.

「I hate to say it, but having amateurs keep watch is dangerous. Only those with the right skills should do it. …I would like former adventurers and soldiers to cooperate on that point.」

Several people attempted to speak out at Rei’s words.

「However, I won’t force anyone on this matter. If you think you can do it, please come and talk with me later.」

Forcing someone unwilling to keep night watch…especially in a location where undead would appear, would only result in unnecessary casualties.

That was why Rei had said that.

「Well then, let’s get going. Once we’re through here, we’ll be in the Mireana Kingdom, there will be a village nearby called Goto. Since we’re not carrying any heavy luggage on our persons, we shouldn’t take too long to cross the Selemus Plains. But, we must remain vigilant.」

Everyone boarded their carriages as Rei got on Set.

As Rei and Set started moving, Vihera came over on her horse.

「Undead aren’t much fun for me since I mostly rely on melee attacks. Using Magic Palm won’t have much of an effect on them either. And, above all, I really don’t want to touch Skeletons, let alone Zombies and Ghouls.」

「…That’s fair.」

Rei didn’t want to fight rotting corpses either.

Of course, he had plenty of long range attacks he could use and he no longer needed to hide Set’s skills.

Taking all that into account, he was confident in handling any Zombies or the like from range.

「Even so, it was still autumn the last time I came through here. The seasons have gone by quickly.」

「No, it’s technically still autumn right now…that just means you’ve had a rather fulfilling time in the Bestir Empire. Well, not fulfilling in a good way though, that’s for sure.」

「Haha, you’re right. It’s been one battle after another. Considering that, I guess you could say it hasn’t been fulfilling in a good way.」

Rei looked back as he spoke.

Seeing that everyone had boarded their carriages, he shouted out loudly.

「We’re setting off!」

『UOOOOOOOH』

Perhaps recalling their civil war days, the former guerrilla unit members all shouted back.

As there weren’t that many of them present though, it wasn’t quite as impressive.

Everyone else just looked at them with surprised expressions.

「Gurururu~!」

Hearing Set’s cry, Rei turned to his right.

It had been a few hours since they entered the Selemus Plains. The sun was already more than halfway below the horizon.

And, as night fell, the undead naturally grew more active.

「Three Skeletons on the right! Skeletons are slow, so we can easily shake them off. Keep pulling away!」

The men driving the carriages immediately reacted after hearing Rei’s words.

But, it didn’t end there.

Several Zombies, swaying as they walked, came into Rei’s eyes.

「Tch, Zombies ahead! I’ll take care of them, so keep going forward!」

Rei took the Death Scythe out from the Misty Ring and began an incantation after shouting.

『Flames, your power is mine. Burn according to my will, consuming our enemies. Spread your flames into an inferno. Use my magic power to fuel your flames.』

As Rei cast his magic, ten fireballs appeared around the Death Scythe…

『Ten Fireballs.』

As the magic was activated, the ten fireballs flew forwards.

Perhaps noticing the fireballs flying towards them, or perhaps out of sheer coincidence, some of the Zombies changed directions. But, the fireballs, which had a certain level of targeting, continued to fly straight towards them.

And, the moment the fireballs hit the Zombies…a fiery flame appeared, burning them so thoroughly that even their bones were turned to ashes in an instant.

As the group, led by Set, charged forward, the charred bodies collapsed as they collided with the carriages.

The group of Zombies was eliminated entirely, leaving only their ashes behind.

Their ashes too were soon scattered across the Selemus Plains by the winter wind.

As for the Skeletons, seeing that the carriages had already left their range of detection, they ceased their pursuit and went back to wandering around the Selemus Plains.

Their bones rattled as they carried around their rusted swords and broken spears, revealing the true nature of the undead.

Skeletons weren’t the only ones seeking the living either.

Something clad in armour also appeared along with the sound of creaking metal.

At first glance they might look like knights in armour, but these metal armours were also a type of undead.

Living Armour, where a person’s grudge possessed a suit of armour.

This undead, which were higher ranked than Skeletons and Zombies, slowly…but surely, started moving in the direction that Rei’s group had gone.

Seeking the warm light of life that they lacked.

Ghosts floated around them as if following the Living Armour.

Several Skeletons that had been wandering around also started to follow the Living Armour in their pursuit of Rei.

+++

# **844**

Night time on the Selemus Plains.

Camping out in a location where undead roamed about naturally meant no time to leisurely do things like pitching tents.

To keep out the cold of the late autumn night, everyone stayed close to campfires while the carriages formed a defensive circle around them. Further out, those on guard duty kept vigilant watch by their campfires.

It was a completely different scene to how their journey had been up to this point. Those in the group, former guerrilla unit members aside, looked out into the darkness with fear.

Even they had expected the journey to the Mireana Kingdom to be easy.

Still, before reaching the Selemus Plains, they had mostly slept at villages. Even when camping out in tents, it hadn’t been as tense, so they all felt the difference this night.

「I wish we could have gone all the way through the night.」

Rei muttered as he leaned against Set, who was lying on the ground outside the ring of carriages.

「Guru~…」

Set gave a cry as if to say it couldn’t be helped.

Both Rei and Set had good night vision.

If they wanted to, they could have flown over the Selemus Plains in no time.

However, that was only the two of them.

Even ordinary humans with good night vision would struggle to see in the dark when the moon was covered by clouds.

「The moon can’t be seen at all. If we had moonlight, we might have been able to push on a little further.」

Rei muttered to himself, but forcing the horses to keep going at night without rest would mean risking injury. Even ignoring that, the horses would still eventually collapse from exhaustion.

Unlike a normal merchant caravan, they weren’t carrying any extra luggage on their persons and the number of people in each carriage wasn’t high, so it wasn’t a problem for the horses to be a little tired. Still, these carriages and horses weren’t rented but owned by them.

They were moving to Gilm, an unfamiliar location to them, so no one wanted to risk such assets which would be of great use once they arrived.

「Considering all that, I guess this was the best option after all…」

「Gururu~」

Set gave a cry at Rei’s words.

However, it wasn’t because he agreed with Rei or because he was hungry. Instead, it was a warning cry.

Hearing Set’s cry, Rei stood up, picking the Death Scythe off the ground.

As he waited, he soon heard the sound of light footsteps.

Rei already knew what monster was coming from the sound.

While he wasn’t an expert in fighting undead, he still had some experience from the time he gone to the dungeon with Elena and the last two times he passed by the Selemus Plains, when going to Exil and the Bestir Empire.

The approaching footsteps belonged to a monster he had fought several times before.

Using only the light from the campfire, Rei’s night vision captured the monster that came into view.

「So it was you after all.」

A fragile looking monster, made of bone.

But, these weren’t ordinary bones, they were somewhat strengthened by magic power.

That said, these were ultimately still Skeletons, the lowest ranking undead.

It might have been a different matter if they were more powerful variants.

「If they were at least a higher ranking or rare species, I might have been able to make good use of their magic stones.」

Rei had already obtained Skeleton magic stones in the dungeon he had explored with Elena.

Both Set and the Death Scythe had absorbed one each, but hadn’t gained any skills.

Considering that Skeletons were low ranking monsters, it wasn’t entirely a surprise.

Rei readied the Death Scythe and, as the Skeletons approached, unleashed a single horizontal slash.

The Death Scythe, empowered by Rei’s magic power, was enough to strike several Skeletons…cleaving them in half at the chest, where their magic stones were located.

Because they were undead, the Skeletons didn’t die immediately.

Rei had to reach into the cavity above their severed ribs to forcibly snatch their magic stones out of their bodies.

Once the magic stones were removed…the Skeletons immediately collapsed to the ground.

For Skeletons, their magic stones were both a material and proof of subjugation.

For a high ranking adventurer like Rei, he could easily ignore Skeleton magic stones…but since he had them, he decided he might as well keep them.

After repeating this several times, all the Skeletons that had attacked him were annihilated.

Storing the magic stones back into the Misty Ring, Rei went back to Set, leaving the remains of the Skeletons behind to enjoy the comfort of Set’s soft fur…when he heard metallic sounds coming from somewhere else.

「Are Skeletons attacking other locations as well? …No, it’s not!?」

At first, Rei thought that more Skeletons were attacking, but the metallic sounds weren’t just clashing weapons, but also the sound of metal armour rubbing against itself.

Of all the people currently on night watch, none of them wore metal armour.

Of course, Rei wasn’t entirely certain of that.

It could be possible that someone who had metal armour had decided to help out, or that a former soldier or adventurer on night watch had pulled out their old metal armour.

But, when hearing the sound of metal armour on the Selemus Plains, where undead roamed about, Rei’s first thought went to Living Armour.

Rei had fought Living Armours before, armour infused with the grudges of the dead.

With Rei’s skills, they weren’t a particularly tough enemy, but their physical defenses, their metal armour, made it extremely troublesome for those who couldn’t use magic to deal with them.

「Set, I’m going to provide support…」

Now.

Rei was about to finish his sentence when he stopped himself.

More footsteps could be heard heading his way along with the rattling of bones.

「Tch, more Skeletons? …No way!」

Emerging from the darkness was a monster that seemed to be made from human bones, undoubtedly a Skeleton type monster.

However, the bones that made up its body was very different from the earlier Skeletons he had killed.

While the bones of the Skeletons from before had been white, this Skeleton’s bones seemed to be made of crystal.

No matter how you looked at it, it was definitely a more powerful monster than the Skeletons from before.

(Come to think of it, someone once told me that with so many undead on the Selemus Plains, they would sometimes fight each other. Those that survived would eventually become a higher ranking species or something. In other words, it’s like raising poisonous insects.)

Realising the true nature of the Skeleton that had appeared, Rei stared at it with a small smile.

「I’ve mostly fought humans in the Bestir Empire. It’s been a while since I’ve fought a new kind of monster.」

He readied the Death Scythe as he stared at the Skeleton with crystal bones…Crystal Skeleton, if you will.

「Guru~?」

「Yeah, leave this to me. Set, go help to deal with the Living Armour. Someone has to stay here anyway.」

Rei gave a brief reply to Set, who seemed to ask what he should do.

Whether he or Set was the one to stay behind, the outcome would probably have been the same, but as it was an unknown monster, Rei decided it would be better for him to fight and learn.

Perhaps guessing Rei’s thoughts, Set gave a short cry before running off.

After seeing Set off, Rei turned his attention back to the Crystal Skeleton with Death Scythe in hand.

Every single bone in its body was made of crystal…and it definitely looked superior to an ordinary Skeleton.

The weapon in its hand wasn’t a broken or rusty sword, like what ordinary Skeletons would have, but a crystal sword, likely created by the Crystal Skeleton themselves.

「Being able to make your own weapons is quite the handy ability. …However, using crystal also means your rank is too low for me.」

Whether it understood Rei’s words or not, the Crystal Skeleton shook its jawbone as it let out what seemed to be a roaring laugh.

It was unclear whether it was genuinely laughing or whether the night breeze had just caused its jaw to let out a laugh like sound.

However, Rei still recognised its reaction as laughter as a ferocious smile appeared on his own face.

「If you have the strength to laugh at me, I’d be more than happy…but I wonder if you really do? As a show of sympathy, I won’t use Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour. I’ll fight you normally. I haven’t had much combat training in my usual form lately.」

Swinging the Death Scythe, Rei sent a slash flying out as he stepped forward.

The Crystal Skeleton watched Rei take one, then two, then three steps towards it…before swinging its own weapon.

It was definitely faster compared to the other Skeletons.

Dodging the long sword that was swung at him, Rei sliced towards the Crystal Skeleton’s outstretched right arm with the Death Scythe.

His attack, a counter attack of sorts, easily slice through the Crystal Skeleton’s right elbow.

「Eh?」

Rei was a bit surprised at the result.

While his attack had been sharp, it had just been a test from Rei.

Surely the Crystal Skeleton wouldn’t be taken out so easily?

Rei’s anticipation for the fight promptly vanished after that.

(I guess a Skeleton is just a Skeleton after all.)

I’ll just take its magic stone and be done with it.

As he thought of that Rei went to swing the Death Scythe again…when he saw the Crystal Skeleton catch its right arm that had flown into the air after he had cut it off.

But, the next moment, all his doubts were cleared away.

Pushing the severed arm against its elbow joint, the arm was firmly reattached a moment later.

「…Wow.」

Rei let out a small exclamation at what he saw.

While he had seen many monsters that could regenerate, he had never seen one that regenerate…no, repair, using crystal.

It might not be particularly strong, but it was hard to kill.

Facing the Crystal Skeleton, Rei felt a sense of joy in his heart.

That was because he knew that the likelihood of learning a new skill from the magic stones of such monsters was quite high.

「Besides, their crystal bones will probably sell for a pretty high price as materials.」

Rei muttered to himself as he spun the Death Scythe around.

The Crystal Skeleton approached Rei with weapon in hand as its jaw clacked together.

「If you can repair yourself with crystal, then a wound doesn’t mean much…but Skeletons already have a weak point!」

Rei dashed straight towards the Crystal Skeleton.

As they approached each other, the gap between them closed in an instant.

The Crystal Skeleton swung its crystal sword to intercept Rei’s Death Scythe.

Before, Rei had counter attacked after the Crystal Skeleton’s attack. But, this time, Rei pulled the Death Scythe back just before they made contact, making the Crystal Skeleton’s sword swing through empty air.

Perhaps expecting a clash between their weapons, the Crystal Skeleton lost its balance as the anticipated clash never eventuated.

Just as the Crystal Skeleton’s body was pulled forward by the momentum of it’s missed attack…the Death Scythe swung out again.

The Crystal Skeleton was slashed right across its rib cage, where its magic stone was located, as the upper half of its chest was sent flying into the air.

Rei saw crystal growing out from where he had cut, an attempt to repair itself, but now that he knew what it was doing, there was no need to watch it happen.

He quickly reached into the empty space above its rib cage and took away its magic stone.

As soon as he did that…the Crystal Skeleton’s body crumpled to the ground.

「…Well, I guess that’s that.」

After storing the magic stone, crystal long sword, and crystal bones into the Misty Ring, Rei muttered to himself as he looked over at the direction Set had gone to.

+++

# **845**

As Rei was fighting against the Crystal Skeleton, Dietz, who was standing guard at the carriages, was fighting against a Living Armour.

The group traveling with Rei numbered about 30 people in total.

With so many non-combatants among them, in addition to those keeping watch further out, it just wasn’t possible to move that many of the capable fighters around.

And, even if they did want to provide support to another area that was under attack, they couldn’t just leave their posts as that would risk Undead attacking from their position.

Doing something like that was only possible if you had a partner, like Rei and Set.

「Tch, of all things, a Living Amour!? What a troublesome opponent!」

Dietz shouted in frustration as he thrust out his spear.

However, as a suit of metal armour possessed by grudges of the dead, it easily parried Dietz’s spear with its battleaxe.

A high pitched metallic clang rang out.

As a pure warrior who couldn’t use magic or magical skills, Dietz clicked his tongue at what could be called his nemesis.

「If Captain Rei…no, if Rei-san was here, this would be easy to deal with, but what am I supposed to do about it!」

He dodged a swing from the battleaxe, which was going to split his head in two, by taking a step back.

The battleaxe passed by his face with a loud whoosh.

It was an attack that would have definitely killed him if it had connected.

That said, Dietz was already familiar with such attacks.

「Compared to the training I received in the guerrilla unit, this is nothing!」

Stepping on the flat side of the battleaxe head after it slammed into the ground, holding it in place, he swung his spear horizontally.

Dietz had been a member of Mercurio’s elite guerrilla unit.

His spear wasn’t an ordinary wooden shaft spear but a metal shaft spear.

The metal shaft swung towards the Living Armour’s head…but just as it was about to hit, the Living Armour released its right hand from holding the battleaxe and used it to shield its head.

Another metallic clash echoed out.

In response, Dietz leaped back to distance himself from the Living Armour.

At the same time, the Living Armour’s gauntlet went right through where Dietz had been just a moment ago.

If he had delayed for even a single second, his head would have exploded like an egg being crushed.

「What a troublesome opponent!」

Dietz spat as he spoke.

It was basically impossible for him to defeat a Living Armour with what he had and could do…well, not really, but it would be very difficult.

(Damn it, the fastest way to take down these types of monsters is to steal its magic stone.)

After putting some distance between him and the Living Armour, Dietz glared at it as it reached back for its battleaxe on the ground.

He knew where its magic stone was. Inside the armour…probably near the chest.

But to get to it, he would have to do something about the armour protecting it, and every time he tried, he was blocked like before.

(I should have brought a club or a battleaxe of my own.)

When dealing with such monsters, a single powerful blow with blunt force was often better than a sharp weapon.

While Dietz was frustrated at his lack of offensive options, the Living Armour didn’t seem to know what he was thinking as it readied its battleaxe again…before raising it up for some reason.

What was it doing? Dietz was confused for a moment, but the reason soon became apparent.

「Gurururururu~!」

Along with that cry, something fell down from the night sky.

Dietz’s body stiffened up for a moment at that cry, but after realising it was a familiar one, he distanced himself even further from the Living Armour.

A moment later, there was a loud crash and the sound of something being crushed.

Looking over at where the Living Armour had been, he saw it lying on the ground, completely crushed.

The battleaxe that it had raised up had surprisingly not been destroyed and had been thrown a short distance away instead.

It was plain to see what had happened from Set’s position atop the remains of the Living Armour.

「Gururu~?」

Set had used Power Crush to destroy the Living Armour before giving a cry to ask Dietz if he was okay.

Seeing Set’s actions, Dietz quickly came back to his senses before hurriedly nodding.

「Ah, yes. Sorry for having to save me. If you hadn’t come, it would have been a lot harder.」

In typical Dietz fashion, he didn’t admit that he might have lost.

「Guru~」

Looking Dietz over and seeing that he didn’t seem to be injured, Set proceeded to pick up the Living Armour’s magic stone before leaving.

「Ah…」

Dietz was about to say something regarding the magic stone, but knowing that Set had just saved him, he decided that it wasn’t worth trying to ask for it.

「…A Living Armour’s magic stone is worth quite a bit. I guess I at least have the battleaxe though.」

Although Dietz said that, he couldn’t help but grumble a bit.

Rei was warming himself up by the campfire, completely ignoring the battle that had taken place just a short while ago

In his hand was the Crystal Skeleton’s magic stone.

「Since there’s only one, it’s either the Death Scythe or Set…but I think it will be Set.」

Rei had acquired the skill Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour while in the Bestir Empire.

He had also gained a new magic item, the New Moon Ring, a relic from an ancient magical civilisation.

In comparison, Set hadn’t acquired any notable skills or magic items during his time in the Bestir Empire.

Of course, he had gained valuable combat experience against Noiz, which held intangible value.

But Rei still wanted to give Set something to properly express his gratitude.

「Well, although it is a magic stone, it disappears once it is absorbed, so it’s not really something tangible either.」

Rei tossed a dead branch into the fire.

As he watched the flames grow as the fire crackled, he noticed the sound of something running towards him.

Rei didn’t even have to guess who it was.

Eventually, as he expected, Set emerged from the darkness.

「Gururururu~」

Set gave a happy cry as he went over to Rei and handed over the magic stone in his beak.

「Hm? Thanks. If you brought it back, does that mean this is the Living Armour’s magic stone?」

「Guru~」

Yes, Set seemed to say with a cry.

Rei gently stroked Set as he took the magic stone.

Set had already absorbed the magic stone of a Living Armour from the last time Rei had defeated one.

Considering that, it would be best for the Death Scythe to absorb this one instead.

(If I do this, it doesn’t feel like a thank you gift any more but a trade of magic stones…I guess I’ll find another way to thank him later.)

Hearing more sounds of combat a short distance away, Rei handed the magic stone of the Crystal Skeleton to Set.

「Set, this is the Crystal Skeleton’s magic stone. I’ll trade you it for the Living Armour magic stone.」

「Guru~!?」

Set gave a happy cry at Rei’s words.

Set couldn’t absorb magic stones from battles he didn’t participate in.

But, having been created from Rei’s magic power, Set could still absorb magic stones from monsters that Rei killed.

…Of course, whether he would learn any new skills was a different matter entirely.

「Gurururu~」

With another happy cry, Set swallowed the magic stone in his beak.

【Set has acquired the skill 『Crystal Breath Lv.1』】

The announcement echoed through Rei’s mind.

「Crystal Breath, huh? I can guess what kind of skill it is, but it would still be best to try it out. Luckily everyone is either keeping watch or asleep right now, so there’s no need to worry about anyone seeing it.」

Rei muttered as he looked around.

Not only could he see the area lit up by the campfire, but his night vision allowed him to see further into the surroundings as well.

As far as Rei could tell, no one was looking in their direction.

Of course, he knew that there were some people in the carriages who weren’t quite able to sleep comfortably in their current environment.

They would have been woken up by the sudden sounds of battle. And, since they were on the Selemus Plains, the only thing that could be attacking would be undead.

Unless they were a former adventurer, someone with an army background, or had grown up in rough conditions, it would be difficult to sleep in such conditions.

「Try it, but not too hard, we don’t want to disturb the others.」

「Guru~」

Set gave a brief cry at Rei’s words and then moved a short distance from the campfire before taking a deep breath and using Crystal Breath towards the sky.

「Gururururu~」

Set used Crystal Breath as quietly as he could and it soon vanished into the air.

「…Huh?」

Rei tilted his head in confusion, having expected something different.

「I was sure the skill would shoot out a crystal spear or arrow, or maybe just chunks of crystal along with the breath…」

「Guru~」

Set bowed his head apologetically and Rei shook his head in a panic as he patted Set.

「Don’t worry about it. It’s not like skills always turn out the way I expect them to. Besides, from what we saw earlier, it seems like it mixes crystals into the breath to inflict physical damage. So…I see, could you try it against this next?」

Saying that, Rei picked up a piece of firewood intended for the campfire.

Seeing Set give a cry in understanding, Rei tossed the piece of wood into the air.

「Gurururu~」

Just like before, Set released a breath attack from his beak again.

The breath struck the piece of wood that Rei had thrown into the air perfectly.

Picking the piece of wood up a short distance away, Rei noticed something strange about it.

The wood seemed to be covered in a thin layer of crystal.

Touching the wood with his palm, it definitely didn’t feel like wood.

However, the crystal coating wasn’t particularly thick nor was it firmly stuck to the wood. When he slammed the wood into his palm, the crystals broke apart and scattered to the ground.

「I see. So instead of mixing chunks of crystal into the breath, it traps the target in crystal. …It could certainly be useful depending on how it’s used, but at level 1, I think it would only slow the target down a little?」

Covering someone in crystal was more likely to surprise and alarm those around the target rather than the target themselves.

While thinking of that, Rei patted Set lightly on the head, who seemed to be in disbelief that the skill might not be of any use.

「It might be hard to use now, but we can always level it up. Well, I don’t know what kind of monster magic stones we’d need to absorb though. Besides, it’s not entirely useless.」

Saying that, Rei picked up some of the crystal that had fallen off the piece of wood as he showed it to Set.

What? What? Set seemed curious as Rei spoke up to persuade him.

Rei spoke as the piece of crystal lay in the palm of his hand.

「This is still crystal, so a craftsman or blacksmith should be willing to buy it. I think such crystals can also be used as alchemy material, so with your Crystal Breath, you’ll never be short of money.」

Of course, Rei already had a lot of money.

Enough to retire for the rest of his life.

So considering that, while the crystals could be used to make a little money in case of an emergency, he didn’t care for it that much.

Rei never had a strong attachment to money to begin with.

Still, money could be used to buy a lot of things, and considering their food expenses, it was always better to have more than not enough.

「Well then, it’s my turn now. Shall we use the Living Armour magic stone that you brought back?」

「Guru~!」

Set gave a happy cry at Rei’s words, as if his previous dejection hadn’t existed at all.

Seeing his reaction, Rei turned to look at the Living Armour’s magic stone.

However, he didn’t have an expression of anticipation for an unknown result on his face.

Set had previously learned Power Crush when he absorbed a Living Armour’s magic stone.

Since that was the case, this would probably level up the Death Scythe’s Power Slash to level 3.

At least, that was what Rei thought.

While Power Slash was a strong attack skill for Rei, it also wasn’t really quite his fighting style.

(Plus, every time I use Power Slash, it has a kickback through my wrist. If I don’t use it carefully, it will end up hurting me more.)

Rei recalled how much his wrists had hurt as he looked at his grip on the Death Scythe.

But, since Set had brought him the magic stone and was now watching expectantly from a short distance away, Rei threw it up into the air.

He then struck it with the Death Scythe.

The blade cut straight through the magic stone.

【Death Scythe has acquired the skill 『Flying Slash Lv.4』】

An announcement echoed through his mind.

「…Eh?」

Rei couldn’t help but be surprised at the upgrade of a completely different skill than he had expected.

---

【Set】

『Water Ball Lv.3』 『Fire Breath Lv.3』 『Wind Arrow Lv.3』 『King’s Awe Lv.1』 『Poison Claw Lv.4』 『Size Transformation Lv.1』 『Tornado Lv.1』 『Ice Arrow Lv.1』 『Optical Camouflage Lv.2』 『Evil Eye Impact Lv.1』 『Power Crush Lv.2』 『Sense Enhancement – Smell　Lv.1』 『Bubble Breath Lv.1』 『Crystal Breath Lv.1』 new

【Death Scythe】

『Corrosion　Lv.3』 『Flying Slash Lv.4』 new 『Magic Shield Lv.1』 『Power Slash Lv.2』 『Wind Hand Lv.3』 『Terrain Manipulation Lv.1』『Pain Burst　Lv.1』 『Penetrate Lv.2』

Crystal Breath: A breath that traps the opponent in crystal. Since the current level is low, it only has the ability to coat the opponent in crystal. However, it can still slow an opponent’s movement.

Flying Slash: A skill that launches a slash. While it has decent strength, only a single slash can be launched at a time.

+++

# **846**

Black clouds covered the sky over the Selemus Plains.

They were clearly rain clouds and it wouldn’t be strange if it started raining at any time.

The temperature had also dropped, with the wind sapping the energy of the carriage drivers.

Even in such weather, Rei, who was leading the carriages, turned to look at the Death Scythe in his right hand.

It had acquired a new skill last night, Flying Slash level 4.

Several more Skeletons had appeared the previous night while he was still on night watch, so he had taken the opportunity to try it out and it was clear that Flying Slash had definitely powered up.

The slash that was released was both larger and more powerful than before.

It easily cut through the Skeletons’ ribs, destroying the magic stone within.

…As a result, he had also failed to collect their magic stones.

(But why Flying Slash from a Living Armour? Dietz told me this morning that the Living Armour had used a battleaxe. Considering that, it would have made more sense to level up Power Slash.)

As Rei thought to himself, a smile still formed on his lips.

It was a matter of course. Flying Slash was one of his most versatile skills after all.

It was extremely convenient for Rei to be able to attack from long distances using the Death Scythe.

In terms of long range attacks, he did have other options, including magic, arrowheads created by Nebula’s Eye, and throwing spears.

Throwing spears in particular were favoured by Rei when attacking from range.

However, throwing spears required Rei to take one out from the Misty Ring, aim, adjust, and then throw while magic needed an incantation.

In that respect, Nebula’s Eye, which could create arrowheads from magic power, was a very useful magic item. The fact it could stay hidden under the Dragon Robe gave it a surprise factor as well.

The downside was that it didn’t really have much range.

Taking all that into account, the Flying Slash skill, which could simply be used by aiming and swinging the Death Scythe, was very useful.

Although he still wasn’t sure why he had leveled up the skill from the magic stone of a Living Armour, Rei still smiled in satisfaction.

As a side note, while Set took the magic stone, the battleaxe that the Living Armour had used was collected by Dietz.

Even though keeping watch at night was a necessity, Rei knew that they wouldn’t take it seriously if there wasn’t any reward. As a result, he had made the decision that the materials, magic stones, or monster parts from any monsters, which could all be sold for money, would belong to the person who defeated the monsters.

Of course, Rei wasn’t exactly the official leader of the group.

But, since the group was mostly made up of former guerrilla unit members, no one dared to disagree with Rei.

There were a couple of people who were dissatisfied with this arrangement, but not to the point that they would say anything to Rei and Set.

As a result, Set, who had been the one to defeat the Living Armour, received its magic stone while Dietz got everything else.

That said, because Set used Power Crush on the Living Armour, destroying it completely, the only thing that Dietz could retrieve was the battleaxe it had used.

As a battleaxe used by a Living Armour, it was by no means an ordinary weapon.

In fact, thanks to the Living Armour, it had become something close to a magic weapon.

…One could even call it a slightly cursed weapon.

Still, it would likely fetch a decent amount of money if sold. Dietz nodded in satisfaction as he asked Rei to store it into the Misty Ring for him.

「Rei, don’t you think we should hurry up a bit? If we keep going at this rate, the rain will fall while we’re still on the Selemus Plains.」

Vihera called out to Rei from on her horse, riding alongside Set.

At her voice, Rei looked up and saw that the rain clouds had become even darker than before. He nodded at Vihera before turning around to speak.

「We’ll be speeding up, any issues!?」

No one objected.

That was a matter of course. If it started raining while they were still on the Selemus Plains, their visibility would drop significantly.

That meant a higher chance of failing to see Undead attacking them in the rain.

The ground wasn’t even properly paved here, meaning that there were holes and large rocks scattered all around.

They all agreed that traveling through the area in the rain would be a bad idea, so they followed Rei’s advice to speed up, even if it was a bit reckless.

This continued for another hour or so. Fortunately, despite the rain clouds, no rain fell and they soon saw the end of the Selemus Plains.

Their speed had only been possible due to the light weight in the carriages and the lack of unnecessary luggage.

Even when Undead did appear, Rei and Set were able to dispatch them easily as they led way. As for Undead approaching from other directions, they were all dealt with by Vihera and the former guerrilla unit members.

(Rei-san defeated the S rank Immovable Noiz and Vihera-sama defeated the A rank Water Dragon Digma. With those two escorting us, they could probably hand an entire country’s army, let alone a few Undead.)

The thought crossed Sergio’s mind as he kept a watchful eye over the carriages.

He was friendly, polite, and skilled enough to work as a solo adventurer.

…That said, he had only become a solo adventurer due his former party disbanding for various reasons.

All that considered, Sergio, who was quite the anomaly himself, found Rei to be even more surprising.

One of the reasons for heading to the Mireana Kingdom was that he didn’t want to fight against Rei, but a bigger reason was that he was intrigued by Rei himself.

「Sergio, Zombies over there! Should we attack with our bows?」

Sergio quickly shook his head at Dietz’s words as he gave his orders

「The Zombies can’t keep up with our speed, ignore them.」

「Got it!」

Giving orders while still deep in thought, they continued straight across the Selemus Plains.

「We’re out!」

Rei’s voice reached everyone.

As they looked around, they noticed that the atmosphere around them had definitely changed.

「Huraaaaaaaaaay!」

Someone let out a joyful shout.

As if in response, others started to do the same.

「We did it! We’re out! We’re in the Mireana Kingdom now!」

「Woooooo-!」

「Yeeeeeees-!」

The former guerrilla unit members weren’t the only ones shouting out. It was the same for those who had been tensely watching their surroundings from inside the carriages.

No, for those who weren’t used to dealing with such difficult situations, their joy was probably even greater.

Rei, who was still leading the carriages, looked around to make sure there were no abnormalities.

Undead generally didn’t leave the Selemus Plains, but that wasn’t a guarantee.

Even after entering the borders of the Mireana Kingdom, there was still a chance that they would run into Undead that had left the Selemus Plains for whatever reason.

「The nearest village is called Goto. We’ll be spending the night there.」

They had already discussed the plan beforehand, but Rei said it again to confirm with everyone.

His words seemed to bring everyone back to their senses as they nodded with serious expressions.

「Goto isn’t a particularly big village either. There’s no lodging there, so we’ll either have to sleep in the carriages or pay someone to let us stay in their houses. …It will probably be just as cramped, if not more so…」

「It can’t be helped. We should just be lucky that we don’t have to keep watch all night at this time of the year.」

Rei nodded at Sergio’s words.

「Well then, let’s get going.」

With those words, the group continued on their way to Goto.

(The Mireana Kingdom…we’re back.）

Rei gave the order to keep going as he hid his feelings in his heart.

The guards standing out in the cold at Goto’s gates could only imagine the warm food they would be able to eat after night fell as they kept watch against any monsters and bandits that might try to enter the village.

While they were wearing warm clothing to protect themselves from the cold, it still couldn’t fully keep out the chill that would freeze their body to the core.

As they stamped their feet to try and warm themselves a little…

「H-Hey! Look!」

One of the two guards called out as he saw something in his vision.

As the other guard turned to look as well, his eyes widened so much that he couldn’t even speak.

That was only natural. A group of nearly twenty carriages was heading towards their village.

Even a small merchant caravan would only have a few carriages at most, so nearly twenty carriages was the equivalent of an army passing through during a war.

「W-What are they? Bandits?」

「You can’t be thinking that bandits would have that many carriages…no, wait. Hey, look. At the front of the carriages!」

Turning to look again at his partner’s words, he saw a figure riding on the back of a Griffon.

The figure was small and their face was hidden by a hood.

However, the guards immediately knew who it was after seeing them riding on a Griffon.

They had stayed in Goto village a while ago after all, traveling to the Bestir Empire with Margrave Rowlocks.

Margrave Rowlocks had returned some time ago but the Griffon was nowhere to be seen. The guards remembered how the villagers, the children in particular, had been extremely disappointed that night.

「Rei…he’s returned?」

「Yeah. Since they’re riding a Griffon, it’s definitely Rei. But, what would have led to him leading a group of so many carriages like that?」

The villages knew that Rei had a Griffon familiar, but he wasn’t the type of person to lead a large group of subordinates.

However, from what they could tell, Rei was definitely leading the carriages behind him.

Furthermore, next to Rei was another familiar figure.

Despite the coming arrival of cold winter weather, Vihera was still clad in her thin clothes that would make others feel cold just looking at her.

Her position next to Rei made it look like she was his second in command.

In reality, they weren’t a mercenary group or even a merchant caravan, just a group of people moving house…but that was impossible for the guards to tell in this situation.

「What do we do?」

「No, not what do we do…what can we even do?」

As they pondered the question, Rei’s group steadily approached.

One of them should have gone to call for the village chief, but due to their confusion by the unexpected sight, they were still there by the time Rei’s group arrived at the village gate.

「It’s been a while. …Do you still remember me?」

Rei called out to them in a friendly voice as he took off his hood. The guards seemed to come to their senses as they replied.

「Yes, I remember. It’s hard to forget someone who has a tamed Griffon following them. But, you went to the Bestir Empire with Margrave Rowlocks, didn’t you? So how did you end up coming back with a group like this?」

「Well, a lot has happened since. Those people behind me want to move to the Mireana Kingdom.」

「…You couldn’t have been involved in the Bestir Empire civil war, right?」

Although it was a rural village, Goto was also the village closest to the Bestir Empire, just across the Selemus Plains.

Naturally, those traveling between the two countries would often stop by Goto to rest.

As a result, word of the civil war had quickly spread here through such people.

「Who knows. Let’s just say it was quite the profitable trip.」

The guard gave a wry smile at Rei’s response.

「I get the general idea from your reply. …Now then, you’re going to enter the village, right? If so, please show us your id.」

At the guard’s request, Rei took out his guild card from the Misty Ring and handed it over to the guard.

At the same time, the others behind Rei also showed their identification documents to the guards, completing the procedures to enter the village without any issues.

Set also received a Necklace of Subservient Monster…and like so, Rei and the others entered the village of Goto.

+++

# **847**

「Well then, village chief, I’ll be happy to stay in the village for the night.」

Goto’s village chief nodded at Rei’s words.

He even had a smile on his face as he nodded, probably because of the monetary compensation they had received for housing so many people in their village.

Housing nearly 30 strangers was an uncomfortable thought for most of Goto’s villagers.

This was in addition to the fact that basically all those people were from the Bestir Empire, so it wasn’t surprising that the villagers would be a little fearful, considering their village was basically on the front line of any war between the Mireana Kingdom and Bestir Empire.

Still, they agreed to house everyone for the night not just because of the extra winter income they would receive, but also because of Rei and Set.

Rei and Set had previously stayed in the village for some time and the villagers naturally remembered him.

The two of them had been well received and accepted by the villagers as well.

Seeing that the group was led by Rei and Set, they believed that problems were unlikely to occur.

That wasn’t to say that many residents didn’t still have concerns though.

That was why Rei had made a promise before the village chief and residents of Goto that if anyone in his group behaved in a manner that was problematic, he would punish them himself.

The villagers, who knew Rei’s strength, were relieved by his words. At the same time, Rei’s words made the newcomers in his group more cautious, knowing that they would face punishment if they did anything bad.

The former guerrilla unit members all admired Rei, so Rei didn’t really need to worry about them too much.

Rei’s real concern were the others who had joined along with the former guerrilla unit members…that said, their journey up until this point had made them realise that Rei was more than he appeared to be, not to mention that many of them had seen Rei fight in the tournament.

Above all, no one really dared to have any strange thoughts with Set around.

In the end, everything was sorted out without any major issues, even though everyone was rather subdued…and somewhat timid.

「Rei-san, Vihera-san, and Set as well. It’s been a while, hasn’t it?」

Rei and Vihera turned to face the familiar voice.

It was a man with a rugged build and face, but a gentle voice.

Standing next to him was a boy about 5 years old.

「Ruchard, Apika. It has been a while indeed. How have you two been?」

「Gurururu~?」

「It really has been a while, hasn’t it?」

The three of them replied in their own ways.

Ruchard and Apika had a close relationship with Rei during his stay in Goto.

Rei had stayed in Ruchard’s house and Apika had become quite attached to Rei and Set.

They were the two people closest to him in Goto.

「Yes. Thanks to you, nothing major has happened since then. A few nobles from other countries did pass through here, but luckily Margrave Rowlocks kept a close eye on them.」

「From other countries?」

Rei was a little puzzled while Vihera nodded in understanding.

「They must have been people passing through the Mireana Kingdom to return to their own countries from the Bestir Empire.」

「…Well, we are next to the Bestir Empire after all, so I guess it’s only natural.」

「Not really though? Most people wouldn’t try to enter the Bestir Empire from a country they have bad relations with, like the Mireana Kingdom. In fact, when we were heading to Bestir Empire, we didn’t see anyone else going this way, right?」

「Then why?」

Rei tilted his head in greater confusion.

His gesture was so charming that it was hard to believe he was the one who had earned the title of Crimson.

Like a boy on the verge of becoming a young man.

…Of course, internally, Rei had always considered himself to be a young man.

(Maybe…I just have a thing for younger guys? Of course, being strong is a given.)

Vihera briefly considered those thoughts in her mind as she looked at Rei before quickly regaining her composure and continuing to speak.

「There’s really only one reason, isn’t there? No matter how well known you might be or the fact that you have a title, it’s unprecedented for a B rank adventurer to fight on nearly equal terms with an S rank adventurer. If those who had come to the Bestir Empire representing their countries wanted to gather even the slightest bit more information on you, the quickest and most accurate method would be to come to the Mireana Kingdom.」

「I guess you’re right. Margrave Rowlocks’ escort said basically the same thing to us. But they also said those people were unlikely to find out much.」

「Well, I basically only work from Gilm after all.」

Rei nodded after reaching an understanding.

Gilm was a frontier town where powerful monsters roamed about both day and night.

As Rei’s sole base of operations, it was hard to find specific information about Rei as a result, even within the Mireana Kingdom.

The only exceptions were what here had done in Baar, which had become well known due to the outbreak of Magic Fever there, and his achievements in the war with the Bestir Empire that had taken place on the Selemus Plains. Rei had also done a few things around the Port City Emoshion as well as the Labyrinth City Exil.

To the average person, Rei might be considered someone who had gone to many towns and villages, but for an adventurer, whose usual work would often bring them from town to town and village to village, there really wasn’t much that could be found out about what Rei had done.

More so because it had only been two years since Rei had first registered as an adventurer in Gilm.

In such a situation, nobles from other countries were unlikely to have been able to find much out about Rei, so their efforts in coming to the Mireana Kingdom were mostly in vain.

They might have been able to find out more if they had actually gone to Gilm, but as most were just taking a detour on their way back home, very few had the time to go all the way out to the frontier where Gilm was.

「Well, all that aside, leave the decision on who stays where for the night to me. I’ll bring everyone through the village.」

「Thank you.」

Rei replied as he watched Apika play around with Set.

「Here, have this, I can’t give you too much though.」

Rei and his group split up to the various homes they would be staying at for the night, leaving Rei and Vihera at Ruchard’s place.

Ruchard offered them some preserved fruit.

To Rei, it was basically what he would call dried fruit.

It went without saying that it was a rather valuable commodity in a rural village like this.

「Is this okay?」

「Yes, it’s to celebrate the safe return of Rei and Vihera…and…」

He turned to look out the door.

Set and Apika were currently playing outside.

Playing outside in a season like this was something only children could do.

(I guess the saying that kids are ‘children of the wind’ is an accurate expression even in this world.)

Thinking like that, the thought occurred to Rei that perhaps he himself was also a ‘child of the wind’. He quickly shook his head to get rid of the thought.

While he might look 15, he definitely wasn’t that young.

「Rei-san?」

「No, it’s nothing. Anyway, let me try some then.」

Rei reached for the dried fruit on the wooden plate.

It seemed that the fruit had become a little denser from being dried as it had a firm texture in his mouth.

As he bit into it, it was as firm and chewy as it had felt in his hand. At the same time a rich sweetness spread through his mouth.

「…Delicious.」

It was a simple taste, but one that Rei found delightful.

「Yes, it really is delicious.」

Vihera smiled like Rei as she savoured the dried fruit.

Of course, the reason reason why Vihera was at Ruchard’s house as well was because she would be staying the night here.

Rei had accepted it because he knew that Ruchard would be present as well.

There were already hardly any other vacancies at all the other houses and considering Vihera’s appearance, it would be careless of Rei to let her stay at any other house.

「Still, I’m really surprised though. I can’t believe you brought such a group back with you, Rei.」

Ruchard spoke again as he ate some of the dried fruit himself. While he sounded surprised, he expression was smiling and didn’t seem to display any of the surprise in his tone.

「Well, a lot of things happened.」

「Fufu~, that’s right. A lot of things happened, in many ways.」

Vihera replied to Rei’s words in a teasing tone as she agreed.

Ruchard watched the two of them with a smile.

Feeling somewhat uncomfortable, Rei took out some ingredients form the Misty Ring.

Among them was the bear that Set had hunted close to the Imperial Capital…but Rei didn’t worry about it too much as he handed everything over to Ruchard.

「I’d like to have a dinner party with all the villagers tonight. What do you think? Oh, I can provide all the ingredients. There won’t be much alcohol though…」

Rei’s Misty Ring naturally held a large amount of supplies that would need for a journey like this.

In addition to those supplies, there were also a lot of ingredients that Rei had bought for his own use, not to mention meat from monsters he had killed.

As for alcohol, the reason there wasn’t much was because Rei didn’t particularly like it himself.

That said, he still had some because he expected he would need it on occasions like this, and maybe for cooking particular dishes.

Aside from what he had in his own reserves, some of the people in the group had also brought alcohol among their luggage that they had left with Rei.

「Are you really sure? Well, we’d be more than happy of course.」

「Yes. We’re causing quite the trouble for the village after all. If you consider that, this is no big deal.」

「I understand. I’ll go and speak to the village chief. It’s true that even if it just one night, it would be better to be on good terms with everyone when sleeping under the same roof.」

「Thank you.」

Rei’s words made Ruchard smile as he left.

「A dinner party. Well, considering we’ve made it out of the Selemus Plains and entered the Mireana Kingdom, this is a good time to do it.」

「Yeah, that’s one of the reasons. Another reason is that even if they are traveling with me, they’ll probably be looked down at quite a bit when they first arrive at Gilm. This is also meant to be encouragement to them to not give in.」

Some didn’t want to fight Rei, some admired him, others wanted to be close to Set, and so on.

Everyone had their own reasons for deciding to leave with Rei, but the fact remained that they were all from the Bestir Empire.

Leaving the adventurers aside, Rei guessed that Daska, lord of Gilm and a leading figure in the Neutral faction, would be unlikely to trust them so easily.

「Cheers everyone!」

『Cheers!』

Although it was a late autumn night, everyone was having a good time around the bonfire.

People from Goto village as well as Rei’s group clinked cups together as they all toasted each other.

In the end, it had been decided that Rei would be in charge of the food while Goto would handle the alcohol.

Of course, this wasn’t a strict restriction.

Rei provided some drinks and Goto helped out with the ingredients as well.

Like this, everyone was able to enjoy a feast without worrying about what everyone else was thinking.

Of course, this wasn’t to say that no one had any reservations, but at the very least, no one showed it.

From the perspective of the villagers, they couldn’t really fight against Rei and Set, and conversely, the people in Rei’s group didn’t want to embarrass him by causing trouble either.

…Of course, the majority of them were just enjoying the feast to its fullest without a care in the world.

「Gurururu~」

Set gave happy cries from next to Rei as he stretched his beak out to the plate of stir fried bear meat.

Set had wanted to eat bear meat on the day they left the Imperial Capital, but his wish hadn’t come true.

Of course, the food he was given was delicious enough and he had been satisfied with what he had to eat. But, his desire for bear meat still lingered in the end.

That was why Set was so happy when Rei had taken out the bear meat from the Misty Ring as part of the dinner.

「Eh? Set was the one to catch the bear!? Wow, amazing. That’s Set for you!」

Apika stroked Set happily after hearing about Set’s bear hunting adventure from Rei.

Set gave a happy cry from being stroked as he ate the bear meat.

「Come on, don’t get in the way of Set enjoying his food.」

Apika’s mother scolded him.

Rei had already been formally introduced to Apika’s parents and they had chatted a little with each other.

But, to Apika, all that mattered was that he was happy to be with Set.

「Guru~?」

Would you like some to? Set seemed to ask as he looked up at Apika from his plate of stir fried bear meat.

「Yes!」

Apika happily reached for some of the stir fried bear meat on the plate.

「…Holding a dinner party was the right decision.」

There had been a bit of tension when Rei’s group had first arrived in Goto.

But now, looking around, it seemed like everyone was enjoying the party and getting to know each other.

That alone made providing the food worthwhile.

As he thought of that, Rei reached for some skewers grilling over the bonfire nearby.

+++

# **848**

The day after the dinner party.

It was still pretty dark outside, but Rei’s group were already preparing to depart Goto.

A few of them were still hungover, seemingly still drowning in drink from the previous night.

Some looked at them with sympathy, but most just held expressions of disappointment from self inflicted suffering.

It was only natural. They had been told before the dinner party that they would be leaving early the next morning and warned to not leave anything behind, yet they were still in this state.

「Here, drink this. It should help you feel a little better.」

「Sorry, auntie…I’ll be glad to accept it.」

An elderly woman, the resident of the house the man had stayed at, handed him a wooden cup filled with some sort of liquid.

The man tried to gulp it down, but grimaced the next moment at the foul tasting liquid that spread through his mouth.

「Hahaha. There’s no way for medicine to taste good. Come on, drink it all in one go. You’re a man!」

「Ugh…I get it. Oh man, be brave!」
