Giving a shout to encourage himself, he chugged the cup in one gulp.

As the man moved the cup away from his mouth, the expression on his face seemed like he had just seen all the despair in the world.

「…Can this really soothe my hangover headache…」

「I don’t know. But we’ll be traveling in a carriage soon, right? Better than suffering from a hangover headache then.」

The man couldn’t help but agree.

Riding in a carriage with a hangover while it rocked around would be pure torture.

Compared to that, it would be better to just suffer the taste of the hangover medicine.

Similar exchanges were taking place elsewhere before everyone was ready to depart.

「Well, thanks for taking care of me for the night.」

「No, last night’s party was fun. You are very welcome. If you’re ever in the area again, please stop by.」

「…If I’m ever in the area, that probably means I have business in the Selemus Plains or Bestir Empire, but I’ll stop by again if I do come by.」

After his brief exchange with Ruchard, Rei turned to look at his feet, or more precisely, to Apika, who was stroking Set as Rei sat on top.

「Thanks for taking good care of Set, Apika.」

「…Yes.」

Apika’s words made it clear he was trying very hard to not show his loneliness.

Apika really didn’t want to be separated from Set.

But he also knew he couldn’t be selfish here, so he had no choice but to nod as he held back his tears.

「Guru~…」

Set rubbed his face against Apika, telling him to cheer up.

But, that seemed to be the final straw for Apika.

The next moment, tears started to spill from his eyes.

「Sniff, sniff…h-hey. You’ll come again, right? This won’t be the last time, right?」

Apika spoke to Set as he rubbed the tears from his eyes.

However, Set didn’t understand why Apika had suddenly burst into tears and just continued to rub his head against Apika to cheer him up.

This only made Apika more determined to not be separated from Set as he cried even harder.

Seeing Apika’s state, several of the former guerrilla unit members nodded in understanding.

「I know…I know. It would be sad if I had to leave Set as well.」

「That’s right. It would be painful to be separated from Set.」

「Ugh, what a tale…」

Seeing everyone murmuring, Rei sighed softly before placing his hand on Apika’s head.

「Look, if I ever come around again I’ll come and see you at Goto. You’d better get over your crybaby ways by then. Otherwise Set will be laughing at you.」

「Uh, yeah…I know…」

Apika frantically wiped his eyes at Rei’s words before getting those words out.

「Gururu~…」

Set rubbed his face against Apika again.

But this time, Apika didn’t burst into tears as he gently stroked Set’s head.

Seeing that, Rei spoke up.

「We’ll probably be camping out tonight, but unlike the Selemus Plains, there shouldn’t be that many monsters. However, we might run into bandits instead, so make sure to stay alert. Also, from here on, we’ll be traveling in the Mireana Kingdom. If you cause any trouble, it could be perceived as sabotage by the Bestir Empire, so be extremely careful of what you do.」

Everyone nodded with a serious look on their face.

They were well aware that a group like them could easily arouse suspicion.

(Come to think of it, it’s a good thing we’re headed for Gilm. If we had gone somewhere else, we might have found ourselves in some kind of trouble.)

Rei thought to himself as he recalled the many nobles he had encountered up to this point before giving a shout.

「Then, we’re heading off!」

Rei lightly patted Set on the back, who started walking without any other signal.

Following behind him were Vihera, on horseback, and the rest of the carriages.

Behind them all, the villagers of Goto waved vigorously as they saw them off.

「How peaceful…」

A few hours had passed since they had left Goto. They had been traveling along the road without any particular incidents when Rei heard a voice say that.

Indeed, they had run into any trouble since leaving Goto, so those words weren’t wrong.

This was especially so because Rei had warned them greatly before they had set off, so they were probably all feeling both tense and bored.

「You know, you might be bored, but you should still keep an eye out on the surroundings.」

「Even if you say that, with Set here, there’s no point in us doing any of that.」

「…That’s…」

The woman driving a neighbouring carriage gave a warning, but the man retorted immediately.

What he said wasn’t wrong either, so the woman just kept quite and didn’t respond.

Any former guerrilla unit member who had fought alongside Rei knew just how sharp Set’s senses were from the civil war.

That was why the woman didn’t try to make any excuses.

「Rei, are you going to do anything about it?」

She must have heard the conversation as well, Vihera pulled her horse alongside Rei as she asked him.

However, Rei shook his head.

「They might be like that right now, but when the time comes, they’ll do what they need to do. They’re still feeling the effects from last night’s dinner party. They were so well welcomed in the first village they arrived at after entering the Mireana Kingdom, so maybe that’s to be expected.」

「…But honestly, the reason they were so welcoming is mostly because you provided all the food, right?」

「I won’t deny that.」

Rei immediately replied to Vihera’s question.

In fact, the main reason why the villagers were so friendly was that they knew Rei, Vihera, and the cute looking A rank Griffon, Set.

If that was all, they would only have been friendly to the three of them. They were friendly to everyone in Rei’s group because Rei had provided food for the dinner party.

Still, Rei felt that it was something he needed to do.

Receiving such a warm welcome in the first village they arrived at after entering the Mireana Kingdom.

It would have some effect on alleviating the anxiety that would come with those who had decided to go to Gilm with Rei.

He wouldn’t go as far as to say it would create a sense of affinity towards the Mireana Kingdom…but it should at least lower their psychological hurdle.

It wasn’t something he had planned for before getting to Goto and the dinner party was mostly a decision made at the moment, but simply providing food had proven to be effective enough.

「Well, it’s fine as long as they can get used to the Mireana Kingdom. They made the effort to move all the way here. If they were to want to go back soon after, it would be a lot of trouble.」

「Oh, you’re so caring. I’d be happy if you could be that caring towards me as well.」

「That’s a separate issue, isn’t it? Anyway…huh?」

Rei, who had been talking to Vihera, stopped mid conversation as he looked over towards a 3m tall boulder by the side of the road ahead of them.

He thought he saw something moving just now…

He sighed after realising what it had been before smiling.

「Autumn is almost over and they’re still working so hard. I wish they would channel their work ethic into helping adventurers instead of stealing.」

「Gurururu~」

Set seemed to realise the same thing as Rei as he gave a cry in agreement.

A few seconds later, Vihera also realised what Rei and Set had noticed.

「I see. They certainly have a strong work ethic. But, showing such a work ethic here is only going to cause trouble for the people around here.」

「Exactly. Besides, this isn’t too far from the Selemus Plains, right? Even if they waited here, hardly any prey would pass by. …Well, whatever. They’ve come all the way out here. Let’s take them out and force them to tell us where their hideout is. It will be a decent pay out. Plus, it would be bad if they ended up attacking Goto.」

Rei spoke, as if trying to come up with an excuse, before turning to look behind him.

「Did they think we were a merchant caravan? That could be possible. Whatever, doesn’t matter. Listen up! There are probably some bandits waiting around the rocks ahead of us!」

Hearing Rei’s voice, the reactions of the passengers in the carriages were split in two.

One reaction was fear.

They had been attacked by bandits several times along their journey, although they had been repelled each time.

They had even saw Rei raid the bandits’ hideout, stealing the treasure they had hoarded.

But still, to the average person, bandits were still something to be feared.

As for the other reaction, it was all smiles.

The smile of a hunter, happy to have caught their prey.

The reactions of the latter belonged to Rei, Vihera, the former guerrill unit members, former adventurers, and former soldiers, who understood that their groups’ current combat strength was something that could be called excessive.

They had seen Rei’s combat strength during the civil war and throughout their journey and they were also confident in their own skills, so bandit attacks were just seen as an opportunity to make some money.

Despite the extreme difference in reactions, Rei’s group continued along the road seemingly unaware of their fate. …Eventually, as they approached the large rock, figures appeared on top of and around it, drawing bows as they shot arrows towards Rei’s group.

(Wow, they even climbed the rock to shoot arrows at us. That’s some thought for bandits.)

Standing on Set’s back, Rei admired their planning as he took the Death Scythe out of the Misty Ring and began to swing it around.

With just those swings, all the arrows heading Rei’s way were swept aside.

Glancing back, he saw the former guerrilla unit members, who were acting as carriage drivers, using their weapons to cut down the arrows raining down on them.

Vihera, the only one among them who specialised in hand to hand combat, didn’t use any weapons to fight back but grabbed the arrows out of mid air instead as she threw them to the ground.

「W-What’s with this group!?」

The bandits were surprised to see the response from Rei’s group.

They had found a group of carriages…and not just any carriagse, but enclosed carriages, which were eve more expensive than covered wagons, so they had assumed it was a merchant caravan and waited here to attack them. But, despite launching the most complete ambush they could, all their arrows had been blocked.

At this point, the bandit leader realised that this was no ordinary merchant caravan and, despite being annoyed by the fact, loosed another arrow.

Now that they had attacked, they could only push through and kill everyone or at least incapacitate enough people to steal their goods.

「Keep shooting! If we let them get any closer, we’re all doomed!」

At the bandit leader’s words, the other bandits shot their arrows desperately.

They knew that their target was stronger than them, but they were already too close to run away.

Even if they did run away, they wouldn’t make it out in time.

As they continued to loose arrows, hoping to inflict a wound on at least one enemy, one bandit suddenly noticed something.

「Boss! Isn’t that a Griffon leading the carriages!?」

「What!?」

Looking more closely at the bandit’s words, the bandit leader saw that there was indeed a Griffon leading the carriages with someone wearing a robe on their back.

They were a lot smaller than the carriages, so they hadn’t noticed it at first, but once they did, it wasn’t hard to figure out who it was.

「It’s the Bandit Eater! Tch, what a troublesome guy…back off everyone! Fighting that monster here is pointless!」

As soon as the bandit leader shouted that, he jumped off the rock as he tried to make his escape, however…he received a Flying Slash from a casual attack from Rei. The shocked bandits were frozen by Set’s Crystal Breath shortly after, preventing them from escaping…and so, the bandit group known as Arrow Storm ceased to exist that day.

+++

# **849**

「Ugh…I’m bored.」

「Hey, I remember you saying that the other day, right? We were attacked by bandits right after you said that, so don’t speak carelessly.」

「No, well, actually, wasn’t it a good thing that we got attacked by those bandits? For the villagers in Goto, a bandit gang that was close to them was cleaned up. As for us, we raided the bandit hideout and got our hands all the treasure they had stored up.」

「…I won’t deny that.」

The man agreed as he replied to Dietz.

They had been attacked by a bandit gang a few days ago, just hours after leaving Goto.

As for the result, as Dietz said, it couldn’t have ended better for everyone.

With winter fast approaching, the bandits likely needed to make a bit more money as several of the bandits had revealed that they had accumulated significant savings back in their hideout.

After dividing what they found at the hideout among everyone, it was quite a considerable amount.

…That said, unlike money, items couldn’t be converted to cash right now, so those were kept inside Rei’s Misty Ring.

「I’ve taken on several bandit subjugation requests before, but never any with such satisfying results. …Rei-san, didn’t it seem like he was quite familiar with the process? We were also ambushed by bandits several times before entering the Selemus Plains.」

「Well, I guess that’s true. Considering they seemed to call him the “Bandit Eater”, I guess he is literally quite familiar with how to deal with them.」

His skill in taking out bandits was truly worth of a well known adventurer.

They looked ahead to the Griffon and adventurer riding him, leading the carriages at the front.

Leaving Set aside, Rei didn’t appear like a very skilled adventurer from the outside.

Clad in robes that looked like they could have been bought anywhere, he looked like a fresh mage apprentice.

(Despite his appearance, he’s powerful enough to defeat an S rank adventurer…isn’t that like attacking a Goblin only to have a Dragon burst out from the Goblin’s skin the next moment? …That’s no joke.)

At the thought, the man talking with Dietz felt a chill run down his spine.

Rei’s disguise, which could almost be considered a form of mimicry, made it extremely troublesome for anyone who tried to attack him.

From the perspective of attackers, the reveal was nothing short of a catastrophe.

(The only saving grace is Set. If they at least notice Set, they’ll probably survive somehow.)

But even that wasn’t easy.

Most people’s eyes would first be drawn to the largest presence among them…the group of carriages.

By the time they were in a position to attack, it would be hard for them to deny that they were bandits.

There was only one way to escape Rei, the terror of bandits. That was to simply hide and avoid drawing his attention at all.

「Still, it’s good an all that we’ve made it to the Bestir Empire, but…」

Dietz muttered as he looked around in boredom.

「What’s wrong?」

「No, it’s just that I feel the Bestir Empire and the Mireana Kingdom are basically the same.」

「That’s true. This is still the countryside though. As we get closer to the Imperial Capital…no, the Royal Capital, we’ll start to see the differences more clearly. That said, we’re going to Glim, which is on the frontier.」

「The Mireana Kingdom’s frontier, huh? Can I think of it as being similar to the area around the Demon Mountains?」

「…I guess that’s close enough?」

As the man replied, his tone indicated it was only a guess as to what it might be like.

「I heard a little bit about it from Rei-san. Apparently, because it’s on the border, it attracts a lot of skilled adventurers. Rumour has it quite a number of them have titles. For example, the father of the guy called Rhodes, who is in one of the carriages…and good friends with Rei-san…is Axe of the Thunder God.」

「You know quite a bit.」

It was Rei, who knew the most about Gilm among everyone, who interrupted their conversation.

「Ah, Rei-san. If we keep going at our current pace, how long will it take to get to Gilm?」

Rei tilted his head at Dietz’ question.

「Well, I’m not sure. We’re definitely a lot faster than when I was heading for the Spring War.」

Rei continued to think as he stroked Set’s neck.

Looking at him now, Rei certainly didn’t seem like the type of person who could easily massacre bandits.

(Perhaps this disparity is the secret to Rei’s unexpected strength.)

The man who had been talking to Dietz thought to himself.

Rei had no idea what they were thinking about as he turned to look back at the carriages before speaking.

「Back then, we had a lot of luggage, so we couldn’t rush along the road. There was also infantry. Considering that, we should arrive a lot faster than back then.」

Everyone’s luggage, including furniture items, were all stored in Rei’s Misty Ring, so there was hardly any luggage in the carriages.

Every time they stopped for food, Rei would take it out from the Misty Ring. Even camping items like tents were all stored in the Misty Ring.

That meant that the heaviest thing in the carriages were the people themselves.

Of course, nothing could be done about that, on board luggage had already be reduced to the bare minimum.

Considering all that, their travel speed was much faster than normal carriages.

And, as Rei had said, when traveling with Daska, their group had to be more formal about their movements, so they hadn’t been rushing.

Looking at the difference in speed, Rei’s group was worlds apart from Daska’s group.

「Ultimately, I can only say that it shouldn’t take too long. …Well, that’s unless we get caught up in some strange incident.」

「A strange incident? Like those bandits from a couple of days ago?」

「Yeah, like that. For some reason, I tend to get caught up in all sorts of unexpected incidents. …Well, catching bandits does make a lot of money, so I actively go after them sometimes.」

「Wow…so that’s why they call you the Bandit Eater.」

Dietz muttered to himself.

「I wouldn’t be too happy if the title of Bandit Eater became popular. I’d rather be known as Crimson.」

「Do you actually care about all that?」

「Not really, but between Bandit Eater and Crimson, Crimson is better no matter how you look at it.」

「…I see.」

He nodded back at Rei, but didn’t seem quite convinced.

To Dietz, Bandit Eater and Crimson were basically the same.

As they continued their conversation, they came across a merchant caravan coming towards them.

The road was quite wide, so it wasn’t an issue for them to pass each other by.

「While I don’t think it’s likely, stay on guard, just in case. We can’t rule out the possibility that they are bandits disguised as a merchant caravan.」

Rei quickly gave out orders before returning to his initial position…at the front of the group.

Hearing Rei’s words, the carriage drives quietly drew their weapons closer, ready to act if anything were to happen.

「Do you think they are enemies?」

Vihera asked as she went over to Rei, but Rei just tilted his head as he replied.

「I don’t know. This is just in case. Besides, it’s hard to imagine anyone attacking me, even if there wasn’t anyone else. …That said, if someone did attack after seeing Set, I guess that would be quite impressive.」

「Guru~?」

Did you call for me? Set seemed to ask as he turned his head to look at Rei, who was riding on his back. However, Rei shook his head to tell him it was nothing as he stroked his neck.

Set gave a happy cry at Rei’s actions.

Although everyone else was preparing for battle, Set himself wasn’t nervous at all.

(Well, considering Rei’s strength, that’s to be expected.)

Vihera thought to herself as she glanced at Rei before slipping in between the carriages, planning to use her agility to ambush any attackers if necessary.

As what seemed to be a merchant caravan approached, they noticed Rei and seemed a little nervous.

If they had been traveling with another group, they might not have been so nervous.

It would be the same if they were close to a village or town.

But, this location was quite far from any villages and towns and no one else was in sight. The only people present were themselves and Rei’s group.

In a situation like this, there was good reason to be on guard.

The gap between them closed as the tension grew.

Rei could see the adventurers guarding the oncoming caravan were ready to draw their weapons at any moment.

(No, it seems like they are just inexperienced.)

Among those following behind Rei, some gave off the same tension and a fighting spirit that showed that they would fight without hesitation if situation escalated.

As the two sides closed in on each other…the merchant caravan came to a halt.

Normally, groups like this would just pass each other by with a wave of their hand.

The fact that the other side had stopped meant that they seemed to have some plan in mind.

(I wonder what they’re thinking.)

Noticing that the passengers in the carriages behind him had become more alert, Rei slowed down as well.

Naturally, the carriages behind Rei also slowed down…and eventually, both sides came to a halt facing each other.

「Hello, I’m Galen, a merchant. Since you have a Griffon with you, perhaps you are Crimson, the B rank adventurer?」

The first to speak was a person who seemed to be leading the merchant caravan.

He was a slightly overweight middle aged man in his forties to fifties.

Rei was surprised by the voice that spoke with a friendly smile.

「It’s true that I am called Crimson…but you know quite a bit.」

「Hahaha. I’ve never heard of anyone other than you who has a Griffon as a familiar. Are you on an escort request?」

As Galen spoke, Rei glanced at the adventurers who were guarding Galen’s caravan.

Perhaps because they heard that the person before them was an adventurer with a title, they watched the exchange with some tension.

That was only natural as they would be asked to stand against Rei if the situation called for it.

Of course, it was unlikely that a titled adventurer would turn to banditry, but as escorts, they still had to be prepared for situations like that.

「Well, speaking of escorting, I guess so. I’m on my way to Gilm. How about you?」

「I have some business at a village up ahead.」

「…Then why did you stop to call out to me? Normally, we’d usually just greet each other and be on our way.」

Rei asked with some doubt, but Galen replied with a smile, as if he had been waiting for the opportunity.

「It’s because I wanted to get to know you of course, Rei-san. A B rank adventurer with a title at your age. It might have been a coincidence that we met in a place like this, but I’m grateful for the chance.」

Rei lowered his guard after hearing Galen’s words.

Because he now knew what he was aiming for.

As a merchant leading a caravan, it was beneficial in many ways to become acquainted with a titled adventurer.

「I see, Galen, was it? I’ll remember that name. However, my usual area of work isn’t around here, it’s in Gilm, on the frontier. I’m not sure if meeting me here will do you any good.」

「No, no. That might be true for now, but we might eventually develop a relationship in the future. With that in mind, it’s not too early for me to ask you to remember my face.」

Rei wondered how to respond to Galen’s words for a moment, which were spoken with a smile. But, since he didn’t sense any particular malice, he just nodded in response.

「I see. If you say so, I’ll keep that in mind. …Anyway, is it fine for us to get going again?」

「Ah, sorry to have taken up your time. You’re right, we’re both in a hurry. It would be a great loss if we were attacked by bandits. Here, please accept this as a token of our friendship.」

With those words, Galen got off the carriage and walked over to Rei before handing him a potion.

From what Rei could tell, it seemed to be an ordinary potion.

「What is this?」

「A potion sold by my caravan. It’s not particularly effective, but it’s quite the bargain to buy.」

「…Huh.」

The price Galen gave was indeed cheaper than buying the same thing in Gilm. It wasn’t just Rei, but several others who were listening from behind Rei who had the same response.

Several people went up to buy potions from Galen.

「As an adventurer, you’ll never have a problem with those potions. My business here might have been by chance, but it was still good business. Well, I’ll be off then.」

With those words, Galen returned to his carriage.

Their business finished, Rei also waved his hand lightly before the group resumed their journey.

+++

# **850**

Rei’s group continued their way along the road.

It had been several more days since their encounter with the merchant caravan.

With basically empty carriages, they were moving at a much faster speed than what normal carriages would usually travel at.

Since then, they had met several other merchant caravans and adventurer parties, but unlike Galen, they simply passed each other by without any incident.

As Rei continued along the road, he started to notice that the area felt somewhat familiar. He realised the time to part ways was soon approaching as he spoke.

「Vihera.」

That along was enough to reveal what Rei wanted to say. Vihera gave a slight nod as she rode up beside Rei.

「Yes, this is the fork in the road to Exil. …It’s unfortunate, but I’ll head to Gilm after I’ve finished my business in Exil. I might not be alone then.」

Rei realised what Vihera was talking about.

Vihera was saying that she might be bringing Byune, whom she treated like a sister, back with her from Exil.

Her plan had been to head to Exil to check on Byune, so it was a perfectly reasonable decision to make.

「That’s fine, but don’t force her. Byune has her own things to do in Exil after all.」

「Oh, did you think I would do something that Byune wouldn’t like?」

「I know, I’m just saying it just in case. …But still, it feels a bit strange to be going our separate ways after you’ve been with us for so long.」

Rei murmured as he stroked Set’s head.

「Really? After leaving Exil, there was the fighting tournament, you went back to escort Frizione out of the Imperial Capital…I think we’ve been doing our own things for quite some time.」

「…Now that you mention it, that is true.」

Vihera was someone who left a strong impression, for better or worse.

Despite being a former princess, her wild personality, beauty, and choice of clothing gave her an overwhelming presence.

She even had the strength to defeat A rank adventurers, so it was honestly hard to not be impressed.

「But still, it feels a little lonely to split up with you.」

「Fufu, thanks. But, like I said before, I’ll head to Gilm as soon as I can after checking on Byune. I haven’t even settled my fight with Elena yet.」

Rei gave a sigh, not realising that Vihera’s battle wasn’t referring just to combat, but also their love battle over him.

「You’ve run away from the Bestir Empire, but Elena hasn’t run from her Duke family or anything of the like. I don’t think it will be that easy to find an opportunity to fight her.」

「That may be true. It would be disappointing though. …Anyway, even if I head to Gilm as soon as I finish up my business in Exil, it will probably be winter already. That means will will be tough to get there through the snow, so it will probably be spring before I see you again, Rei.」

Vihera’s tone and expression were also filled with loneliness as she got off her horse.

Rei nodded back as he also got off Set’s back and took Vihera’s luggage out of the Misty Ring to put on her horse.

Unlike the others, Vihera wasn’t moving from the Imperial Capital or anything, so all her luggage could fit on her horse.

…Of course, carrying all that would still slow her down.

「…Thank you.」

「Don’t worry about it.」

Rei and Vihera exchanged brief words with each others, but soon after, the former members of the guerrilla unit and others they knew spoke up as well.

「Stay safe, Vihera-sama!」

「See you again in Gilm.」

「I don’t believe you have anything you need to worry about, Vihera-sama, but please watch out for bad men!」

「You’re an idiot. There’s no way that Vihera-sama would fall for a bad man. Even if she did, they would be the ones regretting it.」

「What are you talking about? Vihera-sama is a girl in love, so she needs to be careful about things like that, right? Even I, a woman, gets chills from her beauty.」

「It’s probably best to keep the fighting to a minimum. Vihera-sama is incredibly strong after all.」

Voices of praise…or rather encouragement came from the surroundings.

Vihera smiled slightly, understanding that her tone carried some regret about their parting.

Her smile alone was enough to captivate both men and women.

Vihera had often gone over the guerrilla unit’s camp in order to talk to Rei.

Sometimes she would participate in the combat training, looking for a good fight. To the members of the guerrilla unit, Vihera was both noble and approachable.

It wasn’t just the guerrilla unit either. Among the people who had come from the Bestir Empire, many still considered her to be their princess and a symbol they looked up to.

Contrary to her high standing origin, many felt a sense of familiarity around with her due to her casual way of speaking to them.

She had been approachable to begin with and the feeling had only gotten stronger over the course of their journey.

「Fufu~, thanks. But it will be fine. I’m sure there will be plenty of guys who will try to court me. But…」

Vihera cast a meaningful glance in Rei’s direction, causing the people she had been talking with…especially the women, who loved these kinds of stories, to cheer loudly.

For the next 10 minutes or so, Vihera exchanged farewells with various people, including the former guerrilla unit members.

Everyone was naturally disappointed, but since Vihera would be coming to Gilm by next spring at the latest, it wasn’t all that sad of a farewell.

After saying her goodbyes to the others, Vihera went over to Rei.

「Well, I’m heading off now. You might miss me when I’m gone, but don’t cry at night, okay?」

「…Just how old do you think I am?」

「Well, I wonder. …But, it is true that you are irreplaceable to me. So, stay healthy until next we meet.」

With those words, Vihera gently leaned over and sealed Rei’s lips with her own.

It wasn’t a deep kiss like their last kiss, with their tongues entangled, but a simple kiss.

After a few seconds, Vihera released her lips and lightly jumped onto her horse.

「Well, I’ll see you later. If you cheat on me with anyone other than Elena, I’ll never forgive you.」

With that statement, and slightly flushed cheeks, Vihera steered her horse down the road towards Exil.

Rei watched her leave with a small smile, waiting until she was out of sight…before turning around with a gasp.

That was because most of the people in the carriages were looking at him with smiles and mixed gazes.

That was only natural. Everyone here knew how Vihera felt about Rei.

Considering her usual attitude, it was impossible to misunderstand.

If it weren’t for her attitude, some of them might have even tried to court her, risking their lives.

The reason they didn’t was because Vihera had made her feelings for Rei obvious to those around her.

Vihera’s courtship was somewhat awkward, sultry but also seeking strength.

This contrast made many people root for Vihera and Rei’s relationship.

That was why Vihera’s kiss just now was viewed by them as something of a major victory.

Vihera and Rei had shared a much deeper kiss in Exil, but for those unaware of that, this was enough cause for celebration.

The women, especially those who had been cheering for Vihera and Rei’s romance, celebrated as they talked about the spectacle they had just witnessed.

「…Then, let’s get going.」

「Huh? Rei-san, do you have any thoughts about your kiss with Vihera-sama?」

Sergio’s words were met with agreement from Dietz and the others.

Rei sighed as he looked at them before speaking again,

「If you want to talk your time heading to Gilm, I don’t mind flying ahead with Set. It won’t take long for us to get there ourselves.」

「I-I’m kidding, just kidding! Hey, everyone!」

Perhaps sensing the seriousness in Rei’s words, Sergio shouted out in a panic. Those who knew Rei’s personality all agreed.

From the perspective of the former guerrilla unit members, they couldn’t mess with Rei now.

Their hierarchical relatioship from the civil war had already been ingrained in them from all the training they had done, including Rei’s Overlord’s Armour training.

Of course…for those who didn’t know Rei as well, they didn’t want to give up on such a fun story here.

But even they knew what kind of person Rei was.

Some of them had seen the fighting tournament’s finals with their own eyes. Those that didn’t had heard from the former guerrilla unit members about how strong Rei was and had also seen Rei fight many times during their journey.

Still, the reason they didn’t feel as scared by Rei’s threat was because they hadn’t undergone the same training that had put the guerrilla unit members at death’s door.

「L-Look. You said you didn’t want to be pressed on this, Rei-san. So let’s put it aside for now, okay?」

「T-That’s right, that’s right. Yeah. That’s for the best. Just make sure you don’t push ahead on your own.」

「I agree, I agree. I totally agree.」

The former guerrilla unit members all nodded and everyone else agreed.

No, rather, they were all forced to agree by Rei.

「So, no more questions then? Let’s get moving.」

Everyone nodded at Rei’s words.

「Alright, let’s go. Gilm isn’t that far from here. …Of course, we won’t arrive today, but we should still make quite a bit of progress today. …That said, there are a lot of bandits close to Sabrusta, which is on the border of the frontier region.」

「But, isn’t that what you want, Rei-san?」

Rei shrugged at Dietz’s words.

With that exchange, the atmosphere returned to normal.

「It’s true that there are a lot of bandits around Sabrusta, but if we delay there, it will take us longer to reach Gilm.」

「Well, that’s true. After all, it takes more time to go to the bandit hideout to check what they’ve stored up than to actually defeat the bandits.」

「Ah, yeah. That is true.」

A female former guerrilla unit member murmured as she recalled the times they had repelled bandit attacks.

Indeed, bandits were no match for Rei and the former guerrilla unit members.

Instead, it was the interrogations to find their hideout, the travel to the hideout, and then the time to identify anything of worth after killing the bandits that took up more time.

Fortunately, they hadn’t run into any people who were being held captive by bandits at their hideouts, but if there had been, they would also have to escort them to a nearby town of village, taking up even more time.

If any captives had been women, the task would have been even more depressing.

「In that sense, it would be better to eliminate all the bandits at once…but word has spread that there are a lot of bandits around Sabrusta, causing more bandits to come to the region.」

「…So, no matter how many bandits are defeated, there are always more?」

Dietz muttered with a genuine look of disgust on his face as Rei nodded in response.

「Of course, there are also bandits hiding in Sabrusta, bribing the soldiers for information.」

「There are various difficulties in that sense. But still, why are there so many bandits here?」

「The main reason is that it’s town close to the frontier. Merchants coming out of the frontier have monster materials, magic stones, and magic items from there, so they’re aiming for that.」

「Ah…that I can understand.」

Everyone seemed to understand at Rei’s words.

In the Bestir Empire, the equivalent frontier was at the Demon Mountains.

Various materials could be obtained from there, rare items even for the Bestir Empire.

IF they could attack the merchants coming out from there and steal their goods, the profits would be at a whole different level from working as an ordinary bandit.

Of course, since the merchants were transporting such rare items, their guards would also be skilled.

「Well, we’ll deal with bandits as we have done so far. However, many more are likely to mistake us for a merchant caravan.」

Everyone other than Rei was in a carriage and the carriages weren’t uncovered or covered carriages, but box carriages.

Any bandits who saw them would naturally recognise them as good prey…which went without say as people who had come here all the way from the Bestir Empire.

+++

# **851**

That day, the guards at Sabrusta’s gate, who were diligently fulfilling their duties despite shivering in the cold that pierced even their winter clothes, all had expressions of surprise on their faces.

The reason was that a group of carriages was heading towards their city.

No, they wouldn’t have been surprised if it had just been that.

Since Sabrusta was located at the entrance to the frontier, many people passed through here after all.

At this time of year, with winter approaching, the merchant caravans rushing towards Gilm had mostly settled down, but even so, there were still caravans and merchants coming from far away that arrived at Sabrusta with decent frequency.

In other words, the guards at the gate wouldn’t be surprised just from seeing a group of carriages.

As for why they were surprised…

「H-Hey. Am I seeing things? That caravan…it looks like they’re bringing a huge number of bandits with them.」

「Could they be slave traders or something?」

「No way. They wouldn’t tie up their merchandise and force them to walk like that. Besides, everyone they’re dragging along have vicious faces.」

「But, would bandits around here get caught that easily?」

「No, they look like bandits to me too. I even recognise some of their faces. …But, how many are there? Twenty…no, thirty? It looks like there are even more than that.」

「There are a lot of bandits around here, and considering that, it’s not impossible…but still, they did well to capture that many bandits.」

Yes, there were people tied up with ropes and forced to walk, being pulled along by the carriages.

Their hands were tied behind their backs, and their torsos were linked together like a rosary and tied to the body of the carriages. Even though they were moving slower than normal carriage speed, they were still being forced to walk at a speed slightly faster than a normal human’s walking pace.

Several people were tied to each carriage and there were a lot of carriages.

They all had expressions of despair on their faces.

The people watching on found it strange that they all had the same expression on their faces.

Normally, it wouldn’t be strange for some of them to have looks of hatred towards those who captured them or to have thoughts of escaping somehow showing on their faces.

However, among the people currently being brought along by the carriages, there wasn’t a single person with such expressions.

As the guards exchanged words of disbelief, one of them suddenly noticed the person leading what seemed to be a caravan of sorts.

「Hm? Hey, that…could that be Rei?」

「Rei? From Gilm? Come to think of it, I haven’t heard his name recently.」

「Wasn’t he supposed to have gone to the Bestir Empire with Margrave Rowlocks? Margrave Rowlocks came back a long time ago though.」

「Ah, right, right. Now that you mention it, that’s right. …Why is Rei coming back separately?」

「Looking at that, is he acting as a guard for the caravan?」

「…Throwing away his job as a guard for Margrave Rowlocks?」

Hearing the words spoken by one of the guards, the others agreed, thinking that was certainly true.

As a guard for Margrave Rowlocks, a noble with some of the greatest power within the Mireana Kingdom, he had headed to a neighbouring country they had been hostile with for many years. To abandon that escort mission and return while guarding a caravan would normally be unthinkable.

「Then…could it be that caravan was given an important request by Margrave Rowlocks, and Rei was told to guard it?」

『Ah.』

At that explanation, everyone let out voices of agreement.

If that was the case, they could understand why Margrave Rowlocks hadn’t brought Rei along as a guard when he passed through here a while ago.

「Anyway, since they brought bandits, we’ll have to interrogate them and make arrangements to sell them as slaves. I’ll go call some people. With that number of bandits, we won’t have enough hands just by ourselves.」

「Got it, I’m counting on you.」

Watching their colleague leave towards the city, one of the guards muttered out loud.

「Processing that many people is a pain. Thinking about it, it would be a lot easier if they just passed by Sabrusta and headed straight for Abuero.」

「Hey, don’t say something so careless. They’re bandits from around here, you know? If they were interrogated or punished in Abuero instead of Sabrusta, it would just be a disgrace to us.」

「Yeah, yeah. …Ah, so they are coming this way after all. Well, it’s already afternoon, and even if they headed for Abuero now, they’d have to camp out in this cold weather, so it can’t be helped.」

As the guards let out sighs amongst themselves, the group that seemed to be a caravan eventually approached.

「Welcome to Sabrusta. It’s been quite a while, Rei.」

The guard who had processed Rei’s entry when he visited Sabrusta previously spoke with a smile.

Rei seemed to recognise them as well. He nodded as he jumped down from Set’s back.

…The guards were surprised to see Set up close, but although they were surprised for a moment, that was all.

As expected of the guards working in Sabrusta, the entrance to the frontier.

It was also true that Set himself had become famous, and that his reputation had spread all the way to Sabrusta.

「Yeah, I had some business and was out on a long trip.」

While listening to Rei’s words, the man turned his gaze towards the bandits tied to the carriages.

「So, Rei. Those…people tied to the carriages are…」

「They’re bandits. We were attacked on the road while heading here. What’s more, three bandit groups banded together to attack us, so I took the opportunity to round them all up. Normally, dealing with bandits is a pain so I basically just kill all of them, but the others with me need some money. It just so happened that Sabrusta was close by, so I captured them and brought them here.」

「R-Right. …Normally, capturing bandits isn’t something that can be done so easily. Especially rounding up several groups all at once.」

The guard had an expression of mixed exasperation and admiration as the guard who had returned to the city earlier came back with reinforcements.

After that, they took away the bandits tied to the carriages.

「Damn it, you cowards!」

「Do you think you can get away with doing this to me!?」

「Why are there monsters like these guys here, damn it…」

「I’m sorry. It was just a sudden impulse. We might have starved to death at this rate. So please. Please forgive me.」

While watching the bandits being taken away as they each voiced words of regret or sour grapes in such a manner, Rei began the procedures to enter the city.

Of course, it wasn’t just Rei. The people riding in the carriages were also going through the procedures.

「Even so, you did well to capture that many bandits. Wouldn’t it have been tough with just you, Rei?」

「Yeah, probably. Defeating them aside, if they had scattered and run away all at once, I probably wouldn’t have been able to capture all of them even with Set. However, in this case, I had these guys with me.」

Since there were so many of them, he replied while looking at the people going through the procedures all at once with many guards.

「These people…they aren’t a merchant caravan or anything, right?」

Those people, who were visibly highly skilled, didn’t look like they were part of a merchant caravan at all.

Of course, there were some people who ran both a mercenary group and a merchant caravan, but they didn’t look like that either.

「Yeah. They’re people hoping to immigrate to Gilm. I got to know them through some connections. So, I ended up escorting them on my own way back. …Also, Rhodes is in that carriage over there, so please be careful.」

「Rhodes…you mean, from Axe of the Thunder God?」

「That’s right. He’s currently unconscious due to the aftereffects of a magic item.」

The guard was surprised at Rei’s words and widened his eyes.

Rei had become famous around here quite recently and in a very short period of time, but a few years ago, Axe of the Thunder God led by Elk, who held the same title as his party name, were the more well known adventurers in the area, and Elk’s son Rhodes was also famous as a promising newcomer.

「…What about treatment?」

「There’s nothing we can do here. Once we return to Gilm, I think Elk will be able to prepare something though.」

「I see. Then, there’s nothing else for me to say. Please transport him very carefully.」

The conversation regarding Rhodes ended there, followed up by the discussion regarding the captured bandits.

「Even if you sell them as slaves, it would be better to put them up for auction if you want to sell them for a higher price, but…」

The guard trailed off as he looked towards the bandits that had been taken away.

It was only natural. Slaves that sold for high prices at auctions were basically beautiful female slaves or slaves who had some sort of special skill.

Slaves with high combat power could also be sold for a high price, but even so, the skills of mere bandits wouldn’t be worth talking about.

「Personally, I think it would be better to just sell them to a slave trader here in Sabrusta. The price will be lower, but you’ll get the money in your hands that much faster.」

「…When you say we’ll get it faster, specifically when will that be? I’m planning to leave Sabrusta tomorrow.」

At those words, the guard shook his head slightly.

「As expected, getting it done by tomorrow is impossible. Considering the procedures here, it will take a few days…depending on the circumstances, about a week to ten days will be necessary.」

「That’s a bit…no, wait a minute.」

Even though he was leaving tomorrow, taking the trouble to come back all the way here was a pain.

In the first place, the reason he captured the bandits this time wasn’t for his own money, but for the members of the former guerrilla unit…as Rei thought that, he caught sight of Sergio and got an idea.

「Sergio, come here for a bit.」

「Yes? What is it?」

Sergio, who had finished his procedures to enter the city and was chatting to ask what kind of city Sabrusta was, came over to Rei.

「Make him the recipient for the money from the bandits.」

「…Ah, I see.」

With the short words that came out of Rei’s mouth, Sergio probably understood what was going on. He nodded with a smile.

「Yes, I don’t mind. After that, I just need to deliver the amount to you, Rei?」

「No, that’s not necessary. Split it among yourselves.」

「…Pardon?」

Unable to understand what he had been told for a moment, a dumbfounded voice came out of Sergio’s mouth.

As Sergio was someone who normally didn’t show any openings, it was incredibly rare for him to show such a dumbfounded voice and expression.

「Like I said, I’ll give the money from selling these bandits as well as the subjugation reward to you guys.」

「No, but the one who captured these bandits was mostly you, Captain Rei, right?」

「Like I said, I’m not your captain anymore. This is, you know. …Something like celebration gift of sorts? Like a ‘Welcome to Gilm’. Besides, you abandoned your homeland, the Bestir Empire, out of admiration for me, didn’t you? Let me do at least this much.」

「But…」

Ignoring Sergio, who still looked like he wanted to say something, Rei turned his gaze towards the guard.

「That’s how it is. Please do the detailed procedures after this with Sergio.」

「…Haa, well, we don’t mind who it is on our end, but…」

The guard was somewhat bothered by the words ‘Bestir Empire’ that came out of Rei’s mouth, but he didn’t say anything unnecessary.

「Well, that’s that. Listen up, unlike the places up until now, Sabrusta is quite a large city. There are also multiple inns. For that reason, you’re free to do what you want from here on. We’ll be departing tomorrow at 9 AM, so those of you coming to Gilm with me, don’t forget. Well, it’s not like this city is hard to live in either, so if you decide to stay here, just tell Sergio or someone and that’ll be fine. It’s not that far from here to Gilm, and you probably won’t get lost. That’s all, dismissed.」

Deciding that any further arguing would be a pain, Rei declared that and entered Sabrusta together with Set.

It was only something he could do because he had already finished his procedures to enter the city, but Sergio couldn’t chase after Rei.

Now that Rei was gone, he had no choice but to do the procedures for the bandit subjugation reward and selling them as slaves.

「Ah, seriously. It can’t be helped. Look, everyone else, dismissed, dismissed! I’ll take care of the matter with the bandits over here, so everyone else is free to do as you like!」

Sergio gave up as well as he called out to everyone else.

Rei, who was making his way down the main street of Sabrusta, was already holding several meat skewers in both hands, as if it were only natural.

He would give a skewer to Set every time he gave a cry while biting into another one himself.

As he did that, a blacksmith’s shop suddenly caught his eye.

It was because he remembered that he had picked up the magic sword Noiz had been using.

Of course, there had been blacksmiths in the villages and cities they had stopped at so far.

But, the reason he hadn’t stopped by any of them despite that was because he didn’t know if Noiz’s sword could be repaired, and even if it could, he predicted it would take a considerably long time.

There was also the fact that Rei himself wasn’t used to using a long sword.

It was the most common weapon in this world, but Rei had become too used to swinging the Death Scythe around.

He stared at the shop for a few seconds, before shaking his head and giving up.

If he was going to do it, he thought he would have it repaired in a place with a blacksmith even more skilled than here…in Gilm.

「Guru~!」

As he was thinking like that, Set pulled on the Dragon Robe with his beak to draw his attention.

「What’s wrong?」

「Gurururu~!」

At the end of Set’s line of sight, as he gave a happy cry, was an udon food stall.

「I think they were selling udon when we came here before too, but…if we’re going to eat, it might be good to compare it with last time.」

Set gave a cry as if to say ‘I agree!’ as Rei walked over to the stall to eat udon for the first time in a while.

+++

# **852**

The day after spending a night in Saburusta, after Rei finished his procedures to leave the city, he saw that everyone was gathered in front of the gate, fully prepared to depart at any time.

「Everyone wants to go to Gilm? You really are a curious lot. Do you understand that the place we’re heading to is the frontier?」

As Rei muttered while stroking Set’s head, Sergio opened his mouth with a wry smile from a carriage driver’s seat.

「We came all the way from the Bestir Empire because we wanted to spend time with you, Rei, right? Don’t you think it’s impossible for us to go out of our way to live in Saburusta because of that?」

「…Just so you know, it’s not like I’m going to be in Gilm forever, alright? If there’s a request, I’ll go to another city, and I might even go to another country like this time.」

「We understand at least that much. But, don’t you think there’s a big difference in being by your side, Rei, when something happens?」

At Sergio’s words, the people riding in the other carriages nodded as if to say they agreed.

「Besides, if we lived in Saburusta, we wouldn’t be able to see Set.」

At the words of a woman sitting in the driver’s seat of another carriage, many people nodded in agreement to this as well.

「Do as you like. Seriously, there really are a lot of curious people here.」

「Rei, you already said that earlier, you know?」

「That just means there are that many curious people here. …So, Sergio, what happened with the matter regarding the bandits?」

「Ah, yes. That matter has been properly resolved. At first, I thought we would have to come back to this city to receive the money, but there’s a high chance you’ll be too busy for that once we arrive in Gilm, right? Therefore, we paid some money to a caravan that plans to go to Gilm in ten days to have them bring it to us.」

「You did something quite risky. It’s not my problem if they run off with the money, alright?」

Rei offered those words of warning just in case, but what returned was Sergio’s wry smile.

「Rei, you should think a little more about how famous your name is, alright? We are a group brought along by you, Rei. If someone were to steal the reward money for the bandits you captured and the sales from selling them as slaves from a request they received from such a group, that person probably wouldn’t be able to do business around here anymore. …If it were a much larger amount of money, there might be people who would consider doing such a thing though…」

Judging from those words that the amount of money probably wasn’t as large as he had thought, Rei shrugged his shoulders.

「If you guys are fine with that, I have no complaints either. Then, no one has left anything behind, right? Even if you did, we’d have to go through the procedures to enter again, so I can’t wait for you.」

「Rei, there’s no point in asking in that case.」

At Dietz’s words, everyone nodded with smiles on their faces.

Confirming that the faint tension among the group had been broken by those words, Rei opened his mouth again with a smile.

「Then, let’s depart!」

At the words that came out of Rei’s mouth, Set stepped forward.

As if following behind him, the group of carriages also began to move.

The guards working as gatekeepers in Saburusta saw off the group, which could be called a single herd led by Rei, only speaking when their figures were far away.

「They’re gone.」

「Yeah. …Honestly, I didn’t think it would be this busy after the caravans’ active movements had settled down.」

「Ah-…true. Well, there are people who want to head to Gilm before it snows every year, so it’s not like it’s completely impossible, but…considering that, it feels somewhat strange.」

「Even so, it’s not as busy as a little while ago, so it’s not too bad, right?」

In the period before it started snowing, Gilm both welcomed and saw off many caravans.

Their goal was to purchase goods in Gilm before traveling became difficult due to the snow.

If they misjudged the time it snowed, at worst, they would be trapped in the frontier until spring.

Considering that, it would normally be best not to go to Gilm at this time of year, but starting with Gamelion meat, there was prey that could only be caught in the frontier at this time of year, and many people thought to stock up on rare materials and magic stones that were in short supply in anticipation of that.

Weighing the risks and returns, those who chose the option of higher returns gathered in Gilm at this time of year.

However, that commotion had already mostly settled down, it wouldn’t be strange for it to snow at any time, so no one would head to Gilm at this time of the year unless they had very special circumstances.

…Or, people returning to Gilm like Rei.

In any case, heading to Gilm naturally meant passing through this Saburusta, and until recently, the guards in Saburusta…especially those doing the procedures to enter the city, had been spending their days very busily.

Since Rei’s group had come just as that had settled down, it was certainly true that it was easier compared to a little while ago.

「Look, caravans still come, so it’s not like we’re completely free, you know!」

When one of the guards present shouted that, the other guards also returned to their respective jobs.

「Ah, I can see it. Is that Gilm?」

Two days after leaving Saburusta, having spent the previous night in Abuero, which was halfway between Saburusta and Gilm, and having travelled along the highway since early morning today as well, Rei’s group caught sight of the walls surrounding the city at the end of their line of sight.

One of the people in the driver’s seat of a carriage raised a voice of joy at the sight.

That was only natural. From leaving the Imperial Capital of the Bestir Empire to Gilm on the frontier of the Mireana Kingdom.

This journey was something that people living normally would rarely be able to experience.

The fact that they had been able to travel safely despite that was definitely because Rei and Set had been guarding them, and because the members of the former guerrilla unit had been there.

Rather, a group with such powerful guards was quite rare.

「In the end, the bandits that attacked us before we arrived in Saburusta were the last ones we would run into.」

Sergio muttered deeply, but depending on who listening, they might have sensed a somewhat regretful tone in his voice.

Sergio was polite man, but as an adventurer, he didn’t dislike rough business.

「Well, that’s how things should be normally. Anyway, since we’ve arrived safely in Gilm like this, the complaining can wait.」

「That’s right. It wouldn’t be funny if you said something weird here and it became reality. …More importantly, the walls surrounding Gilm are quite thick, aren’t they? It might not even lose out to the Imperial Capital.」

A woman driving one of the carriages muttered in admiration as she gazed at Gilm’s walls, which could be stood out even from afar.

「That’s only natural. Since it’s the frontier, powerful monsters will naturally appear. If they were to attack the city, thin city walls would be breached immediately, wouldn’t they?」

「Because it’s the frontier, huh. We’ll be living there from now on too, so isn’t it good that it’s reliable?」

「Yeah, yeah, it’s good to know that the place you live in has ironclad defences.」

「Come to think of it, I heard a strange rumour in Abuero. Something about a dungeon…」

「Ah, I heard that too. But, the story about there being a dungeon near Gilm was from a while ago, right? Why bring it up now?」

「Who knows? Maybe there’s some new movement or something in the dungeon.」

While they were conversing in such a manner, the city of Gilm steadily approached.

Around this time, they started to come across increasingly more adventurers, caravans, merchants, and travellers on the highway leading to Gilm…and their reactions were split neatly in two.

On one side were the people who knew Rei and Set.

These were the people who rejoiced that Rei and Set, who had been away from Gilm for a while, had returned, and gave Set any dried meat or bread they had on them.

And on the other side were the people who didn’t know Rei and Set…or, those who knew them only through rumours and had never seen them directly with their own eyes.

Such people were surprised at the figure of Set, a Griffon, and even more surprised at the figure of Rei riding on his back.

There were also quite a few people who almost collapsed to the ground at the sight of an A rank monster that had suddenly appearing before their eyes.

…However, those who knew the circumstances lent a hand to such people.

The reactions towards Rei and Set were split into two groups like that, but their reactions to the group of nearly twenty carriages Rei was leading were basically the same.

All of those carriages were expensive box carriages, they wondered why such a group being led by Rei.

In the end, they just assumed he had been hired to escort it or something.

There were some people waiting to enter the city in front of the gate, but those people also turned surprised eyes towards Rei’s group, which suddenly appeared behind them.

「Huh? We haven’t been passed by anyone since we left Abuero, right?」

「Yeah. Well, there probably aren’t many people who can catch up to our speed.」

Not to mention Rei and Set, there were only people riding in the carriages. Furthermore, the horses pulling the carriages weren’t first-class, but they possessed above-average abilities.

Because of that, the travel speed of Rei’s group was extremely fast.

Despite that, there were people lined up to enter the city ahead of them…Rei spoke up to answer that question.

「It’s not that strange. We stayed a night in Abuero, but the guys over there probably travelled through the night, or camped out.」

「…At this time of year?」

「Everyone has their own circumstances. Not everyone has full pockets like us.」

Rei’s group had received a massive amount of reward money for the matter regarding the civil war, and naturally, their pockets were quite full.

Also, on their journey here, whenever they were attacked by bandits, they would capture the bandits, make them spit out the location of their hideout, and then attack the hideout in reverse to steal their treasure, doing this multiple times.

Naturally, even if their earnings were split among the people who participated in the combat, it was be a considerable amount of money so they had cash to spare.

However, normally, most people wouldn’t have that buffer.

That was why there were also people who camped out on the highway, prepared for monster attacks and the cold, without staying at an inn in the city.

「Hmm…well, it’s true that I also thought quite a bit about saving money when I was an adventurer in the Bestir Empire, so I understand that feeling.」

「Pfft, you, saving money…that’s not something a guy who was engrossed with prostitutes should say.」

「Ugh…」

While they exchanged such words, Rei’s group finally arrived at the front of the line, and…

「Rei! You guys don’t have to line up! Come over here first!」

Called by one of the guards, they headed straight for the gate from the end of the line.

Naturally, the carriages followed behind Rei, and for the people lined up, they didn’t find that amusing.

However, shouting that it was unfair in a place like this had almost no meaning, and in the first place, if they knew who Rei was, they could probably guess that there were some special circumstances.

Because of that, although the people lined up seemed somewhat dissatisfied, no voices of complaint came out.

「That would be a great help, but is it okay?」

At Rei’s words, the guard nodded in return.

「Daska-sama told us to let you through immediately when you return.」

「Ah-…I see.」

Rei had an expression of understanding on his face, figuring that Daska probably wanted to hear the report regarding the civil war directly from his own mouth.

Although a rough report had already been given through Elena, it was only natural for Margrave Rowlocks, a central figure of the Neutral Faction, to want to know more detailed information.

In the first place, this civil war in the Bestir Empire was a plot planned in cooperation between the Neutral Faction and the Aristocratic Faction.

If it became known that Rei, an adventurer from Gilm who was recognized as being on close terms with Daska, had returned, it wouldn’t be strange for people to think of ways to get in contact with Rei before Daska did.

「Got it. Then I’ll go right away. …Come to think of it, what about these guys?」

As Rei asked while turning his gaze to the people in the carriages behind him, the guard nodded in return.

「Yes. Everyone who came with you, Rei, was told to go to the Lord’s residence.」

With a brief exchange, they each immediately began the procedures to enter the city.

As Rei also handed his guild card to the guard, he suddenly noticed that Ranga was nowhere to be seen.

Ranga, the captain of the guards, had become somewhat like Rei’s exclusive handler.

Normally, if something like this happened, he would have gone straight over to Rei…

「What happened to Ranga?」

「Captain Ranga is currently away on work. To the dungeon.」

「Dungeon? You mean, the one near here?」

What crossed Rei’s mind was the dungeon with the Altar of Inheritance that he had delved into together with Elena and the others.

It was a dungeon he had bitter memories of in various ways, but if he was told there was a dungeon near here, that was the only one he could think of.

However, the guard shook his head at Rei’s question.

「It’s not the one you’re thinking of. No, it is near here, but it’s a different dungeon to the other one. …It was newly discovered a few days ago.」

The guard’s words were more than enough to shock Rei.

+++

# **853**

Rei was surprised by the guards’ words about the new dungeon, but he couldn’t exactly head there to take a look immediately. He entered Gilm after being told that it would be better to get the details directly from Daska.

Of course, Rei wasn’t entering the city alone. He was accompanied by the former guerrilla unit members as well as the people who had come with them to live in Gilm.

As soon as they passed through the gates, Rei’s group started making their way towards the lord’s residence.

The people in Gilm casually called out to Rei and the others as they passed by.

This greatly surprised the former guerrilla unit members.

Naturally, people had called out to Rei in the Bestir Empire too, but most of their attention had been on Set. Rei’s title of Crimson in addition to his past actions were well known by others, so few people actually dared to approach him casually.

「Wow. They’re just casually calling out to Rei.」

「It’s hard to believe. Even we wouldn’t just call out to him like that.」

「Right. Ah, but the way they treat Set is the same.」

They sighed in relief at the familiar sight of a passing adventurer give Set some dried meat from their pocket.

「Even so…did you hear the story from earlier?」

「Story? About what?」

「The dungeon. I’ve heard rumours they can occur naturally, but to actually see one with my own eyes…」

「You haven’t even seen it yet. We just know it’s there.」

「Even so! A dungeon is great news for us. You know why, right?」

The man looked intently at the woman sitting in the driver’s seat of a neighbouring carriage.

The woman sighed before replying.

「I know. A dungeon means we can earn money there, right? Especially since we’re newcomers to Gilm. Rather than fighting over the few requests available in winter, we’d be better off getting monster materials and magic stones from a dungeon.」

「There aren’t many requests in winter, but those who haven’t saved enough to survive the season are desperate for them. …If we just push our way in, they won’t look kindly on us. It’d be different if there was a surplus of requests.」

「…Wouldn’t those people also go to the dungeon? Well, rank might be an issue, but still.」

As they talked, they eventually reached the lord’s residence.

Glancing at each other, they were surprised by the building that looked more like a fortress than a lord’s residence. Rei lowered the hood of his Dragon Robe to call out to the familiar gatekeeper…but was beaten to it.

The gatekeepers had naturally noticed the group of carriages approaching, and they knew that Rei was leading them.

「Rei, you’ve returned.」

「Yeah, finally. Anyway, I was told at the city gate to head straight to the lord’s residence to meet with Daska?」

One of the gatekeepers glanced at his colleague, who immediately headed inside the residence.

「I heard you’ve been pretty busy. You can tell me about it next time.」

The gatekeeper spoke to Rei like an old friend.

Rei had visited Daska at the lord’s residence countless times, so it was natural for him to get to know the gatekeepers. While some treated their job strictly as work, this particular gatekeeper was happy to chat casually.

「Maybe if you treat Set and me to some food.」

The man looked back at Rei in disgust.

「If I feed you and Set until you’re full, what am I supposed to eat tomorrow?」

「Just get Daska’s chef to make you something.」

「Hey…haah.」

「Don’t praise me so much.」

「How could you possibly think I was praising you just now!?」

The former guerrilla unit members watched their exchange, dumbfounded.

They had almost never seen anyone interact with Rei this casually. Vihera was the first to come to mind, followed by Theorem, Frizione, and Angela.

「So? I heard when I was entering the city that a new dungeon has appeared?」

「Ah…so you’ve already heard. Yeah, it caused a huge uproar when it was first found. The city has only calmed down in the last few days. Captain Ranga helped a lot by heading over there. It also fortunate that the dungeon itself is quite small.」

「…It’s a small one?」

Rei looked down at his hands.

He wasn’t worried about his own size; he was thinking about the dungeon core at the deepest part of the dungeon. He remembered destroying one previously with the Death Scythe.

(I don’t know if a dungeon core counts as a monster, but the Death Scythe has already absorbed one before. Skills like Terrain Manipulation are pretty useful. I don’t know what Set will learn if he absorbs it, but…it’s worth a shot?)

If the dungeon was small, getting the core probably wouldn’t be too hard. Rei smiled slightly at the thought.

「Yeah. It was pretty sudden. Things were tough at first because monsters came pouring out of the entrance. Fortunately, they were weak monsters like Goblins, so there wasn’t any real damage. The entrance was small, so large monsters couldn’t get out.」

「Is that why Ranga is there?」

「Yeah. Since the dungeon appeared so suddenly, his presence helped to calm people down.」

「…Are people allowed to freely enter that dungeon?」

The gatekeeper’s eyes widened slightly.

「Hey, you just got back from the Bestir Empire, and you’re already looking for your next job?」

「I don’t have much to do during winter anyway, and having a dungeon nearby is troublesome for Gilm, right? …By the way, how close is ‘nearby’?」

「About a few hours’ walk.」

「…It certainly is close.」

The dungeon with the Altar of Inheritance that Rei had explored with Elena was a few days away by carriage. Compared to that, a few hours on foot was practically on their doorstep.

「Right? That’s why it caused such an uproar in Gilm. Anyway, the location is…」

Just as the gatekeeper was about to continue, his colleague returned.

「Daska-sama will see you, so head on in. Just you, though. We’ve prepared a room inside for the others to go over the rules for immigrating to Gilm.」

Normally, the lord or his subordinates wouldn’t go out of their way to meet new immigrants to the city.

However, these circumstances were far from normal. This was a group from the Bestir Empire, and they were former guerrilla force members who had fought in the civil war with Rei. Daska needed to personally understand the situation.

Sergio looked at Rei, silently asking if it was okay to trust them.

Rei nodded back. Relieved, Sergio and the other former guerrilla force members nodded to the gatekeeper.

(Elena should have already passed on the message that people were coming with me. It should be fine.)

The returning gatekeeper called out to him.

「Rei, you’ll…ah, the maid will guide you. It’s over at the usual office.」

「Understood. …Well then, see you later.」

Rei called out to Sergio and the others before heading inside. Set started walking towards the stables on his own before Rei could even say anything, proving Rei wasn’t the only one used to going over to the lord’s residence.

「It’s been a while, Rei-sama. I’ll take you straight to Daska-sama.」

「Yeah, please.」

Guided by the familiar maid, Rei entered the lord’s residence.

「Daska-sama, I have brought Rei-sama.」

Even though he had been to the lord’s residence countless times, the luxurious office door still surprised Rei.

The door alone was worth enough to let a commoner live in luxury for several generations.

「Enter.」

The maid opened the door and let Rei in.

Upon entering, Rei saw a massive mountain of documents piled on the desk. A sullen Daska sat among the paperwork, looking deeply displeased.

「Rei, you’re back.」

「…Yeah. But what on earth is all this?」

「Hmph, haven’t you heard? A dungeon suddenly appeared near Gilm.」

「I heard, but…is that why it’s like this?」

Being a noble was tough work, Rei thought casually. Daska let out a large sigh.

「Just so you know, the paperwork for the people you brought is in here too.」

「…Thank you.」

Rei didn’t know what else to say.

Realising he was just taking his stress out on Rei, Daska stood up and scratched his head.

「Bring us something light to eat. Ah, make it a large portion.」

Knowing exactly how much Rei ate, the maid smiled, bowed slightly, and left the office.

Daska told Rei to sit on the reception sofa and took the seat opposite him.

「…Sounds like you had a rough time.」

「Yeah, you could say that. It wasn’t all bad, though.」

「The Immovable Noiz, huh.」

Rei nodded with a complicated expression.

The battle with Noiz had been incredibly beneficial, but he still felt like he had lost…or at least been let lightly.

「Also…there’s the matter with Set.」

「…An A rank monster is surprising enough, let alone a rare species. You did well to tame a monster equivalent to S rank.」

「We’ve been together since I was a kid. It’s less like he’s tamed and more like he’s my brother.」

Daska gave a wry smile.

If you could tame a monster just by growing up with it, there would be a lot more tamed monsters around. He decided there was no point in mentioning that and moved on.

「Then there are those guys you brought.」

「Right. But wouldn’t you consider poaching skilled people from the Bestir Empire a decent result?」

「It’s a problem if they’re still connected to the other side.」

「I don’t think you need to worry about that…」

They absolutely did not want to be hostile to Rei. They’d rather abandon their country than to fight him. Or, they just wanted to be with Set.

Since they had openly said these things, Rei didn’t think they were lying. Rei explained this, but Daska shook his head.

「I might believe you, Rei, but I can’t just blindly trust them. There’s no clear evidence, just your gut feeling. …In my position, I can’t completely accept that reasoning.」

「I see.」

Rei had to agree with Daska’s reasoning.

It was one thing for Daska to trust them himself, but he needed a solid basis if he had to explain it to anyone else.

「…So, is it going to be dangerous for them?」

「Not dangerous, but they’ll be under surveillance for a while. …Don’t worry, we won’t make it obvious and they won’t be uncomfortable.」

「Egg?」

「Yeah.」

Rei thought back to the men he had fought near Sabrusta and their leader.

Egg used to lead the Prairie Wolves bandits, but Daska had hire him to handle the darker side of the Rowlocks territory.

The Prairie Wolves were all fairly skilled. If they were running surveillance, they wouldn’t be easily noticed.

(The former guerrilla force members are also skilled though. It wouldn’t be strange if a few of them noticed.)

Recalling a few of their faces, Rei nodded back to Daska. He didn’t think it would be a problem.

「Yeah, I think that’s for the best. Besides…if they try anything, it’s my responsibility for bringing them here. I’ll take care of them if it comes to that. …Though I doubt it will.」

Daska nodded as Rei smiled confidently.

Since Daska already believed Rei, this was purely a precaution.

「…Now then, setting the immigrants aside, tell me what happened during the civil war.」

They were finally getting to the main topic.

Rei started talking about everything that happened after he parted ways with Daska in the Imperial Capital.

+++

# **854**

「…I see. I mostly understand your actions. I think some of the things you did were dangerous, but what’s done is done. Above all, successfully ending the civil war and creating what could be called a pro-Mireana Kingdom faction within the Bestir Empire is a sufficient gain. Besides, the civil war drained the Bestir Empire’s national power to some extent, which is a very satisfactory result for us.」

After hearing everything from Rei, Daska nodded slightly as he spoke.

He had been surprised several times as Rei told his story, but ultimately, he accepted Rei’s reasoning behind his decisions.

While taking a bite of a sandwich the maid had brought earlier, Daska fell into thought.

Watching him, Rei also reached for the sandwiches on the table.

Perhaps because he had asked for a large portion, the sandwiches were piled up like a mountain on the plate. If a normal person were told this was a light snack, they would have never believed it.

The tea had cooled down a bit while they talked, but it was still good enough.

As Rei bit into a ham and vegetable sandwich, Daska spoke again.

「So…I heard from Elena that you received something rather troublesome?」

「Troublesome? …Ah, this?」

At first, Rei didn’t know what Daska was talking about, but he quickly realized what it was. He took a metal card out of his Misty Ring and placed it on the table.

Engraved on the metal card was the phrase, 『This person is a friend of the Bestir Empire.』

It was what Rei had received from Tragist, the Emperor of the Bestir Empire.

In a way, it was the most troublesome thing from Rei’s trip to the Bestir Empire this time.

「…May I see it?」

Given what it was, Daska carefully picked up the metal card.

「I see. …A friend of the Bestir Empire, huh. What a subtly troublesome item.」

「Subtly troublesome?」

「Yeah. Among the nobles, there will probably be some loudmouths who will claim that you, holding this, are colluding with the Bestir Empire. And usually, the loud ones, even if they are a minority, stand out so much that their opinions are often seen as the majority.」

Daska made a bitter face.

It was only natural. Rei was not officially treated as Daska’s subordinate. However, he was definitely an adventurer affiliated with Gilm, which Daska governed. With the mobility of his Griffon, Set, he was an extremely reliable asset.

Considering the Magic Fever incident a while ago, the advantage of that mobility was obvious.

Furthermore, Rei possessed combat power equivalent to an entire army on his own and specialized in wide-area annihilation magic. In a war, he would be an unparalleled asset.

He also had the transport capability of his item box, just as he had demonstrated by transporting supplies during the Spring War.

His lack of interest in money was also something Daska welcomed.

…Although he had no attachment to money, he did have the eccentric hobby of collecting magic items and magic stones.

Regardless, there was no doubt that Rei was an extremely useful person to Daska.

The fact that Rei was attached to Gilm was also a big benefit.

But…thinking about it the other way around, Rei was an extremely troublesome existence for those hostile to Daska.

That wasn’t just limited to enemies like the Bestir Empire. It was the same for those within the Mireana Kingdom who opposed Daska.

The largest group was, naturally, the large number of Royalist Faction nobles.

Next was the Aristocratic Faction. …However, in the case of the Aristocratic Faction, they had cooperated during the recent Bestir Empire civil war, and the good relationship between the head of the Aristocratic Faction and Daska highlighted the complexity of the faction, which was formed by many other nobles.

There were even nobles in the Neutral Faction, which was currently united around Daska, who didn’t approve of the current situation.

As for nobles who didn’t belong to any faction, and it wouldn’t be strange if they viewed Rei with hostility either.

As such, there were many who were hostile or potentially hostile to Daska within the Mireana Kingdom. If they keep Rei, one of Daska’s greatest military assets, in check, there was no doubt they would make a move without hesitation.

And the metal card handed directly to Rei by the Emperor of the Bestir Empire carried enough persuasive power to make that possible.

That was exactly why Daska spoke while holding the metal card with a difficult expression.

「Rei, try not to use this metal card as much as possible. No, it would be better not to show it to anyone else either. If word of this spreads, there will probably be someone who will try to mess with you in some way. You wouldn’t find that amusing either, right?」

「…Well, that’s certainly true. I don’t want to cause unnecessary commotion either.」
