Fundamentally, Rei was merciless towards his enemies.

If things went wrong, others might use a hostile noble getting injured as an excuse to make a move on him.

To prevent such a situation, Daska decided that keeping the existence of the metal card itself a secret was the best option.

Normally, this metal card would be an extremely convenient item, and it would be normal to complain if told not to use it.

However, Rei had no intention of using this metal card to begin with, so he easily nodded at Daska’s words.

「Are you sure?」

At Rei’s reaction, Daska ended up asking back, ‘Are you really sure?’

「Yes. I received various warnings when I consulted Elena. Well, even if something happens, I plan to manage it with my own power anyway.」

Even Daska was surprised that Rei would so easily declare he wouldn’t use an item given by the Emperor of a nation and just tuck it away.

This metal card was something that other people might even try to attack and steal from him if they were to know about it.

However, Rei felt that there was no use thinking about it at this point.

Countless opponents had already attacked him trying to steal Set or the Misty Ring, so a few more wouldn’t make much of a difference now.

「…I’m sorry.」

「No, don’t worry about it.」

With a short exchange, they decided to end the conversation about the metal card, and Daska handed it back to Rei.

Receiving it and storing it in his Misty Ring, Rei reached for another sandwich as he spoke.

「Speaking of which, about the new dungeon.」

「Ah, that source of trouble. What about it?」

「I heard it’s a small dungeon, but aren’t you going to clear it? I think it would be resolved if you just destroyed the dungeon core.」

「We don’t have anyone free. Well, we do have people, but many of them are busy preparing for winter right now.」

「Still, it can’t be everyone, right?」

It was already the time of year when it wouldn’t be strange for it to snow at any moment.

Despite being so close to the deadline, it was impossible that many of the adventurers in Gilm hadn’t finished their winter preparations yet.

「Yes. But a newly formed dungeon isn’t very profitable. Even its dungeon core hasn’t fully grown yet, so it can’t attract significant monsters. There are a few other problems too, but basically, there’s no profit for the effort that needs to be put in.」

「…I see.」

It was true that adventurers entered into dungeons for the money they could get by selling monster proof of subjugation parts, various materials, and magic stones.

There were also a small number who sought greater strength and wanted to fight stronger enemies.

However, the dungeon Daska described had weak monsters that could hardly be called strong enemies, and it didn’t yield decent materials either.

Of course, it would be a slightly different story if it were the so-called boss monster guarding the dungeon core.

But since the profits were clearly small and there were only weak enemies, they couldn’t expect much from the boss monster either, so there were hardly any people willing to challenge that dungeon.

Hearing Daska’s explanation, Rei tilted his head.

「I heard you dispatched Ranga…but if it’s such a weak dungeon, is there really a need to go that far?」

「That’s right. If I hadn’t dispatched Ranga, it wouldn’t be strange if someone judged that having a dungeon near Gilm was dangerous and tried to clear it. But with Ranga there, even if monsters appear from the dungeon, they will be easily defeated. Because of that, no one feels any sense of crisis anymore.」

「…What about the knights?」

「Yes, I was just thinking about that worst-case scenario. However, knights and adventurers might seem similar, but they are very different. Setting aside training to fight monsters, knights aren’t trained to explore dungeons like adventurers do.」

Those words made sense to Rei.

Knights originally trained to fight people and monsters, but they didn’t usually go into dungeons like adventurers.

That was because there was an understanding that such work belonged to adventurers.

Although it wasn’t an absolute rule, as there were some who went into dungeons as a hobby, just like Daska did during his knight days.

「In other words, there’s no one available to clear the dungeon?」

「That’s right.」

Daska nodded casually at Rei’s words, which were meant for confirmation. …While nodding, he directed a look of expectation at Rei, who had asked such a question.

The story he heard from Daska was also appealing to Rei.

Setting aside the fact that the enemies were weak, it meant that the dungeon core could be obtained easily――compared to the dungeon with the Altar of Inheritance or the dungeon in Exil.

「But, won’t the dungeon grow if we leave it alone?」

That’s right, regardless of their initial size, dungeons grew over time.

An extreme example of a dungeon that had grown like that would be the dungeon in Exil, which was also a labyrinth city.

It was also obvious that the dungeon with the Altar of Inheritance would gradually grow larger if it remained uncleared.

「Even if you say it will grow, there are differences in growth speed depending on the dungeon core. Even a fast-growing dungeon rarely grows at an absurd speed like adding one floor a year.」

「…In other words, since anyone can clear it whenever they feel like it, you’re fine leaving it for now?」

「That’s right. Well, it will probably take some level of strength to defeat the boss monster guarding the dungeon core, so it’s not like ‘anyone’ can do it.」

Daska let out a sigh.

It was obvious to anyone watching that he was extremely troubled, and at the same time, it aligned with Rei’s intentions, so Rei spoke up.

「How about it, Daska. If you’d like, could you let me clear that dungeon?」

Despite his expectations, Daska looked surprised, perhaps not actually thinking Rei would offer.

It was only natural. The monsters that appeared were weak and didn’t bring in money, and they were lacking in terms of strength.

It was completely unexpected to be asked to let him clear such a dungeon.

Of course, Daska had hoped Rei would clear the dungeon if possible.

But even so, he had thought he would probably…no, definitely be refused.

Because of that, he couldn’t help but ask back in surprise.

「Are you really sure? I’m repeating myself, but I absolutely don’t think this will be profitable for you, you know?」

「Not necessarily. There are a few things I’d like to test…and above all, I also have an attachment to Gilm.」

「That would be a great help. However, you probably won’t be able to take Set into the dungeon, will you still go?」

Rei frowned slightly, and Daska nodded.

「That’s right. The dungeon entrance is only wide enough for one person to barely fit through. It’s difficult even for someone slightly tall to enter. It would be especially tough for someone wearing armour and carrying a long-handled weapon like a spear. …Actually, this is also one of the reasons why adventurers hate entering that dungeon. It seems there’s some space once you get inside, but it’s still quite hard to move around.」

While there were skilled adventurers who were small like Rei, many adventurers had large builds since their main job inevitably involved rough work.

If such people couldn’t enter…furthermore, even if they went through the trouble of getting inside, if there was little to be gained, Rei had to agree that few people would challenge the dungeon.

Rei was about to say something in response, when he suddenly sensed a presence rapidly approaching the office. He stood up from the sofa and stepped forward to protect Daska…The next moment, the office door was thrown open as if it had been smashed apart.

+++

# **855**

「-!?」

Rei instantly pulled the Death Scythe out from the Misty Ring and took a combat stance to counter whoever, or whatever, had suddenly burst into the office.

Since he had to protect Daska behind him, he couldn’t make any reckless moves, but Rei was still confident he could handle any ordinary opponents.

However, the presence that had forced the door open with enough momentum to nearly shatter it was ferocious. Rei judged them to be a threat that warranted his caution.

As he was about to launch a preemptive Flying Slash from the Death Scythe, he suddenly realised the intruder was a familiar face and lowered his weapon.

The only reason he didn’t store the Death Scythe back into Misty Ring immediately was because the person before him was radiating bloodlust.

If anything happened, he still had to protect Daska. With that thought, Rei called out the name of the person who had stormed into the office.

「Elk, it’s been a while.」

Rei’s voice was somewhat stiff, but it was still a tone used when talking to a friend.

The main reason for that stiffness was partly because of the sudden intrusion, but more than anything, it was the way Elk had practically kicked the door down. Rei didn’t know the door’s exact value, but knew enough to know that it was far from cheap.

Hearing his name being called, Elk finally noticed Rei. His fearsome, beast-like aura he had been radiating began to subside.

「…Rei.」

「Hey. I literally just got back. What’s the matter with you? Charging into the lord’s residence while giving off an aura like that.」

「…O-Oh. Sorry. I heard a rumour that you’d returned, and well…sorry.」

After apologising twice, Elk took a deep breath to calm himself and bowed his head toward Daska.

「My apologies, Daska. I heard about Rhodes’ situation, so I…」

「Indeed. Normally, I would have to punish you for your disrespect. I’m only letting it slide because it’s me.」

Daska was a man of considerable skill himself. That was why he could continue speaking without showing any signs of fear, despite being subjected to Elk’s ferocious aura. If anyone unrelated to combat had been in his place, they likely would have collapsed or even lost consciousness from the pressure Elk exerted.

Rei looked around for Min, Elk’s wife and the one usually responsible for reining him in. He spotted her just as she poked her head through the open door, having chased after her husband.

「Elk, could you…」

Min was about to complain about her husband’s rampage, but she stopped in her tracks when she noticed Rei inside the office.

She looked away, surveyed the surroundings, and then looked back at Rei. After a few seconds of silence, she directed a suspicious gaze at him before finally speaking.

「Who are you? You’re…not Rei, are you?」

「Huh?」

Rei let out a dumbfounded sound in response to Min’s words.

It was only natural. While it might have been understandable if he were wearing his hood, he currently had it down since he was meeting with Daska. In other words, his distinctive feminine face was clearly visible.

Including his small stature—which could even be described as petite for a man, Rei’s characteristics were obvious to anyone. That was why everyone in the room, Elk included, froze, taken aback by Min’s words.

The first to move was Elk, who believed his wife’s words without a shred of doubt. Although he was unarmed since they were in the lord’s residence, he positioned himself to shield Min while glaring at Rei with a sharp gaze, ready to intercept him if he moved toward Daska.

「You…who are you?」

「Look, I’m sorry to interrupt your serious question, but I am the genuine Rei you know. In the first place, who else could I possibly look like?」

Elk frowned slightly at Rei’s words. Although they had only exchanged a few words, the person in his line of sight looked like no one but Rei.

Then there was his presence. The way Rei carried himself while holding the Death Scythe was clearly not that of an ordinary person. He was undoubtedly a warrior of equal or greater skill than Elk himself. Above all, the Death Scythe in his hand was proof that Rei was Rei.

The handle was nearly 2m long, and the blade was about 1m. A scythe was already a difficult weapon to use, and a scythe of this size would usually be impossible to handle. The only person Elk knew who used such a weapon was Rei.

To Elk, there was no doubt the person before him was Rei. Yet, despite his own impression, he trusted his wife’s judgement. In fact, he suspected that Min’s intuition might be more accurate than his own. Even so, the person in front of him still looked exactly like Rei. He was conflicted.

「…Min, to my eyes, it can only be Rei. Are you saying he’s different?」

The momentum he had when charging into the office was gone. Now, plagued by indecision, he looked back at Min.

「Yes. From the outside, he certainly looks like Rei. That item box and the Death Scythe are undoubtedly the items Rei possesses. However…even so, from my perspective, I cannot believe he is Rei.」

Rei was actually the one most surprised by Min’s firm assertion.

「How can you be so certain I’m not Rei? You should know that the item box can’t be used by anyone other than its owner, right? Since I’m using it, I don’t see how I could be anyone else.」

「Then let me ask you this. Why can’t I feel any magic power from you? No, I feel about as much as an ordinary mage. But the Rei I know possesses so much magic power that it’s a wonder it even fits inside a human body. To someone with the ability to sense magic power, it’s the kind of power that one can never forget once they’ve seen it.」

「…Oh, I see.」

Rei finally understood what was going on at Min’s words and looked down at the ring on his finger.

It appeared to be a perfectly ordinary ring. In reality, however, it was a magic item from the ancient magic civilisation, the New Moon Ring, which had the effect of hiding the wearer’s magic power.

Rei hesitated for a moment, wondering if it was okay to remove the item in front of her, but he firmly considered Min an ally and a fellow adventurer of Gilm. He decided that leaving her suspicious would only lead to a troublesome situation later, so he quietly slipped the ring off his finger.

In that instant, Min felt a sudden surge of magic power radiating from Rei’s body and stumbled back several steps.

「Th-This is…」

「It seems you’re convinced now.」

Judging by Min’s reaction that there were no further issues, Rei slid the Ring of the New Moon back onto his finger.

「Wha-!?」

Another cry of shock escaped Min’s lips. It was only natural. The magic power she could sense just a moment ago had been suppressed back down to the level of an ordinary mage in the next heartbeat.

To put it in perspective, it was like looking at a vast ocean, only to find that the ocean had been replaced by a few drops of water in the blink of an eye.

「Do you understand now?」

「…It’s that ring, isn’t it?」

「Yeah. It’s a magic item called the New Moon Ring, and it has the effect of hiding my magic power. I don’t have the ability to sense it myself, but apparently, to those who do, I’m very easy to identify for a number of reasons. This magic item prevents that.」

「Even so, a magic item capable of hiding your level of magic power…where on earth did you get it? If you don’t mind, can you tell me?」

Min looked at the ring on Rei’s hand with intense interest. The doubt had already vanished from her face. She understood that the magic power she felt when he removed the ring was undoubtedly Rei’s.

Under Min’s gaze, Rei stored the Death Scythe to the Misty Ring and spoke as he sat back down on the sofa.

「It’s a magic item I received as a reward for my work in the Bestir Empire. The effect is as you saw, it hides my magic power. Thanks to this, people who can sense magic power can only see me as an ordinary mage, and people can’t identify me by my amount of magic power.」

「…I know such magic items exist, but I didn’t think any of them could actually contain your magic power.」

「It’s a relic from an ancient magic civilisation, so it was probably made with more advanced technology than what we have now. …Anyway, what did the two of you come here for in the first place?」

「Indeed. I never expected my office to be the target of a literal assault. I’d like to hear an explanation.」

Daska’s remark seemed to remind Min of where she was. Or rather, she realised that her attempt to unmask an impostor had been meaningless.

「My apologies, Daska. I truly thought some enemy agent was infiltrating this place disguised as Rei.」

Min bowed deeply. Seeing her like that, Daska let out a small sigh.

「Well, don’t worry about it. It’s understandable that someone like you, who can sense magic power, felt something was wrong with Rei. …That’s fine. So, what did Elk come here for?」

「Hm? That would be, you know…」

Elk looked around as if trying to recall his original purpose, and soon enough, he remembered.

「Right, that’s it! It’s about Rhodes! How did he end up like that!? I mean, I heard he hasn’t regained consciousness!」

Elk’s gaze was fixed on Rei. Having heard that Rei had returned to Gilm, Elk and Min had naturally assumed Rhodes would be there as well. But when they arrived at the lord’s residence, they found Rhodes in a state of unconsciousness.

They had heard about Rhodes’ situation beforehand, but seeing him with their own eyes was clearly a different matter.

Rhodes had no visible severe injuries and looked as if he were simply sleeping. In reality, he had sustained significant injuries during his fight with Rei, but those had already been erased by the effects of magic items. To Elk and Min, his condition looked utterly abnormal.

「If you’re asking why, it’s likely the influence of the magic item Kabajid gave him. His will was essentially stolen, or rather, he was brainwashed, in order to attack me. I had to repel him. As time passed, the brainwashing either progressed or he was intended to be disposable from the start…anyway, Vihera found him wandering the battlefield during the final battle and took him into custody.」

At Rei’s explanation, Elk struggled to suppress his anger, while Min knit her brows slightly. Naturally, their displeasure was not directed at Rei. It was directed at Kabajid for doing such a thing to their son.

「…That Kabajid fellow, he’s dead, right?」

「Yeah. He took his own life to atone for losing the civil war.」

Strictly speaking, Rei felt it was less about taking responsibility for the defeat and more that Kabajid had been seeking an end. Considering that Kabajid seemed to have been in a similar circumstance to himself, Rei found him to be a person of great interest.

(If I had known the circumstances when we met at the castle, we could have talked about a lot of things.」

Even though some time had passed since that battle, Rei still couldn’t help but feel that way.

「I see. I would have preferred to deliver the final blow myself, but if he’s dead, there’s nothing to be done. …So, do we know when Rhodes will wake up?」

Rei shook his head at Elk’s question.

「I have no idea. I’ve never anything like this before. I don’t know if he’ll wake up naturally if we wait, or if we need to take some kind of action.」

「From what I’ve seen, we have no choice but to give it time. Using a standard potion won’t be enough to wake him. I’ll look into whether there’s any other method, though.」

Min murmured and Elk nodded in return.

「If you need any tools or materials, let me know. I’ll go harvest them as quickly as possible.」

Listening to their exchange, Rei suddenly remembered something he needed to mention regarding Rhodes.

「I brought Rhodes from the Imperial Capital to Gilm while he was bedridden…I paid a reward to the person who took care of him during the trip, so I’d like you to reimburse me for that.」

「Hm? …Ah, I see. He was bedridden the whole way. Understood. How much was the reward?」

「About 2 gold coins.」

「I see, 2 gold coins then. Understood.」

Min nodded as she took a pouch from her pocket and handed the gold coins to Rei.

Watching his wife, Elk let out a breath. Whether it was a breath of relief, a sigh, or something else entirely, only he truly knew.

+++

# **856**

By the time Rei finished discussing the events that had happened in the Bestir Empire at the lord’s residence, it was already getting dark outside.

It was only just past four in the afternoon, but at this time of year, the darker environment was to be expected.

Leaving the lord’s residence, Rei headed straight to the stables to pick up Set.

Set, who had been sleeping in the stables as if he owned the place, noticed Rei’s arrival and gave a happy cry.

…None of the horses in the stables seemed surprised by Set’s presence, likely because they were the same ones that had travelled with him all the way from the Bestir Empire to Gilm.

「Gururururu~」

Rei patted Set as he rubbed his face against him.

After enjoying the feel for a few minutes, Rei left the stables with Set.

The other horses in the stable watched the pair go, and although Rei doubted they could understand his words, he spoke up anyway.

「Your masters won’t be back for a while yet. You lot can just take it easy here.」

「Brrrr.」

The horses whinnied, though whether they understood Rei was anyone’s guess.

To ensure they didn’t do anything suspicious in Gilm and to teach them the necessities of living here, Sergio and the group of nearly thirty others would be unable to leave the lord’s residence for some time.

Those assigned to explain things to them naturally doubled as their guards.

As the lord governing this land, Daska couldn’t simply grant freedom to thirty people from the Bestir Empire so easily.

Even so, the fact that they were treated with a relatively lenient attitude because they were Rei’s associates was a stroke of luck for everyone involved.

Given his role in bringing Sergio and the others here, Rei normally would have had to stay at the lord’s residence as well, but Daska hadn’t bothered to keep him, stating that it was far too late to start doubting him now.

As for Rhodes, whom Rei had also brought back, Elk and Min had taken him with them. They were likely looking for any clues to help him regain consciousness.

「Well, I hope they do their best…but it’ll be difficult.」

「Guru~?」

Rei muttered to himself as they left the residence and walked toward the city. Set, walking beside him, let out a cry as he tilted his head.

Rei patted him, telling him it was nothing, as they continued down the path leading to the main street…

「Ah! Set-chan! Look, I knew it! Set-chan is here! My information network was right!」

A voice echoed through the passage Rei and Set were walking along.

Rei looked around at the sound and soon spotted a familiar face.

She had well-defined features and could easily be called a beauty, but currently, her face wore an entranced expression.

It was Milein, the leader of the adventurer party Scorching Wind, who had a long standing acquaintance with Rei. Or rather, it would be more accurate to say she was obsessed with Set.

The raid on the Orc settlement, Rei’s first large-scale request in Gilm, was the first time he had met Milein, making her one of the adventurers he had known the longest.

Since she had been there when they defeated the Orc King, she was also someone who knew a fair few of Rei and Set’s secrets.

「You found out we were back quite quickly.」

「It wasn’t quick at all! I’ve been searching everywhere since I heard Set-chan was back, and I’ve finally found him! Set-chan, long time no see!」

「Gururururu~」

She gave Rei a short reply before cutting the conversation short and heading straight for Set.

After handing Set some dried meat, she began stroking his head.

Set had known Milein for a long time and understood perfectly well that she held great affection for him. Set was naturally friendly, and someone like Milein, who doted on him and always gave him treats, was more than enough to earn his favour.

Because of that, Set gave happy cries while eating the dried meat she provided, clearly enjoying the reunion.

「Yes, yes. Set-chan was happy to see me too, after all. I’m happy too!」

「Guru~?」

As Set rubbed his face against her, Mileine’s expression softened even further.

She continued to feed him dried meat while enjoying the feel of his fur to her heart’s content.

As Rei watched Milein with an exasperated look, another figure approached.

「It’s been a while, Rei.」

The one who spoke was a middle-aged man in his forties. It was Sulunin, a member of the same party and Milein’s “stopper”.

「Sulunin.」

「Yes. …My apologies for our leader’s behaviour, especially since you’ve only just returned to Gilm.」

Sulunin bowed his head while watching Milein frolic around with Set, but Rei shook his head, telling him not to worry about it.

「It makes me feel like I’m really back in Gilm.」

「Ahaha. Well, that’s a bit of a problem for us. Milein becomes quite useless as an adventurer when she’s like this.」

「…That’s true.」

Looking at Milein playing with Set now, few would believe she was the leader of a C rank party. C rank was a level where one was recognised as a full-fledged veteran adventurer.

(Well, the world of adventurers is one where strength is everything. It’s not strange for someone young to be C, B, or even A rank. Even I still look like I’m in my mid-teens.)

As Rei thought to himself while watching their interaction, Sulunin asked curiously.

「Is something wrong?」

「No, I was just thinking that seeing this makes it feel like I’ve returned to Gilm.」

「…Why did you say the exact same thing twice?…」

As a member of the same party, Sulunin silently wished Rei wouldn’t view them that way.

「You’ve got it tough too, Sulunin.」

「Haha, not really. Aside from times like this, Milein is usually a capable party leader.」

「I wonder how many people would believe that after seeing this.」

Sulunin could only offer a wry smile at Rei’s blunt words.

While Rei and Sulunin were watching Milein play with Set in that indescribable atmosphere, although they were in a side street, it was still quite close to the main street. Even though it was starting to get dark, there was no way they wouldn’t stand out doing this.

「Ah! It’s Set-chan!」

The voice rang out, and when Rei looked toward the source, he saw a ten year old girl. The girl ran straight toward Set.

「Yay! Set-chan, long time no see! Hey, I haven’t seen you lately, where did you go?」

「Gururu~?」

Set gave a cry in response to the girl’s question. He understood her words, but unfortunately, he couldn’t speak.

「Eh? Set-chan? Ah, it really is him! Wow, it’s been a while!」

「Whoa… just looking at Set is so healing.」

When Milein had first called out, few people had come over, likely because there hadn’t been many passers-by at that time. But now, Set was quickly surrounded by the residents of Gilm.

Watching Set being mobbed, Rei remembered that among those who had come to Gilm with him, there were also some fanatical Set fans.

(I hope they don’t clash with Milein.)

A former guerrilla unit member versus a C rank adventurer like Milein. In terms of raw strength, Mileine was likely superior, but the gap wasn’t insurmountable. If anything, it was the kind of difference that could be overturned by a small slip-up.

(Especially since she tends to go out of control where Set is concerned…it wouldn’t be surprising if her combat power increased through raw emotion.)

The best-case scenario for Rei was that they would bond over being fellow Set fans. But how it would actually turn out…he wouldn’t know until they actually met.

The people wishing to immigrate were currently undergoing procedures and interviews at the lord’s residence, but Rei could easily predict they would be allowed to move freely soon enough.

「Er… Rei, what should we do about this?」

Sulunin gestured toward the crowd. Set was surrounded by so many people that, while fine for now, they would eventually become an obstacle if a carriage tried to pass.

「Should we move somewhere with fewer people?」

「Yes, definitely.」

Sulunin nodded immediately. Rei agreed and called out to Set in the middle of the crowd.

「Set! We’re moving!」

「Gururururu~!」

Set’s voice echoed from the crowd, and the people parted to let him through. Despite so many people wanting his attention, no one tried to block his path, likely because they all understood what kind of creature Set was.

There were also people nearby who didn’t know what the fuss was about, and some of them nearly collapsed in shock at the sudden appearance of a Griffon.

A fair amount of time had passed since Rei left Gilm for the Bestir Empire, and since it was the transition from autumn to winter, many new people had arrived in Gilm during that time.

…Luckily, the number of people was much lower than during the peak season. Most people who were new to Gilm at this time were either latecomers or those who had travelled from very far away.

The reactions of such people were already familiar to the residents of Gilm. When the bystanders explained that Set was Rei’s tamed monster, the newcomers were shocked again, though for a different reason.

Rei was famous in many ways, and many had heard the rumours. However, seeing him in person was a different matter entirely.

Set ignored the stunned gazes and walked over to Rei. Rei patted the Griffon as he rubbed his head against him and spoke to the crowd.

「If we make a scene here, we’ll be blocking traffic. We’re moving elsewhere, so those who want to play with Set can follow. But as you can see, it’s already dark. Those with errands should head home. Both Set and I will be back for a while…」

Rei’s mind briefly flashed to the dungeon.

「We’ll be in Gilm for a few days, so if you really want to play with Set, it would be a huge help if you came by during the day.」

「You say that, but playing outside in this cold during the day is a bit much.」

「Excuse me? You’re playing with him right now in the evening when the temperature has already dropped.」

Voices called out from the crowd in response to Rei’s words, but nearly half of the people seemed to remember they had things to do. Looking disappointed, they began to disperse. However, they didn’t forget to give Set a little wave to make sure he noticed them before they left.

(Well, it’s evening, so many people have to prepare dinner. I suppose if they went home and said they were late because they were playing with Set, they’d probably get scolded.)

Rei watched them go, then noticed Milein looking at him expectantly. He led the way to a nearby spot that wouldn’t obstruct passers-by.

In the end, about ten people followed them, which made Rei feel the strength of Set’s popularity.

「Ahahahaha! Here, Set-chan. Eat this sandwich.」

「Oh, this fruit is delicious too!」

「Here, I’ve got some dried fish!」

「I’ve got dried fruit with concentrated sweetness!」

「Ah, I have honey!」

「Yay! Set!」

Rei watched the people immediately start doting on Set in the space away from the path. Nearby, Sulunin watched his own party leader, who was the most enthralled of all, with an indescribable expression.

「Um, Rei. I know it’s not for me to say, but…shouldn’t we stop them?」

「…Even if you say that, Set doesn’t seem to mind, so why not? It’ll be a problem if it goes on too late, though.」

Set was naturally friendly, so he didn’t mind being pampered and given food, in fact, he enjoyed it. If someone tried to pull his wing feathers or pluck his fur, he’d certainly object, but there was no way Milein and the others, who were obsessed with his cuteness, would do such a thing.

If anyone had tried to do it to harvest materials from Set, Milein would likely have been the first to stop them. To Milein, who loved Set from the bottom of her heart, it wasn’t hard to see through someone who only pretended to care.

Watching the scene, Rei spoke up.

「By the way, could I meet with the members of Scorching Wind soon? Including Ekril.」

「Huh? Well, we’ve finished our winter preparations, so we’ve got plenty of free time. I don’t mind, but… did something happen? A request?」

Sulunin tilted his head at the sudden proposal. Rei looked toward Set as he spoke.

「I’m thinking of removing the Seed of Contract I placed on you all previously.」

「…Eh?」

Sulunin stared at Rei, his expression clearly asking what on earth he was talking about.

+++

# **857**

「Huaah… Mmm…」

Yawning, Rei sat up in his bed.

Looking around and turning his still slightly sleep-addled gaze toward the window, Rei remembered he was back at the Dusk Wheat Pavilion.

Outside, the weather was unbelievably good for autumn. Not a single cloud could be seen in the sky, a clear autumn day that felt closer to summer.

It almost seemed as if the sky itself was blessing Rei’s return to Gilm.

「…Well, it’s probably just my imagination.」

Rei muttered softly, his mind finally clearing up as started to properly wake up.

The Dusk Wheat Pavilion was his usual inn in Gilm. Since he hadn’t known how long the civil war would keep him away for when he left for the Bestir Empire, he had vacated his room. However, now that he was back in Gilm, he had rented a room here once again.

The day before, when he returned to Gilm, it had taken him quite a while to tear Milein away from Set. By the time Rei finally arrived at the Dusk Wheat Pavilion, dinner time was nearly over.

Even so, the proprietress, Lana, hadn’t forgotten Rei, who was an excellent customer and had left a strong impression in many ways. She readily agreed when he told her he planned to stay for a while again.

Fortunately, even though autumn was deepening, there were still some rooms available.

The Dusk Wheat Pavilion was one of the highest-class inns in Gilm. Naturally, large merchant caravans and veteran mercenary groups often stayed there. Just a short while ago, it had been packed with guests preparing for winter.

However, things had settled down now. It wasn’t completely empty, but a fair number of rooms were available again. That was why Rei was able to secure a room so easily despite arriving unannounced.

Of course, the fact that Rei had previously stayed at the Dusk Wheat Pavilion for a long time probably played a part as well.

「Today…firstly, the guild. There’s those Gamelion requests, but I also want to meet with Lenora and Kenny. It’d be great if they had any information about the dungeon too. …No, the dungeon is the priority.」

Rei decided on his schedule for the day while getting ready, taking his clothes and the Dragon Robe, out of the Misty Ring.

The room he was currently staying in was the same one he had used before. While he had already been back for a day, the room was still quite barren.

Since he kept all his necessary belongings stored in the Misty Ring, the room would likely remain barren whether he stayed for a few days, a few weeks, or even months, even if the contents of the Misty Ring increased.

Having finished getting ready, he headed down to the first floor of the Dusk Wheat Pavilion for breakfast, but…

「Hm?」

Rei tilted his head at the sight before him.

There was something slightly off about the dining room as he entered.

He stared at the dining room for a moment…before finally realising what was bothering him.

「There aren’t many people around?」

Normally, since the inn prided itself on its food, there would be people other than the guests coming in for breakfast. While it wouldn’t be overflowing, it should have been crowded enough that finding a seat would take a moment.

Yet, right now, nearly 70 percent of the seats in the dining room were empty.

Feeling a vague sense of foreboding, he took his pocket watch out of the Misty Ring to check the time. It was nearly 10:00 AM.

「…Eh?」

Realising he had let out a dumbfounded sound at how badly he had overslept, Rei checked the pocket watch again.

However, the merciless reality remained, it was nearly 10:00 AM.

「Rei? Breakfast time is already over…would you like an early lunch?」

A familiar voice called out from behind him. Turning around, he saw Lana, the proprietress, carrying some laundry.

「Ah, no…yeah. Right, I’ll just have something light, whatever you recommend.」

Rei handed her a few copper coins and took a seat, looking around the dining room once more.

Those currently left in the dining room were either eating an early lunch, as Lana had suggested, or had overslept like Rei… Even so, the fact that nearly 30 percent of the seats were occupied was likely because those who had already finished their winter preparations were gathered here to relax.

「I never thought I’d oversleep by hours.」

Rei could understand oversleeping by a few dozen minutes…or even an hour. But if it was nearly 10:00 AM, that meant he had overslept by three or four hours.

Oversleeping to this extent was quite rare for him.

(I guess I must have been on edge the whole time I was in the Bestir Empire. Then I came back to Gilm, slept at the Dusk Wheat Pavilion, finally felt safe, and completely crashed.)

Rei hadn’t felt particularly tense during that time. He hadn’t felt like he was pushing his body either, he thought he had just been acting normally.

…Though, if he were to call the rampage he unleashed in the Bestir Empire “normal”, very few people would agree.

Returning to Gilm, which he could practically call his hometown, must have finally let him fully relax.

(Well, I was planning on resting my body a bit anyway, and I have a lot of other things to do, so oversleeping a little is fine.)

As he stretched lightly and thought to himself, Lana arrived at his table with a plate of sandwiches and a bowl of soup.

「Please, take your time.」

After saying that, Lana quickly hurried off. It wasn’t that she disliked Rei or anything, she was just busy with her inn duties.

「First up…definitely the guild. Then I have what I promised Scorching Wind, I also want to see if the magic sword I took from Noiz can be repaired.」

Rei muttered to himself as he took a bite of a sandwich.

True to the inn’s reputation for delicious food, the sandwich was incredibly tasty, hard to believe it had been made in such a short time.

Rei particularly liked the ones made with Gamelion meat.

(I guess Gamelion meat is already back on the menu. …Should I just take today off and head out tomorrow instead?)

Rei pondered this while eating the sandwich filled with grilled Gamelion meat marinated in sauce, but a few other people in the dining room had already began to notice his presence.

「Hey, that guy…could it be Crimson?」

「Eh? No, he’s supposed to be out of Gilm right now, isn’t he? Maybe it’s just someone who looks like him? Besides, Crimson’s robe is supposed to be incredibly plain.」

「Eh? But do you think someone wearing such a plain robe could afford to stay at this inn? You can’t afford to stay here without the skill to back it up, you know?」

「Well, it’s not like he’s guaranteed to be staying here. The food here is great, so maybe he just came to eat.」

Hearing the voices around him and judging that things would get bothersome if he stayed, Rei quickly finished his sandwiches while savouring the taste. Downing the vegetable soup, he left the dining room and headed for the stables.

「…Well, I figured she’d be here, but this is exactly as I expected.」

The moment Rei entered the stables, the first thing he saw was Milein feeding a sandwich to Set.

Moreover, the sandwich Milein was holding looked rather familiar.

…It was a matter of course. It was the exact same type of sandwich Rei had just been eating in the dining room.

In other words, Milein had gone out of her way to buy a sandwich from the Dusk Wheat Pavilion’s dining room just to feed it to Set.

「Ah, Rei. …You’re up pretty early. You could have slept in a bit more, you know.」

「It’s past ten already.」

Rei replied to Milein’s somewhat dissatisfied greeting as he looked around the stables.

Naturally, there were many horses present, but about half of them looked somewhat frightened.

The remaining half that weren’t frightened were either rigorously trained horses or horses that had been in the stables when Rei had stayed at the Dusk Wheat Pavilion before leaving for the Bestir Empire.

(Could it be that the frightened horses…are scared of Mileine, not Set?)

Rei suddenly had that thought as he looked around the stables, but he decided that couldn’t possibly be the case as he spoke up.

「More importantly, did Sulunin talk to you?」

「Eh? Ah, you mean about you needing something from us? Removing the Seed of Contract or whatever? Honestly, as long as I can stay with Set-chan, I’m perfectly satisfied.」

「…You really are something else. Well, as long as you understand. So, what do you want to do? Since we ran into each other here, should I just remove it for you now?」

Rei added that removing the Seed of Contract in a stable felt a bit anticlimactic, but Milein just stared at him intently.

It wasn’t the soft, affectionate gaze she directed at Set, but a sharp one.

「Hey, Rei. I’m happy you’re removing the Seed of Contract. Really, I am happy. But why so suddenly? The whole reason you cast that magic was because we saw Set-chan use powers that normal Griffons don’t have, right? So, why?」

For Milein, removing the magic that binded her was a joyous occasion. …It was a shame she would lose the strong fire resistance that came as a byproduct, but she was still glad she wouldn’t have to die if something happened.

However, she knew how much Rei cared for Set, and she also knew how incredibly attached Set was to Rei.

It was frustrating…truly frustrating from the bottom of her heart, but Rei was the absolute most important person to Set.

Knowing the bond between the person and Griffon, she couldn’t help but wonder why he was suddenly removing the Seed of Contract.

「Is it that strange?」

「Of course it is.」

「Well, to put it simply…I participated in the civil war that broke out in the Bestir Empire, and during that time, I used Set’s skills completely out in the open in front of a massive crowd. It’s known to the point where there’s no hiding it anymore.」

「…What on earth have you been doing? Better yet, what were you thinking!? Set-chan already draws enough attention just by being a Griffon! And why are you getting involved in a civil war in the first place!?」

「A lot of things happened, alright? A lot of things.」

He couldn’t exactly reveal his reasons for getting involved in the civil war here, so he dodged the question.

This civil war had been orchestrated by the cooperation of the Neutral and Aristocratic Factions of the Mireana Kingdom. He couldn’t just casually talk about it in public.

「Even so, with your power, Rei, you didn’t have to go out of your way to reveal Set-chan’s secret, did you?」

「…Maybe, but if I hadn’t, I would have died.」

Milein’s eyes widened dramatically at Rei’s words. She was so shocked she nearly crushed the sandwich in her hand.

「You nearly died…what kind of situation could possibly cause that?」

The Rei that Milein knew possessed enough power to overwhelm an entire army on his own. She couldn’t even begin to imagine a scenario where someone like that would struggle…let alone nearly die.

「Well, I ended up fighting a rather strong opponent.」

「…Exactly what kind of opponent would make you say something like that?」

Hearing Rei’s words, Milein urged him to continue, her interest clearly piqued.

Rei hesitated for a moment, wondering if he should tell her, but he decided there was no need to keep it a secret and answered plainly.

「The Bestir Empire’s S rank adventurer, Noiz, the Immovable.」

「-!?」

That name was completely unexpected for Milein. Her eyes widened, and she stared at Rei for a few seconds, as if trying to gauge the truth of his words, before asking timidly.

「Really?」

「Yeah. Well, as for the result… how should I put it? Set and I fought together, and technically he retreated, but considering how the fight went, it was more like we lost, or he let us go. He really lived up to his S rank. I was pretty confident in my fighting ability, but I never expected it to turn out like that…that’s how it felt.」

「Well, of course! S rank? Your rank is…B, right? It’s honestly more surprising that you managed to fight him at all with that rank difference.」

「Anyway, because of that, I went all out with Set’s skills during the final and biggest battle of the civil war. Once I used his skills in front of a huge crowd, I figured there was no hiding it anymore, so I just spammed them against the enemy. …Right now, a lot of people in the Bestir Empire know Set is a Griffon rare species. Because of that, there’s no need to keep you bound by the Seed of Contract anymore.」

「Gururu~」

Set gave a cry at Rei’s explanation. Milein hesitated for a moment before finally speaking.

「But I’ll miss the fire resistance. If we aren’t going to talk about Set-chan anyway, the Seed of Contract is basically just a blessing, isn’t it?」

「It’d be highly unnatural if you were the only one unable to speak while everyone else was talking about Set. …Don’t worry, I’ll leave the fire resistance intact.」

「You can do that?」

「Yeah. Though it’s only possible because the Seed of Contract has been inside you, constantly interacting with your magic power, for such a long period. And you have an affinity for it.」

Milein thought for a moment before giving a small nod at Rei’s words.

「…I understand. Please, go ahead.」

Hearing Milein’s consent, Rei took the Death Scythe out from the Misty Ring and began an incantation.

『Fire, use the Seed of Contract within them as fuel to become her strength.』

A small flame appeared at the tip of the Death Scythe…and Rei directed that flame toward Milein.

『Quiet Flame.』

The moment the spell activated, the small flame was sucked into Milein’s body…and she clearly felt the sensation of something burning within her.

# **858**

「Ah, it’s Set! He really did come back!」

「Oh, it really is Set. I heard rumours he came back yesterday but…I guess Gilm is about to get lively again.」

「No, no, it’s not like Gilm was gloomy just because Set wasn’t around.」

As Rei and Set walked through the city, voices like that rose from those who saw them.

Among them, the food stall owners seemed especially happy.

It was already close to noon, and the stalls were busy preparing for the lunch rush. Despite that, the stall owners called out to Set while cooking in the cold, steam rising all around them.

「Oh, if it isn’t Set. It’s been a while. Here, want something to eat? The skewers are grilled perfectly!」

「Set, it’s been a while. When it’s cold out, how about our soup filled with plenty of vegetables and meat?」

「Set, we have sandwiches, want some? The bread is freshly baked, once you take a bite you won’t be able to stop!」

「We’ve got stewed udon over here! It’s not chewy, but it’s incredibly soft and delicious to make up for it!」

Responding to the voices from the surrounding stalls, Set went back and forth, happily receiving food.

…Of course, it wasn’t free. Rei paid them each time and bought his own share as well.

However, Rei was given far more food than what he actually paid for. The reason the stalls gave Rei such massive extra portions wasn’t just because he was an excellent customer who bought a lot at once, but also because he always ate their food looking like it was truly delicious.

Anyone who saw the sight of Rei and Set eating would immediately want to eat as well, given how deliciously they ate. The fact that it was lunchtime and many people were already hungry only added to the effect.

(If Milein were here, she probably would have bought up most of the food at the stalls by now. And if that continued, she wouldn’t have enough money to survive the winter and would end up tearfully taking on winter requests to scrape by.)

Remembering the figure of his friend who had rushed off to inform her two companions that the Seed of Contract inside her body had been removed, Rei gave a small smile.

(As expected, even Milein chose having the magic removed over staying with Set…well, it’s only natural.)

Satisfied that despite her obsession with Set, she hadn’t forgotten her duties as the leader of a C rank party, Rei headed towards the guild while doing a massive amount of shopping at Gilm’s food stalls for the first time in a while.

The closer they got to the guild, the more stalls there were targeting adventurers, and naturally, the number of adventurers increased as well.

With that being the case, there were many who directed their gazes at Rei and Set…

「Hey, that’s…Rei, isn’t it? When did he get back?」

「Ah…from what I heard, he apparently got back yesterday.」

「As usual, he doesn’t look like a B rank adventurer at all just from his appearance. We can tell because Set is with him, but if Set wasn’t there, it wouldn’t be strange to mistake him for some beginner wandering around.」

「Well, there is that. If he took his hood off we could tell by his face, but he usually keeps it on.」

The adventurers who knew of Rei exchanged words with their respective companions.

Since Rei had appeared in this city, for better or worse, he had been involved in numerous massive disturbances. Because of that, to the adventurers operating in Gilm who had seen it all, he was recognised as someone they shouldn’t carelessly mess with or antagonise.

That said, many thought that he wasn’t such a bad guy if you just talked to him normally, and the sight of him with Set was somewhat heartwarming.

However…it was also a fact that Rei didn’t look strong purely from his outward appearance…

「Hey, hey, is that really Crimson? Aren’t the rumours heavily exaggerated? No matter how I look at it, I can’t believe such a short, delicate guy is that strong.」

「Right? …He probably got this famous thanks to that Griffon, right? Hah, being carried by his tamed monster. Must be nice.」

「But, if you think of him as a tamer who subdued a Griffon, isn’t he pretty skilled?」

「Huh? What are you saying? After all, a tamer is just someone who can only hide behind their monster, right? A guy like that, we could take him out in one hit. One hit. …How about we just beat up that kid Rei and take his Griffon?」

「Idiot. No matter how weak that Rei is, a Griffon is a Griffon. Do you think you’d get off easily if you messed with a monster like that?」

A short distance away, a group of adventurers who had arrived in Gilm while Rei was away in the Bestir Empire, and so were likely seeing him for the first time, gathered as talked with each other.

In a way, it was a familiar sight in Gilm, and those who knew Rei looked at those new adventurers with somewhat pitying eyes.

…Although, there were some who directed sharp glares at those who talked about targeting Set.

The appearance of such people was somewhat unavoidable in Gilm.

Gilm was located on the frontier, and aside from those who grew up in the city and became adventurers naturally, everyone else who came to Gilm from other regions possessed a certain level of skill and the confidence that came with it.

Since skilled adventurers gathered in Gilm, newcomers were often treated as rookies, but naturally, they had a corresponding amount of pride because they were confident in their own abilities.

Well, if it was just pride it would be fine, but there were many who firmly believed that their skills would naturally cut it even in Gilm. Precisely because their half-baked skills had worked for them up until now, there were many who couldn’t comprehend an existence that was completely beyond their imagination.

To such people, regardless of Rei’s ability to tame a Griffon, they judged that his actual strength as a fighter was just exaggerated rumours. …They couldn’t help but assume so.

Of course, rumours that Rei’s own strength was extremely high had spread, but looking at his small stature and apparent lack of muscle…seeing Rei like that, even if they didn’t think all the rumours were lies, it couldn’t be helped if they assumed that the results of the Griffon’s battles had been mistakenly attributed to him.

In that case, they could be the ones to expose his true colours.

With that thought in mind, several adventurers tried to step forward and call out to Rei, but…

「Hey, give it a rest. There’s no way people with your level of strength could beat Rei. Besides, messing with him leads to all sorts of troublesome things.」

At that voice, the several adventurers who were about to call out to Rei stopped in their tracks.

They reflexively tried to shout back at the words that seemed to be looking down on them, but when they realised the person in their line of sight was a heavily muscled giant who clearly possessed immense strength, they swallowed their words along with their breath.

「If you’re scared just looking at me, there’s no way you can beat Rei.」

Having those words thrown at them, the newly arrived adventurers in Gilm were spared from receiving Rei’s harsh baptism.

「…Well, whatever.」

Rei muttered as he watched the several adventurers who had directed malicious glares at him being led away by an adventurer he remembered seeing in the guild a few times.

If they had kept messing with him, he was planning to fight them under the guise of self-defence, knock them out, and strip them of some weapons or armour…he had his eye on a spear one of them was holding in particular. However, judging that it was fine since the trouble was gone, he continued shopping at the food stalls while heading towards the guild.

By the time he arrived in front of the guild, he was already holding an unmanageable amount of food. He kept out a portion for Set to eat and stored the rest into the Misty Ring, as it would be a waste if it got cold.

「Well, this might take a bit of time…no, I suppose you won’t be bored.」

「Gururururu!」

At the usual waiting area for tamed monsters and carriages, Set gave a cry in a good mood while lying down.

Nearly twenty residents, ranging from five-year-old children to elderly people in their sixties, had already gathered around Set, each trying to pet him, talk to him, and feed him.

「Set-chan, Set-chan, Set-chan!」

Rei felt like he saw a face he had just seen in the stables of the Dusk Wheat Pavilion among them, but telling himself it was probably his imagination, he entered the guild.

Because it was already close to noon, there weren’t many people inside the guild.

Many adventurers had already finished their preparations for winter, and their absence was likely the reason there were fewer people than a usual afternoon.

Perhaps to make up for it, there was a fair number of people eating and drinking in the tavern attached to the guild.

「Rei!」

As he looked around the guild, that voice echoed out.

Turning his gaze towards it, Rei saw the figure of a cat Beastkin jumping right over the counter.

It was Kenny, the cat Beastkin receptionist who had a crush on Rei.

Despite pulling a stunt like jumping over the counter, her short skirt didn’t flip up at all. According to Kenny, this sort of thing was also part of a receptionist’s etiquette.

「Hey, Kenny!?」

Lenora shouted as if to reprimand Kenny for her sudden action.

However, Kenny didn’t seem to care about her friend’s voice at all and ran right up to Rei’s side.

「Rei, I heard you went to the Bestir Empire, were you okay? I was told you were with Daska-sama, so I was really surprised when you weren’t there when he came back!」

「Ah… yeah, sorry. I had a bit of business to take care of over there. Things just kind of happened.」

「Things happened… well, fine. Are you hurt anywhere?」

Saying that, Kenny reached out to touch Rei’s face and his body under the Dragon Robe to check for injuries.

If it were someone trying to steal from him, Rei would have stopped them immediately, but knowing she was just worried about him, he silently accepted her actions.

Confirming that Rei wasn’t injured, Kenny breathed a sigh of relief…but soon, her eyes became glued to Rei’s hand.

In her line of sight was the ring sitting on Rei’s finger.

Normally, a ring was something given to a person of the opposite sex one had feelings for. There were individuals who wore them as a fashion statement, but Rei, at least, didn’t have the kind of personality to care about fashion.

In other words, someone had made a move on Rei.

Reaching that conclusion in an instant, Kenny slowly turned her gaze back to Rei with a rigid movement that practically screamed with a creaking sound.

…Incidentally, many of the adventurers in the guild, though few in number, had been watching the exchange between Rei and Kenny with interest. But the moment they saw Kenny’s movement just now, their bodies inexplicably froze. This was despite the fact that there were not only low rank adventurers, but even C rank adventurers present.

「…Hey, Rei. What’s with this ring? Did you get it from someone?」

However, Rei, entirely oblivious to the terrifying atmosphere Kenny was giving off, replied without any hint of tension.

「Yeah, I got it from Theorem.」

「…Eh?」

Kenny froze, as if time had stopped.

The reason she froze this time was completely different from when she first saw the ring.

Naturally. No matter how you looked at it, Theorem was a man’s name.

In other words, Rei was wearing a ring given to him by a man…
