『Nothing. I just thought that even you had some longing to be in a party, Rei.』

Rei wore a dissatisfied expression, feeling that her words were completely unexpected.

「It’s not like I preferred being solo, you know? I only flew solo until now because of Set’s situation. But after what happened this time, there’s no need to hide Set’s skills anymore. In that sense, it’s true that forming a party has become much easier.」

『That’s true. However…unfortunately, I think it would be difficult for me to become an adventurer.』

「Ah…」

At Elena’s words, Rei finally remembered the position of the person on the other side of the Paired Orb.

She was someone who held the title of General Princess, and a figure who could be called the symbol of the Aristocratic Faction.

No matter how he thought about it, operating as an adventurer would be impossible for her.

Since he had been looking forward to acting as a party, Rei wore an even more disappointed expression. Seeing this, Elena gave a small smile as she continued.

『Well, we might not be an official party, but if it’s just tagging along, I think I can make some time. …Though my workload before and after heading over there will probably become quite brutal to make up for it.』

「Really? Then I’m looking forward to spring. …Maybe it would be a good idea to clear the dungeon in Exil. Ah, or we could clear the dungeon with the Altar of Inheritance. Last time, it wasn’t really a situation where we could worry about the dungeon core.」

『Fufu, that’s true.』

For both of them, what happened back then was a bitter…a truly bitter memory, but even so, they were able to talk about it like this now.

「Though, the floor with the Water Monkeys is a pain because of their sheer numbers.」

『But unlike last time, you don’t need to hide Set’s skills now, so it shouldn’t be that bad…』

Just as Elena said that.

As if timing it perfectly, a knock echoed on the door.

And before Rei could answer, the door swung open and a voice rang out.

「Rei, I finally managed to escape from that flat-chested girl! Honestly, Lenora is always so nagging, no wonder she doesn’t even have a single lover…」

The person who had barged into the room was Kenny.

Kenny smiled when she saw Rei in the room, but the next moment, she noticed the orb sitting on the table near him.

Well, if it had just been that, it wouldn’t have been a problem.

But the fact that a dignified beauty was projected in the crystal made it a different story.

The guild had an orb for communicating with other guilds, and Kenny had seen it used for work several times.

Because of that, she understood that the Paired Orb was something similar, and she was surprised that Rei possessed such an item, which was normally not something an individual could own.

…But, as expected, the biggest problem was the woman projected in the crystal.

Kenny was confident in her own looks as well.

She wasn’t being conceited, guild receptionists were specifically hired for having attractive features.

She also had plenty of experience being hit on by numerous adventurers.

Yet the person projected in the crystal was someone even Kenny had to admit was undeniably more beautiful than herself.

「…Rei, who is that?」

「Look, just barging into someone’s room…well, whatever. This is…」

Rei was about to introduce Elena, but a voice from the other side of the crystal interrupted him.

『It’s fine, Rei. I’ll introduce myself.』

Elena’s gaze as she looked at Kenny through the crystal was sharp.

Elena had known about Kenny’s existence for a long time.

When she sent Yellow to Gilm during the winter, Yellow had encountered Kenny, and Elena had seen those memories.

That was why she knew exactly what kind of person Kenny, who was currently standing near Rei, was. And she knew Kenny’s feelings as well.

『I am Elena Kerebel. It feels strange saying it myself, but would you understand if I said the General Princess?』

「-!?」

Kenny gasped at those words.

As a guild receptionist, she naturally had more opportunities to obtain and view various kinds of information than the average person.

Because of that, when the woman on the other side of the crystal…Elena, gave her name, Kenny was immediately able to match her face to the person in question.

「…My apologies, Elena-sama. My name is Kenny, and I work at the guild in Gilm.」

『Yes, I know of you, Kenny. And your relationship with Rei as well.』

「…」

With that single sentence, Kenny understood.

The person projected in the crystal was undoubtedly a duke’s daughter and someone who held a title.

But that wasn’t what mattered right now. That was irrelevant.

The person currently before her wasn’t just a high-ranking noble…she was her enemy, a rival in love.

Judging that Kenny had grasped their dynamic, Elena turned her gaze toward Rei.

『Rei, I’m sorry, but could you leave me alone with this Kenny for a moment?』

「Are you serious?」

That question carried several meanings.

Someone in the position of a duke’s daughter and an title holder wanted to speak privately…and in Rei’s room, no less.

If any problems arose from this, it would undoubtedly bring disaster upon Kenny.

Rei directed a slightly sharp gaze at Elena, silently asking if she understood that when she made the request.

However, the one who reacted to Rei’s words wasn’t Elena, but Kenny.

Of course, Kenny also knew she couldn’t do anything careless against a duke’s daughter…especially one known as the symbol of the Aristocratic Faction.

Even so, she couldn’t back down here.

「Rei, please. I also have something I want to talk to Elena-sama about. …Right, I’ll come get you when we’re done, so could you kill some time in the dining room downstairs?」

At those words, Rei hesitantly looked toward Elena.

In terms of social standing, Elena was overwhelmingly superior.

That was why, if Elena was making an unreasonable demand, he felt he had to stop it. But if Kenny also wanted this, Rei couldn’t interfere.

If that were the case, all Rei could do was ask Elena not to make things rough.

Receiving that look from Rei, Elena gave a small nod and spoke.

『Rest assured. There is no way I’m going to do anything to her over this. But, well. …Let’s just say we need to have a talk between women.』

「Alright. …Well, I’m feeling a bit hungry anyway, so I’ll head down to the dining room on the first floor for a bit.」

Saying that, Rei left the room.

Leaving them in his room was nothing short of careless, but Rei trusted Kenny.

Besides, there was also the fact that there was practically no luggage or personal belongings in this room anyway.

A few minutes passed after Rei left the room. Surprisingly, the first one to speak was Kenny.

「Honestly, couldn’t Rei have been at least a little suspicious?」

『Rei is ruthless towards his enemies, but he becomes endlessly soft on anyone he considers an ally.』

「Is that from personal experience?」

『Yes. But considering Rei’s personality, wouldn’t you know that better than I do?』

「That’s true, I can’t deny it. Apparently, when he first came to the guild to register, he provoked a party that messed with him into a fight and shook them down for their money and weapons.」

『Hah, that sounds just like Rei. …Now, enough with the preamble. Why did I want to speak with you? You understand, don’t you?』

After a moment of silence at Elena’s words, Kenny nodded.

「Of course. It’s about Rei, isn’t it?」

『Indeed. …Considering Rei’s personality, abilities, background, and the fact that he has Set as a tamed monster, he will undoubtedly get dragged into various disturbances from here on out. When that happens, I don’t want someone who would be a liability near him. …No, that’s just an excuse. Allow me to be honest. Personally, I cannot accept you being by his side. Not even on an emotional level.』

Elena anticipated that Rei would eventually take several wives in the future.

However, she still felt that she should be the primary wife. It was one thing if it was someone she approved of, like Vihera, but having an unknown woman enter that circle was not something she welcomed.

Kenny felt herself flinch for a moment at Elena’s words, but she immediately replied.

「I’m sorry, but I cannot obey your words, Elena-sama. My relationship with Rei is very important to me as well.」

『Hmm… I see. I suppose it is. But are you sure? It feels strange saying this myself, but I hold a great deal of influence. Aren’t you worried about that?』

Rather than a threat…it was said to test Kenny’s resolve. Pushing down her inner apprehension, Kenny nodded back.

「Of course I am worried. But I have judged that someone who is called the General Princess…and someone who holds feelings for Rei, would not do something like that.」

『…Don’t you think I might take such actions precisely because I care for Rei?』

「Someone planning to do something like that wouldn’t say it out loud.」

『Oh?』

Elena murmured as if impressed by Kenny’s words.

A light resided in her eyes, as if she were acknowledging Kenny’s existence a bit more than before.

『I see. Working at a guild in a frontier land like Gilm, you certainly have quite a bit of nerve. But…that alone is not enough for me to accept you being by Rei’s side.』

「Elena-sama. I am sorry, but the person who stands by Rei’s side is decided by Rei himself. I do not believe that is something for you to decide.」

『…Fufu, that’s certainly true. I might have gotten a little ahead of myself.』

Elena’s laughter echoed through the room… and the oppressive atmosphere from earlier vanished.

In the end, it was about thirty minutes later when Kenny called Rei from the dining room, and Rei never learned what they discussed during that time.

+++

# **862**

「So, this is the location of the new dungeon?」

Lenora nodded at Rei’s words.

「Yes. That is correct. But are you absolutely sure? You can hardly expect to earn anything from this dungeon, you know?」

Several adventurers had already gone to explore the newly formed dungeon near Gilm.

However, the materials and magic stones obtainable from the monsters inside were all worth very little. Lenora knew that almost everyone who went said they ended up operating at a loss, which prompted her warning.

Traveling to the dungeon wouldn’t cost anything if they walked. But regardless of what kind of enemies they faced, their weapons would wear down from fighting, and they could get injured if they took a hit. Because the dungeon was narrow, some had even damaged their weapons by striking them against the walls.

Considering all that, Lenora couldn’t recommend that Rei try to clear the dungeon.

Also…

「Besides, I don’t think Set will be able to enter the dungeon either, you know? The entrance and such are apparently quite small.」

「I’ve heard about that. Well, I’ll test it out just in case, but if he can’t get in, I’ll have him wait outside.」

「I was entirely sure you would go after Gamelions instead. As a representative of the guild, it would be much more helpful if you did, since we are short on Gamelion meat this year.」

Lenora herself loved Gamelion meat, and the fact that prices had gone up this year due to the low numbers hunted was not a very happy situation for her.

Of course, it wasn’t a lie that it was for the guild’s sake either.

「Well, it’s true that finding Gamelions wouldn’t be difficult for you, Rei.」

Beside Lenora, Kenny agreed with a smile.

Kenny had spoken with Elena a few days ago, but it didn’t seem like anything had particularly changed because of it.

Of course, Kenny herself had definitely felt something, but she didn’t let it show.

Because of that, from Rei’s perspective, Kenny was exactly the same as always.

However, her long-time bad influence and best friend, Lenora, sensed that Kenny’s demeanour was slightly different than before.

「Gamelions, huh. I thought about that too. But right now, I’m more interested in the dungeon. Besides, the dungeon apparently isn’t that large, so I might try hunting Gamelions after I challenge and clear it. …I like Gamelion meat too, after all.」

「Understood. …Most of the monsters that appear in the dungeon are low rank, and their strength is apparently nothing special. However, a dungeon is a dungeon. You never know what might happen inside, so please make absolutely sure not to let your guard down.」

「The first floor of the dungeon is made up of stone corridors, and the second floor is a cave. Both are narrow, making it hard to fight as a party. Is that right?」

「Yes. Depending on the location, there are many places where it would be difficult to swing your large scythe…the Death Scythe, was it? Please be careful. A dungeon is a dangerous place where a single moment of carelessness can cost you your life. Especially since you are solo, Rei. Even if you think you can keep going, please judge the situation calmly.」

「Yeah, I know. I’ll do my best with the Gamelions after the dungeon too.」

Saying that, Rei left the guild.

At this time of year, when it wouldn’t be strange for it to snow at any moment, most adventurers had naturally already finished their winter preparations, and many were enjoying a long break at the tavern attached to the guild.

Contrary to those people, there were also those taking on requests for one last push before winter truly set in.

The guild contained both types of adventurers, but both groups directed suspicious gazes at Rei.

Everyone here naturally knew how skilled Rei was.

If so, he should be making a considerable amount of money. Why would someone like Rei head to a dungeon that would only yield pocket change?

Though, from the perspective of the adventurers currently looking for requests, they had no complaints about a highly skilled adventurer like Rei not taking requests, as it meant one less powerful competitor.

Furthermore, even the adventurers who didn’t know Rei and had previously looked down on him had now heard from senior adventurers what kind of existence he was, and they had decided to avoid getting carelessly involved with him.

(Well, based on the description of the dungeon, I can understand why no one wants to willingly challenge it, so these gazes are only natural.)

While muttering to himself, Rei felt that he absolutely could not overlook this dungeon.

When he was in the Bestir Empire, the thing he looked forward to most upon returning to Gilm was Gamelion meat.

But right now, Gamelion meat was a secondary priority for Rei.

That was how much of a treasure trove the dungeon was to him.

(What kind of skills will Set be able to absorb if he eats the dungeon core… I’m looking forward to it.)

Doing his best to ignore the gazes directed at him, Rei left the guild.

If it had been anyone other than Rei heading to the dungeon, they undoubtedly would have been bothered and gotten into trouble… It was probably fortunate for everyone involved that there was no one foolish enough to pick a fight with Rei.

「…Ah, come to think of it.」

Leaving the guild and walking towards Set, who was surrounded by people as usual, he suddenly remembered something.

He still had the magic sword he had obtained from Noiz exactly as it was.

The image of a blacksmith with a scary face who looked like nothing more than a bandit at first glance crossed Rei’s mind.

「If I remember right, Pamidor’s shop shouldn’t be too far from here.」

Muttering to himself, he decided to drop by quickly before heading to the dungeon, and pushed his way through the crowd towards Set.

(I don’t mind since Set is enjoying it, but I’d appreciate it if things settled down soon.)

Set would never dislike anyone who approached him without malicious intent.

Also, because Set was a Griffon, he had an abundance of stamina, and since he hadn’t been born that long ago, he returned affection to anyone who showed it to him.

As long as Set was having fun, he felt almost no mental fatigue. Ultimately, the people doting on Set would be the ones to run out of stamina first.

Though, since adults also had issues with time, there were hardly any who played with Set for that long.

(Except for this one, though.)

Rei directed an exasperated look at Milein, who was happily watching Set eat a chunk of ham.

「You’ve been here every day. Do you have that much free time?」

「I do. At the very least, there is no errand more important than being with Set-chan like this. Besides, we’ve already finished our winter preparations, so there’s no problem, right?」

「If you get too invested in Set, you’re going to run out of savings halfway through winter, you know?」

Even to Rei’s eyes, the ham Set was currently eating looked like quite a luxury item.

She was feeding Set ham like that by the kilogram, so the cost must have been considerable.

But Milein just smiled, not caring in the slightest about Rei’s words.

「It’s fine. If I run out of money, I’ll just earn more.」

If the adventurers who were desperately working right now were to hear her, their veins would pop on their foreheads.

The other people around her could only offer wry smiles at Milein’s words.

「Well, you can do whatever you want. But unfortunately, Set and I are heading to the dungeon now.」

「…The dungeon? The new one nearby?」

「Yeah.」

「Why go out of your way to do that? There’s no point in going to that dungeon, you know?」

Milein, finally turning her gaze towards Rei, asked curiously.

Among those around Set, those who knew the situation nodded in agreement with Milein’s words.

「Have you gone there?」

「Yes. Sulunin said he wanted to take a quick look inside. Though we ended up just fighting a few times and coming back.」

A sigh escaped Rei’s lips at Milein’s words.

He had been gathering information about the dungeon, but to think there was an information source this close by…he thought to himself.

Still, the stories he had heard from Lenora and a few people at the guild tavern and the Dusk Wheat Pavilion’s dining room certainly hadn’t been a waste.

Thinking that to convince himself, he prompted her to continue.

「So, how was it?」

「We mostly fought Goblins and Kobolds.」

「…Kobolds, huh.」

He had already absorbed a Goblin magic stone.

But since he hadn’t fought a Kobold before, he wondered if he might be able to get a new skill… However, he then remembered that he actually had fought them at an oasis in Exil’s dungeon previously and his expectations were instantly shattered.

He had only fought Kobolds during that oasis incident, but he had fought Goblins countless times before, so his impression of the former was inevitably weak.

「Yep. Well, since even we managed, I think you’ll be fine, Rei. …Ah, but.」

Milein’s words paused for a moment, and her gaze turned towards Set.

「The entrance is narrow, so Set-chan probably won’t be able to get in.」

「I’ve heard quite a bit about that. Having Set would make things a lot easier, though. If not just the entrance but the corridors aren’t that wide either, I’ll have to ask Set to wait outside.」

「Guru~…」

Set let out a disappointed cry.

His round eyes looked straight at Rei, but even with that gaze directed at him, Rei had no intention of taking Set into the dungeon.

He had the Size Transformation skill, but he couldn’t keep using it indefinitely.

Since the corridors were wide enough for some degree of combat, Set would probably be able to move… but if any trouble occurred, it could result in a fatal wound.

「Apparently, monsters sometimes come out of the dungeon. If you can’t enter the dungeon even with Size Transformation, I’m sorry, but could you handle things outside, Set? I hear Ranga and the guards are stationed there, but just in case.」

「Guru~…Gurururururu~, Guru~」

Set hesitated for a few seconds, but ultimately nodded in agreement with Rei’s words.

「Actually, if Set-chan can’t enter the dungeon, wouldn’t it be fine for you to just go alone, Rei? I’ll look after Set-chan while you’re gone.」

Although she was showing her desires honestly, Milein’s words were also sound logic.

However, Rei shook his head in response.

「With Set, a journey that would have taken hours on foot would only take about ten minutes.」

「Guru~!」

At Rei’s words, Set gave a cry as if to say, Leave it to me!

Watching them, Milein muttered in disappointment.

If Rei had been trying to forcefully take Set along, Milein would have had a word or two to say about it.

But since Set himself was showing through his attitude that he wanted to go with Rei, there was nothing she could say.

「Well, I’ll give it a shot. If it really turns out to be so utterly unprofitable that nothing can be done about it, I’ll quickly come back and to hunt Gamelions instead.」

「…I’d actually prefer it if you did that instead.」

Since Milein was also based in Gilm, she naturally looked forward to Gamelion dishes at this time of year.

However, Gamelion meat was scarce so far, and the prices were set higher than usual.

「Then why doesn’t Scorching Wind go hunt Gamelions? You guys are a C rank party, so you can definitely fight C rank Gamelions.」

「True, if it’s not a request and just for us to eat, I might consider it…but considering it might end up being a wasted trip…」

Up until now, several adventurers Milein knew had gone out to hunt Gamelions, but almost all of them hadn’t even been able to find a single one.

Among them, a few lucky parties had managed to hunt some, but she strongly felt that even if they went looking for Gamelions, they probably wouldn’t find any.

In the first place, Scorching Wind didn’t have a thief.

The archer, Ekril, could do a passable imitation of a thief, but they were overwhelmingly lacking in a dedicated scout.

On top of that, Gamelions were fast, despite their massive size.

And since they were ferocious, it wasn’t rare for them to launch surprise attacks.

In a straightforward fight, Milein prided herself on having enough strength to put up a decent fight, but if they were hit by a surprise attack, it would be a different story.

The Gamelion’s high physical abilities, its ears that acted as blades, its sharp fangs, and its tail that was like a whip or a spear.

Their only saving grace was that they had no means of long-range attack.

「I fought Gamelions last year too, so I understand that much…they certainly were quite something in terms of strength.」

「Right? It would be a different story if they were the type to challenge you head-on.」

While they conversed, Set quickly finished the remaining food and got ready to depart. Rei gave a brief farewell to the people gathered there before leaving.

「Ah, Set-chan…let’s meet again later! Rei, if you bully Set-chan, I won’t forgive you!」

Milein’s voice echoed around them…but most of the people there just smiled wryly at her words.

+++

# **863**

Walking down a back alley, not far from the library in Gilm, Rei finally found the building he was looking for.

「Right, Set.」

「Guru.」

At Rei’s call, Set gave a cry as if to say he understood and lay down in a spot that was mostly hidden from the surroundings.

If one ignored his size and the season, the sight of him lying there could easily be mistaken for a curled-up cat.

…If cats had wings growing from their backs that is.

With a quick glance at Set, Rei opened the building’s door.

In an instant, a warm, no, hot air enveloped Rei, completely opposite to the cold outside.

Frowning slightly at the heat, Rei checked to see if anyone was around before shouting loud enough to be heard at the back of the shop.

「Pamidor, are you here?」

「Yeah, I’m here! …What, it’s just you, Rei?」

A man who looked like nothing short of a hardened criminal at first glance came out from the back of the shop while saying that.

Not only did he have a brutal-looking face, but his physique was muscular enough that he looked like he could easily lift someone Rei’s size with one hand. He looked more like a bandit than an actual bandit.

Perhaps because he had been forging just now, his forehead was covered in sweat, adding to his intimidating aura.

That must have been the source of the heat when the door opened.

Knowing exactly what kind of person Pamidor was, Rei wasn’t particularly bothered by his appearance as he called out.

「What do you mean, ‘just you’? I’m still a customer, you know. …Is Kumito not here?」

「Kumito is out. What, you call yourself a customer, but you actually came looking for Kumito instead of me?」

「No, it’s nothing like that. I was just asking.」

「Well, whatever. So what’s your business? I heard from Kumito that you were back, but you aren’t the type to go out of your way just to say hello, right?」

At Pamidor’s words, Rei gave a small shrug and pulled the magic sword out from the Misty Ring.

Well, since it was broken in half along the blade, it was more accurate to say it was two pieces of a former magic sword.

In any case, Rei pulled the magic sword out and handed it to Pamidor.

「Hey, this is…quite the piece of work, isn’t it?」

「I suppose so. I know at least that much. It was used by an S rank adventurer, so it’s not just any ordinary weapon.」

「S rank!? From where?」

「The Bestir Empire.」

Hearing Rei’s brief reply, a single name immediately came to Pamidor’s mind.

「Noiz, the Immovable, huh.」

「Yeah. I had a bit of business in the Bestir Empire, and we ended up fighting.」

「…And his magic sword was broken, which means…you won?」

「No, more like he let me go.」

「Heh. So even you couldn’t do much against an S rank opponent.」

「I managed to put up some resistance, at least. But if he hadn’t retreated…」

He probably would have lost.

Pamidor inwardly felt a sense of admiration as Rei swallowed the rest of his sentence.

Rei was definitely strong. He was strong to the point where an ordinary adventurer couldn’t do a thing against him.

Pamidor himself was nothing more than a blacksmith, but as a highly skilled one, he understood just how strong Rei was.

He had also heard about, although he hadn’t directly seen, Rei’s strength when he clashed with the Azoth Firm.

Pamidor understood that it was difficult for someone with that much strength to admit they were weaker than someone else.

「Even so, you managed to break the Immovable’s magic sword. That alone feels like a minor feat to me.」

He stared intently at the pieces of the magic sword in his hand.

Looking at the blade, broken cleanly in two, he could understand the sheer destructive power behind the blow that had caused it.

「I’ll say this first…I’m just a blacksmith. If we’re going to reforge a magic sword, we’ll need the help of an alchemist or a mage well-versed in this sort of thing. What do you want to do? Will you leave it with me for now? Once I finish my current work, I’m planning to head over to an alchemist’s place.」

「Ah…right. To be honest, I kind of want to tag along, but I’m planning to head to the dungeon soon.」

While replying to Pamidor, Rei also felt a certain appeal in meeting an alchemist.

Because Gilm was a frontier city, it attracted many alchemists seeking rare materials.

Of course, their level was probably lower compared to the Bestir Empire, which poured national resources into alchemy, or Ozos, known as the Magic City.

Even so, Rei wanted to meet a proper alchemist.

…As far as improper alchemists went, he had encountered one during the incident with the Azoth Firm a while ago.

「Hmm, I won’t force you. In that case, I’ll take care of it on this end, so drop by tomorrow or whenever you’re free.」

「Understood. I’ll drop by when I get back from the dungeon then. I’m counting on you.」

Despite his villainous face, Pamidor was a man who valued duty and obligation.

Knowing that he was highly skilled, Rei had no reservations about leaving the magic sword to him.

However, the main reason was that the magic sword was just something he had picked up along the way.

If it were the Death Scythe…or even something he used regularly like the Thorns Spear, Dagger of Flowing Water, or Nebula’s Eye, he would definitely have gone to meet the alchemist together with Pamidor.

Furthermore, if it were something made by Esta Nord, like the Dragon Robe…he probably would have headed to the Imperial Capital back in the Bestir Empire or Ozos, assuming it couldn’t be fixed here.

Because he had only acquired Noiz’s magic sword by chance, Rei just thought that it would be nice if he could use it again.

「Yeah, leave it to me. A magic sword used by an S rank adventurer sounds like it’ll be a good job for me too.」

Receiving Pamidor’s words at his back, Rei stepped outside.

「Guru~?」

Seeing Rei come out of the shop, Set approached with a cry, as if asking how it went.

Rei patted Set’s head and prompted him to get going.

「It’s a long shot, but he said he’ll show it to an alchemist to see if anything can be done. Anyway, our business here is finished, so…let’s head to the dungeon. I don’t know if we’ll be able to clear it today, though.」

「Gurururu~!」

Set purred happily at Rei’s words.

He understood that he might not be able to enter the dungeon himself, but he seemed happy just to be able to fly alongside Rei.

Walking through the city with Set, they were naturally called out to by various people, but they eventually reached the gate.

「Hey, Rei. You too, Set. Heading out of the city?」

The guard who had handled Rei’s paperwork when he returned to Gilm called out to him.

The peak time for people passing through the gate had already passed, so he was probably quite free right now.

In fact, while it wasn’t completely empty, there were only a few people undergoing the procedures to leave the gate.

「I’m heading to that dungeon I heard about the other day.」

Wow. The guard frowned as he expressed his thoughts.

「You really have some strange tastes. Didn’t I tell you what kind of place it was?」

「Yeah, and I gathered a lot of other information too. But even so, I want to check it out at least once.」

「…Well, you’re a high rank adventurer with a title, so I doubt anything I say will be of any use…but be careful. Actually, it’s that dungeon, so maybe there isn’t even a need to be careful.」

「That’s not necessarily true. A dungeon is a place where you never know what might happen.」

Rei handed the guard his guild card, taken from his Misty Ring, along with the Necklace of Subservient Monster from Set’s neck, and asked him to process the paperwork.

Because there were so few people, the process was finished quickly.

「Well then, do your best.」

「It must be tough out here in the cold, but keep at it.」

Calling out to the guards braving the cold when it could snow at any moment, Rei left Gilm with Set.

Normally, he was asked to refrain from flying near the gates, but fortunately, there was hardly anyone around right now.

「Alright Set, let’s go.」

「Gurururururu~!」

Set gave a loud cry in response after Rei got on his back. After a few running steps, he flapped his wings and soared into the sky.

Rather than flying, it was more like he was running through the air.

The few guards near the gate could only stare in speechless distraction at the sight.

「Set, the dungeon is that way. Just fly straight.」

Set flapped his wings, heading in the direction Rei indicated.

With every flap, they covered a considerable distance.

By flapping continuously, their speed increased even further.

Normally, the sky at this time of year would be freezing cold and it wouldn’t be strange to be shivering instantly. But Rei had his Dragon Robe, and Set was a Griffon, so they weren’t bothered by the cold in the slightest.

Watching the scenery on the ground rapidly pass by, Rei was once again reminded of how amazing Set was.

When traveling on the ground, one generally followed the roads, but roads were rarely perfectly straight.

If there was a mountain, it would go around it. If there was a valley, it would go around it. If there was a river, it would go around until a section narrow enough to be crossed could be found.

It wasn’t an exaggeration to say the paths were winding.

But when Set flew, none of that mattered. He could just fly in a straight line.

And his speed was on a completely different level compared to traveling on the ground.

「Ah, Set. Turn right at that pile of stones on the road.」

「Gurururu~!」

Prompted by Rei, who had spotted the pile of stones serving as a marker to leave the road, Set gave a cry and changed directions.

As they flew straight away from the road, they eventually saw several tents pitched on the ground. It was their destination, the dungeon.

The tents were likely used by the soldiers stationed here.

Normally, it was a distance of a few hours by carriage, but they had arrived in about ten minutes after taking off from Gilm. This truly demonstrated the sheer speed of Set’s flight.

And that was even while enjoying a stroll through the sky, not even flying at full speed.

「Tents, huh. …Using tents at this time of year must be pretty brutal unless they’re magic tents.」

If it were a magic tent, they wouldn’t feel the cold outside air.

But ordinary tents didn’t have such functions, so naturally, they would still need to sleep in proper winter.

Some of the people tending a campfire near the tents noticed something…or someone approaching from the sky.

The soldiers reflexively reached for their bows, but upon realising it was a Griffon flying towards them, they immediately lowered them.

…However, the fact that they didn’t place their bows on the ground meant they were ready to intercept immediately if the approaching Griffon wasn’t the Set they knew.

Though, if it really were a Griffon other than Set approaching, the bows and arrows the soldiers had wouldn’t be of any use…in fact, it would probably only serve to anger it.

Seeing Rei riding on the back of Set as he landed on the ground, the soldiers finally lowered their guard.

Rei dismounted and called out to the soldiers.

「I’m an adventurer, Rei. I’m here to clear the dungeon…」

「Is that you, Rei!?」

Before he could finish his sentence, a voice called out.

Turning his gaze towards the sound, Rei saw a middle-aged man with a stern, bearded face.

It was Ranga, the captain of Gilm’s guards. Currently, he was stationed here, leading the soldiers in keeping watch for any monsters emerging from the dungeon.

He must have been on a break, as he had just stepped out of a tent. Rei smiled as he spoke to him.

「It’s been a while.」

「Guru~!」

As if echoing Rei’s words, Set also gave a cry.

Perhaps finding the interaction amusing, Ranga smiled and raised a hand slightly.

「It really has been a while. From what you just said, are you here to clear the dungeon?」

Rei nodded in response to Ranga’s question.

「I heard it was a small dungeon, so I felt like trying my hand at it. If I can clear it today, great. If not, I still want to experience what kind of place it is. Is entry restricted or anything?」

He had heard that adventurers were normally allowed to enter dungeons, but Rei asked just to be safe.

At Rei’s words, Ranga nodded as if it were obvious.

「Of course not. But I hear this dungeon doesn’t offer much in the way of rewards…if you’re fine with that, that is.」

「I already heard about that while gathering information, so it’s not a problem. Well then, without further ado… Ah, I’ll be having Set wait outside, is that alright?」

「Hm? Ah, I see. With the entrance to that dungeon, it would be impossible for Set to get inside. Yeah, I don’t mind. However, monsters do occasionally come out of the dungeon, so when that happens…」

Understanding what Ranga wanted to say, Rei gave a small nod.

「If monsters come out, I’ll have Set fight them too. Even if I don’t say anything, he knows what to do.」

「Gururu~!」

As Set purred as if to say ‘Leave it to me!’, not only Ranga but the other soldiers breathed sighs of relief as well.

Since they lived in Gilm, they naturally all knew about Set.

That was why they were relieved, knowing they wouldn’t have to be busy dealing with the things that would come outside for a while.

The monsters that came out of the dungeon weren’t very strong. No, they were clearly weak, but there was no telling when they would appear… Furthermore, since this was the frontier, the monsters attacking from the surrounding area were actually much more formidable than those coming out of the dungeon.

They understood that with Set around, they wouldn’t have to worry about those monsters either.

+++

# **864**

「So this is the entrance to the dungeon.」

「Guru~」

At Rei’s words, Set, who had accompanied him right up to the dungeon, gave a disappointed cry.

Set had agreed to wait outside while Rei went into the dungeon, but seeing the entrance up close like this, he couldn’t help but feel disappointed that he wouldn’t go inside together.

I’ll be lonely, Set seemed to say as he rubbed his head against Rei. While responding to Set’s affection, Rei looked at the dungeon entrance.

Huge rocks stood on either side, with another rock placed on top like a roof. Rather than an entrance, it was more accurate to call it a gap between rocks.

That gap was quite narrow, barely wide enough for Rei to slip through without any weapons equipped.

Even if Set used his Size Transformation skill, Rei was certain that it would be impossible for Set to fit, without even needing to try.

In fact, let alone Set, it would probably be difficult for even a tall adventurer to squeeze inside.

「This really is narrow…」

「Isn’t it? Well, thanks to that, the monsters that come out are only small, weak ones, and they only come out a little at a time.」

「In that case, is there really a need to wait in ambush here? If you just leave them be, they’ll probably just get killed by other monsters anyway.」

This was the frontier, a place where a wide variety of monsters roamed.

Especially at night, it wasn’t rare for high rank monsters to appear, so a few Goblins wouldn’t be a problem.

In response to Rei’s question, Ranga shook his head.

「It’s not that far from the highway. Not many people are using the highway at this time of year, but that doesn’t mean no one is using it. The monsters that come out of here might head that way, and since it’s a dungeon, you never know what might happen. Considering that, we can’t just leave it alone.」

「Dungeons grow, huh.」

「Exactly. Considering that possibility, we absolutely have to keep watch.」

As he spoke, Ranga directed an expectant gaze at Rei.

Precisely because he knew how much power Rei possessed, he was hoping Rei would clear this dungeon if possible.

Receiving that look, Rei nodded back.

「I can’t guarantee anything, but I’ll do what I can. Fortunately, I won’t have any trouble with food.」

His Misty Ring contained a massive amount of food.

…A large portion of which was the food Rei had bought from Gilm’s stalls over the last few days.

「I don’t know how long it will take, so if you get hungry, just hunt some monsters and eat them, okay?」

「Guru~!」

I’ll be fine! Set gave a cry. Rei gently patted his head and looked at Ranga.

「Well then, I’m heading in.」

「Be careful.」

After a brief exchange, Rei slipped through the gap in the rocks, which was barely wide enough for him to pass through…

「Gugya?」

As Rei entered the dungeon, he found himself face to face with a creature coming up the stairs from the underground.

More accurately, since the other party was coming up the stairs, it was a head or two below Rei.

The creature Rei had bumped into seemed completely taken by surprise as well. It tilted its head as if to say, What’s going on?

However, its face was ugly, and tilting its head didn’t evoke any of the adorable charm that Set possessed.

…Naturally, the creature before Rei was one of the most famous types of monsters, a Goblin.

「…Whoa!」

Rei hadn’t expected to bump into a Goblin right away either. He paused for a moment before letting out a surprised shout and reflexively swinging his fist.

The visceral sound of flesh being struck and bones breaking echoed out as the Goblin’s face caved in and it tumbled down the stairs.

Furthermore, there seemed to be a few more Goblins right behind the one Rei had just punched, and they all tumbled down the stairs leading underground together with the one that had been sent flying.

「Gyabububububu!」

「Gyoaaaa!」

「Gyayaaaaaa!」

While watching the Goblins disappear from sight with such cries, Rei suddenly heard a voice from behind.

「Rei, what happened?」

Ranga, likely having heard the Goblins’ screams, peeked his head through the gap in the rocks and asked.

Rei shook his head, telling him it was nothing.

「Right as I came in, some Goblins were just coming out. So I reflexively punched one, and they all fell down the stairs.」

「…You have my condolences.」

Ranga smiled wryly. Rei lightly shook the fist he had used to punch the Goblin and sighed.

「Well, I heard it was this kind of dungeon, so it can’t be helped. Alright, I’m going in for real this time.」

「Be careful.」

Receiving the same words from Ranga as before, Rei descended the stairs.

The stairs looked as if they had been carved from stone, created not by human hands but by the dungeon core when the dungeon was born.

(Dungeons really are amazing in various ways when you think about it. It makes sense that I could learn the Terrain Manipulation skill from one. …Though this dungeon core is going straight to Set.)

Rei reached the bottom of the stairs in less than a minute. He ignored the Goblins that had died from tumbling down the stairs and continued onward. Before him lay a stone corridor.

The stone itself emitted a faint glow, providing enough visibility. Though, in Rei’s case, he could see in the dark to some extent anyway.

However, the moment he saw the corridor, Rei frowned.

The corridor was barely wide enough for two people to walk side-by-side.

There was clearly no room to swing the Death Scythe. The most he could do was use the shaft like a spear.

But if he was going to do that, he might as well just use a spear meant for thrusting to begin with.

「The only effective weapons here are spears and daggers? …I guess a spear will do.」

He might have been able to swing a long sword, but Rei wasn’t particularly good with them anyway. Long reaching weapons like the Death Scythe or a spear suited him better.

He took out a spear he had looted from a bandit he had defeated on the way back to Gilm from the Imperial Capital.

It couldn’t be called a high-quality spear, but it was perfectly fine for killing Goblins.

Spear in hand, he took a step into the stone corridor…when a question suddenly crossed his mind.

「I heard an Ogre appeared before, right? …In this corridor?」

Even for someone with a petite build by Elgin’s standards, the corridor was only wide enough for two people to walk side-by-side. The ceiling was reasonably high at about three meters, but even so, it would be impossible for an Ogre to walk through a place like this.

「I should probably ask about that.」

Muttering to himself, he turned back the way he came with his spear in hand and climbed the stairs.

Poking his head through the gap in the rocks, he saw Ranga giving instructions to his subordinates.

「Guru.」

Seeing Rei, Set gave a happy cry and that sound alerted Ranga to Rei’s presence.

「Rei? Did something happen?」

「According to the information I gathered in Gilm, there are Ogres in the dungeon…but there’s no way an Ogre could move freely in that corridor, right? I was wondering if you knew anything about that.」

「Ah, the Ogres. There are some fairly spacious rooms inside the dungeon. The people who fought Ogres probably fought them there. Well, because Ogres are so big, they can’t leave those rooms anyway.」

「I see. That helps.」

After that brief exchange, Rei gave Set a small wave and re-entered the dungeon, descending the stairs once more.

He walked past the corpses of the few again Goblins as if they weren’t even there and stepped back into the stone-paved corridor.

The narrowness he had seen a few minutes ago hadn’t changed, and as he walked forward with a slight frown…

「Gigigigi?」

「Gyagyo.」

He heard those familiar voices once again.

Rei furrowed his brow, looking somewhat annoyed.

However, since there was only one path from the entrance to this point, there was no point in turning back now.

He continued forward, spear in hand.

Soon, familiar figures appeared in the dim light of the dungeon.

The owners of the voices he had just heard were, naturally, more Goblins. Two of them.

They were armed with a rusted dagger and a club made from a broken branch.

(Come to think of it, what did that Goblin from before have? Well, it’s just a Goblin’s weapon, so there’s no point in collecting it.)

While thinking that, he readied his spear and waited for the Goblins, who had spotted him and were charging at him with shrieks.

「Gyagagyaga!」

「Gyojojogyo!」

Goblins had small builds, even smaller than Rei.

In other words, they could fight in this corridor without any movement restrictions.

「…Well, that doesn’t mean a few Goblins gathering together makes any difference.」

Along with his mutters, two streaks of light flashed out.

With Rei’s physical abilities, two thrusts were unleashed in an instant, piercing the Goblins’ foreheads and blowing their heads apart.

The two Goblins took a few more steps forward with their remaining momentum before collapsing, scattering blood, brains, bones, and eyeballs across the stone floor from their missing heads.

Rei jumped back to avoid the mess. Not wanting to smell the foul stench any more than necessary, he used his Shoes of Sleipnir to walk through the air and jump over the Goblin corpses.

「If only an unknown monster would appear. Well, since this is a dungeon where Goblins are the main monsters, I can’t expect much in terms of magic stones, but still, maybe…」

He continued walking through the dungeon and eventually reached a T junction.

He hesitated for a few seconds about which way to go.

But while he was hesitating, he heard footsteps coming from the right. …And from the left as well.

Three Goblins appeared from the right. Two Goblins from the left.

A total of five Goblins had shown themselves, but…

「You’re in the way.」

The moment they noticed him and entered a combat stance, Rei was already right in front of them.

Once again, flashes of light streaked out.

A few seconds later, only Goblin corpses remained.

「I don’t care about Goblins, give me a monster I haven’t encountered yet.」

He used the Shoes of Sleipnir to walk over the Goblin corpses again and continued onward.

Normally, he would harvest proofs of subjugation and magic stones, but in the case of Goblins, both the proof of subjugation parts and the magic stones were worth basically nothing.

For Rei, it wasn’t worth the effort to harvest them.

Because of that, he just ignored them and walked past.

Even if he left them alone, Slimes, the dungeon’s cleaners, would eventually take care of them, so it wasn’t a problem.

For the time being, he turned right at the T junction and continued for about five minutes.

Before him appeared a door to the left, and a path continuing straight ahead and to the right.

「A door, huh. I’m certainly curious what’s inside, but what bothers me more is…」

His gaze was directed at the path continuing straight.

Acting on a hunch, Rei ignored the door and the path to the right and went straight.

Continuing onward, he turned left twice and eventually emerged at a spot with a path going straight and one branching to the right.

And on the stone floor lay the corpses of five Goblins.

They were clearly the Goblins Rei had defeated just a moment ago.

「So, I just walked a full circle around whatever room is in the centre. Quite spacious.」

Just to be safe, he used the Shoes of Sleipnir to jump over the Goblin corpses again and proceeded down the path he believed he had already taken.

Naturally, the door on the left and the path on the right appeared before him.

「Now then, what to do? A door might have traps. In that case, I’ll check this way first.」

Rei directed his gaze at the corridor continuing to the right.

Keeping his spear ready to use at any moment, he ignored the door and proceeded down the right corridor.

He walked straight ahead for about ten minutes.

Eventually, he emerged into an area spacious enough to be called a large hall.

And standing there was an Ogre, possessing a massive frame that was incomparable to a Goblin.

However, upon seeing it, Rei couldn’t help but frown.

The reason was that Ogres he had seen before were about five meters tall, whereas the one currently in his line of sight was only about three meters tall.

Of course, it was still massive, and to Rei, it was nearly twice his height.

He had to look up to see its face, but compared to the Ogres he had encountered in the dungeon with the Altar of Inheritance, he could only say it lacked presence.

「Is it a younger Ogre? Or maybe there are only weak Ogres because this dungeon was only recently formed?」

Perhaps hearing Rei’s mutter, the Ogre gripped its club and roared, though it likely didn’t understand the meaning of his words.

「Gaaaaaaaaahhhh!」

However, even its roar felt severely lacking in presence to Rei.

+++

# **865**

「…Is that really all there is?」

Rei muttered as he looked at the Ogre’s corpse lying on the stone floor.

The Ogre blood dripped from the tip of the spear in his hand to the floor

There was a wound on the Ogre’s forehead where the spear had pierced through, causing a strong metallic scent to spread into the surroundings.

An Ogre, as Rei knew it, should have been able to shrug off at least some wounds rather than dying from a single blow.

「Is this really an Ogre? Or maybe I’ve just gotten that much stronger since then?」

Rei murmured to himself before shaking his head.

It was true that he felt he had become stronger since he had gone into the dungeon with Elena’s group.

But even so, looking at the way this Ogre died, it felt like the problem lay somewhere else entirely.

「In the first place, is this really an Ogre?」

The Ogre he had fought before was about five meters tall, yet the corpse before him was only about three meters in height.

That was a difference of two meters, and its strength certainly didn’t seem befitting of a C rank monster.

Rei tilted his head in confusion, but then he remembered hearing that the materials from the monsters in this dungeon were of poor quality. If so, maybe this was the reason? He pondered over it.

「Actually, considering the Goblin’s head exploded while this Ogre’s head is intact, it must be fairly strong for this dungeon, but…」

It was still too weak, as he sighed.

「I wanted you to put up enough of a fight to at least make me use the Fire Emperor’s Crimson Armour.」

Although he complained, Rei knew that standing around wouldn’t change anything, so he touched the Ogre’s corpse and stored it into the Misty Ring.

「I got a skill from the Ogre’s magic stone last time…but is this one really going to work?」

He tilted his head again as he looked around.

It was a spacious area with nothing in particular inside.

There were no treasure chests, and naturally, there were no stairs leading further down.

「…How did that Ogre even get here?」

It was much smaller than the Ogre Rei had seen before, but it was still about three meters tall.

It would have been impossible for it to pass through the corridor Rei had just come from…well, maybe not impossible, but definitely extremely difficult.

「If it didn’t just appear here directly…did it force its way through that narrow corridor? Well, it probably isn’t impossible, but still.」

The image of an Ogre squeezing through the corridor by turning sideways or crouching down crossed his mind and he couldn’t help but give a wry smile at the strange thought.

However, that would explain how the Ogre had ended up in this room.

「It somehow managed to squeeze through the narrow corridor, finally making it to this room. But because it didn’t want to go back into the narrow corridor, it just stayed here…is that it? Although it’s also possible it just spawned here directly.」

Having convinced himself of that, he examined his current surroundings once more.

However, once the Ogre’s corpse was stored away, the only things left in the room were the bloodstains and a club.

「I’m not asking for a treasure chest, but I would have at least liked some stairs. …If there aren’t any stairs here, they must be in the other room. …I guess I’ll take this at least.」

Picking up the club the Ogre had been holding, Rei stored it into the Misty Ring.

It seemed like it had been made by breaking off a tree branch and it hadn’t even been shaped properly.

The only thing that had been done was to trim off the other branches that would have gotten in the way of swinging it. It was a weapon more accurately described as a large branch rather than a club.

Even so, Rei decided it could at least be used as firewood.

「Did I miss anything…nope.」

He gave the spacious room one last glance before leaving.

「For a newly formed dungeon…it feels both narrow and wide.」

Of course, compared to the dungeons Rei had explored before, the one with the Altar of Inheritance, let alone the one in Exil, this dungeon was incredibly small.

In that sense, it was narrow, but the fact that it already had this much space despite being newly formed was already surprising enough.

It wasn’t much of a threat right now, but if it continued to grow, it might not be that long before it would start causing damage to Gilm.

As he walked straight down the path with such thoughts in mind…he heard the cries of Goblins once again.

「Again? There really are a lot of Goblins. They’re weak, but their numbers make them extremely annoying.」

He sighed, readied his spear, and dashed forward to close the distance to the Goblins walking down the corridor ahead.

He couldn’t help but feel that this was nothing short of bullying the weak.

「Gururururu!」

Along with Set’s cry, his Fire Breath covered the three Goblins that had emerged from the rocks leading to the dungeon.

He then swung his front claws at the Goblins, who were thrashing about and rolling on the ground after being set alight.

There was no way a mere Goblin could withstand a blow from a Griffon…especially one empowered by the Bracelet of Herculean Strength. Their lives were snuffed out instantly.

Seeing that, Set gave a satisfied cry before heading back to the spot he had been lying in earlier…

「Wait, hold on a second!」

Ranga, who had been watching the scene, shouted with his eyes wide open.

In fact, it was impressive that Ranga was able to act so quickly after seeing what just happened.

The other soldiers were all frozen, unable to comprehend what they had just seen.

「Guru~?」

What is it? Set gave a questioning cry.

The round eyes he directed at Ranga were so pure and innocent it was hard to believe he had effortlessly slaughtered three Goblins just a few seconds ago.

Are you going to play with me? Or maybe give me food like usual? Receiving a gaze filled with such expectations, Ranga likely realised that voicing his current questions to Set would yield no answers.

He sighed and scratched his head.

「I guess I have no choice but to wait until Rei gets back.」

「R-Right. …Even so, to think Set can use Fire Breath…」

One of the soldiers, finally recovering, muttered as if he couldn’t believe what he had just seen.

When Rei returned to Gilm, Ranga had already been stationed at this dungeon.

Because of that, the explanation Rei had given Daska, that Set was a Griffon rare species, hadn’t reached them yet.

「Normally, wouldn’t that make him either a higher ranking species or a rare species?」

「No, but he’s a Griffon, you know? Actually, he’s Set, right?」

「…To me, the fact that it’s Set makes it easier to accept he’s a rare species. I can’t imagine a normal Griffon, even a tamed one, understanding human words that well.」

「Is it definitely a rare species? Not a higher ranking species?」

「I’ve never heard of a higher ranking species of Griffon.」

「Well, a rare species is pretty similar then. In the first place, our senses have been numbed by Set, you normally don’t just get to see a Griffon so easily.」

Listening to the soldiers talking behind him, Ranga gently reached out his hand towards Set, who was looking at him with expectant eyes.

「Gurururu~」

Set stretched his head out towards the approaching hand.

Pet me, pet me, Set seemed to say. Or perhaps, praise me, praise me. In response to those demands, Ranga met his expectations.

Perhaps enjoying being petted, Set gave a happy cry.

「Set is just Set, huh.」

As Ranga muttered while watching Set, the other soldiers nodded in agreement.

At the very least, the Set currently being petted by Ranga was undeniably the Set they all knew.

Ranga truly felt from the bottom of his heart that even if Set was a rare species, there was no need to fear him.

The other soldiers watching Set act so affectionately towards Ranga felt the exact same way.

「He’s so cute…」

「Yeah.」

「I’m so jealous of Rei…」

「Yeah.」

「I want to be a tamer too…」

「Yeah.」

Amidst that conversation, one of the soldiers suddenly spoke up as if realising something.

「Wait a minute. Set is a Griffon, which is an A rank monster. And rare species are generally treated as being one rank higher than their base species, right? Doesn’t that mean Set is an S rank monster?」

「Whoa, that’s amazing. I’ve never seen an S rank monster before.」

「So he’s on the same level as a Dragon?」

「…Wow…I don’t even know what to say besides wow…」

Despite expressing their surprise in words, no one was actually afraid of Set.

They knew what kind of existence Set was, he had lived in Gilm up until now. The fact that they had just convinced themselves that Set was just Set played a big part as well.

Everyone was smiling affectionately at Set despite their surprise.

It was the ultimate proof that everyday behaviour truly mattered.

「H-Hey, Set. Can you do anything else besides Fire Breath? If you can, show us!」

Asked by one of the soldiers, Set turned his head towards an empty space away from the tents.

「Gururu~!」

With that cry, two water balls, each about 40 cm in diameter, appeared around Set.

The two water spheres chased each other, crossed paths, and moved around as if dancing in the air.

The soldiers, including Ranga, were captivated by the sight…and the next moment, the water spheres crashed into each other, spilling water onto the ground.

「Awesome!」

「…Wow, that’s amazing.」

「I never thought I’d see something like this out here.」

While some voiced their admiration, others expressed surprise for a completely different reason.

「Water Ball on top of Fire Breath? Aren’t those opposing elements?」

「And two water balls at the same time. …Just how strong is he?」

「At the very least, Goblins won’t stand a chance.」

Set, who could freely use skills of conflicting elements like fire and water, was an unbelievable existence to the soldiers.

But that wasn’t all.

「Gurururururu~!」

Facing the rock at the dungeon entrance, Set exhaled his Crystal Breath.

The soldiers, who had expected him to use Fire Breath again, stared at the dungeon entrance, unable to understand what was happening… More accurately, they saw a single Goblin that had emerged from the entrance become coated in crystal.

However, since Set’s Crystal Breath was low level, it only formed a thin layer of crystal over the Goblin’s body.

If it were just that, even a Goblin could have slowly chipped away the crystal on its surface…

「Gururu!」

As soon as Set finished using Crystal Breath, he leaped forward, attacking the Goblin in a flash.

With a single swing of his front paw, the crystal clinging to the Goblin’s body shattered, and the Goblin’s body was pulverized along with it.

Normally, Set’s strike would have looked nothing short of a brutal attack, but the shattering crystal caught the sunlight, turning it into a somewhat fantastical sight.

Of course, that was only on the surface.

After the Goblin’s body was destroyed and Set landed on the ground, the intense smell of blood and the foul stench of internal organs filled the air.

「Gururururu.」

Perhaps finding the smell unpleasant, Set exhaled Fire Breath once more, completely incinerating the remains of the Goblin scattered on the ground.

The smell of blood from a few seconds ago was replaced by the smell of burning flesh.

While that smell was still unpleasant, the soldiers felt it was much better than the stench of Goblin blood and guts.

A few seconds passed. One of the soldiers finally came back to his senses and approached to check the charred remains of the Goblin.

「…Wow…wait, what’s this? This is…」

The soldier, who had been exclaiming over the burnt remains of the Goblin, noticed a piece of crystal lying nearby.

「I see. This was from earlier…Captain Ranga, what should we do with this? It feels like a waste to just leave it here.」

Ranga hesitated for a moment when the soldier asked while holding the crystal fragment he picked up from the ground, but he quickly answered.

「You’re right, it might be a bad idea for us to dispose of these crystal fragments ourselves. Let’s collect them for now and ask Rei what he wants to do with them when he gets back from the dungeon.」

「Aww…what a waste.」

A different soldier, not the one who picked up the crystal, complained regretfully.

「No, seriously… how can you say that after watching that scene? That’s a crystal covered in Goblin meat and blood, you know? Even if I was told I could have it, I think I’d pass.」

「Huh? What are you talking about? A crystal is a crystal. Even if you say it was covered in Goblin meat and blood, the person you sell it to won’t know that, right? Still, Set’s attack just now is incredibly convenient. A rare species that can use multiple skills, huh.」

「Hey, hey, don’t get any weird ideas, okay? If you antagonise Rei, you’ll end up just like Azoth Firm.」

Just to be safe, one of the guards warned the soldier who had called the crystal a waste, and the soldier nodded as if it were obvious.

He had absolutely no intention of doing something as foolish as making an enemy of Rei just to earn some pocket change.
