# **866**

「Whoops! I should have seen that coming!」

Another room on the first floor of the dungeon.

Sensing a presence inside the room, Rei prodded the door with the shaft of his spear. But, as nothing happened, he judged there were unlikely to be any traps and decided to enter. The moment he did, he felt a presence attacking from above.

Reacting to the unexpected attack, Rei dashed forward to dodge the attacker dropping down.

As if waiting for that moment, two small, dog faced monsters lying in ambush ahead thrust out their spears.

Rei twisted his body to dodge the spears thrust towards him, closing the distance and swinging his own spear horizontally in an arc at the same time.

Through the spear, he felt the sensation of striking flesh and crushing bone. This was followed by the sound of wooden spear shaft snapping.

Clicking his tongue at the sensation, he turned his gaze to the left.

The monster Rei had struck had been on his right.

Since there were two monsters, the one on the left was naturally still there.

However, perhaps because Rei’s forward movement was faster than expected, the other monster had completely lost sight of Rei.

The broken spearhead spun through the air, flying off in a random direction, but Rei completely ignored it as he thrust the remains of his spear shaft towards the head of the monster that was still there.

The shaft of Rei’s spear was made of wood and the break had created a naturally jagged tip

That pointed edge pierced the monster’s head…specifically, its eye. Driven by Rei’s strength, the remains of the spear easily pierced into the monster’s brain, destroying it.

「Gyan!」

With the remains of the spear shaft still sticking out of its eye, the monster let out a short scream before being knocked back. It rolled on the ground and twitched a few times while letting out a faint whimper before dying.

Without even taking the time to watch it die, Rei pivoted on one foot. With his now empty right hand, he reached inside his Dragon Robe and activated the magic item equipped at his waist, Nebula’s Eye.

He flicked the arrowhead that was created in his right hand with his fingers, sending it flying.

「Gyan!」

A scream echoed from behind Rei.

Even so, the arrowhead created by Nebula’s Eye wasn’t enough to finish it off. The monster readied the spear in its hand while clutching its face and screaming.

At this point, Rei was finally able to observe the monster properly and he frowned slightly.

It was only natural. Standing before him was a small monster with the face of a dog. Its height was about the same as a Goblin, or perhaps slightly taller.

Rei naturally knew the name of the monster.

Although this was only his second time encountering it, it was a monster as famous as the Goblin.

The E rank monster, Kobold.

That was the name of the monster in Rei’s line of sight.

In terms of pure physical ability, it was only slightly better than a Goblin, but it was smarter than a Goblin and would attack in a coordinated manner like the three that had just attacked him.

They were also dextrous, capable of wielding weapons more proficiently than Goblins.

「Well, it’s still just an E rank monster in the end, though.」

He pulled the Death Scythe out from the Misty Ring and swung it in a horizontal strike.

His attack was so sharp that it took a few seconds after the swing before the Kobold’s torso finally split into two.

「Their materials and proof of subjugation parts fetch a higher price than a Goblin’s, but…even considering that, compared to the effort of dismantling them, it’s not really worth it. If only they were higher rank monsters, I could at least use their meat to feed Set.」

In the end, he didn’t store the Kobolds into the Misty Ring, leaving their corpses exactly where they lay.

Just like the Goblins, if he left them here, the Slimes would eventually take care of them.

He gave the Death Scythe a single swing to flick off the blood before storing it back into Misty Ring and taking out a spear similar to the one he had just broken.

The reason he didn’t use the Kobold’s spear was probably because it was of even worse quality.

It might have been fine to throw and use as a disposable weapon, but it was clearly unsuited to be used as a normal spear.

Ultimately, he decided that the Kobold’s spear could at least be used for throwing and stored it in his Misty Ring.

Having taken a moment to pause, Rei looked around the room.

「So, the stairs are…ah, there they are.」

Alone in the centre of the room were the stairs leading to the next floor.

Other than that, there was nothing in particular, it was just an empty room.

Well, aside from the corpses of three Kobolds lying on the ground.

「It would have been nice if Ogres or something were here instead. …Wait, maybe it left this room because it was empty?」

While feeling somewhat doubtful, Rei headed towards the stairs…

「Gyagya.」

「Gyogyogyaa!」

Hearing those voices coming from the bottom of the stairs, he frowned in displeasure.

「Again? Seriously, there are way too many Goblins coming out.」

He sighed, wondering how many Goblins he had encountered today. Readying his spear, he dashed forward to launch a surprise attack on the Goblins who hadn’t spotted him yet.

Rei rapidly closed the distance to the Goblins.

However, the two Goblins at the front showed no signs of noticing Rei’s approach as they peered up the stairs.

(There are probably more of them down there.)

Thinking that it was going to be slightly troublesome, he thrust his spear forward sharply, piercing the head of one Goblin. Before that Goblin had even collapsed onto the stone floor, he pulled the spear back and thrust again, piercing the head of the second Goblin.

Two Goblins were killed in an instant, but a third Goblin who hadn’t noticed what happened poked its head out from the stairs, just as Rei expected… The next moment, Rei’s spear shot out again, piercing its head and killing it just like the two before.

He waited just in case, but there was no sign of a fourth or fifth Goblin showing up.

「Well, I guess that’s it.」

He watched the headless Goblin corpses slide down the stairs and looked around the room one last time, just to be sure.

Confirming that there were only Goblin and Kobold corpses and absolutely nothing else of value, he went down the stairs.

「If I remember correctly, the second floor is supposed to be like a cave?」

Muttering to himself as he descended the stairs, he stepped over the Goblin corpses and exited the small room at the bottom of the stairs. Before him was a cave like environment, exactly as he had been told.

Unlike the stone pavement of the first floor, the ground was made of dirt, and small rocks were scattered everywhere.

Stalactites resembling faintly glowing icicles hung from the ceiling, illuminating what would normally be a dark corridor just enough that visibility wasn’t an issue.

However, the width of the corridor was barely different from the first floor, leaving very little space for combat, just like the information Rei had gathered in Gilm suggested.

「It really is a nasty corridor in various ways. If a party challenged this, the number of people who could actually fight would be very small. Well, it might be fine if they brought a lot of archers. …But in that case, they’d end up operating at a loss.」

The monsters that appeared were basically only low rank monsters.

Even the Ogre Rei had fought was clearly weaker than the one he had fought before.

If so, it would be difficult to even recover the cost of the arrows consumed in battle.

If they were lucky, they might be able to retrieve the arrows, but the chances were low; they could hit a rock and break, the arrowheads could chip, or they could become useless from monster bodily fluids.

「Thinking about it that way, my Nebula’s Eye seems pretty convenient since it can mass-produce arrowheads, which is the most expensive part of an arrow. …Well, they disappear pretty quickly, though.」

He continued down the path, thinking about the difficulties of using the magic item on his waist.

If he were an archer, maybe the unmodified Nebula’s Eye would have been an incredibly useful item.

…It was a strange thing to be realising now, but from the very beginning, Rei had no intention of using a bow as a weapon.

If he was going to attack with a bow, he might as well just throw the spears stored in his Misty Ring.

That was the thought process behind it.

「A bow, huh. In my case, I have the Misty Ring, so even if I used one, I probably wouldn’t have any trouble with the number of arrows. …Whether they would hit or not is another story.」

Given his physical abilities, and the fact that his five senses and even his sixth sense were extremely sharp, he thought he might actually have a high aptitude for bows…but once the Death Scythe appeared through the Magic Beast Art, not using it was never an option.

「Whoops, I was too distracted thinking about things.」

Hearing a monster’s cry from down the single path, Rei understood an enemy was approaching and readied his spear so he could attack at any moment… At that moment, he realised there wasn’t really a reason to wait for the monster to get close before he attacked.

(Well, I was just thinking about throwing spears, so it’s only natural I’d realise it now.)

Muttering to himself, he leaned the spear he was holding against the wall and took out the poor quality spear he had just taken from the Kobold earlier.

(I didn’t expect the spear I took from the Kobold to get its turn so quickly.)

Since it was literally disposable and he didn’t care if it broke, Rei readied the spear…and directed a sharp gaze down the corridor.

No matter how much illumination stalactites on the ceiling provided, it still couldn’t be as bright as daytime.

Since that was the case, pinpointing the enemy’s location based on sensing their presence was more reliable than relying on sight.

The voice drawing closer was clearly a monster’s cry. The moment he was certain it wasn’t an adventurer, he took a few running steps before throwing the spear, adding the force of twisting his body into the throw.

The spear flew through the air, tearing through the wind as it flew straight ahead…

「Bumoh!」

That scream reached Rei’s ears.

「Judging from that presence and cry, it’s not a Goblin. This is…heh.」

Recognising the monster, Rei’s mouth formed a smile. He grabbed the spear leaning against the wall before dashing foward.

Unlike the stone pavement of the first floor, the dirt ground of the second floor, with rocks scattered around, didn’t allow Rei to fully utilize his leg strength.

But even so, it was an overwhelming speed compared to how fast ordinary adventurers could move at. In the blink of an eye, the figure of a monster with the head of a pig crouching on the ground came into view.

It was a D rank monster, by no means a high rank monster, but for a D rank monster, its meat was quite delicious.

Rei still had a fair amount of the meat obtained from the previous raid on the Orc settlement stored in his Misty Ring.

It was a meat that both Rei and Set liked, and because of that, he had been hoping to restock if possible… However, despite having its abdomen pierced by the spear Rei threw, the Orc in his path was still trying to stand up.

In addition, there was a second Orc next to it, just staring at its companion, seemingly unable to comprehend what had happened.

It was in such a daze that it still didn’t come to its senses even when it heard Rei’s approaching footsteps.

Rei’s thrust aimed at the throat of the Orc he had already injured with his spear throw, destroying its neck. Only when its head rolled onto the ground did the remaining Orc finally realise it was under attack and raised the club in its hand towards Rei.

But there was no way Rei would wait around leisurely for that. Before the club could swing down, his spear shot out swiftly.

Three times, almost simultaneously.

The thrusts instantly pierced the Orc’s belly.

Although the Orc’s body was protected by thick fat and muscle, it apparently couldn’t completely kill the momentum of the spear thrusts powered by Rei’s strength and collapsed to the ground.

Its limbs were still twitching slightly, proof that the Orc wasn’t completely dead yet.

Blood flowed from the spots pierced by the spear, staining the dirt ground.

Watching this, Rei readied the spear in his hand…and delivered a final blow to its head, snuffing out the Orc’s life.

「Are the Orcs weaker than the ones I fought before too…?」

Rei muttered while looking at the corpses of the two Orcs.

Though, that might just be because he was currently stronger than when he had previously fought Orcs.

But what Rei was actually worried about wasn’t the Orc’s strength, but the quality of the Orc’s meat.

Since he had gone through the trouble of restocking his Orc meat, it was only natural to hope that, regardless of their strength, the taste of the meat hadn’t changed.

He stored the Orc corpses lying on the ground and their weapons into his Misty Ring before continuing to walk.

Rei proceeded down the only pathway.

Continuing straight ahead, he eventually arrived at a junction where the path split left and right.

Unlike the first floor, it wasn’t a T junction, but a Y junction.

「Now then, which way should I go…」

On the first floor, the corridors had ended up circling the room with the stairs leading to the second floor, but he wondered if this Y-junction would lead to the same result.

With that thought in mind, Rei followed his intuition and stepped onto the path leading to the right.

++++

## **Blessing From the Goddess and Transfer to Another World – Chapter 125: The Silver Knight and the Golden Dragon**

**AN:** Regarding the attacks of the Progenitor Divine Dragon and the Demon God, I am making downward adjustments to their effects.

Specifically, for El, the size of her death-throes strike will be reduced from 1 km to 100 m. For the Demon God, “Absolute Zero” will be adjusted from 1 km to 500 m, and from -200°C to -100°C.

The reason is that while writing the Yellow Dragon battle, I reread things and thought, “Aren’t these attacks way too strong?” To put it more bluntly, they ended up looking even more impressive than the Yellow Dragon.

As for El, I went overboard just because it was the first final trial.

El: “Cutting it down to one-tenth is way too cruel!”

---

After finishing preparations for the Yellow Dragon battle, we arrived at the central region of the Brown Wall Kingdom, or more simply put, right in the middle of the desert.

Even though it is called the middle of the desert, only the surface is sand. Dig just a little, and nutrient-rich soil appears.

This area was originally where the “Spirit World” existed, and it has been most strongly affected by Rain’s terraforming.

It is expected that one day it will become lush green land and, in both name and reality, the central city of the Brown Wall Kingdom. Since the land rights belong to the Advance Trading Company, it will surely generate outrageous profits.

At present, it is the most open space farthest from human settlements, so there could be no better location to fight the Yellow Dragon in the sky. Calling it a “location” even though it’s in midair feels odd, but still.

Incidentally, the Yellow Dragon will be passing directly above this spot as well.

“In case something goes wrong, Rain, can I count on you?”

The Great Spirit Rain nodded vigorously and struck a pose like flexing her muscles.

As always, everything was conveyed through expression and gesture alone.

I have asked Rain to protect the ground just in case. If a Yellow Dragon measuring 1 km in length and weighing 500 tons were to crash into the ground, it would be catastrophic.

Now that Rain has become the Spirit Queen and stands in a position that governs the spirits, it seems that if she truly exerts herself, she can suppress even that level of damage.

A dragonkin unit to collect falling debris, Sera to erase magic, and Rain to prevent the Yellow Dragon from falling.

With all that in place, unnecessary damage should be minimized.

“Well then, I guess it’s time to go.”

“Jin-kun… please be careful…”

《Do your best!》

“Leave the ground to me.”

“Then call us later!”

Seeing me off, Sakura, Dora, Sera, and Mio watched as Maria and I mounted the Sky Dragon.

“Blue, can you go?”

“Of course! Anytime!”

“Then let’s go!”

“Yeah!”

At my signal, Blue beat her wings powerfully and soared straight into the azure sky.

She must have been really fired up, because she ascended at an incredible speed.

Blue’s Unique Skill, \<Heaven and Earth Unbound>, is a special skill that allows her to ignore the effects of gravity while flying.

It works even in normal flight, but its ability really shines during ascent.

Because she can move vertically with the same effort as horizontal movement.

In less than ten minutes, we had passed through two areas.

To put it more clearly, if the ground surface is Area 1, then we moved upward two areas and reached Area 3.

We should soon arrive near the stratosphere where the Yellow Dragon is, namely Area 4.

A: The Yellow Dragon is approaching, Master.

A report came in from Alta.

Huh? Since it’s heading toward its patrol route, that’s only natural, isn’t it?

A: No. It is heading straight toward Master’s current location, that is, toward a lower area off its patrol route. Additionally, its movement speed has clearly increased compared to before.

So it has left its patrol route and is coming straight for us.

What on earth is going on?

There was no point in stopping to worry, so I had Blue continue toward Area 4, though I asked her to slow down a bit.

Before long, the Yellow Dragon came into view.

The Yellow Dragon was exactly what one imagines a dragon to be, its entire body yellow… no, more like dazzling gold.

Since I was wearing silver-based knight armor, the contrast would make for an incredible visual.

The title is settled: “The Silver Knight and the Golden Dragon.”

…The only regret is that “golden dragon” is already a deduction-worthy cliché.

That aside, it is huge.

At 1 km long, it is longer than two bullet trains lined up end to end.

The sight of such a dragon advancing while writhing its colossal body is truly awe-inspiring.

…Oh, and as expected, it’s holding a jeweled orb in its hand. I’ll take that later.

Now that I’ve seen it with my own eyes, it’s about time to recheck its status.

Name: Yellow Dragon

LV 1000

Gender: None

Age: Unmeasurable

Race: Dragon God

Skills:

Physical System

\<Complete Resistance LV >

Other

\<All Things LV >

Notes: A god that rules the sky. One of the final trials imposed upon humanity.

\<All Things>

An integrated skill that governs skills befitting a Dragon God.

Yeah, I’m not going to comment on the level, gender, age, or notes at this point.

It’s a being that wouldn’t be strange even if it had lived since the primordial era, after all.

That said, this is really sloppy…

To have no individual skills other than \<Complete Resistance LV > and wrap everything up with a single integrated skill is just too lazy.

The skill name sounds grand, but it explains nothing.

A skill whose effects can’t be inferred at all from its name is lazy design.

If you look into \<All Things>, you can see what kinds of skills are integrated into it.

In addition, it seems to have unique effects exclusive to \<All Things> as well. They’re quite powerful, but unfortunately, none of them seem like a threat to me.

Its status is overwhelmingly weaker than Orihara’s, and if we fight, I could probably win with room to spare.

After that, if it can converse, we talk. If it’s a good guy, it goes home. If not, we subjugate it.

It’s coming straight toward us anyway.

Oh, right. It’s about time to call Mio.

It would be too late once the battle with the Yellow Dragon starts.

《Mio, I’m about to use ‘Summon’. Are you ready?》

《Okay! I’ve already set \<Environmental Adaptation>!》

I had Blue stop for a moment, and during that opening, I “Summoned” Mio.

“Master, sorry to keep you waiting. So that’s the Yellow Dragon… wow, the presence and stats are amazing.”

Mio stared at the Yellow Dragon in amazement.

Since I had called Mio, I went ahead and explained what would happen next.

“First, I’ll use \<Skystride> and handle the Yellow Dragon myself. Maria and Mio, stay on Blue and keep your distance. Depending on how it responds, we’ll decide whether to fight or let it go home.”

I have three ways to move in the air.

The first is my mount, Blue.

The second is the magic item “Wings of the Undead.”

The third is the former Blessing Unique Skill \<Skystride>.

Blue will be carrying Maria and Mio, so she’s out.

“Wings of the Undead” is a black cloak, which doesn’t match my knight armor, so that’s out.

By elimination, my only aerial movement option is \<Skystride>.

I instructed Blue, carrying the two of them, to move away, and I used \<Skystride> to stand upright in midair.

Since the Yellow Dragon is enormous, I had Blue move several kilometers away.

The Yellow Dragon was flying straight toward me.

Earlier I compared it to a bullet train, but in reality, it’s far faster than that.

If it showed no sign of stopping and came charging in, I would brace myself and receive it with my sword.

If it went well, we’d end up with sliced Yellow Dragon. …Can you eat Yellow Dragon?

A: It is edible.

Like eel?

…No, I’ll be absorbing it, so I’m not planning to eat it.

Unfortunately, the Yellow Dragon did not charge straight into me.

More precisely, since it showed no sign of stopping, I readied my sword, but at a point about 1 km away from me, it came to an abrupt halt.

As if mocking inertia itself, it stopped right there. Not a sudden brake, but a complete stop.

《Small one. Why do you violate the sky, the domain of the gods?》

The Yellow Dragon turned its massive eyes toward me and spoke via \<Thought Wave>.

\<Thought Wave> is a Unique Skill included in \<All Things>, allowing one-way communication similar to the telepathy of \<Bond of Contract>.

“If you’re going to ask someone something, shouldn’t you give your name first?”

《There is no need to name oneself to one who is about to die. Answer my question, and I will erase you in an instant so that you do not suffer.》

“I don’t think anyone would answer honestly after being told that.”

At this point, the possibility of “it’s a good guy, so we let it go home” dropped to nearly 0%.

By the way, it seems to have good hearing, because even though I spoke normally, it could hear me.

《Very well. Then die in agony.》

Saying that, the Yellow Dragon twisted its body.

That single motion sent shockwaves raging through the surrounding space.

This is the effect of the skill \<Heavenly Might>, included in \<All Things>.

\<Heavenly Might> is an ultra-powerful skill that manipulates the weather.

When the already enormous Yellow Dragon twists its body, winds naturally rage around it.

By enhancing that with \<Heavenly Might>, it is sublimated into shockwaves.

Incidentally, I took the shockwave, but there was no damage in particular.

The armor must have done a good job.

A: Even without the armor, you took no damage.

I know.

《What? You did not even waver?》

Even the Yellow Dragon sounded surprised (via \<Thought Wave>).

“You thought you could take me down with something like a greeting shockwave? You’re underestimating me.”

《A small one speaks boldly. Very well, I will accept your provocation. Receive my attack and regret it.》

To the Yellow Dragon, that shockwave apparently didn’t even count as an attack.

I know it’s hard to picture since it’s fighting me in midair, but if that shockwave hit directly, most national capitals would suffer devastating damage.

As proof, even Blue, far away, nearly lost her balance. …Oops. Since Blue is specialized for flight, that actually makes it harder to convey how impressive the Yellow Dragon is.

While I was thinking about that, the Yellow Dragon made its next move.

《’Black Clouds’, ‘Great Thunder’.》

With those two words, the Yellow Dragon covered about a 1 km radius of sky around me in black storm clouds.

Within them, lightning ran again and again, all of it assaulting me.

This is also one of the effects of \<Heavenly Might>, the Yellow Dragon’s single-target attack.

Calling it single-target when it covers 1 km is questionable, but on the Yellow Dragon’s scale, the effect area is quite limited.

If it wanted to, it could manipulate the weather over a far wider area, even an entire country.

However, after seeing how I handled the shockwave earlier, it must have judged that wide-area attacks would not deal damage to me.

Thus, it chose a narrower but higher-powered attack, equivalent to \<Lightning Magic LV10>.

Well, attacks of this level can be dodged or blocked easily.

Sera could even nullify this. It looks like a natural phenomenon, but it’s treated as magic…

Even if the attack isn’t particularly dangerous, having it continue endlessly gets annoying.

I swung the “Ultimate Holy Sword Ultimesia” and blew away the surrounding storm clouds. This was not due to the holy sword’s effect, but simply raw strength.

《Impossible…》

“Next, it’s my turn.”

Ignoring the shocked Yellow Dragon, I ran through the air, kicking off the void.

Come to think of it, the Yellow Dragon didn’t even comment on a human floating in midair.

It didn’t press deeply during our initial exchange either. It probably just doesn’t care about human circumstances or logic.

《Guh!》

“Haa!”

Sensing instinctive danger as I closed in, the Yellow Dragon hastily fired an enormous lightning strike from the jeweled orb in its hand, which I deflected with the holy sword.

So that orb can do that too. I really want it.

In that brief moment, the Yellow Dragon attempted to evade and put distance between us.

But given its massive size, there was no way it could fully escape.

As I approached the Yellow Dragon, instead of slashing it, I leapt onto its back.

《What!?》

I then plunged the holy sword into his back beneath my feet.

《Guh!?》

I began running along the Yellow Dragon’s back.

The holy sword I had stabbed in continued to tear through its body.

As an aside, there was no spray of blood. It doesn’t seem to be an ordinary living creature.

《Gyaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa!!!》

The Yellow Dragon screamed and violently shook its body.

Of course, it couldn’t shake me off.

Even if I did fall, I could always return with \<Skystride>.

《Damn you!》

The Yellow Dragon sent lightning coursing through its own body.

If its surface is being attacked, then attack the surface in return. As a response, it’s basically correct.

I made small jumps at the instant the lightning flowed to avoid it, pulling the holy sword out for that moment.

Then, using the momentum of landing, I stabbed the holy sword in again and kept running.

《Gugyaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa!!!???》

It was definitely in intense pain, but in terms of HP, it hadn’t dropped that much.

The Yellow Dragon’s HP is absurdly high, so it doesn’t feel like these are effective hits.

In human terms, it’s like having needles repeatedly stuck into your body. Well, eventually you’d die of blood loss. Even against a Yellow Dragon, its HP will run out eventually.

The Yellow Dragon repeatedly launched surface attacks, but I dodged every single one.

If you look at the techniques it uses, you can tell that most of the Yellow Dragon’s attacks are area attacks. In other words, they’re crude.

They would be devastating against large enemies or many targets. But they lack finesse. There are no attacks designed to deal with a single human.

The earlier “Black Clouds” and “Great Thunder” are good examples.

Of course, it’s a being that never encounters such an opponent.

There’s no reason for it to have techniques it never needs.

In other words, a single human with overwhelming power is the Yellow Dragon’s greatest natural enemy.

If such a human existed, that is.

And such a human was here.

《Guuuuuuuuuu!!!》

Growling, the Yellow Dragon began flying upward.

This time, it must be trying to shake me off through sheer speed.

I was starting to get tired of repeating the same thing… well, at that point, it became difficult to keep running on its body, and I was finally shaken off its back.

《Huff, huff… You insignificant human, you dare to wound me. You will pay for that with your life.》

Even though it said that arrogantly while panting, there was no intimidation at all.

By the way, the Yellow Dragon is more than 10 km away from me. It seems more skittish than I expected. I don’t know where a Yellow Dragon’s waist is, though.

A: From the head, around 600 m would correspond to the waist.

Ah, okay.

Just now, knowledge labeled “the location of a Yellow Dragon’s waist” was stored in my mind, knowledge I will never use again. …I want to delete it.

《In the end, you are but human. You can only defend against distant attacks. You blocked ‘Great Thunder’, but that cannot continue forever.》

It seems the Yellow Dragon has decided to stick to long-range attacks.

Its waist, about 600 m from the head, is really pulling back.

…I tried using that phrasing, but it’s harder to use than I thought.

《’Thunder Orb’, ‘Flame Orb’, ‘Ice Orb’, ‘Wind Orb’, ‘Light Orb’.》

Each time the Yellow Dragon chanted, a massive sphere, each about 100 m in diameter, appeared. They resembled the jeweled orb the Yellow Dragon held and floated around it.

Checking the map, I could see that each one carried magical power corresponding to its attribute.

In an aerial boss fight, when spheres start floating around the boss, what happens next?

《Go, ‘Five Orbs’.》

Of course, it turns into a shooting-game-style bullet hell.

-DO DO DO DO DO DO DO DO DO-

From each sphere, attacks of their respective attributes began firing nonstop.

From the Thunder Orb, roaring lightning.

From the Flame Orb, fireballs hot enough to melt iron.

From the Ice Orb, massive ice lances.

From the Wind Orb, invisible shockwaves.

From the Light Orb, blinding beams.

Each of the five orbs fires attacks that could annihilate the Castal capital in a single hit, in rapid succession.

Why the Castal capital was singled out is unclear.

“‘Flying Sword Barrage’.”

Faced with an excessive attack that could erase the Castal Kingdom from the map with just a few dozen shots, the tactic I chose against the most powerful attack I’ve faced in this world was interception.

I unleashed rapid-fire, ultra-high-power flying slashes using \<Flying Sword Art>.

Those slashes collided with the Yellow Dragon’s attacks and vanished.

There are surprisingly few shooting games where enemy bullets have hit detection.

Logically speaking, intercepting with attacks is easier than dodging…

Scenes where long-range attacks clash like this are really exhilarating.

Especially since I’m playing the role of a knight right now, I want to emphasize coolness.

《Why!? Why can you block even this!? …No, you cannot block it forever. I only need to keep pressing on.》

Though shocked that not a single attack had reached me, the Yellow Dragon chose to continue attacking, believing it could eventually overwhelm me.

This was its greatest and final mistake.

《My magic power and stamina are truly inexhaustible. There is no way I could be pushed back by a mere human.》

“We’ll see about that.”

《What?》

I increased the pace of “Flying Sword Barrage” just a little.

《Guh!? Gah!?》

Immediately, the balance of interception collapsed, and excess flying slashes began striking the Yellow Dragon.

Little by little, truly little by little, I increased the pace of “Flying Sword Barrage.”

《Gah!? Gweh!? Gaf!? Goba!?》

Gradually, the number of hits the Yellow Dragon took increased.

At one point, a “Flying Sword Barrage” struck one of the spheres floating around it, destroying it, triggering a very game-like event.

《St-stop… guh!? Al-already, stop… beb!? Stop it…!》

In the end, all the spheres were destroyed, and a pitiful Yellow Dragon, stripped of any means of resistance, was left to be battered by “Flying Sword Barrage.”

It seems “Flying Sword Barrage” is more damage-efficient than stabbing and running.

Maybe because the \<Flying Sword Art> skill level is added to the attack power? Just stabbing and running probably doesn’t even get the \<Sword Art> bonus…

When its HP dropped below 10%, I used the holy sword’s “Power Control” to suppress the damage.

And the Yellow Dragon’s absurd HP was finally reduced to under 1%.

“This is the end!”

Maintaining \<Skystride>, I activated \<Short Distance Shift> and raised the holy sword high right before the Yellow Dragon’s eyes.

《P-please, stop…》

As the Yellow Dragon tried to evade, fear seeping through, I stopped my sword.

“Well, delivering the finishing blow isn’t actually my job.”

《Huh?》

The next moment, an arrow fired by Mio from directly below pierced the Yellow Dragon’s head.

《Keh?》

“Sorry, that was kind of a sneak attack.”

Scattering strange \<Thought Waves>, the Yellow Dragon’s HP hit 0.

I had promised to let Mio deliver the finishing blow. Promises should be kept.

Losing the power to remain aloft, the Yellow Dragon began falling toward the ground.

I immediately touched it and absorbed it using the Level 8 effect of \<Life and Death Authority>.

I also picked up the jeweled orb that slipped from the Yellow Dragon’s hand.

Alta, you don’t need to pseudo-personalize the Yellow Dragon, but at least check its memories.

A: Understood.

I want to know why it was wandering around near the stratosphere.

Based on past experience, it probably doesn’t have any significant information… I mean, the Progenitor Divine Dragon and the Archangel had grand titles but hardly any useful information either.

L: Such cruel treatment.

Oh right, El was with us too, wasn’t she? She’d been quiet the whole time, so I forgot.

L: Truly cruel treatment. I stayed silent so as not to interfere with the battle…

It wasn’t an opponent that would put me at a disadvantage just because El spoke to me.

L: To have such composure against a “Final Trial” ranked above me… Master, when we fought in the Dragon Forest, if you’d wanted to, you could have killed me in an instant, couldn’t you?

Well… yeah, I could have.

When there’s time to spare, I have no intention of doing something as wasteful as killing in an instant.

L: Hah, Master really is extraordinary in so many ways. Well then, I’ve seen a Dragon God get thoroughly beaten, so I’ll head back ahead of you.

Saying that, El’s presence vanished from within me.

Through the effect of \<Multiple Existence> enhanced by \<Expanded Interpretation>, a new ability was added to El, who is a pseudo-personality.

That ability is “Manifest near any chosen subordinate.” Put simply, it means she can freely teleport between my subordinates.

She probably manifested near someone on the ground. Incidentally, incoming calls can be rejected.

Expanded Interpretation has reached LV6.

A new ability has been unlocked.

\<Expanded Interpretation LV6>

The number of effect targets has expanded to 60.

Expanded Interpretation has reached LV7.

A new ability has been unlocked.

\<Expanded Interpretation LV7>

The number of effect targets has expanded to 70.

The level-up speed of \<Expanded Interpretation> is really fast.

It’s not even comparable to the level-up speed of \<Life and Death Authority> or \<Multiple Existence>.

In fact, it’s overtaken \<Multiple Existence> in level (\<Life and Death Authority> is still ahead at Level 8).

As usual, \<Expanded Interpretation> leveling up only increases the number of effect targets, which honestly isn’t that important.

Today’s main event is Mio’s enhancement.

“Master, I did it!”

Mio, riding on Blue, shouted as she approached.

“My weapon became Mythical-grade, and I got the \<Transcendence> skill and the ‘Transcendent’ title too! Last Attack bonuses are seriously delicious!”

She said happily while holding up her newly Mythical-grade weapon.

Comet Bow – Comet

Classification: Short Bow

Rarity: Mythical-grade

Notes: Converts magic power into arrows, automatic tracking, extreme range bonus, indestructible, owner-bound

The meteor became a comet.

Can this really be called a pure promotion?

Well, it’s definitely stronger, and nitpicking would be boorish.

Still, the addition of “automatic tracking” is interesting.

I can’t help wanting to say, “This isn’t something you do in a sword-and-magic fantasy world.”

“With this ‘automatic tracking’, when combined with your map, Master, it seems incredibly powerful. As long as it’s within the range you can check on the map, it looks like I can snipe anywhere with automatic tracking…”

Mio was also focused on “automatic tracking.”

As always, she has a similar perspective to mine.

“In the assassin sense, that’s truly a sniper.”

“Isn’t that a terrible way to put it?”

“You can defeat monsters while staying at the mansion.”

“Isn’t that too lazy?”

Even though I was proposing useful ways to use “automatic tracking” Mio didn’t seem pleased.

“Monster hunting while cooking…”

“It’s not impossible, but if I do extra things, the food might lose its flavor, you know?”

“Sniping during cooking is prohibited!”

“Master, that’s just normal. Perfectly normal.”

After finishing our trivial exchange, I mounted Blue again.

“Blue, take us back to the ground.”

“Got it.”

With nothing left to do in the sky, we returned to the ground riding Blue.

Since “Portal” can’t be set up in midair, we had no choice but to descend directly.

---

**AN:** Because the stage was the sky and the opponent was Jin, I’m a bit worried whether the Yellow Dragon’s strength came across.

This applies to the other Final Trials as well, but Final Trials are originally beings capable of easily destroying a single country.

If the Yellow Dragon had descended in altitude and altered the weather, it could have caused catastrophic damage on a continental scale.

Letting it cause devastation once before defeating it would better convey the enemy’s threat level, but Jin often doesn’t allow that, so it’s quite difficult.

+++

## **126: Sera’s Knight Equipment and a Tea Party**

**AN:** It ended up feeling like a short story, but it got too long, so I shoved it into the main story.

It’s almost entirely dialogue. Even though this is supposed to be the subordinate arc, I dumped in a bunch of people who hadn’t had any screen time.

---

A leisurely Day 14.

The morning after the battle with the Yellow Dragon.

After that, once we returned to the surface, we thanked the subordinates who had helped us and headed back to the mansion.

I tried to give the subordinates who had helped some kind of reward, but they said, “It is only natural for servants to devote themselves to their master” and flatly refused.

Instead, what they asked for was a dinner party with the subordinates.

Calling it a demand sounds bad, so to clarify, they asked politely, saying “if it pleases you.”

By the way, the party title was “Celebration: Subjugation of the Yellow Dragon.”

Despite also being a reward for those who helped, it was clearly a party with me as the main focus.

Also, Mio had been on the side that subjugated the Yellow Dragon, so there were no dishes made by Mio.

“Mmm, this is really delicious. Who made it? Miyuki-san? …Impressive.”

Mio was lavishing praise on the dishes made by Miyuki, the mother of the Naruse mother-daughter pair who had returned from demonfolk to human.

According to her, without the bonuses from the \<Cooking> skill, Miyuki would be at about the same level as Mio.

I tried it too, and it was extremely good. As expected of a former single mother. …Though I’m not sure if I should really say “former” in this case.

This time as well, I tried to speak to as many party participants as possible, but naturally I couldn’t talk to everyone.

I had to prioritize talking to subordinates I’d never had a chance to converse with at other times.

Apparently, from the believers perspective, they want me to hold parties more frequently.

The number of subordinates has grown to a ridiculous level, so the old goal of “talk to all subordinates” has already become impossible.

Even I can’t handle over six thousand people.

The party didn’t go particularly late, so waking up today was nice and easy.

At breakfast, Mimi gave a report that Sera’s equipment had apparently been completed early this morning.

After breakfast, Sera, Maria, and I headed to the forge.

Sakura and Dora were out on other business. Mio just wasn’t tagging along.

“Sera-san’s… equipment… is finished… Please… try it on…”

“I understand. As expected, compared to my master’s equipment, it’s a step down, isn’t it?”

“I am… sorry…”

As Sera muttered while looking at the knight equipment Mimi presented, the gear forged for Sera was Legendary grade, one rank below my Phantasmal grade equipment.

It looked almost exactly like my equipment, but only the performance was inferior.

“I couldn’t… make it… on the same level… as Jin-sama’s equipment…”

“That can’t be helped. For you, Mimi-san, it’s only natural that our master comes first… Besides, even Legendary grade is excessive as temporary equipment meant to conceal one’s identity.”

Apparently, even though the materials and procedures were the same, the quality of the finished product changed drastically.

When forging my equipment, Mimi said her emotions had been heightened, and as a result, \<Holy Demonic Smithing>, which is affected by the smith’s mental state, performed at its absolute best, producing Phantasmal grade equipment.

Even if it was at my instruction, just making Sera’s equipment didn’t take her that far.

Of course, Sera understood this as well.

As she herself said, even Legendary grade is excessive for equipment meant to hide one’s identity.

“For now, I’ll try it on.”

“I will assist.”

With Maria’s help, Sera began putting on the knight armor.

It seems she has little experience wearing full plate armor, so she struggled more than expected.

“I’ve finally… finished putting it on. It’s quite… troublesome.”

“We usually wear at most light armor, after all.”

With the helmet on, Sera spoke in a slightly muffled voice.

She’s tall and well-proportioned, so full plate armor suits her extremely well.

To be honest, I think it suits her better than it does me.

At the very least, she gives off more of a “hero who saved the kingdom” vibe than I do.

As an aside, unlike my equipment, Sera’s includes a shield. Because of that, her gear looks even more impressive than mine.

I basically never use shields. I don’t like having one hand tied up.

“Once I put it on, I barely feel like I’m wearing it. I can move very naturally.”

Sera lightly moves her body, checking how the equipment feels.

She lightly swings a sword, getting used to it. For Sera, it’s unusually a normal-sized sword.

Well, a knight guarding a queen wielding a huge sword that’s hard to swing indoors would be ridiculous.

If you’re committing to role-play, you should commit fully.

If you’re going to play, you should put your all into that play.

“So, what do you want to do? Want to go hunt some random monsters to break it in, like I did yesterday?”

“Yes, that sounds good. Since we have the chance, I’d like to try fighting in this equipment. Rather than taking on a big target, I’m thinking of dealing with many small ones. What will you do, my master?”

I think for a moment after Sera asks.

“Hmm, I fought pretty hard yesterday, so today I kind of want to relax at the mansion. If it’s just grinding small fry, there probably won’t be anything very interesting, so I’ll pass today.”

I don’t mind watching Sera fight, but watching endless break-in fights against weak enemies doesn’t really appeal to me, especially right after fighting a major opponent yesterday.

“I understand. Then I’ll try inviting Mio-san.”

“I will… go along… as well… If anything feels… awkward… please tell me…”

“Thank you. That helps a lot.”

Mimi also seems unwilling to compromise when it comes to equipment she made herself, so she chose to accompany Sera.

“By the way, why are you bringing Mio?”

“Huh? Because Mio-san also obtained new equipment yesterday.”

“Oh right, that’s true. I completely forgot.”

The weapon Mio used to deal the finishing blow to the Yellow Dragon had become Mythical grade, after all.

“Even Mythical grade equipment leaves that little impression on you, my master…”

“I need to… hurry up and make… Genesis grade…”

Sera said that in exasperation, while Mimi, for some reason, looked serious, as if filled with resolve.

After seeing Sera, Mio, and Mimi off, I headed to a certain room.

This room is called the “Fluffy Room” and I often use it to summon beastfolk or beast-type familiars and fluff them.

If there’s a symbol of relaxation, it has to be fluffing.

“And so, this is Myao, borrowed from Mio.”

“Myaau…”

Myao, held in my arms, let out a disgruntled-sounding cry.

“Will you be fluffing that one as well? It looks rather unhappy…”

“‘It’s like, whatever, I don’t even matter.’ That’s what it’s saying.”

Tsukiyo, the representative fluffing attendant, asked curiously.

The one who translated Myao’s cry was Tsukiyo’s daughter, Tokoyo.

I have a policy of not using the ‘Translation’ magic during fluffing, so this is a big help (it would ruin the mood to understand beast language while fluffing them).

The beasts and beastgirls present here are all volunteers. Forcing unwilling participants isn’t my thing.

I confirmed with both Mio and Myao beforehand, and fluffing itself was apparently okay.

By the way, today’s participants are Myao, Tsukiyo, Tokoyo, Maria, and four others, for a total of eight (including beasts). Since it was a sudden call, it’s fewer than usual.

“She’s just sulking because Mio left her behind.”

“Myaao…”

“‘I’m so depressed’, she says.”

Myao wanted to go with Mio, but since they were apparently fighting fairly tough opponents, Mio refrained from bringing along Myao, whose level and stats are low.

“So I thought I’d take advantage of that opening to do some fluffing. Myao’s usually glued to Mio inside the mansion, so I haven’t had a chance before. We promised we’d fluff at some point, so it’s fine, right?”

“Myaau.”

“‘That’s okay’, she says.”

She doesn’t seem opposed to the fluffing itself.

“I see… She hasn’t learned \<Transformation>, it seems. Will you be fluffing her as a beast?”

“Yeah, that’s the plan. Since it’s Myao’s first time, I’ll keep it super mild. As for the others… since many of them are used to it, I’ll raise the level by one stage.”

Looking around, I realized there were many veteran fluffing attendants, so it was probably time to move on to the next stage.

“What exactly do you intend to do?”

“That’s something you can find out by experiencing it…”

…

“Haau…”

Thirty minutes later, with Tsukiyo, the last one standing, fainting, today’s fluffing session was forcibly brought to an end.

Hmm… I really didn’t expect everyone to fail to endure it.

“Myaauuun♡ Myaauuun♡”

And as you can see, Myao is completely smitten.

She rubs up against my feet as I stand, repeatedly pressing her face against my legs.

There’s no trace left of her earlier bad mood about being left behind.

“U-uun…”

Maria, the first to faint, wakes up.

She’s quick to faint, but also quick to recover.

“I fainted again… How careless.”

Maria said that with a dejected expression, like it needed a “thud” sound effect.

“Seems like Maria is weak to fluffing.”

“That is… because it is Jin-sama. I would not have the same reaction if anyone else were to pet me. In the first place, I would not allow others to fluff me.”

Apparently, the pleasantness of the fluffing gets a big boost because the one doing it is me.

Still, fainting almost instantly feels a bit much…

“As Jin-sama’s guard, perhaps I should decline fluffing that might make me faint… But opportunities to be touched like that by Jin-sama are rare, so it is a difficult choice.”

Maria seems to have her own inner conflict.

Indeed, a guard who passes out from being petted by her master is kind of fatal in many ways.

“How about you stop when Sera isn’t around?”

“…Yes. When Sera-chan isn’t here, I must serve as your guard.”

“Except today, Sera is out.”

“Huh!?”

Maria takes a massive shock.

It’s rare for me to tease Maria, but the only time she really breaks her composed demeanor is during fluffing, so once in a while is fine.

After that, I left Tsukiyo and the others in the maids care and left the Fluffy Room.

Ah, and Myao followed along at my feet.

After lunch, and once the combat training with subordinates reached a stopping point, Sakuya invited me to a tea party. Isn’t she busy?

Even though it’s a tea party, it’s apparently being held normally at my mansion, so I headed to the designated room.

“I’m coming in.”

I open the door without knocking. It’s my mansion, so I’m free to do that.

“Ah, big brother. Welcome.”

Sakuya, dressed formally (something like a twelve-layered robe), greeted me as the host of the tea party.

This room is one of the larger ones in my mansion, easily spacious enough for over ten people.

And the people present are quite something.

“Welcome. Thank you very much for coming today.”

The one bowing as she said that was Cattleya, princess of the Kingdom of Estea.

Cattleya was wearing a pale crimson dress that wasn’t overly flashy. She’s originally quite beautiful, so it’s a striking sight. It’s hard to believe she’s the same person who normally eats like a glutton at the mansion.

“We have been waiting for you, Jin-dono.”

“Indeed we have.”

In addition, Tooru and Kaoru, the princess sisters of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, are here.

Tooru is wearing a men’s kimono, while Kaoru is wearing a women’s kimono. Both are somewhat lavish, so this might be their formal wear.

Also, a trivial note: Tooru is wearing men’s clothing, but she isn’t cross-dressing. To put it simply, she isn’t wearing a sarashi, so even in men’s clothes, the curve of her chest is clearly visible.

“We couldn’t even touch the sweets unless Jin-sama was present, after all. So it’s no exaggeration to say we were waiting.”

“Don’t say unnecessary things!”

“Exactly! Even if you think it, you mustn’t say it out loud!”

“S-sorry…”

The one who slipped up and got scolded by Tooru and Cattleya was Rouge, the imperial princess of the Crimson Empire.

She’s wearing a red dress with a design reminiscent of a cheongsam. It’s adorned with flashy gold embroidery, so it must be her best outfit.

“I’m looking forward to the sweets.”

“They told you not to say that, and yet you’re still so laid-back…”

Those two are the dragonoids, Deep Green Dragon and Sky Dragon.

They’re wearing green and blue dresses, respectively. There’s no way dragonoids would normally own dresses (prejudice), so they probably borrowed them from someone.

There are also a few other women in the room, but I don’t recognize them, so I’ll skip over them.

“Um… is the theme something like a royal tea party?”

“Correct!”

Sakuya answers while making a circle over her head.

Everyone here is someone connected to royalty, such as queens or princesses (probably including the unfamiliar girls). The two dragonoids are a bit of a gray area, though…

“By the way, we didn’t invite Dora-chan because she’s out with Sakura-chan. Also, we didn’t invite that Great Spirit girl named Rain. Apparently she became a ‘Spirit Queen’, but it doesn’t seem like she has any territory or authority.”

It seems Sakuya gathered this group after doing some research on my subordinates.

Naturally, the former Eldia princess is not present.

“So then, why did this turn into a tea party with this lineup?”

“Heh heh heh. That is because…”

Sakuya unnecessarily builds suspense.

“To entertain you, big brother!”

She strikes a smug pose, like it needs a “bam” sound effect, and says something incomprehensible.

“_What_?”

“Um, I’ll add some clarification.”

As an English question escaped my mouth, Cattleya stepped in to explain.

“There will be a summit in the Theocracy of Elgant soon, correct? Upon hearing that, we thought that since so many of Jin-sama’s subordinates are connected to royal families, it would be good for us to deepen our exchanges to align our positions. Thus, in order to foster that exchange, we decided to hold a tea party.”

Looking at this room, it does indeed feel like there are a lot of royal subordinates.

More specifically, a lot of ‘royal’ women.

Aside from Sakuya, none of them seem to be the actual heads of their countries, but for aligning intentions between nations, it’s not a bad idea for royals to interact with each other.

In fact, when the Kingdom of Eldia tried to attack the Kingdom of Estea, Sakuya, who had interactions with Cattleya (mostly during meals), ended up taking the role of stopping it.

“I see. I understand that much. But how does that turn into entertaining me?”

Why not just have a tea party among the royals?

Why do I have to be involved?

“Since Jin-sama has royals as his subordinates, it stands to reason that he is above royalty. Don’t you think that’s more than sufficient justification to invite you to the tea party?”

“When it was suggested that we invite Jin-dono, there was no one who opposed it.”

“That’s right. It was decided unanimously that we should invite you.”

Tooru and Kaoru supplement Cattleya’s answer.

“And that’s where the entertainment part comes in.”

Sakuya takes over the explanation.

“If we, who are lower in position, invite you, big brother, it inevitably looks like we’re just fawning over you. …So we decided to be upfront and push the ‘entertaining you’ angle to the forefront!”

“You’re as bold as ever.”

For some reason, Sakuya occasionally becomes very manly.

“Yup! When it comes to dealing with you, big brother, I think it’s better to declare outright that we’re fawning over you, rather than hiding it while fawning over you!”

“So either way, you’re fawning over me.”

Indeed, I’d rather have their intentions laid out plainly from the start than have them do things behind the scenes.

Even if that intention is the somewhat delicate matter of “fawning over me”…

“Of course, taking someone home is also okay. I’m always okay with it, you know?”

“Wait a minute! I didn’t hear about that!”

The one who reacted to Sakuya’s bombshell was Rouge.

Is the “taking home” comment just a joke? If so, it’s concerning that most of the girls around her look embarrassed but not entirely opposed.

“Huh? You think you have a chance of being taken home? I didn’t tell girls with no chance, though…”

“Isn’t that treatment a bit cruel!?”

Sakuya mercilessly cuts Rouge down.

It seems that “taking home” wasn’t a joke after all.

Be that as it may… Yeah, no, Rouge is out.

– Knock knock –

“Please come in.”

“Excuse us.”

The door is knocked on, and when Sakuya gives permission, the serving maids push a service wagon into the room.

“Tea and sweets. Here you go!”

Thanks to the maids efficient movements, the tea is prepared in no time.

“Now then, big brother, have a seat, have a seat. Since the tea is here, let’s start the tea party right away.”

Prompted by Sakuya, I take a seat.

The table is round, with Sakuya on my right and Cattleya on my left.

The tea party begins, and casual conversation starts among everyone.

“By the way, there are a few unfamiliar royals here. Which royal families are they from?”

I ask while pointing at the girls I don’t recognize.

There are two unfamiliar royals: one girl around my age, and another who looks about five years old. Both are wearing warm-colored dresses.

“Y-you don’t remember…”

“…”

The older girl staggers in shock at my words. She’s a delicate-looking beauty, though not quite to Cattleya’s level.

The younger girl doesn’t move at all, remaining seated.

“From the way you put it, it sounds like we’ve met somewhere before.”

“Big brother, that girl is the princess of the Kingdom of Narunka.”

As I cross my arms, trying to dredge up my memory, Sakuya explains from the side.

The Kingdom of Narunka. One of the Atto Confederation countries, ruled by Tsukiyo, the Golden Fox. While taming Tsukiyo, the palace staff were enslaved, leading to effective control of the kingdom.

I’ve had almost no direct involvement, though.

I look at the girl’s face again.

“Ah, the princess who was imprisoned and covered in filth. You were one of the first to have \<Brainwashing Arts> undone, right?”

Now that I looked closely, I recognized her.

She was one of the royals who’d been imprisoned in the royal castle’s dungeon by Tsukuyo. Back then she was smeared in filth and completely out of her mind, with a terrifying expression, but… in a normal state, she was actually quite beautiful.

“F-filth-covered… I-it is true, but that wording is a bit much…”

“Big brother, that description hits me too, so could you not?”

The girl teared up, and Sakuya made a displeased face.

When I first met Sakuya, she was also imprisoned in the castle’s underground dungeon and covered in filth. Come to think of it, you could say they were in similar circumstances.

“W-we did meet once after that as well, but…”

“…Ah, but that time you stayed kneeling the whole time, right?”

“Yes, that is correct.”

I do remember gathering Narunka’s royal family once for a face-to-face after taking control of the Kingdom of Narunka.

It seems she was there then too, but at that time only the king spoke, and the other royals remained kneeling the entire time. There’s no way I’d remember faces from that.

“I have always wished to speak with you, but I was unable to obtain Lady Alta’s permission, and I was not blessed with an opportunity. This time, with a tea party that only royals may attend, I have finally been granted that chance. Allow me to introduce myself properly once more. I am Lena, First Princess of the Kingdom of Narunka. I humbly ask that you remember me from here on.”

The girl – now Lena – bowed her head.

“Yeah, nice to meet you. So, who’s that little girl?”

The one who answered my question was Cattleya.

“This is Mia, the former Sixth Princess of the former Kingdom of Eldia. She is not royalty at present, but we invited her as a representative of Eldia’s former royal family. Naturally, we could hardly invite the former Princess Cristia.”

If former Princess Cristia were here, I’m confident I’d have immediately turned around and left.

“They’re all still young, so there’s still time to re-educate them. I brought the best one – the least tainted by Eldia – out of the bunch.”

As Sakuya added, all of Eldia’s former royals aside from Cristia are currently young.

Even if they are former royals, they still have their uses, so they are in the middle of being re-educated. If they grow up under Eldia’s ways, they will be useless.

When I turned my eyes to the little girl, she flinched, trembling as she timidly looked my way.

“H-hajumemashite, M-Mia to mo, moushimashu.”

Tearful and trembling, she gave a stuttering, tongue-tied greeting.

What is with this reaction…?

A: During the strict re-education, she was firmly instructed that participating in today’s tea party is an event that absolutely cannot be failed, and she seems to have buckled under the pressure.

Ah… Right. The believers are the ones doing the former Eldia royals re-education, weren’t they…?

I’ve heard that the way they are treated is extremely harsh, a result of the believers considering my feelings. It’s not like they’d go easy just because she’s a little girl.

“Yeah, nice to meet you.”

“I-igyo, o-mishirioki wo…”

The stuttering little girl stared in a certain direction with tears in her eyes, making a face of utter despair.

In the direction of her gaze, a maid who had been standing by was writing something down in a memo pad.

A: She is being graded. It will affect how she is treated going forward.

…Former Eldia royal re-education is pretty brutal.

If I make her do anything extra, her evaluation will probably drop, so it might be better not to talk to her.

“To put it bluntly, those two are here to pad the numbers. Seven people alone just felt a bit lacking.”

“It’s a cruel way to put it, but thanks to that I was able to greet Jin-sama, so I cannot complain…”

Hearing Sakuya’s brutally frank remark, Lena slumped her shoulders.

Once the greetings were finished, I asked about one more thing that had been bothering me.

“Speaking of which, why isn’t Tooru wearing a sarashi wrap? I’m pretty sure you wore one when you were dressed as a man, right?”

Specifically, Tooru’s outfit.

Even though she’s wearing men’s clothes, since she isn’t wearing a sarashi wrap, her fairly sizable chest is jutting out. I’m pretty sure she wore a sarashi when I stripped her before.

Kaoru is wearing women’s clothes, so there’s no issue there, but Tooru has… various issues.

“This tea party is to entertain Jin-dono, you know. We were being considerate, thinking you wouldn’t be pleased if you were entertained by a manly appearance, you know?”

“Then wouldn’t it have been better if you both used your female appearances?”

Since they can swap, I asked why they didn’t both use their female appearances, but Kaoru shook her head.

“If we did that, even though there are two of us, our impression would become weaker. We are leaving the oddball role to big bro… big sis.”

“That’s right, you know!”

She said “oddball role” without the slightest hesitation.

“Even if you call it oddball, the base material isn’t bad, and you’ve dressed it up to look a bit more feminine, so it’s not that jarring, right?”

“Yeah, that’s true.”

As Sakuya said, Tooru isn’t fully cross-dressed, and she’s using feminine accessories, so she just looks like a slightly boyish woman.

It looks like she’s wearing light makeup too, so calling her an oddball is kind of mean. …Though since she’s calling herself that, maybe “mean” isn’t the right word.

“Speaking of outfits, what is that getup of yours, Rouge?”

This time I threw the topic to Rouge.

Rouge was wearing a dress resembling a cheongsam.

“It’s a special outfit I brought from the Empire. Supposedly it’s a dress an ancient hero passed down to our Crimson Empire.”

As always, that Japanese hero really went all-in on his tastes.

There’s a non-zero chance it was actually a Chinese person who got isekai’d, but it was probably a Japanese person overall.

“We specified each country’s traditional attire and dress.”

“That’s right. That’s why I came wearing this heavy, hard-to-move-in outfit too.”

Cattleya pinched the hem of her dress, and Sakuya flapped her junihitoe irritably.

“So we’re the only ones wearing borrowed dresses, huh.”

“Yeah, it’s not like we own formalwear.”

The only ones without dresses were Blue and Leaf, the nudist pair.

“Both of you are normally beautiful in human form, and I think the dresses suit you too.”

“Th-thanks…”

“Ehehe, master praised meee~”

When I complimented the two of them, Sakuya stood up.

“Big brother! How about me? Does my outfit suit me?”

Looks like she’s fired up with a competitive spirit toward Blue and Leaf.

“Normal.”

“Normal!?”

Sakuya took psychic damage with a loud “gahn” sound effect.

No, she definitely is cute, but… sorry, I’m pretty used to seeing her like this…

“S-surely that’s where you say something polite like ‘it suits you’ or ‘you’re beautiful’…?”

“No, this tea party is supposed to be entertaining me, right? Why do I have to lie about how I feel?”

“Jin-sama, I knew it, but you really are free…”

When I answered Cattleya’s question, even Rouge’s face twitched as she looked at me.

Sakuya was still frozen in place.

---

**AN:** I was really planning to wrap up with the talk about Sera’s equipment, the fluffing, and some smaller bits.

But unless it’s a situation like a tea party, there aren’t many chances for all the royal women to gather, so I thought it would be fine once in a while…

I feel bad that the story isn’t progressing despite updates every ten days. The tea party will continue for one more chapter. Sorry.
