## **127: Tea Sweets and a Leisurely End**

**AN:** Please bear with another slice-of-life chapter without any real climax.

Ah, and with this story, Volume 8 comes to an end. The volume transition happens at a pretty good timing.

**Editor Note:** The short-story and V8 Character list do appear after this.

---

Sakuya, who had been dejected after being told she was “ordinary” by me, managed to recover.

“I shouldn’t have expected lip service from you, Onii-chan…”

“To be treated so roughly by Jin-dono… Sakuya-dono is enviable, you know.”

As Sakuya muttered with a slightly depressed look, the mentally masochistic Tooru said something stupid.

The fact that everyone except Rena and Mia was not put off by Tooru’s comment probably meant this was already common knowledge. Is Izumo Wa really okay?

“Then, want to switch with me?”

“By all means.”

“…”

Seeing Tooru answer instantly, even Sakuya froze for a moment.

“…Sorry, never mind. This is also communication with Onii-chan.”

“So regrettable, you know…”

Tooru slumped his shoulders, looking genuinely disappointed.

Was Sakuya actually enjoying being teased? …A pervert?

“It’s only because it’s you, Onii-chan, okay? Don’t get the wrong idea.”

Reading my expression, Sakuya cut in with a tsundere-like line.

It seemed the top of the Castal Kingdom was not a pervert after all.

Also, the tsundere position overlaps with Blue over there.

Blue is a tsundere in the proper sense, and once she turns dere, she never goes back to tsun…

“Still, it would help if you could go a bit easy on me.”

“I don’t need you to go easy on me, you know!”

Despite having just said something that made it sound like teasing was fine, Sakuya shrank back a little.

In contrast, Tooru looked as if to say, “Bring it on!”

If someone tells me not to hold back, even I have no choice but to get serious.

So, I activated \<Fear> on Tooru without any restraint.

“Ababababa…”

With just three seconds of the skill, Tooru’s face became something a girl her age should never make.

It was an R18 face, with fear and pleasure mixed together (Tooru is fourteen).

“O-Onii-chan. Please don’t do that at a tea party…”

Sensing what had happened from Tooru’s condition, Sakuya looked at me with a disgusted expression.

Yeah, that wasn’t something to do at a place where people eat and drink.

“We’ll have to use \<Purification>. Is there anyone who can use it?”

Rouge said that and looked around.

“I-It’s fine, you know… J-Just in case, I wore a diaper.”

“I don’t think that counts as fine.”

Tooru, who had gone limp and was slumped back in her chair, declared this confidently.

Hearing it, Cattleya shook her head and immediately denied it.

“What exactly were you expecting at a tea party when you said ‘just in case’?”

“I thought there might be one chance for Jin-dono to torment me…”

And she had seized that chance perfectly.

Idiot.

“Not only Big Sister Tooru, but I am fully prepared as well. I would like you to torment me physically.”

Her twin sister, Kaoru, was just as much of an idiot.

“Jin-sama, what are they talking about…?”

Rena, who did not know the twins’ proclivities, asked while visibly recoiling.

Mia beside her stared blankly for a moment, then went back to eating sweets.

“There are people with tastes like that. That’s all.”

“I-I see… The world really is wide.”

She did not seem to understand, but she accepted it for now.

Hopefully, Rena would not awaken to any strange tastes.

“Kaoru. If you like pain that much, I’ll lend you a magic sword later.”

“Onii-chan, you don’t mean…”

Sakuya seemed to realize something and turned pale.

“A magic sword? What kind of effect does it have?”

“‘Magic Sword: Eternal Pain.’ When you stab someone with it, intense pain assaults the body, but you won’t die. Perfect for you, right?”

“Just as I thought…”

Sakuya muttered, clearly traumatized by Magic Sword: Eternal Pain.

“That is a wonderful effect. I would love to borrow it.”

I had said it half as a joke, but Kaoru accepted eagerly.

I shuddered at the depth of the twins perversion.

As an aside, two days later Kaoru returned Magic Sword: Eternal Pain.

According to her, “I did not think it would be this much. It only felt good at first, and after that it was unbearably painful. I seem to be bad with long-term pain…”

“Jin-sama, would you like another cup of tea?”

Ah, yes, please.”

Seeing that my tea was empty, the maids refilled it.

Tooru left her seat for a moment to change her diaper. It seemed she was hoping for another chance.

“By the way, these cookies are delicious. No, there’s no other way to put it. They’re really delicious.”

Rena, who had been drinking tea and eating sweets, muttered that while eating the cookies served as tea snacks.

I thought she had been quiet since the tea party started, but it seemed she had been savoring the cookies the whole time.

“Nino-chan, could you explain the sweets?”

“Understood. Yes.”

Prompted by Sakuya, our head cooking maid, Nino, began explaining the cookies.

“The basic ingredients, such as flour, sugar, and butter, were obtained from the farms and ranches within the labyrinth. Yes.”

“For explorers like us, the fact that such things are spread out on the lower floors where we risk our lives fighting is something we can never get used to…”

From Rouge’s perspective as an explorer, the state of things past the fiftieth floor was hard to accept.

“Then you should stop eating, you know?”

“…No, I’ll eat.”

Asked by Tooru, Rouge hesitated, then chose to eat.

Once you choose to eat, you lose the right to complain.

“I’ll continue. Yes. All of these ingredients are of the highest quality. Recently, Midori the dryad has also been coming to the labyrinth and enriching the soil.”

I had wondered why I had not seen Midori in the mansion lately, so she had been going to the labyrinth.

A: It seems that with more people in the mansion, it became less comfortable, so she moved her base to the labyrinth. She is meeting her quota for producing secret medicines. As a plant-type monster, simply being there helps circulate nutrients. It also slightly affects the flavor of ingredients.

If she just lounges around in the mansion anyway, and if simply being in the labyrinth is useful, then that is obviously better. Midori does have a NEET disposition…

“And on top of that, the eggs are so high-class that we work desperately to ensure the other ingredients are not inferior. Yes.”

“What kind of eggs are they?”

Rena, who did not come to the mansion and did not know what eggs were normally used, asked. Well, those eggs.

“Harpy eggs. Yes.”

“H-Harpy eggs!?”

There were large quantities of harpy eggs here, something even royalty could not eat in this world.

In the true sense of the phrase, we had “more than we could sell” so using some for cookies was no problem at all.

Incidentally, the harpy girls currently lived quite freely aside from laying eggs.

Some transformed into humans and worked as maids, others transformed and joined mercenary groups, and some did nothing but eat and sleep besides laying eggs. The last group had a slightly stricter egg quota.

“S-Such high-class ingredients…”

“They are simple sweets, but made by someone with the \<Cooking> skill using carefully selected ingredients. Yes! One cookie would probably wipe out a typical noble’s monthly income. Yes!”

“Awawawa…”

Although she was technically royalty, it seemed Rena had never eaten harpy eggs.

The Kingdom of Narunka was not that large, so such luxury goods probably did not circulate.

She had been eating them normally until now, but suddenly began handling them as delicately as if they were gemstones.

…However, she did not stop eating!

Meanwhile, the young girl had not stopped eating cookies since she started, stuffing them into her mouth and puffing out her cheeks like a squirrel.

I could see the maid behind her writing a demerit in her notebook. …Stay strong.

“Well, a small amount does circulate in Castal through the Advance Company.”

“It’s the same in Estea.”

Since Castal Kingdom and Estea Kingdom were practically my home ground, I gave them slight preferential treatment in various ways.

One of those was the distribution of harpy eggs.

“P-Please, Narunka Kingdom as well!”

“Izumo Wa wants them too, you know!”

“Indeed!”

The royalty of Narunka Kingdom and Izumo Wa, who did not receive such preferential treatment, desperately appealed.

Mia, from the former Eldia Kingdom, looked completely unconcerned.

Since she was not treated as royalty in practice, she probably had no interest in domestic distribution.

“It has nothing to do with me, since I am away from my country. As long as there is enough for us to eat at Jin-sama’s mansion.”

“We feel the same. It would be impossible to provide for everyone in the Dragonkin Sanctuary, and we could not prepare adequate compensation…”

“We are just happy we could come to Master’s place.”

Rouge, who had left her country, and Blue and Leaf, who bore no responsibility for the Dragonkin Sanctuary, were carefree.

“Do we even have enough harpy eggs to distribute to other countries right now?”

“Unfortunately, we do not. Yes. If we reduce the amount sent to the countries currently selling them…”

“Rejected.”

“That is unacceptable.”

Sakuya and Cattleya cut off the cooking maid’s response to my question.

“If demand increases, the best solution is to increase supply, right?”

“Onii-chan, what are you planning to do?”

“Wouldn’t it be fine to tame more harpies?”

If there were not enough harpy eggs, then we just had to tame more harpies.

It was a bit pitiful for harpies to be tamed for egg-laying purposes, but worrying about that meant losing.

“You say it so easily, but do you have a lead?”

“If we go to the forest where the harpies were, we could probably manage to tame a few.”

If I remembered correctly, the place where Chocolat and the others lived was called Ende Mountain.

“Then I’ll go tame some.”

“Eh? Onii-chan, you don’t mean right now?”

“They say good deeds should be done promptly.”

Since people would cry if I acted alone, I called Maria just in case and used \<Portal> to transfer to Ende Mountain.

“Kyuiiiii!?”

Five minutes later.

What came back with me were twenty-one harpies and one Harpy Queen.

The Harpy Queen pressed her chest against my arm and rubbed her head against me.

It seemed I had a natural affinity for being liked by Harpy Queens.

“Onii-chan, isn’t that fast?”

“It was in the middle of a tea party, so I tamed them quickly. With this many, we won’t be short on harpy eggs, right?”

The harpies behind me were making kyui-kyui noises. It sounded like they were saying, “Leave it to us.”

“It might be enough, but… what about that Harpy Queen?”

“Apparently, the annihilation bonus from when I transferred to the gray world was a Harpy Queen, and the area became a harpy forest again. It was smaller scale than when Chocolat appeared, though.”

When a powerful monster is born as an annihilation bonus, the monster territory tends to overflow with monsters of the same type.

Just like with Chocolat, a Harpy Queen was born, so it became a harpy forest again.

Since harpies are more profitable than other monsters, it was a good outcome for me.

Come to think of it, Asha the monster tamer was training annihilation bonuses, but maybe she had not gotten around to everything?

A: The Harpy Queen was a strong enemy, so it was left for later.

So she did plan to fight it eventually.

Well, if you leave it unattended, it is only natural for someone else to take it.

“Kyui kyui.”

“Who is Chocolat? Ah, your senior Harpy Queen.”

“Gyui!?”

The Harpy Queen was shocked upon learning of Chocolat’s existence.

“Kyui!”

“She seems to be at this mansion right now. At the training grounds.”

“Kyu!”

When I answered where Chocolat was, she ran off, apparently saying, “I’ll make it clear which of us is superior.”

“The other harpies, follow your senior’s instructions…”

“Kyui!” x21

All the harpies except the Harpy Queen obediently followed instructions and were led away by the summoned harpies.

And so, small amounts of harpy eggs began circulating in Izumo Wa and Narunka Kingdom as well, of course via the Advance Company.

Apparently, there were fierce negotiations with major trading companies over harpy eggs, but that is a story for another time.

After a while, Chocolat entered the room carrying the new Harpy Queen.

The newcomer was battered and completely limp.

“Master, what is this thing? It suddenly appeared and challenged me, so I lightly dealt with it…”

It really did seem “light” as despite looking battered, the damage was not severe.

It seemed Chocolat had learned to hold back without me noticing. Impressive.

“Kyu…”

“Who are you calling old!? You little fledgling!”

The new Harpy Queen was not even a month old.

From the perspective of the four-hundred-year-old Chocolat, she was nothing but a baby.

A harpy calling someone a fledgling… was this a place where it was okay to laugh?

“It is a monster I tamed. I went to Ende Mountain to tame harpies, and she was there, so I tamed her too.”

“Kyu!?”

“‘I was just an extra!?’ you say? Of course. Master already has me.”

Well, I could not just tame harpies and then kill a Harpy Queen.

And Harpy Queen eggs are priceless luxury items, far too valuable to kill her.

“I do have complaints about Master going out of his way to tame another Harpy Queen when you already have me, but… Since she has already been tamed, it cannot be helped. I cannot say to kill her now.”

“Once I add someone as a subordinate, there is no way I would do that.”

“Kyui.”

It sounded like she was saying, “Thank goodness.”

“So, what do you plan to do with her?”

“She seems newly born and lacking in experience, so for a while she’ll train and study at the mansion or labyrinth. Chocolat, as her senior Harpy Queen, can I ask you to educate her?”

There could be no better instructor than a senior of the same species.

“Understood. I will train her as one of my subordinates for a while. …However, offering eggs to Master is my job.”

“Kyu!? Ky-kyui!”

“‘Let me have a turn once every three days’, you say? Do not get carried away. If you want that, be more useful to Master than I am.”

“Kyu!!!”

The new Harpy Queen shouted, “I will absolutely not lose!!!” as she was taken away by Chocolat.

After that, I gave the Harpy Queen a name. Her name is Moka.

The tea party continued peacefully after that.

Sakuya probably meant “hospitality” as something of a joke from the start.

Honestly, I did not feel like I was being entertained.

“A lot of time has passed. It is almost time to wrap things up…”

“Yes. Then shall we call them in?”

Cattleya nodded at Sakuya’s words and left the room.

Checking the destination on the map… I see. This really was a noble-like tea party.

After a short while, over a dozen maids entered the room.

They all carried instruments. Yes, they were the house music ensemble.

The ensemble, composed of interesting members such as their leader, the former duke’s daughter Fille, Mira who returned from vampire to human, and a former assassin, was currently active around Estea.

Thanks to Fille’s talent, it seemed all members had achieved a high level of performance skill (secondhand information).

They were now said to be the best ensemble in Estea and earned quite a lot.

After all, music appreciation is a noble pastime…

Despite royalty from various countries being present, none of the ensemble members looked nervous as they began to play.

It had been a while since I listened to their music calmly, and it was clearly different from before.

Previously, the music had been centered entirely around Fille, and the others’ sounds were merely decoration to highlight her.

The gap in ability had been too large, so only Fille’s playing stood out.

But that was no longer the case.

There was harmony as a whole, while still clearly placing Fille at the center.

She was still above the others, but the distance between them had clearly narrowed.

It was no longer “Fille’s recital” but a true “ensemble performance.”

So, to sum up this impression in one phrase… “It was very good.” That is a grade-school-level review.

When the performance ended, the ensemble exited to loud applause.

Finishing a tea party with a concert was quite tasteful.

“Well then, since the performance is over, shall we conclude?”

“Yes. Everyone, thank you for gathering today despite your busy schedules.”

Sakuya and Cattleya moved to close things out.

“It was fun.”

“I want you to invite me again. This was my first time having friends my age.”

“Big Sister, please do not publicly announce such embarrassing circumstances.”

“S-Sorry, you know.”

The twins from Izumo Wa made a sad declaration.

“W-Well, it is not easy for royalty to make friends their own age…”

“Yes. There are close retainers, but friends… Guh…”

“I-I have Sakura-chan, after all.”

Stray bullets hit Cattleya, Rouge, and Sakuya. Only Sakuya held her ground.

As Cattleya said, it is only natural for royalty not to have close friends.

Rena and Mia quietly averted their eyes.

You too, huh…

“So human royalty cannot even make friends.”

“That is sad.”

The unconcerned ones were the two dragonkin.

Even though they were clan head candidates, they seemed to have normal friendships.

Wait, now that I think about it, I had never heard about Dora’s friendships…

That would probably lead to a sad answer, so I stopped thinking about it.

“Now that I think about it, I do not really have friends outside of Onii-chan-related people either…”

Earlier she had said Sakura was her friend, but thinking calmly, Sakuya could not come up with anyone else and slumped her shoulders.

Thus, all the non-inhuman royalty became dejected.

“S-So, today had a strong social aspect, but from now on, I would like to hold tea parties that go a bit deeper into each country’s circumstances. Will everyone participate?”

Regaining her composure, Sakuya asked the participants.

“Of course, you know. I will actively participate in gatherings with friends.”

As if agreeing with Tooru, the others nodded.

Perhaps the earlier declaration of having no friends had hit hard.

“Lastly, we will give today’s tea sweets as souvenirs…”

“Is that true!?”

Before Cattleya could finish, Rena leaned forward.

“Y-Yes. We will give each person one small bag.”

“…Could I have two?”

“Please refrain.”

Rena collapsed to her knees on the spot.

Our maids cooking and sweets were very effective on royalty.

As the tea sweets were distributed and the gathering broke up, Sakuya spoke to me.

“Onii-chan, did you have fun today?”

“Yeah, it was quite fun.”

“Good. Then it was worth inviting you.”

It was a type of relaxation I was not used to, but it was nice once in a while.

Surrounded by beautiful princesses from various countries, enjoying the finest sweets, and listening to Estea Kingdom’s top-level music… That was quite a luxury.

While eating dinner at the mansion, Mio and Sera returned from their outing.

Sera had gone to test knight equipment for the Elegant Divine Kingdom, and Mio had gone to hunt monsters to test her newly mythic-class bow.

They had defeated enemies smaller than the Yellow Dragon, but still significant ones.

“Welcome back. How was the equipment?”

“Yes, it was very easy to use. It felt a bit light, but I got used to it quickly.”

Since Sera normally used heavy equipment, she was not used to light weapons.

Still, it was just a matter of getting used to it, and she seemed to have already adapted.

“And the armor?”

“I had Mimi adjust it several times to fit my body. After that, there was no discomfort at all.”

“No problems with sword or armor, then. Next is Mio.”

When I prompted her, Mio nodded.

“Mio-chan’s was exactly as expected. The auto-tracking was completely broken.”

“It was amazing. From outside the forest, she wiped out monsters inside the forest, without causing any damage to the forest itself.”

“That is impressive. If I tried to do something similar, the forest would definitely be gone.”

From outside the forest, exterminating only the monsters inside without damaging the forest.

For me, the ‘without damaging the forest’ part is the problem.

“I surprised myself doing it. I recommend it for annihilation battles.”

“Dragon hunts in the Dragonkin Sanctuary and demon hunts in Eldia Royal Capital already make annihilation battles feel kind of finished…”

“Yeah, it is a bit late…”

Mio slumped her shoulders.

There would be opportunities for annihilation battles eventually.

But would there be anything comparable to “an army of over a thousand demons” or “a horde of over ten thousand dragons” again? I doubted it.

“W-Well, if there is an annihilation battle, Mio-chan will do her best, so please count on her.”

“Yeah, I am looking forward to it.”

Even outside annihilation battles, the effect would not be wasted, so I had high expectations for Mio’s future.

Still, the combination of map and auto-tracking was way too suited for assassination.

Of course, I had no intention of making Mio do that…

“Hm? Looking closely, why is Myao rubbing against Master’s leg?”

Mio noticed Myao at my feet.

“Well, after I fluffed her for a while, she would not leave me…”

I could not bring a cat-like creature to a tea party, so I had pried her off then, but otherwise she had been clinging to me constantly.

It looked like there were heart marks floating in her eyes.

Mio approached Myao and reached out her hand.

“Come here, Myao-chan. Here is Master.”

“Myaun…”

However, Myao swatted her hand away with her tail.

“‘Let me stay like this a bit longer’ she says. Right?”

“Right?”

Mio muttered with a look of despair.

“I have been cuckolded!”

Mio’s extremely rude shout echoed through the mansion.

After that, Mio begged on her knees, so I lightly intimidated Myao and adjusted things so she would see me as “someone she loves but fears.”

She still rubs against me sometimes, but not excessively.

Leisurely Day 17.

Two days after the tea party, Sakuya contacted me to say she would be departing for the Elegant Divine Kingdom.

It seemed the leisurely days were over.

## **127.5: Latina’s Battle Diary**

**AN:** This is really just a very short side story.

This is actually a typo-correction update, but the main story is a bit stuck right now, so I will fix things all together later.

Making corrections when I have no mental leeway is a burden, after all…

For reference, I am currently writing the latter part of Volume 9.

I have a condition where I die if I do not have at least one volume worth of buffer.

---

○ Month × Day

I had been keeping records of my battles for some time, but due to the effects of my berserk state, I lost my belongings, and along with them my previous diary. Because of that, I have decided to start keeping a diary again from scratch.

The purpose of this diary is to record the details and results of my battles, and to make use of them next time.

I have become Jin-dono’s servant and will be living in a residence within the Castal Kingdom. It seems there are many formidable warriors in this residence, so it should be a valuable learning experience.

○ Month □ Day, Morning

The first person I fought after coming to this residence was a girl named Tiramisu.

She did not even flinch after taking my attacks, and her rough fighting style of immediately counterattacking after being struck threw me off completely. When an opening appeared, I took a single hit, lost consciousness and was defeated.

She could not properly respond to \<Shukuchi>, but when I panicked at the lack of damage and my attacks became sloppy, she took advantage of it beautifully.

My lack of stamina and concentration has been an issue since before, so I would like to continue focusing on improving those. I would also like to have a trump card for dealing with opponents who have extremely high defense.

That aside, I wonder why Tiramisu-dono is so incredibly tough despite her appearance?

It seems her main profession is party-based combat against monsters, but in battles against people (I am a monster, but still), she apparently fights in the previously described manner, taking advantage of her sturdy body.

She dislikes Jin-dono seeing her fight like that, so we ended up being taken to an unfamiliar arena.

She is a powerful opponent, but not one I felt was absolutely impossible to defeat.

Among everyone I have fought so far, the only ones I thought I could never defeat no matter how much I grew were Jin-dono and Maria-dono. That is precisely why they are worthy of my absolute devotion.

○ Month □ Day, Afternoon

Today, I fought a female monster named Tsukiyo.

Apparently, she was on her way to take a bath after receiving Jin-dono’s affection.

I said that I also wanted to receive his affection, but I was told it would not work since I am a vampire. I do not understand.

She looked like a strong opponent, so I somehow managed to persuade her to give me a mock battle.

It was an unbelievably fierce fight. My consciousness was hazy, and I cannot remember the details of the battle, but I clearly remember just how overwhelming it was.

When I realized what had happened, I alone was sprawled out flat on my back.

I probably lost.

Strangely enough, the clothes that I thought had been torn to shreds during the fight were completely restored.

When I woke up, Tsukiyo-dono was just returning to the room after finishing her bath. I think we fought for about thirty minutes, but only around forty minutes had passed. Tsukiyo-dono must be a fast bather.

○ Month △ Day, Morning

Today, I fought a girl named Cynthia.

At first glance, she looked like a maid you would often see around the residence, but her ability was high enough that my instincts reacted to it. I find it interesting that appearances and actual strength do not match at all in this residence.

Cynthia-dono’s fighting style was the same as mine, barehanded combat.

It seems she previously focused on staff techniques, but recently she has been in the middle of exploring unarmed combat.

She spends most of her time fighting monsters in the labyrinth, and does not seem accustomed to fighting humanoid opponents.

Perhaps because of that, there were some awkward moments in the early stages, but her growth rate during combat was terrifyingly high. The same trick did not work twice, and even my reliable first move was dodged with frightening reaction speed.

Despite facing a person, I felt as if I were fighting a wild beast. She is a truly frightening girl.

The result was a double knockout due to a mutual strike. I barely managed to secure a draw by using my trump card, \<Dragon Blood Awakening>. Considering that growth rate, I probably would not be able to win if we fought again next time.

○ Month △ Day, Afternoon

In the afternoon, I fought a young adventurer named Claude.

I was surprised when I heard about it before the fight, but it seems Claude-dono has fought my father before.

Hearing that Claude-dono was one of the four people who defeated my father made my expectations rise whether I wanted them to or not.

The sword Claude-dono uses is a wooden sword for mock battles that Jin-dono brought, so there is no risk of accidentally killing someone. I have also been instructed to use the skill \<Holding Back>, so there is no chance that either of us will die.

He said that even if someone did die, it would be fine, but what on earth does that mean?

Claude-dono used a straightforward tactic that is rare among the warriors in this residence. He deflected attacks with his shield and struck with his sword when an opening appeared.

It was a good experience, since opponents who can use \<Shukuchi> like myself are rare. \<Shukuchi> creates a momentary gap when the scene one is seeing suddenly switches, even if only for an instant. We were able to have a tense battle where we aimed for that opening against each other.

When I tried to decide the match by using \<Dragon Blood Awakening>, Claude-dono looked as though he had steeled his resolve as well. Before I knew it, I was face-down on the ground.

Just like my fight with Tsukiyo-dono, my consciousness must have been cut away before I realized it.

According to what I heard later, he used a finishing move he is currently practicing. He would not tell me the details, but it seems to be a technique he is training in order to face my father alone.

He said that he wants to be able to fight on his own, rather than relying on four people.

He is a boy with truly admirable ambition.

However, why does he become like a frightened puppy only when he is in front of Jin-dono?

Month  Day

Today… Tamo… battle… (the writing is so messy that it cannot be read)

○ Month ☆ Day

There is one more person I absolutely cannot defeat now. It is Tamo-sama.

There are no plans to post on January 1. Unless passion overflows.

## **Volume 8 Characters**

**Editor’s Note:** Title is different from previous ones because of NU (v8 Characters vs V8).

**AN:** Because the chapter theme focuses on subordinates, there are relatively few new characters.

---

Main story only. In principle, only people whose names are explicitly shown are included. Skills are excluded.

Information that is not explicitly stated is excluded.

**Protagonist Side**

Name: Ayano

Gender: Female

Age: 0

Race: Gray Person (Otherworlder) x1024

Title: Transferee

Notes: One of the Gray People residing within Aya. Because they share memories and the like, they are effectively the same person. Since there was an opportunity, she was introduced as a character. She is just as fond of Jin as Aya is, and takes every chance to appeal to him. Her strongest skill-type ability is \<Sewing>, and her technique surpasses that of professional clothing maids. She appeared in order to assert that personalities other than Aya exist among the Gray People, so her future appearances are undecided. Even so, compared to the other 1022 who do not even have names, she is better off.

Name: Latina (Reappearance)

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Vampire

Title: Jin’s Familiar

Notes: A vampire who appeared in Volume 6. She was defeated by Maria, fell for her strength, and was heading toward Castal. Along the way, in the Atto Confederation, the curse mark of \<Greed> manifested. In a berserk state, she was defeated by Jin and ended up falling for him as well. She seems to have a tendency to fall in love with those who defeat her by an overwhelming margin. Currently, she is in love with Jin, Maria, and Tamo-san. Even if she fought Sera, the outcome would likely be the same, but Sera has not accepted Latina’s challenge.

Name: Myao

Gender: Female

Age: 0

Race: Young Divine Beast

Title: Mio’s Familiar

Notes: A monster tamed by Mio that looks like a dog and also like a cat. At present, it is pitifully weak. It is a late-bloomer type monster, and may eventually become a Final Trial-class existence… perhaps. On the other hand, there also seems to be a route where it becomes a guardian of humanity, and depending on how it is raised, it has the potential to transform into anything. Humanity’s future has been entrusted to Mio. It has been completely knocked out by Jin’s fluffiness, so the possibility of it becoming a Final Trial is quite low. Also, in the unlikely event that it does become a Final Trial, Jin would probably start thinking about whom to grant the \<Transcendence> skill to. There is no mercy.

Name: Erincia (Reappearance)

Gender: Female

Age: 22

Race: Human

Title: Labyrinth Guardian, Jin’s Property

Notes: A knight of the Kingdom of Estea who appeared in Volume 3. She was betrayed by nobles of the city of Lyria, nearly died within the labyrinth, and was saved by a Labyrinth Guardian, becoming one herself. Without meeting Jin, she entered into a political marriage, and at the point she became a Labyrinth Guardian, it was discovered that she was pregnant, leading to quite an exciting life. That a character once nicknamed the “Iron Maiden” is pregnant is ironic.

Name: Rena (Reappearance)

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Human

Title: Princess of the Kingdom of Narunka, Jin’s Slave

Notes: A princess of the Kingdom of Narunka who appeared in Volume 4. At the time of her appearance, her name was not explicitly stated. At that time, she had become a living doll due to Tsukiyo’s \<Brainwashing Arts>, resulting in a horrific scene where she convulsed while naked and smeared in excrement and urine.

Name: Mia

Gender: Female

Age: 5

Race: Human

Title: Former Princess of the Kingdom of Eldia, Jin’s Slave

Notes: The sixth princess of the Kingdom of Eldia, who became Jin’s slave in Volume 7. One of the surviving members of the Eldia royal family, she is now being educated by the maids under Jin’s command. Because the Kingdom of Eldia has magical tools that can only be used by royalty, it was judged necessary to secure a certain number of royals. There is a rumor going around that “Jin likes royalty (in the sense of making them his subordinates),” and for the rough reason that it is better than not having any, she was dressed in princess-like attire and made to participate in a tea party.

Name: Moka

Gender: Female

Age: 0

Race: Harpy Queen

Title: Jin’s Familiar

Notes: The Harpy Queen who was the lord of Mount Ende. After Chocolat and the others disappeared, there was no Harpy Queen for a while, but when Jin went to the Gray World, the monsters of Mount Ende were exterminated to secure status values, and she manifested as an extermination bonus. Her battle scenes were entirely cut, and she became Jin’s familiar, but like Chocolat, she seems to be in love with Jin. As befits a Queen, she may be searching for a partner.

**Castal Kingdom**

Name: Unknown (Rude Receptionist)

Gender: Female

Notes: A foolish receptionist who was in love with Claude and neglected her treatment of Jin in order to prioritize Claude. At the point where her treatment of Jin was poor, she was completely removed from Claude’s romantic prospects. Truly, this was self-inflicted.

Name: Kuga

Gender: Male

Notes: An S-rank adventurer familiar with Claude. He appears frequently in side stories. He is in love with Lucea, and in an attempt to show off, he challenges Jin to a duel. A handsome man with real ability, he has a somewhat goofy side and a likeable personality. Although there are parts where he spins his wheels, he is an upright person, so Jin’s treatment of him is relatively gentle.

**Atto Confederation**

Name: Douglas (Berserk: Pride)

Gender: Male

Age: 711

Race: Dark General

Notes: A former human who became a monster through forbidden power. The black armor is not worn, but is almost fused with his body. He bares his fangs at the Atto Confederation with completely misguided vengeance, but is slain by the monster mercenary group. Through the curse mark of \<Pride>, he is able to manipulate monsters and people. That he originally intended to carry out his revenge alone, yet the curse mark he obtained granted the ability to create puppets, is one form of irony.

Name: Lucifer

Gender: Indeterminate

Age: 10529

Race: Demon God

Notes: One of the Final Trials, a demon god who appears after the Seven Deadly Sins relay ends, ruling over all sins. His goal is purely the extinction of all life. Both his ideology and abilities are extremely vicious, and he is a disaster-class monster on a national scale. When facing Jin and his group, he ends up looking like an insignificant opponent, but he has enough power to easily destroy an ordinary great kingdom. Throwing anti-magic at a magic-specialized enemy is fun. However, Sera’s raw strength does not come across.

Name: Titaniel

Gender: Female

Age: 23204

Race: Great Spirit

Title: Spirit Queen

Notes: The Great Spirit who governs all attributes and space, and the queen of spirits. She basically thinks only about the spirits in the Spirit Realm, and has no consideration whatsoever for life other than spirits. She was designated a harmful existence by Jin, and was ultimately absorbed by Rain. As a result, all of her skills were transferred to Rain. Unlike other Great Spirits, there was no benefit in reconstructing her and making her a dependent, so Rain is leaving her alone.

**AN:** As a characteristic of the work, most named characters face only two choices: becoming subordinates or dying.

In that sense, Mr. Kuga is a rare case.

## **128: Carriage Journey and Fake Bandits**

**AN:** Volume 9 begins.

I have already finished writing through to the end of this volume, so it will not stop partway through.

---

After receiving word from Sakuya that she would be departing for the Eldant Theocracy’s leaders’ conference, we (+ Vega) decided to transfer to the city closest to the border with the Kingdom of Sanokia, at the northernmost edge of the former Kingdom of Eldia.

From the former Kingdom of Eldia (now Eldia Territory), the Kingdom of Sanokia lies to the north, and going even farther north brings you to the Elgant Theocracy.

The shortest route between Eldia Territory and the Elgant Theocracy is a carriage route that cuts straight through a forest in the Kingdom of Sanokia. Normally it takes two weeks by carriage, but using this route reduces it to one week.

This time, we will be taking the forest route. There is some risk since it means traveling through monster territory, but with us accompanying them, the danger should be reduced to the absolute minimum.

Ideally, going all the way to the Elgant Theocracy on a Lesser Wind Dragon would be the fastest option, but according to Sakuya, you cannot just fly over other countries like that.

So, we traveled by Lesser Wind Dragon as far as this city closest to the Kingdom of Sanokia, then continued by carriage through Sanokia toward the Elgant Theocracy.

“Alright then, let’s go meet up with Sakuya.”

“Yeah!”

《Yeah!》

The younger ones are as energetic as ever.

At present, Sakuya is preparing for departure at the lord’s manor in this city.

Naturally, we could not just transfer directly into the lord’s manor, so we decided to use an Advance Trading Company branch as an intermediate transfer point.

Well, the one managing the lord’s manor is our maid, so even if we did transfer directly, there would be no one to complain about it.

Walking through a city that, as a defeated nation, naturally lacks vitality, we head toward the lord’s manor.

You wouldn’t get lost if you looked at the map, but a company staff member guides us anyway.

Six carriages were lined up in front of the lord’s manor.

From what Sakuya told me beforehand, the number of participants in this leaders conference was reduced as much as possible. Excluding Sakuya herself, only five key figures would be accompanying her.

Including guards and attendants, the total group would be under fifty people. Considering this is a royal journey, that is an awfully small number… normally.

A: Even at the meeting held in Castal, there were voices saying the numbers were too small. However, once Sakuya said, “Gene and his companions will be accompanying us” those opinions faded away. In fact, people argued that if the numbers were too large, Gene would not be able to protect everyone, and the trend shifted toward reducing the number of attendants.

Am I trusted a little too much by Castal’s key figures?

A: Yes. The policy is to leave Sakuya entirely in Gene’s hands.

That is a remarkably casual way to treat the queen of a major power.

When we enter the grounds of the lord’s manor, the maids working inside notice us and immediately bow.

“Welcome.”

As an aside, one of the maids who bowed just now is the lord governing this city and also holds a noble rank. She is that infamous slave-maid noble.

Being guided by the maids through the grounds, we spot Sakuya approaching us.

“Ah, big brother. Perfect timing. We’re about to depart, so could you change into your knight gear?”

“Yeah, got it.”

“I suppose I should as well.”

“I’ve prepared maid outfits for Sakura-chan and the others.”

“Thank you very much, Sakuya-chan…”

Sera and I will wear the “Silver Knight” set and act as guards, while the others will accompany Sakuya as maids.

This is the first public unveiling of Sakura’s and Dora’s maid outfits.

We split up by gender and head to the changing rooms.

I ask the maids to help me put on my armor. Doing it alone is a pain.

“How does it look…?”

《How is it?》

After regrouping, Sakura and Dora, now in maid outfits, ask for my opinion.

Is saying that maid outfits suit them actually a compliment?

《Mio, should I praise them here?》

When I am not sure, I ask Mio.

After all, Mio has the longest history of being a girl among us.

《Huh, you’re asking me now!? Well, fine, since you’re the master… Yes, you should praise them. They asked “How is it?” so of course they want to be praised.》

“Yeah, it suits you.”

Taking Mio’s advice, I immediately compliment the two.

“I’m glad…”

《Yay!》

As an aside, the maid outfits the four of them are wearing are the long-skirt, classic type.

Obviously, royal attendants wearing miniskirt maid outfits would make no sense.

Another aside: Vega is wearing a secretary-like suit, so she stays as she is. She is participating not as a maid, but as a secretary, so there is no issue.

“It’s been a long time since we wore maid outfits.”

“Indeed. We leave that to the professionals now.”

Mio and Maria used to wear maid outfits before, but since the number of maids increased, they almost never do anymore.

Since they are not doing serious maid work, it feels awkward wearing the same outfit next to real, professional maids. Cosplaying next to the real thing takes a lot of nerve.

This time, they seem to have accepted it as simply playing a role.

“Looks like everyone’s ready. Then shall we board the carriages?”

“By the way, what about Castal’s key figures? They don’t seem to be in the manor…”

I ask as Sakuya starts heading toward the carriages.

I checked the map, but right now only maids and Sakuya are in the manor.

“Master, it looks like they’re heading this way now.”

“Ah, you’re right.”

Prompted by Mio, I check the map and see a group that looks like them approaching, led by maids.

“We were working on the assumption of your abilities, big brother. People not directly involved were waiting elsewhere. Preparations are complete, and since you arrived, we had them called over.”

“Then should I switch to more knight-like speech now?”

After all, Sakuya is still a queen.

Externally, we need to show respect.

“There’s no need. Everyone accompanying us is aware of who you are. I was very careful with the selection so that no one would cause trouble with you. They’re close enough that I can speak casually as well.”

“Sakuya-chan is really serious about this…”

“Of course! There is absolutely no way I want to make an enemy of my big brother!”

Sakuya nods strongly at Sakura’s comment.

Apparently, she chose people who broadly understand the situation, because it would be unbearable if some foolish noble caused trouble with me.

“I see, I understand. Then I don’t need to be overly careful?”

“Yeah. The guards and attendants were also selected from among your subordinates, so there are no issues there either.”

“Maid attendants aside, even the guards are my subordinates?”

“Yes. I decided to bring maid knights. In terms of combat power, that’s more reassuring. And in an emergency, we can also receive support related to you.”

To protect Sakuya, an important person, maids have been mixed into Castal’s knights.

They are not ordinary knights, but hold the position of Queen’s Knights, serving as Sakuya’s personal guard, and their abilities are highly regarded… apparently.

Incidentally, this is the first time they have guarded Sakuya, but I am also a Queen’s Knight.

“There’s no way they’d cause trouble with big brother…”

“For you, Sakuya-chan, that second point is the more important one, right…?”

“Of course, Sakura-chan!”

Sakuya nods vigorously at Sakura’s words.

Well, if you surround yourself with insiders, the chances of unnecessary trouble drop to zero.

After a short while, the key figures in question arrive at the lord’s manor.

Four middle-aged men and one woman in her late twenties.

One of the middle-aged men notices Sakuya and me and approaches.

“Knight Gene. This is our first time greeting each other directly. I am Finance Minister Rudolf. Thank you for accepting the duty of guarding Her Majesty the Queen.”

Minister Rudolf clearly was not treating me as a mere knight.

After all, a minister would never thank a knight for guarding his own queen…

Although he said this was our first meeting, it is not actually the first time I have met Minister Rudolf.

When I was doing paperwork in Castal, he greeted me, and we exchanged a few words.

He is the minister who addressed me with honorifics, the one who punched a foolish noble in the stomach. That description might be more recognizable.

A: He is also the leading supporter of marriage between Sakuya and Master.

What…?

“There’s no need to thank me. I was deeply involved in the invasion of the Kingdom of Eldia myself. I can’t exactly ignore it. Guarding Sakuya is just a side job.”

“Eh? My protection is the side job?”

“Yeah, a side job.”

Sakuya muttered that in her usual tone, but since none of the key figures reacted, it seems clear they are people she can speak to without the usual royal speech.

“Even so, as the guard of Her Majesty Queen Sakuya, there is no one more reassuring than you. We are truly grateful.”

“Aren’t you placing too much expectation on me?”

“After seeing you display that level of ability, I think it would be difficult not to.”

I am being treated completely as Shindo Jin.

Honestly, I haven’t hidden my abilities much around Castal.

I never explained them in detail, but the ministers have probably experienced strange events around them more than once.

“Well, if I’m doing it, I won’t hold back.”

“Please, we are counting on you.”

Minister Rudolf bows deeply.

After that, I receive greetings from the other four, but I will omit them.

They are familiar faces from Castal Castle. I recognize them, though there are about two whose names I do not know.

All of them spoke as if they understood my true identity.

Once the greetings were finished, we boarded the carriages immediately.

It seems we are running slightly behind schedule.

There are six carriages in total: one carrying only guards; one carrying two key figures (+ guards and maids); one carrying Sakuya and us; one carrying two key figures (+ omitted); one carrying one key figure (+ omitted); and finally another carrying only guards.

Sakuya’s carriage is placed in the center to ensure safety.

“In the event of an emergency, you may abandon us. Please prioritize the safety of Her Majesty Queen Sakuya.”

That was Minister Rudolf’s statement, with the other key figures nodding behind him.

As expected from those Sakuya values highly, they are fine retainers.

Escorted by our subordinate maids, about two hours after departing the nameless city (note: it does have a name), we finally see the border with the Kingdom of Sanokia.

The reason I say “finally” after only two hours is because I could already see the border on the map before we even departed. If you can check four areas, the border comes into view.

Being told it takes two hours to reach a place you can already see on the map makes it feel excessively long.

My sense of travel speed has become completely abnormal lately.

As an aside, the horses pulling our carriage now are the ones we bought when leaving Eldia. We have not had many chances to ride in carriages recently, so they will be working hard for the first time in a while.

“It’s been a long time since I passed through here.”

“Hm? Sera, have you been here before?”

I catch Sera’s murmur as she looks out the window and ask her about it.

“Yes. I believe I passed along this road when I was sold. The scenery feels vaguely familiar.”

“Come to think of it, Sera-chan was originally from the Kingdom of Sanokia…”

As Sakura says, Sera was originally a noble daughter of the Kingdom of Sanokia, but due to the food consumption caused by the skill \<Proof of the Hero>, she was sold into slavery (an extremely obvious recap).

There are other routes from Sanokia to Eldia, but it seems this was the one Sera took.

“Ah, sorry. Did I make you remember something unpleasant?”

“No, it’s nothing for you to worry about, Master. I suspected as much, but it was not something that needed to be said.”

When I apologize, Sera shakes her head.

Looking at her expression, she does not seem bothered at all.

“It’s the same as Mio-san and Maria-san. I have no sense of belonging to that country. I am fulfilled now, so I have no interest in it, nor do I feel particularly drawn to return or avoid it.”

“Given that you don’t have any good memories, that’s only natural.”

“Even if I did have good memories, I believe they would have been ruined the moment I was sold.”

“That’s true.”

Mio and Maria nod at Sera’s words.

“To be honest, my memories from before Master bought me are becoming quite faint.”

“Oh, I get that! The events after being bought by Master were so impactful that memories from before that just keep fading away!”

“Yes, exactly. What about you, Maria-san?”

“I discarded everything I was before the moment I pledged my loyalty to Jin-sama.”

“So you didn’t forget them, you threw them away… That’s very Maria-chan.”

“Indeed…”

The three former slaves no longer seem to consider being sold into slavery as a mental scar.

In a way, these three are incredibly mentally strong.

《Masterrr, I’m hungryyy》

Along with a loud stomach growl, Dora declares her hunger.

At that point, there is no stronger assertion possible.

“It’s about lunchtime. Let’s eat near the border. Once we cross, it’ll be less than thirty minutes before we enter the forest, so it’s better to eat before that.”

At Sakuya’s suggestion, we decide to eat before crossing the border.

There’s no need to deliberately eat inside a monster-infested forest. Just leaving Tamo-san out would ensure safety, but the key figures do not know that.

We advance the carriages and arrive at the border.

While the key figures deal with the guards, the attendants prepare the meal.

“This is… far more luxurious than I expected. Ever since I heard we would be taking the shortest route to the Elgant Theocracy, I was prepared for meager rations…”

Minister Rudolf exclaims in surprise upon seeing the prepared food.

“We have an Item Box.”

“I see. Then this level of luxury will only last until dinner at best, correct?”

Normally, food is not preserved in Item Boxes or via the \<Storage> spell.

Unlike my \<Infinite Storage>, food inside deteriorates over time.

As Minister Rudolf says, if you put food in within a city, you should finish it by dinner.

When nobles travel by carriage, they usually avoid camping outdoors and try to pass through cities.

They eat in cities as much as possible, put food into Item Boxes, and use that as provisions until the next city.

This time, we are taking a route straight through a forest.

In other words, we cannot replenish food along the way, so dinner should be the last luxurious meal…

Except that is not the case.

Do you really think I would let the quality of our meals drop?

There is no way that would happen.

“No, my Item Box is a special model, so it can maintain food freshness.”

A perfect excuse.

“You can expect meals of roughly this level while we pass through the forest.”

“I have never heard of such an Item Box… No, I will refrain from questioning further.”

Minister Rudolf looks shocked, then resigned.

That should have covered up \<Infinite Storage>, right?

A: …

For security reasons, we eat inside the carriages.

During that time, the guards rotate: those on duty stand outside, and those not guarding eat.

We eat together with Sakuya. Guarding is not our job. At this point, that goes without saying.

One of the reasons for eating inside the carriage is that Sera and I remove our helmets.

You can technically eat with just the mouth exposed, but honestly, I do not want to.

From outside the carriage, we hear voices like “This is delicious!” and “What is this incredible flavor!?”

It seems the key figures are shouting in delight at the food. It must have been far better than the food at the castle.

“Yeah, the food from your place is really good, big brother.”

“Right?”

Mio, the head cook, puffs out her chest proudly at Sakuya’s praise.

“We knew it would be a long journey, so we prepared everything together in advance. There’s enough for about a hundred people to live for a month. And of course, there’s plenty of menu variety.”

“One hundred people times three meals times thirty days… 9000 meals!?”

That is a number you do not hear every day.

A: The cooking maids under Master became very enthusiastic since he was going on an expedition.

That is a bit too enthusiastic.

Well… not having to worry about food on the journey is a good thing, so I will let it go.

Just to be sure, though, this did not affect market food distribution, right?

I do not want to hear that a city experienced food shortages because of my expedition.

A: Naturally, only internal ingredients, including those from the labyrinth, were used.

Then all is well.

“After the expedition, if there is any left, may I eat it?”

“No, you may not. Any leftovers will be preserved as emergency rations.”

“Mio-san! Please stop copying my manner of speech!?”

After finishing dessert and resting properly, we prepare to depart again.

As an aside, the key figures tried to negotiate poaching the maids who prepared the meal.

It seems their souls were stolen by the cooking. Of course, I refused.

We cross the border without incident and the carriage journey continues.

“…Do you think information leaked from somewhere?”

“What is it…? Ah, Jin-kun’s soliloquy…”

“The usual pattern. Let’s see…”

Sakura and Mio pick up on my mutter and check the map.

They really understand my behavior patterns.

“Look, it’s the normal route we didn’t take.”

Since there is nothing to hide, I give them the answer.

“Ugh, what is that group…?”

“They’re probably bandits, right…?”

One glance at the map makes it obvious: over a hundred armed individuals are lying in wait near the route that avoids the forest.

“They’re not ordinary bandits.”

《Prey?》

“Not in that sense either.”

In Dora’s mind, bandits seem to equal prey.

Ah, that is the result of my education…

“Their equipment is not appropriate for bandits.”

“Yes. Standardized, high-quality equipment… Without a doubt, military or knight order gear.”

As expected from combatants, Sera and Maria notice immediately.

The equipment is uniform and high-grade, far beyond what common bandits would have.

Their concealment is also clearly disciplined.

They are almost certainly assassins. Knights or soldiers disguised as bandits, without a doubt.

“Should we assume information leaked and they set up an ambush?”

“Hmm, there aren’t many routes from the former Kingdom of Eldia to the Elgant Theocracy, so maybe they predicted the route and prepared an ambush?”

“Master. Sakuya’s assessment is correct. There are individuals among the bandits who were hiding in the city earlier. Since you did not send out an advance party, they planned to attack along the way.”

Vega answers our questions.

When speaking so everyone can hear, the terminal voice is clearer than Alta’s telepathy.

When wealthy nobles travel by carriage, they sometimes send advance parties to secure safety.

Apparently, the plan was to hide while the advance party passed, then attack the main group.

Since we did not send an advance party, the infiltrators rushed ahead to relay information, and the bandit group prepared the ambush.

“Even so… that is a spectacular waste of effort.”

“Indeed… To ambush on a route we are not even taking…”

Yes, their actions are completely futile. Because we are not taking that road.

“Well, normally you wouldn’t expect royalty to cut straight through a monster-infested forest. Without you, big brother, we would never choose that route…”

Thinking normally, you would not expect a royal carriage to pass through monster territory.

Conversely, the fact that they did not know means the information did not leak from Castal.

It must be someone from another country that knew about the leaders’ conference.

“Master. They are soldiers of the Kingdom of Granz, located east of the Elgant Theocracy. Some of them are registered as nobles of the Kingdom of Granz.”

Naturally, the one who answered was Vega.

“I’ve never gone north of Eldia at all, so I have no idea what kind of country it is.”

I avoided the Eldia region until the war started, so I have no information on the northeastern countries.

I am extremely indifferent to things that do not interest me.

“Master. The Kingdom of Granz is smaller than Castal and Estea, with no notable characteristics or history. Recently, their king passed away, and a nine-year-old prince ascended the throne. Since we did not dispatch subordinates there, that is the extent of our information.”

“A decorative king, maybe… or perhaps a demon plot.”

Choosing a nine-year-old prince because he is convenient for those around him is one possibility.

Another is demonic interference.

The demon impersonation incident involving Sakuya in the Kingdom of Castal is still… well, not exactly recent anymore.

“That’s the successful example of the Castal plot, right? Ugh, this hits close to home…”

“Without Jin-sama, Castal would not have escaped unscathed.”

“Yeah, seriously, all thanks to big brother.”

Sakuya grimaces bitterly, having personal experience with this.

“But what would the demons gain by taking control of the Kingdom of Granz?”

“If I recall correctly, the Kingdom of Granz borders the Elgant Theocracy, does it not? Could this be an attempt to repeat what they tried with Castal and Eldia?”

Sera, remembering the geography, offers an opinion.

The demons plan was to use Castal’s high-level adventurers to invade Eldia.

Now, most Heroes are in the Elgant Theocracy, so controlling a neighboring country would make many things easier.

However…

“Sera. That would be difficult.”

“Oh? Why is that?”

“Sera. That is because the difference in military power between the Elgant Theocracy and the Kingdom of Granz is too large. Even without Heroes, Granz would have no chance of victory. The plan with Castal worked only because Castal had multiple S-rank adventurers comparable to Heroes.”

As Vega explains, simply reusing the Castal plan seems unlikely.

Unless demons act openly, a covert war would be unwinnable for Granz.

“Besides, would you really reuse a plan that already failed somewhere else? It feels unlucky. There might be another motive… Also, I don’t understand why the Kingdom of Granz would target us specifically.”

“If Granz has fallen under demon control, could this be retaliation? Castal slaughtered demons en masse in Eldia.”

Mio raises a sharp point.

I had not considered that.

The mysterious knight Gene killed nearly a thousand demons in Eldia.

Using Granz to retaliate by attacking us is entirely plausible.

“Alright! Since there seem to be nobles from the Kingdom of Granz among them, it will be faster to ask directly!”

“Jin-kun… what are you planning to do…?”

“Obviously, bandit hunting. Bandits within my field of view have no right to live.”

If they attack us pretending to be bandits, then treating them as bandits is only fair.

The six carriages enter the road where the bandits lie in wait.

“Attack!”

At the man’s shout, the soldiers of the Kingdom of Granz hiding nearby reveal themselves all at once.

All of them are dressed in filthy clothing, indistinguishable from ordinary bandits.

However, their movements are refined, and nearly a hundred bandit-soldiers rush toward the carriages in perfect order.

“The enemy is here! Everyone, take up arms!”

The drivers stop the horses and shout, and armed knights jump down from the carriages.

The knights block the bandit-soldiers’ attacks with shields while protecting the carriages.

They do not attack recklessly, instead buying time for more knights to disembark.

“Press the attack!”

A captain among the bandit-soldiers shouts, but they cannot break through the knights’ defense.

More and more knights emerge from the carriages, and the balance gradually turns against the bandit-soldiers.

Still, the knights barely attack at all.

“Hey… what is this…?”

When the captain mutters that, the number of knights who had emerged from the carriages already exceeded one hundred.

And more knights continue to disembark.

After a while, a knight wearing especially luxurious silver armor steps down from a carriage.

He surveys the surroundings, then declares loudly:

“Capture the women and nobles! Kill all the rest!”

“Yes!” x250

At that moment, the number of knights who had emerged exceeded 250.

---

**AN:** We proceeded safely toward the Elgant Theocracy.

Well, at the start of a new volume, something like this is bound to happen. What happens afterward? I have no idea.

+++
